an preost wes on leoden laȝamon wes ihoten he wes leouenaþes sone liþe him beo drihten he wonede at ernleȝe at æþelen are chirechen vppen seuarne staþe sel þar him þuhte onfest radestone þer he bock radde hit com him on mode and on his mern þonke þet he wolde of engle þa æþelæn tellen wat heo ihoten weoren and wonene heo comen þa englene londe ærest ahten æfter þan flode þe from drihtene com þe al her aquelde quic þat he funde buten noe and sem iaphet and cham and heore four wiues þe mid heom weren on archen laȝamon gon liþen wide ȝond þas leode and biwon þa æþela boc þa he to bisne nom he nom þa englisca boc þa makede seint beda anoþer he nom on latin þe makede seinte and þe feire þe fulluht broute hider in boc he nom þe þridde leide þer amidden þa makede a frenchis clerc wace wes ihoten þe wel couþe writen and he hoe ȝef þare æþelen þe wes quene þes heȝes kinges laȝamon leide þeos boc and þa leaf wende he heom leofliche biheold liþe him beo drihten feþeren he nom mid fingren and fiede on bocfelle and þa soþere word sette togadere and þa þre boc þrumde to are nu biddeþ laȝamon alcne æþele mon for þene almiten godd þet þeos boc rede and leornia þeos runan þat he þeos soþfeste word segge tosumne for his fader saule þa hine forþ brouhte and for his moder saule þa hine to monne iber and for his awene saule þat hire þe selre beo amen nv seiþ mid loftsonge þe wes on leoden preost al swa þe boc spekeþ þe he to bisne inom þa grickes hefden troye mid teone biwonen and þat lond iwest and þa leoden ofslawen and for þe wrakedome of quene elene was ihoten alþeodisc wif þa paris mid pretwrenche biwon for hire weoren on ane daȝe hund þousunt deade vt of þan fehte þe was feondliche stor þe duc mid ermþen atwond nefede he boten anne sune þe was mid him isund was ihoten nefede he bern no ma and þes duc mid his drihte to þare sæ him droh of kunne and of folke þe fulede þan duke of monne and of ahte þe he to þare sæ brouhte and tuenti gode scipen he guþliche fulde and þa scipen foren wide ȝeon þare wintrede sæ mid wolcnen and mid wedere heo þoleden wensiþes ant mid muchelure care heo to londe bicomen on italiȝe heo comen to londe þar rome nou on stondeþ fele ȝer under sunnan nas ȝet rome biwonnen and heuede þe duc mid his drihtfolcke widen iwalken ȝend þat wide water moni lond umberowen redes him trokeden on italiȝe he com on lond þat him was iqueme a þon londe he fund mete and he hine mid monscipe biwon and mid golde and mid gersume and he griþliche spac i þere tyure he eode alond þer þa sea wasceþ þat sond ful neh þan ilke stude þar rome nou stondeþ þe king was ihoten latin þe on þan londe wes hey wes and riche and he wes redesful mid wintre he wes biweaued swo hit wolde godd þar com and grette þen alde king and he hine feire onfeng mid allen his folke muche lond he him ȝef and mare him biheyte anlong þare sea siden and widen þare quene hit ofþouhte noþeles heo hit þolede þe king heuede ane douter þe him was swiþe deore he heo biheyte to habben to wife and after his daye al his drihliche lond for he nefde nenne sune þe sarure was his heorte þat maiden wes ihoten lauine seþen heo wes leodena quene feier wes þe wimmon and wunsum hire monnen ah turnus was ihoten þat wes of tuskanne duc þet lufede þet maiden and hire monscipe bed þat he heo wolde habben to heiȝen are quene þa com þat word to him þat was widene cuþ þat þe king latin ȝef lauine his douter to are brude for heo wes his deore bearn þa wes turnus sari and soruful on his mode for he heo heuede swiþe ilofed and lufþing hire biheite weorre makede turnus mid teonen he wes idrefed wiþ he nom an feiht þat wes feondliche strong hond wiþ honde fuhten þa heȝe men teone wes on compe þar turnus feol mid mechen toheawen his monscipe wes þe lasse nom lauine leofliche to wife he wes king and heo quen and kinelond heo welden inne griþe and inne friþe and freoliche loueden seoþen lauine heuede inomen and þa leodene biwnnen he makede enne stronge castel mid starke ston walle lauine hehte his leuemon þene castel he clepede lauinion þat wes for hire worþscipe wel þat he hire uþe feour winter he heuede þat wif mid wrþscipe to welden after þa feourþe ȝere he was dead his freonden hit ofþuhten heuede lauine þa quene kinebearn on wombe þa quen þerefter sone ænne sune hefde to froure for æþelen he wes ihoten his broþer þe mid his fader com from troie mid muchele worscipe þis kinebearn biwiste wes þes childes broþer ah heo nefden noht ane moder his moder wes ihoten creusa kinges dohter þe his fader in troie forleas inne þane fehte his feon heo him binomen heold þis drihliche lond daiȝes and ȝeres and he makede ane heȝe burh albe lingoe wes ihaten þa burh wes wel iȝarwed binnen lut ȝearen he ȝef heo his stepmoder for þon lofe of his broþer and lauinion þene castel and muchel lond þarto þe his fader hefde imaked þe wile þe he on liue wes þis lond he hire lende þat come hir lifes ende ah heo nom þene þe heo tolden for godd þe mid his ferde brohte from troie in albe lingue he hine sette ah sone he þonene iuatte forþ aȝein mid þan winde þe feond hine ferede þe kene þe wes i kinges stude four and þritti winter he heold þat lond and þa leoden mid blissen þa com his lifes ende laþ þah him were his broþer þe wes lauine sune he bitahte al þat lond þat heore fader hefde on hond ænne sune heuede þe wes ihaten þis child hefde his eames nome ah lut ȝer he leouede for his ahne sune seoþen hine sceat to deaþe þa þis child was feir muche þa luuede he a maide þeo was lauine mawe mid darnscipe he heo luuede hit iwerþ þere swa hit deþ wel iwere þat þeos ȝunge wiman iwerd hire mid childe þe ȝet leouede þe on þan londe was duc vnderȝetene weren þe þinges þat þeo wimon was mid childe þa sende þe wes lauerd and dux after heom ȝend þat lond þe cuþen dweomerlakes song witen he wolde þurh þa wiþercraftes wat þing hit were þat þeo wimon hefde on wombe heo wrpen heore leoten þe scucke wes bitweonen heo funden on þen crefte carefule leoþes þet þeo wimon was mid ane sune þat wes a selcuþ bearn þat boa sculde fallen fader and his moder þorh him heo sculden deiȝen and þene deaþ þolien and þurh his ealdren deþ idreuen out of londe and umben longne first mid wrþscipe comen liþen þo leoten weren iworpen and swa hit al iwearþ þa þe time com þat þe cnaue wes iboren in þere burhe þa brude dead iwearþ þe child wes iboren isund to baluen his moder þat child was ihaten þat bearn nas nowit feie þis child leuede and wel iþei and þeweas hit luuede he was fiftene ȝer ald þa he to wode ferde and his fader mid him and feiesiþ makede heo funden ane heorde of heorte swiþe greate þe fader heo bieode to his aȝre unneode to his sune he heo draf himseolfue to balewe sette on his flo he wende to sceoten þat hea der and ihitte his aȝene fader þurhut þere broste wao wes þerfore wa wes him on liue þa þe fader wes on deaþe þa þat iherde his kun þe he of icumen wes þat he þe flo heuede idrawen and his fader ofslawen heo hine flemden out of þane londe and he iwende sorhful ouer seastreames into griclonde þer he his cun funde of þan folck of troye þe mid teonen wes todrefed þere quene cun heleineþes kinges sune and muchel folc of his þeoden ah al heo weren þeowe and of his aȝne kunne moni kineborene mon moni ȝer was agan seoþþen his cun hider com þa wepmen weren iwexan þa wimen wel iþowene and heore nutene neotsume weren nes i þon londe bute lutel ane wile þat alle monnen he wes leof and muchele monscipe biwon for cniht he was swiþe god þan folke to queme he was metecusti þat is monscipe steor alle monnen he was leof þe him lokeden on heo him ȝeuen gersume and feire hine gretten heo seiden him mid rede and mid stilliche runen ȝif he were swa þriste and he hit don durste þat he heom wolde leaden out of þane leoden out of þeowedome freo þat heo weoren heo hine wolden maken duc and deme ofer his folke we habbeþ seoue þusund of gode cnihten wiþouten wifmen þe noht ne cunnen of wepnen children and hinen þa ure nete sculen ȝemen for muchel we wlleþ driȝen and habben care of ure life ær we nulleþ mid frescipe faren from ure feonden alle þe weren at þisse reade biluuede þeos runen inne griclonde was a ȝung mon of þriti ȝeren ihaten of swiþe heie kunne his fader wes a gric ikoren ah his moder wes of troien iboren and heo wes a cheuese hire cheap wes þe wrse noþelas hit ilomp inne lut ȝere þat þe fader wes dead his duȝeþe he bilefde he ȝef his sune sele þreo castles and al þat ligginde lond þe þerabuten lei heuede enne broþer þe wes under wedlac iboren after þen heþene tidende þe wes in þan londe þes cniht hefde his fader lond and loþ him wes his broþer for he heold þe stronge castles þurh staþele his fader ȝefe his broþer heo him wolde binimen ah he ne mihte speden þar aros wale and win and wiþerheppes feola wes god cniht wiþ grickes he heold moni fiht ah he hefde muchele strengþe of meren his cunne of þan troyscen monnen þe weren his moder isib for þare sibelaȝe luue hem wes bitweonen hit redde mid diȝenliche runen þat þat troynisce folc mid his fulle fultume nomen þene cniht brutun and makeden hine to duke and he heora monredne mid monscipe onfeng he sende his sonde wide ȝend þane londe he heihte his folc sumunen and cumen to himseoluen wapmen and wifmen þa weoleȝen and þa weaþlen alle he heom sumunde and to wode sende bote seoue þusend kempen þa he into þane castlen dude þa lette he riden vnirimed folc biȝeoten wepnen and mete muchel wes þa neode and al þat smale monkun he dude ȝeond þea muntes and himself mid his ferde biforen and bihinden seoþen he nom to rede and to somrunen þat he an wriht makede al mid wisdome þene king he grette mid greiþlicre speche and þat wriht he him sende and þeos word seaide for þan weorldes scome and for þan muchele grome þat dardanisc kun þe we beoþ of icomene woneþ in þisse londe leode to sconde inne þeowedome þrelwerkes doþ heo beoþ togadere icumene kuþies mæȝes al swa þat ilke folc þe freoscipe wole biwinne heo habbeþ idemed þat ich am duc ofer heom ich abbe i min castlen seoue þusend kempen ich habbe in þane munten monie þusund leouere heom his to libben bi þan woderoten al swa þat wilde swin þat wroteþ ȝeond þan grouen þane heo þine þeowedomes lengre iþolien ȝif heo wlleþ frescipe biwinnen ne wndre þou nawiht þerfore heo biddeþ þe mid freonscipe þat þu heom ifreoie þes word he sendeþ al swa þe wriht þe seiþ þat heo moten wonien werswa heo wolleþ inne griþe and in friþe and heo wlleþ þe freonscipe don ȝif þou þis nult iþolien þe scal beon þa wrse þe king nom þat writ on hond and he hit wrodliche biheold seolcuþ him þuhte swulcere speche þa he alles spac mid þræte he spilede to wroþer heore hele habbeþ heo such werc idon mine þralles i mire þeode me suluen þretiaþ wide he sende ȝeond þat lond for he wes leoden king þat come to hirede riche men and weþlen al þat wapmoncun þa mihte beren wæpen vppen lif and uppen leomen al þes londes folc an horsen and an foten forþ heo ifusten þe king þræted brutun swa he dude þat he heom wolde biliggen mid laþen heora feonden ȝif he heom mihte biwinnen mid his woredstrencþe alle heo sculden hongien on heȝe treowen iherde seggen al swa hit soþ wæs þat þe king him towardes com mid muchelere ferde ah heo weren summe faie nom to reade þat him best was he nom his kene men þa to compe weren gode he ferde to þan wode to þan wilderne to þan ilke weie þe he ful ȝeare wuste þat þe king mid his ferde forþ sculde iwenden hefede gode cnihtes to neode þre þusund mid him ilead to þære þruppe þe king him com riden mid riche his folke heom smat on mid his grime smite isowte he þe grickes mid his grim ræsen þa grickes neoren noht warre of heore wensiþe wenden him þeo rugges flowen haȝe men heihte an flum þe nes noht feor from heom þider in iwenden moni þusunde heom com æfter and æfer he heom leide on mid sweord and mid spere al he todrof þes kinges here a londe and a watere he heom adun leaide and þe king himself fleh he iseih his frend fallen muchel folc þer was ofsclawen on moniare wisen þe king hefde ænne broþer neafde he nenne oþer wes ihoaten inne griclonde he wes heh iseih his broþer ferden hu heo iuaren weren a wætere and a londe swa heom læþest wes mid his weapnen and mid his wælkempen iwenden toward brutun to his balesiþe heo comen togadere mid greatere heorte þar he mihte bihalden þe bihalues were moni wensiþes wiþerhappes feole moni heaued moni hond fallen to foten monie þar fuhten monie flæm makeden monie þar feollen þurh heora feonþewæs þa troysse men sloȝen al þa grickes þea heo neih comen þer nom þes kinges broþer mid him he hine lædde for leof he him wes to habben he hine leatte wel witen mid wnder stronge benden and alswa his iferen þe mid him ifunden weren þat iherde þe king hit neas him noht iqueme þat his broþer wes in armliche benden þe king sende swa wide swa ileste his riche and heihte eulne mon þe mihte riden oþer gan þat heo comen mid him to þane castle of sparatin nes castel nan swa strong i þon londe of griclond he wende hit to soþe soþ þeh hit neore þat hefde þa men þe he mid fihte biwon idon into þan castle and þear heom quic heolde and himseolf þer forþ mide for þære muchele biȝæte ah dude betere read and him þa beth ilomp in þon castle he dude hende six hundred of his cnihten himself mid his fenge he to wode ferde þe king to þan castle forþ mid his ferde þer he lei abuten þarinne weren his laþe feond his ferde he sette on ælchere siden ofte heo ræsden and ræmden togadere mid stelene orde and mid starka biten mid stocken and mid stanen stalfiht heo makeden mid grickisce fure feollen þæ fæie þar was muchel blodgute baluwe þer wes riue þa cnihtes of þan castle quicliche heom wiþstoden þaet ne mihte þes kinges folc of heom fael makien ah þe king of his monnen monie þusund læs þe king wes on mode sar þat wes for his monne lure he tæh hine aȝein ane þrowe and þreateþ þene castel and þat folc þerinne þenne he hit hefde biwnnen þat he heom wolde quellen oþer quic al forbrennen he lette makien enne dic þe wes wnderliche deop abouten his ferde and feiede heo mid þornen and leai þerabuten and abat his balesiþes þe king wes swiþe wraþ and swar muchelne oaþ þat nolde he þonne faren ar his feonden feie weore i þon castle weoren monie men and muchel mete þer bihofede þe mete forþ iwat for þer fengen feole to heo nomen ænne ærendrake þe æþele wes to neode heo sende to heore læuerde þa leof heom wes on heorten heo hine gretten mid godene heore worden heo beden hine come to helpe mid allen his strengþe þe wile þe heo weren isunde þe weren his sele men hine biþohte of swlchere neode and þas word seide mid soþere heorte he deþ himselua freoma þa helpeþ his freondene swa ich wlle mine bi mine quicke liue þa wes þere a welibore mon anacletus wes ihaten mid þes kinges broþer he was itaken and þer læi inne benden him ræmde to mid grimmen his rasen bi þone toppe he hine nom alswa he hine walde ofslean and his nakede sweord leide on his necke and þas word saide þe sele niþing þou ært al dead buten þou do mine read and þi læuerd alswa bote þu min lare do ah ȝif þu wlt þu miht wel helpen inc seluen lauerd quaþ anacletus don ic wille þine lare help mine lauerd and me mid alle mire mihten do swa and þe scal beon þe bet ȝe sculen habben lif and leomen and beon mine leofe freond him swar an æþ breken þat he hit nælde þus seide þe wes cniht mid þane beste anacletus leofe freond toniht þu scalt faren a þeon time biþ best þonne men gaþ to bedde þu scalt forþ wenden to þas kinges ferde wonne þu comest to þon cnihten þat þene king biwiteþ þær þu findest seouen houndred þa hæleþes beoþ kene and þu heom clepe to and cuþliche wiþ heom spec ich am anacletus ich am mid ærmþen abroken vt of þon benden þe me heuede on idon and ȝet ich ou sigge on oþer ibrout ich habbe þes kinges broþer vt of þon quarcerne of þan qualehuse þær hin hefde idon for tomarewene he hine wolde anhon and ich hine habbe idon i þisse wude derne cnihtes fuseþ me mid leteþ slæpen þene king and fare we on sele riht al swo stille stelen swa we wolden and ich eou wlle leden forþ to mine lauerde i þon woderime þer he vnder rise liþ ȝif ȝe hine mawen bringen biforen ure kinge wel biþ him þere bringe oeu biþ þe beþ þerfore and for he is his broþer for nafþ he nenne oþer cuþ he wes þen cnihten and heo hine icneowen heo wenden þat his sawen soþe weren ah alle heo weren lease for he wes his leodene swike nis nawer nan so wis mon þat me ne mai biswiken anacletus ferde biforen þe cnihtes him fuleden ferde æfter ane bache alswa him hefde itaiht hæfde his folc biforen and bihinden wes þe wei holh and long þa clude weren stronge heom ræsde to mid richere strengþe alle togadere he heom nom nane he ne lafde summe he sloh summe he bond þa beste quike he atheold and alle he heom biwuste swa him best þuhte nom his ferde on feowre he heo todælde and he hehte alle his men monscipe biwinnen þa ȝunge and þa alde æþela iwurþen wihte walkempen on heora wiþerwinnan and an hihinga faren to þan kinge and ich forbeode heolde mine þeinen vppe þere muchele lufe þe us bitueiȝen þat nan ne beo so wilde nan swa unwitti þat word talie ne talkie mid speche ær he ihere minne horn mid græte hiue blowen for miself ich wlle teo toforen to telde þas kinges anan swa ich lihte of blonken swa ich wlle blawen anan swa ȝe hit ihereþ hende mine kempen ohtliche heom slæþ on and weccheþ heom of slepa leteþ þa grickisca gliden to grunde fallen þa feie for heo beþ vre fulle fan duden alle þa cnihtes swa heom taute and he himseolf teih biforen to telde þæs kinges of his horse he þreou his horn he vastliche bleu iherden hit troynisce and tuhten to þon gricken heo heom aweihten mid heora wæles igrure þar fluwen haueden on felde fæiþe þer feollen moni hond moni fot þe hæp wæs þe wrse moni þusend þer flowen þærmes heo droȝen and mid his cnihten þene king ifeng al ihal and al isund heihliche he cleopede ich habbe þisses folkes king fælleþ his leoden ne lete ȝe nenne quick quecchen to holte and ich wlle þesne king læden mid me seolfan þar bifeng al þat him biforen wes sparatin he aredde heh an his castel amarewen þa hit dai wes and þa niht todælde sumunde his folc heo weren his fulle freonde he heihte for his lufe al his leodeferde þat heo nomen þat wæl and wel hit biburiede inne deope seaþen setten þa deade and hit wes sone idon for monie þusend þerto fengen al þa biȝetene æhte he delde his cnihten and alle his leoue men he mid monscipe grette þa al þis wes idon þa dude he on oþer he lette an heh climben and lude clepian þat on þane daȝe amarwen come his drihtliche folc and alle his heȝe men comen to hustinge and heo swa duden blisse wes on daie þat folc com togadere guþliche cnihtes and heora lauerd spac and þus heom wiþ spelede lusteþ mine cnihtes lusteþ mine leofe men suggeþ me to runun ræd þat eou þunche ich habbe þesne leodking ileid in mine benden and his broþer alswa hit is þe bet mid us and his leoden ofslawen ihc am him þa laþere and alle his ahte iȝeuen mine æþelinge ȝif ȝe hit rædeþ ȝe beoþ mine riche men ich wulle mid swerde his heued of swippen and ȝif ȝe hit willeþ ich hine wlle spillen and ȝif ȝe me readeþ ich hine wille freoien ȝif he me ȝefeþ gersume gold and seoluer alle his maþmas wiþ þon þa he mote libben þa ansuereden æþela cnihtes summen hit weora iqueme þat heo hine sculden quellen himseolf habben þat lond and beon þere leodene king summe queþen ælles and þus þa quides eoden ȝeue us þe king and al his gold and þa maþmes of his lond ȝef us peal ȝeue us hors ȝeue us haihe scrud ȝeue us ænne ende of his kinelonde ȝeue us ȝislæs þerto and þis mei beon wel idon þer wes moni riche mon þe cuþe lutel reden weþer heom weore wnsumre to faren þe to wonien þa wile þe heo tweoneden þus clepede þet wes a riche mon þe wes swiþe wel idon wys and witful wel he hit cudde wet speke ȝe cnihtes wet speke ȝe kempen vnder eou alle nis þar nan swa god þa ȝet habbe isæid þat us is selest to don ȝif ȝe hit lusten wlle mi lauard and ȝe alle biluuien gode mine lare ich eou wlle seggen selast ræden and þa ansuerede al þat folc faihn we wllen hit iheren þa quaþ ludere stefne ȝirne we to þane kinge ȝeuen suiþe gode þat is alreforwarde þat he us ifreoie sone þarafter ȝurne we his dohter þat he heo ȝeue ure lauerde brutun to his bedde of his corne he us ȝeue swa muchel þat we beon iquemed gold and garsume and his gode hors and al his beste mætecun þe his men habbeþ and alle þa liþinde scipen þe on his londe beoþ and alle þat bihoueþ þa scipen to driuen of monnen and of wapnen þat we mawen wel faren fare uorþ ouer sæ sel þat we wrþen and liþen swa longe þat we to londe comen varen wide ȝeond þat lond and fondia þeo leoden wer us beo iqueme king þat we makien of brute ure lauerde þe is best of us and to quen þe is þis kinges dohter for ȝif we hit ȝeorneþ to wonien her mid gricken heo beoþ ure fulle feond for we beoþ ifead wiþ heom for heora kun we habbet islaȝen in eorþe heo sleopeþ we beoþ heom loaþe for heora muchele lure heo wlleþ us biwiȝelien þurh heora wiþerecraftes a swa heom beoþ iwrþ swa us wrse biþ for mid ure wepnen heora kun we aqueald habbeþ mid ure honden monie þusunde ȝif we sceoteþ to heora mæþe þat biþ ure imone deaþ ȝif we heom ilefeþ þat biþ ure muchele lure ȝif heo wel wexit heo wlleþ wonien us wel ich hit mai suggen to soþe ich hit wene nis þar nan swa heih nis þar nan swa laih þat we nabbet his freond ifelled to grunde for þon ȝif hit eow biloueþ þe wise beoþ on þonke fare we from þisse londe þa leodene us beoþ laþe al heora god we sculen nimen and lutel hem læuen wonien heo sculen unbalde for hora muchela bursten and we mæwen faren riche ȝif we ræd luuieþ for al þat god of þisse londe we sculen leden mid us and heo bilæuen wrecches and wælde heom scal fulien for þe riche haueþ muchel rum to ræsen biforen þan wrecchan þas word weoren iqueþene þeo quides weoren leoue þa he mihte ihere þe bihalues were muchel dom muchel dune muchel folkes dream and alle heo clepeden þus soþ seiþ and alle hit biluueden gode weren his lære þa letten bringen þene king vt of quarcerne and his broþer mid him beine togadere mid yrene benden biforen brutone heo him to clepeden and laþ spel him cudden heo seiden þat he sculde beon anhongen an one heȝe treowe oþer mid horsen todrawen mid droflicen vitan buten heo heom lette freo ta faren of his londe ȝeue heom al his aȝte þe he biȝeten mahte and alle his scipen gode þa floten bi sæflode and his dohter heore duc to quene þe king hine biþoute wat he don mahte sari he was on liue þæs tiþende him weren læþe of deaþ he hefde care drof he wes on mode answerede mid seorhfulle worden ȝe biddeþ mine dohter swa hende and haldeþ me inne bende and mine broþer mid ærmliche witen and mine men ȝe habbeþ isclawen and ȝeorneþ mine maþmas and mine leoue dohter to swa laþe mannes bihoue ah heo mot nede beien þe mon þe ibunden biþ eouer axe ich eow leue laþ þeh hit me were and ȝif ȝe bilæuen wolden inne mire þeoden al þridden dale mi lond ich wolde setten brutan on hond and freoien al his folc and freonscipe makien and mine dohter ȝeuen eowre duke and swa we sculden bileauen leoue mæȝes vre lif læden liþen tosumne þa ænswerede þe wes borene duke nulle we noht þis onfon ah we faren wlleþ and þu swiþe hiendliche scild þe wiþ dæþe ȝef us þat we wilniaþ ȝif þou libben wlt þe king sende his sonde ȝeond al griclonde þat me hit him to brohte alle his aihte and greiþede his scipen gode bi þan sæflode and al þat þærto bihouede hahliche ifunden alswa heo wolden heora lauerd from loþen alesen al his men duden swa þe king hehte þa scipen weoren igreþede mid gode grundfulled þe king ȝef brutun his dohter þe wes his bearn deora and al þat forward wes ilest þa fusden þa ferde wenden riht to þare sæ sela þa þeines muchel wæs þa blisse þa hafde mid him nom and into scipe lædde heo rihten heora rapes heo rærden heora mastes heo wunden up seiles wind stod an willen sixtene siþe tuenti scipen tuhten from hauene and feower scipen greate þe weren grundladene mid þat beste wepnen þa hauede heo fusden from stronde vt of griclonde heo wenden vt i wide sæ þa wilde wurþen itemede tweiȝe dawes and niht inne sæ weren þen oþer dai heo comen liþen on æuen to londe logice hatte þat eitlond leode nere þar nane ne wapmen ne wifmen buten westiȝe pæþes vtlaȝen hefden iræued þat lond and alle þa leoden ofslaȝen and swa hit wes al west and wnnen biræued ah swa monie þar waren wilde deor þat wnder heom þuhte and þa troinisce men tuhten to þon deoren and duden of þan wilden al heora iwilla to þan scipen lædden swa muche swa heo wælden heo funden i þon eitlonde ane burh swiþe stronge tohælde weoren þe walles weste weren hallen temple heo funden þar ane imaked of marme stæne muchel and mære þe wrse hit hafde to welden þerinne was an onlicnesse a wifmonnes liche feier hit wes and swiþe heih an are hæitnesse nome diana wes ihaten þe deouel heo luuede heo dude wnder craftes þe scucke hire fulste heo wes quen of alle wodes þe weoxen on eorþen a þon heþene lawen me heold heo for hehne godd to hire weoren iwoned þa wndercreftie men of þa þingen þa weren to kumen heo heom wolde cuþen mid tacnen and mid swefnen þonne heo weren on slæpe þe wile þeo on þan eitlonde wes folc woniende heo wurþeden þat anlicnes þe scucke hit onfeng hit herde siggen þurh his sæmonnen þe ær weoren on þan londe and þa lawen wusten nam twelf witiȝen þe weren his wiseste men and enne preost of his lawen þa weren on þan heþen dawen gerion hehte þe preost he was an hirede hæh he ferde to þere stowe þar diane inne stod ferde into þere temple and þa twelfe mid him and lette al his folc bilæuen þervte ana scale he bear an honde al of reade golde milc wes i þere scale and win sume dale þa milc wæs of are wite hinde þe sceat mid his honde he makede bi þon weofede a swiþe wunsum fur niȝen siþen he bieode þat weofed for his neode he clepede to þere leuedi heo wes him on heorten leof mid milden his worden he ȝirnde hire mihten ofte he custe þat weofed mid wnsume lates he halde þa milc in þat fur mid milden his worden leafdi diana leoue diana heȝe diana help me to neode wise me and wite me þurh þine wihtful craft whuder ich mæi liþan and ledan mine leoden to ane wnsume londe þer ich mihte wunien and ȝif ich þat lond mai biȝeten and mi folc hit þurhgengen makian ich wlle on þine nome mæren ane stowe and ich þe wulle huren mid wrhscipe hæȝan þus spec seoþþen he nam þe hude þa wæs of þare hinde biforen þan wefede he heo spradde swlc he leie on bedde he cnelede þarufenan and seoþþen he adun læi swa he gon slomnen and þeræfter to slepen þa þuhte him on his swefne þar he on slepe læi þat his lauedi diana hine leofliche biheolde mid wnsume leahtren wel heo him bihihte and hendiliche hire hond on his heued leide and þus him to seide þer he on slepe lai biȝende france i þet west þu scalt finden a wunsum lond þat lond is biurnan mid þære sæ þaron þu scalt wrþan sæl þar is fuȝel þar is fisc þer wuniaþ feire deor þar is wode þar is water þar is wilderne muchel þet lond is swiþe wunsum weallen þer beoþ feire wuniaþ in þon londe eotantes swiþe stronge hatte þat lond ah leode ne beoþ þar nane þerto þu scalt teman and ane neowe troye þar makian þer scal of þine cunne kinebearn arisen and scal þin mære kun wælden þas londes ȝeond þa weorld beon ihæȝed and þu beo hæl and isund þæ awoc wel wes him on life he þoute of his swefne and hou þe læfdi him sæide mid muchelere lufe he seide hit his leoden hu him imette and þa læfdi hine igrette he þonkede hire ȝeorne mid liþfulle worden he biheite hire biheste and he hit wel laste þat to hire he wolde teman and wrchen hire ane temple and on licnesse of ræde golde whenne he come to londe and æ to his liue hire willen idriȝen at hire heo nomen læue and to scipe liþden heo hefden wind heo hefden water þe heom wel ferede þritti dawes and þritti niht heo ferden efer forþriht bifore affrike heo ferden forþ and eeuer heo drowen west and norþ ouer þen lac of and ouer þen lac of bi ruscikadan heo nomen þa sæ and bi þe montaine of in þære sæ heo funden vtlawen þa kenneste þa weoren o þon dawen fifti scipen fulle þer weore feondes to feole wiþ bruten heo fuhten and fealden of his monnen ah hefde þa ouere hond þa fæie he sloh þe quike he bond þar biwon feole kunnan wunnan muchel garsum and mete his monscipe wes þa mære nefde nenne swa wreche man þat gold and pal ne dude him on þeonene he ferden forþ wel feole dawen ȝong ouer maluan æne flum suiþe long i londe al þat heo wolden þa ferden heo forþ heora færþ wes on sæle muchel ahte heo hæfden biwunnen þa comen heo to þan bunnen þa makede mid muchelen his strengþe þat weoren postes longe of stane stronge þat taken makede hærcules þat lond þe þerabuten wes swiþe brod and swiþe long al hit stod an his hond þer heo funden þe merminnen þat beoþ deor of muchele ginnen wifmen hit þunchet fuliwis bineoþe þon gurdle hit þuncheþ fisc þeos habbeþ swa murie song ne beo þa dai na swa long ne biþ na man weri heora songes to heræn hit is half mon and half fisc hit hafþ þes wurse taken fuliwis for his troye þa grickes hit biwnnan mid heora wælslahte wes heora duc seþþen atenor was dead wes a strong mon and he heuede muchele ban he wes swa kene he wes swa strong swilc hit weore an eotand þa tiþind him answerede and ich þe wulle mid fare mid mine drihtfolke and habben dale mid þe and halden þe for herre and here þe for lauerd þis feoreward was imaked heo ferden tosomne heo ferden from spaine clepede mid ludere stefne whonene beo ȝe cnihtes ȝe fareþ mid unrihte ȝe huntieþ i þes kinges friþe þerfore ȝe sculen beon fæie ȝe doþ þan kinge muchel scome þerfore ȝe sculen han grome forboden he haueþ his deorfriþ þerfore ȝe sculen liggen stif iwerþ him wroþ and wende him toȝeines and saide þas ilke word mid muchelure wreþþe cniht þu ært muchel sot þat þu swa motest ȝif þe king hit haueþ forboden ne scal him neuer beo þa bet ne nawit for his forbode nulle ich hit bileuen to nimen his heortes and his hindes and al þa deor þat ich finde þa iwreþþede þa kinges stiward of þat eard he leadde an his honde enne bowe stronge and he þene streng up braid balu com on ueste on he sette ane fla and he feondliche droh and þa fla lette gliden bi siden bleinte and þene scute biberh and towardes he leop swilc hit an leon weora and þene bowe igreap mid muchele strengþe he smot mid þon bowe þat his hæfdbon tobrec þat his blod and his brain ba weoren todascte fluȝen his iferen feondliche swiþe to þon kinge and saiden hine tiþende sære þet islawen wes þe wes his awene stiward þe king wes swiþe særi and seorhful on mode and sende his sonde ȝeond his kinelonde gaderede his ferde þer weoren men fæie þa ferde wes isumned and heo forþ fusden toward sele brutun þer he bi sæ wonede wes swiþe war for wisdome him fulede haures he sende to hirede þes kinges to witen of his farcost wher he wolde feihten þa hawres ferden and sone aȝein comen and comen to heora læuarda þer he lai bi hauene and þeos word him seiden al swa hit soþ iwarþ hal beo þu þu ert þe hexste of us nu hafþ þe king igadered his ferde muchel ferd and riche and heȝe word he spekeþ þat alle heo wullet quellen quic þat heo findeþ and þa scipen todraȝen and þa wif drenchen nulleþ heo leaue nenne of ous aliue nom al his ȝunge folc and hem to scipe fusede and alle his æhte his folc bitahte and to heom seide þe sele ȝe beoþ mine leofe men hercniaþ mine lare ne cume ȝe neauer wiþvten scipes bord ær ich ou sende sutelword wheþer ich maȝe þe ufere hond habben of þan kinge nom his cnihtes and iwende forþrihtes to þon ilke weie þer him iwised wes þer þe king walde forþ mid muchelere his ferde togadere heo comen hardliche heo onsloȝen þer wes swiþe strong feht feollen þe feie þer wes moni steap mon mid stele toswngen longe a dai leste þat feht þer feol moni god cniht com quecchen and to himseolfe hefde twa hundred mid sweorde tohewen þa brac þat sweord in his hond riht be þere hilte þa wes wroþ and þas word cleopede wa wrþe auer þene smiþ þa þe mid honden smeoþþede abuten biheold for þe bearn was abolȝen and igrap of onnes monnes honde ana wiæx swiþe stronge al þat he neh com þermid he hit aquelde þe king sette to fleonne and al þa ferde eafter and heom eafter com kenliche swiþe and heom to clepede þe unimete kempa mid þire ferde wi wolt þu fleam makian ne miht þu nawiht so fleon ȝif þu us wlt heonne fleman þu most swiþer fehten er we heonne iwenden ne ganninde ne ridinde ne durste him nan abiden þe king hefde enne þein swiþe heard he was ihaten he biheold þe heom after com hefde to iferen þreo hundred ridearen he wende onȝean sone and he ohtliche feaht nes hit noht longe þat mihte stonde for him geinde to mid his guþstrencþe he gurde on þat hæfd þat he grund sohte and he hine forsmat amidden a twa riht bi þon ribben nes þer nan swa stæþeli þat lengore mihte stonden heom himseolf atbreac he fleih ut of his londe and bilæfde his leode into france he ferde þer he freond funde to þon kaisere and to his tueolf iferen and tolde heom of þan balwe þe him hefde idon inne franse weren italde twelfe iferan þa freinsce heo cleopeden dusze pers þa weren drihtliche men kinges heo weoren icleopede þat heo ofte cuþden heo bihæihten þen kinge þat heo hine wreken wolden wreken his muchele biȝate ȝeond þat lond he gon ernen and þa tunes forbearnen and herȝede þat lond and tæh hit to his aȝre hond al þat lond he wiste and al he hit awalde swa he ferde mid his here þat he on ænne hul bicom he wes feir and heih and he hine swiþe biheold he nom ræd æt his monnen þat he wolde þar castel makian þa þe castel vp stod he wes strong and swiþe god nes hit buten lutel wile þat king com him liþen mid vnimete ferde of frenchisce folke and of alle þon londen þa leȝen into france þa þe king þene castel kennede swa swiþe wa him was þat al his wit he forlæs swiþe he fusde þiderward kene his ferde heo todælden heom atweolfa and tuȝen on alchere halue and þa troynisce men heom comen aȝein and anan leiden to þan grunden of þane freinsce þreo þusende þa freinsce weoren isturmede and noþelas heo stal makeden and heo bi niþinges beard driuen heom onȝeinwærd brutun and his kempan heo driuen into þan castle and in þera ilke uore heo fælden of his iueren and æl dai heo ræmden and resden to þan castle þat com to þere nihte þat lengre heo ne mihten i þon castle wes muchel dred a þa midniht heo nomen read þat heo wolden to þon wode senden mid alle þon folke þat he hefde on his ferde and ferden vt swa stille swa heo stelen wolden into ane þicke wode þa þer on uest wes wes i þon castle and hine wel wuste amarwen þo hit dawede and dai com to folke wes onbolȝen swa biþ þa wilde bær wenne hundes hine bistondeþ i þon wodelonde hehte his beornes don on heora burnan and heora wæpne gode for heo to feht sculden vp heo duden heora castles ȝæten and cofliche vt wenden fusden to þan feie iwerþ he feolde þa frensca on feole kunne wisen mid his aȝene honden he falde monie hundred ah he ferde to feor ut from his iueren and heo him to liþden on elchere siden mid wepnen hine wundeden and seoþþen hine slowen hine funde dead and into þane castle dude and þerinne biburiȝede bi ane stan walle þuru þan ilka turnus turs wes ihaten turuine al þat lond þurh turnus deaþe ferde ut and fusde to fihte wreken he wolde his teonen and turnus his wine leoue togadere heo comen and grundliche onslowen þer wes bil ibeat þer wes balu muchel and feht unimete fæie þer feollen þat feht wes wnder strong þa of wode com mid michelene ferde brutun to fulste wes on ane half an oþer heo letten togliden gares swiþe scarpe heo qualden þa frensce alle þa heo funden þus heo westen þat lond and slowen þa leoden nes næuer þa mon iboren ne swa wis mon icoren þe cuþe i þon daȝe tellen of þan deade hu monie þusende þer weoren ileid to grunde þa bleou and bonnede his ferde and speken togadere of feole wisdomes and funden on ræde þat heo faren wolden heo letten lude clepian and cuþen ȝeond þat ferde þat þe sele to þare sæ wolde swa heo ferden to heora scipa mid allen heora uenge and mid seoluere and bliþe liþden þa leoden þat heo on londe comen æt dertemuþe i totenes wel wes þes þa scipen biten on þat sond and al þat folc eode an lond þa hefde þa ȝeue þat diana him biheihte i logice þan eitlonde þer heo weoren atstonden muchel wes þa murþe þe þat folc makode and heo godd þonkeden mid þeufulle worden þat heo heora wildaȝes wælden weoren heo funden i þon londe twenti eotandes stronge heora nomen ne herdi neuer tellen a leoda ne a spella boten þes anes name þa heore alre lauerd wes ihaten þat was þe heihste godes wiþersaka þe wrse hine luuede and his gode folc underȝeten þeos feondes and heora stelane flon fusden to þon feonden þa flan heom weoren laþe and heo liþden to þon munten and i þon wilderne an hudlese wuneden hit ilomp on ane daȝe þat and his duȝeþe makeden halinesse mid neoren nauer er on liue þa comen þære twenti teon of þan munten eotendes longe muchele and stronge heo tuȝen alle togadere treon swiþe muchele heo leopen to folke þer heo hurtes duden in are lutle stunde heo slowen fif hundred mid stocken and mid stanen stalfeht heo makeden and þa troynisce men mid strengþe wenden aȝein heo letten gliden heora flan and þa eotendes fluȝen and heo letten heom to gæres liþen þa heo best wende to fleonne þa weoren heo faie þa niȝentene heo slowen heo nomen and he quic wes ibroht biforen brutone hine lette witen wel mid þan beste for to leten fondien of his main stronge to wreastlene biforen and hit demdæ uppen ære dune vppen þære sæcliua þat folc com tosome forþ com and fusde hine sulfne and þe eotend alswa þat alle hit biheolden þer wes moni wepmon þer wes hurten heora hafden hæleþes biheolden ofte heo luten adun alse heo wolden liggen ofte heo up lupan alse heo fleon wolden laþliche læches heo leiteden mid eȝan al was heora gristbatinge al swa wilde bares eȝe whil heo weoren blake and ladliche iburste whil heo weoren ræde and hehliche wenden heora eiþer wilnada oþer to wælden mid wiȝeleden mid wrenchen mid wunderliche strengþen hine biþouhte and biþoute wat he don mahte nom him heorte to and streahte his ærmes and breid þat him þe rug forberst igrap hine bi þon gurdle and him grimliche heaf wes þa clude swiþe heh þer heo acliue fuhten hine lond was ihaten þa cum heron þa nolde namare þat hit swa ihaten weore ah scupte him nome æfter himseluan he wes ihaten þis lond he clepede brutaine and þa troinisce men þa temden hine to hærre æfter brutone brutuns heom cleopede and ȝed þe nome læsteþ and a summe stude cleouieþ faste ȝef þe wes his kempa deora ana dala of his londa and sette hit him an honda þe lauerd hehte and þat lond seoþþen þurh þa leoden þe i þon londa weoren heo clepeden hit cornwaile þurh heora sotliche cure heora aȝene speke troinisce and seoþþen heo hit cleopeden brutunisc ah englisce men hit habbeþ awend seoþþen com in þis lond draf out þe brutuns and his folc wes ihaten sexuns of ane ende of alemaine angles wes ihaten of angles comen englisce men and englelond heo hit clepeden þa englisce ouercomen þe brutuns and brouhten heom þer neoþere þat neofer seoþþen heo ne arisen ne her ræden funden brutaine hefde and cornwaile nom alle his freond þe comen in his ferde neh him he heom lænde for heo him broþer wes ihaten þe wes þe wiseste þe wes þe warreste þe wes þe strengeste stif he wes on þonke he hæfde to dæle þat suþ lond þat æfter him locres wes icleped and hehte þe oþer þat wes þe midleste broþer him þat lond to dale com þat cambrie wes ihaten þat is þat wilde lond þat welsce men luuieþ seþþen hit is icleped wales for þere quen galoes and for þan duke wælsce men me heom hateþ þe þridde broþer hehte seoþþen hine biswac nom his lond i þon norþ ende þat nu ure leodene scotlond clepiaþ ah on his daȝe hit clepede mær eode suþ and east forþ hefde al þat norþ hefde al himsulf bi westen sæuarne þo þa þre breþeren hefden þis lond þa luueden heom þeos leoden mid sibben and mid sahten seouentene winter æfter seouentene ȝere sone þeræfter cum liþen to londe þat wes an leodisc king was ihaten king of hunuze vuele weoren his þewes his þeines weoren kene he hefde moni lond awest and leodene biswikene and moni hundred eitlonde þa weoren bi sæstronde mestendal alle heonne to alamaine king and al his fleote and his muchele scipferde comen on londe and fuhten wiþ his leodene mid fure and mid here mid feole kunne hærme him fusde to mid muclan his ferde and heo togadere comen kempen awemmed he nom of þan monkunne þreo swiþe feire mæidene þeo an wes ihaten astrild anes hahȝes kinges dohter þa alre feireste wifmon þe þa wunede on folke þas mæidenes weoran i þan scipen mid monnen þe wuste fæi þe whilen he wende to fehten þa was dead in adrunken and to þon scipen comen for to habben al þa æhte þe king aute imong þon scipmonnen i funden þa þreo maidenes iseh þer and he heo leofliche biheold and he heo mid armen inom eþ him wes on heorten and he hire to seide sel þe scal iwurþen wifmon þu eart hende and ic þe wlle habben mid wurþscipen hæȝe to richen are quene þa while mode he ferde to þisse londe þat he com to he lædde on his exle ane muchele wieax he stod biforen and laþelich him lokede on and þas word him iqueþ þe kempa seie me saie me læþe mon saie me þu ebare sot seorwe þe beoþ ȝeueþe ne scal þe nan man scilden wiþ scondliche deaþe þu hauest mine dohter þat is mi bearn deore and me seolfan iscend þerfore þu scalt scrinkin ic liþde mid þine fader and ledde his ferde moni swinc moni swæt monine seorhfulne pleiȝe moni grimne reas moni greatne dunt moni ane wnde moni wnderlich feht þolede ich on folde biforen brutone þe wes mi deore wine mi drihliche lauerd þerfore þu scalt beon feie for nes he neuer þi fader for ȝif þu were sune ne deodest þu me nane sceome for his luue moni eotend ic leide dead a þene grund an þu mi muchele swinc mid sare forȝeldest bileafest feier and sceone mine dohter for alþeodisc meiden ihate þu nast of whulche londe heo com heder liþen ne whulc king is hire fader ne whulc quen hire moder ah þu scalt habben for hire luue þat þe is alre laþest þat al þu scalt toscæne mid scearpe mire eaxe up ahof and his eax adun sloh and smat in enne muchele stane þer stod vuenan þe stan al tosceande and atsturte alle heo hiȝeden to an elcher halfe and todeleden heom atwa teona wes on hirde þer wes moni hah word and þa alre seleste eoden tosumne hulden muchel husting þa hehste of þan hirde þat heo nolden iþolian for alþeodene gold þat þeos laþþe weore bituxe and ah we wlleþ ræden and we wlleþ runan þat weo nimen to are quene and halden alle vre aþes bitwux and and halden hiredes luue mid soþfasten huiȝe and luþere weren his craftes þus ferde þe wilde þat astrild wes mid childe and alswa mid childe heo weren ba twa ane dohter hefde inne þon eorþhuse þe king heo lette fulwen æfter þon lawen þe stoden a þon cuþe gan and speken wiþ folke þe king hine nom his feire sune madan and to hine sende into his londe þat he hine sculde wel iteon and tuhlen him teachen and swa he dude mid mæine þa while þe he mihte þa com þe time gliden þa ælc monne abideþ þat þe stronge makede his liues ende þet iherde þe king hit wes him swiþe queme þa he wuste to soþe þat was dead he nom of his hirde tweolf hende men and he sende into hire fader londe into cornwaile into hire cuþþe þa wæs at hame and hire sune madan and swiþe heo hit mænde to alle monnen þe hire fader wolde þe while he wes on liue heo gæderede tosumne burstes me cudde þe wes þisse leodene king þat mid ferde fusde to þisse londe to wreken hire teona of þon kinge and of þer quene þe king mid his folke fusde hire toȝeines and heo togadere comen vppen muchel fleam makeden hæfde þa vfere hond and iahnede hire al þis lond and heo ferde to þan castle þer wes inne heo nom and abren and lette heom ibinden and lette heom worpen in ane deope watere þer heo adronken and þer heo deaþ þoleden þa wes leodene læfdi þa hehte heo ane heste mid haiȝere witte þat me sculde þat ilke water þer abren wes adrunken clepian hit auren for þane mæidene abren and for lufe þe wes hire kinelouerd þe streonede abren vppen astrild þa hefde heo isclawen þene king and þa neowe quene and heora child and auren hatte ȝet þas æ at cristeschirche heo falleþ i þare sæ wes swiþe strong for al brutenne wes on hire hond and heo was swa swiþe wel biþouht þat ælche monne heo dude riht ælch mon mihte faren ȝend hire lond þaih he bere ræd gold ten ȝer heo wes mid often heo hæfde seorwe and pine fiftene ȝer and niȝen dawæs seoþþen wes dead al brutaine heo wuste wel mid þon beste inne griþe and in friþe wun wes on folke seoþþen heo ȝef madan an hond al his fader kinelond to cornwaile he ferde aȝein þe hire fader ahte and þer heo wonede in þon londe þa leoden weoren þe bliþre madan hire sune nom a wif þe wes swiþe hende bi hire he hæfde twein sunen ah beine heo weoren unseli haihte þe aldre þe ȝungre ah fourti wintre heore fader madan mid mensca heold his riche and þa his liues ende com he wende swiþe wel to don his tuæin sunan he sette on hond al his riche kinelond ah þa heora fader wes dæd þe sunen duden vuelne ræd bitweonen heom aræs wale and win wiþer heo weoren beien sleȝht and muchel seorwa al for heora uniselþe ah dude vnwreste he wes swike mid þan meste wiþ his broþer he nom griþ and bihahte to halden friþ and swa he nom enne dai þat come heore drihtliche folc to makian saht and some bituxen him and his broþer a þon daie þat wes iset þa comen heo tosumne hefde inomen þat griþ ah sone he makede unfriþ he dude þer serwe inoh for þer he his broþer ofsloh and þus he iwon al þis lond þat hit stod on his awene hond hatede al his cun for non nes him iqueme þa riche he makede wrecchas þa hæne hine awarieden ȝif þar was swa hah mon þat he ne durste fordon mid attere he hine adrengte þat he sone dæd wes a wif he nom swiþe hende enne sune on hire he streonede ebrauc he wes icleped ȝeond al he wes cuþ dude an vuel weorc and him ec þa wrse ilomp vuel þing him wes iqueme he forheowede al his quene his hiredmen he nom to bedde and wifmen he al bilafde twenti ȝer he heold þis lond þa leoden al to hærme and seoþþen him a time com mid teonen he wes ifunden þat he to wode wende to wundre himseoluan to huntien after deoren werfore he deþ þolede in þon wode he funde feier ane hinde þa hunten wenden æfter mid muchelen heora lude swa swiþe heo liþþeden forþ þat þe king heom forleas þat nefde he næfer enne of alle his monnen he bicom in a bæch þer he bale funde vppen ane weorede of wlfan awedde heo him to lupen on alchere halue and toluken þene king and his leomen todrowen and his hors alswa þat deade heo weoren bo twa and þus ferde þe his broþer biswac enne sune he hafde bi seoluan his quene þe was ihaten ebrauc æþelest alre kingen þe æuer sculde halden lond oþer biwiten leode al his cun he wurþede richen and wrecchen þa richen he lette beon stille þa wrecchen hefden heore wille þat lond heo lette tilien him tuwen hiredmen to blisse wes on londe a feole kunne þinge heo heold swiþe god griþ ne breac na man his friþ cnihtes he hæfde gode stronge and wode heo wilneden after worre for heom wes heora drihten wroþ þe king hit wel wuste þeh he hit suggen ne durste he lætte bi sæflode ȝearkien scipen gode vmben ane stunde þa scipen ȝaru weoren and he dude þerinne his drihtliche cnites and sende heom into france mid muchelere ferde and heo herȝeden france and feor þer biȝeonden and alle þa londes þa þerto leȝen muchel wes þa gersume þe heo hæfden inome and comen eft hider ham al isund and ihal þes wes þe æreste king þe ferde vt to ræuing þat ouer sæ wende vt of þisse londe swiþe longe þerafter wes al þis leodisc folc vnimete riche of þere ræuinge þa com hit to mode ebrauc þon gode þat he wolde bulden twa burh stronge he nom his folc and ferde forþ and droh him rites norþ a þas half scotlonde þer he wolde atstonde ærest he makede ane burh and kaer ebrauc heo clepede þa oþer on are dune adud he heo hahte þa heo wes icleped kaer ebrauc seþþen wes icleped eborac seoþþen comen vncuþe men and eoverwic heo hahten and þa norþerne men nis hit nawiht ȝeare þurh ane unþewe ȝeorc heo ihæhten þa ferde þe king norþur ma and ane neowe burh makede vppen angnetes munte mærliche feier maidene castel he wes icleoped nat ich for wan hit was swa idon ebrauc leofede swiþe longe and lond heold mid mensce sixti winter he wes king i griþe he heold his kinelond ah he hæfde moni wif þe his cun of awachede he hefde on liue tuenti sunen and alc hefde sundri moder he wes þritti dohtrenne fader þeo wifmen weoren feire of his sunen hercne þa nomen and ich heo þe wulle nemnen uært bladud moruit lagon ebedloan spaden gaul pardan ældad gangu kerin luor ruc assarac buel hector þeos weoren ebraukes sunen þes aþeles kinges his dohter nomen hercna nu þa hæȝe weoren iborene þa eldeste was ihaten gloigin ourar guardid radan angarad guenboden meþelan malure ecub scadud kambreda gaz echem nest gorgon wladus ebræn blangru egron bedra aballac eangnes andor scadiald galoes efter þissere galoes wales wes inemned galoes wes feirest of alle þan oþren leouest þone kinge of þan sustren and of þon breoþeren and anoþer wes alre best itowen hire tuhtlen weren gode gloigin hehte þa alre elduste þeo wes þurh alle þing þa æþeleste alle heo weoren wel bihedda þe king of lumbardie he wes heora nexta cunnesmon richeliche he nom his sonde and sende to ebrauke kinge of þisse londe he bad hine senden him alle his dohtren and he heom wolde ȝeuen richen his monnen swiþe riche cnihten of troinisce cunne þa weoren in lumbardie of heore strund þah stræmes heom todæleden and þa wifmen of lumbardie weoren heom swiþe laþe for þi þe king sende after þisse maidenen to ȝeuen his riche monnen swa he dude and þus hit wes wa wes lumbardisce folc þes þa hefde þe king his wille and lumbardie he walde and al his troinisce cun tuhten to himseoluan summe þa breoþeren ebraukes sunen comen þider mid heora sustren heo biȝeten wepnen heo biȝeten scipen heo biȝeten men þe heom cuþen witen heo senden ouer al þan ærde to biȝeten muchele ferde þa comen þas cnihtes ut of brutaine ferden of lumbardie to alamaigne assarac þe com ut of þissen eard his broþren hine cleopeden heora lauerd heo færden mid ȝeapscipe and mid wisdome swa longe þat heo to alamaine comen muchele castles heo bigunnen heo slowen heo barnden and þæt lond biwunnen ebrauc heora fader heold þis lond sixti winter he wes heore king he hæfde her his eldeste sune iholden mid himseoluan his nome wes wel wide cuþ he hehte uært tueolf ȝer he heold þis kinelond seoþþen his fader hit bilefde ænne sune he hefde ihaten leil he heold þis kinelond after him fulle fif and twenti ȝer æfter his fader daie he makede ane heȝe burh feier and hende to imonien leil þene king and kaer leil heo clepede in alle þon norþ ende nes nan burh swa hende leil þe king heold wel þis lond and lawen he hafde stronge ah toward his lifes ende him ilomp wel luþere þat alle his riche eorles and alle his heȝe beornes makeden muchel unfriþ and for þon kinge heo nolden holden griþ nefden heo of heore kinge buten heora scærninge and euerælc wilde mon hefde al his wil to don þa iwerþ þe king sec þurh hefeȝere seorwe and sone þerafter com þe dai þat þe king dead lai þes king hefde enne sune þe wes swiþe god mon he wes swiþe god knit ihaten þe cniht nom þæs riche and þene kinedom æke and niȝen and þritti winter he heold þæs leoden æfter leuen his fader þe leil was ihaten he sette þis lond he sahtnesse wrohte he sette stronge lawen he wes sturne þon dusien he luuede þeo leoden þe his lawen heolden æueralcne godne mon he aþelede mid gode he hehte hælden griþ and friþ vppe leome and vppe lif he makede ane riche burh and hehte heo winchestre swlc werc him þuhte swiþe muri and seoþþen he makede cantwareburi and cestesburi castel an waladunes dune ne com nauer seoþþen nan swa seolcuþ þing þat an muchel ærn spec a þon castle þer he set þet þe king himseolf hit iherde and alle his cnihtes þe mide him weoren þes fuȝel tacnede faiesiþ þes kinges was sone dead wa wes his duhþen his sune hehte bladud he wes a swiþe bisi mon he wes strong and swiþe muchel riche he wes and mæhti he cuþe þene vuele craft þat he wiþ þene wurse spæc and al þat euer he wolde þe wurse him talde þes ilke king bladud baþen iwrohte þurh swiþe muchele ginne mid ane stæncunne al swa great swa a beam þe he leide in ane wallestream þe ilke makeþ þat water hot and þan folc halwende he makede an temple onfest þe baþe an ære hæhtnesse nome þe hire nome wul iheren minerue heo was ihaten to hire he hefde loue and læfdi heo hehte in þere temple he lette beornen enne blase of fure þe neuer ne aþeostrede wintres ne sumeres ah euer me þat fur bette swa þe king haihte to wrþscipe his læfdi þe leof him wes on heorten þus dude bladud þe king þat him wes wide cuþ þa he hefde þus idon þæ þohte he on oþer he ȝealp þat he wolde fleon on fuȝeles læche þat al his folc mihte iseon and his fluhtes bihalden he makede his feþerhome and þaruore he hæfde muchel scome to lunden he ferde mid muchelen his folke his feþerhome he dude him on and he his fluht þer bigon mid wiȝeful his fluhte tæih him to þon lufte he ferde swiþe hehȝe þere weolcne he wes swiþe nih þe wind him com on wiþere weoþeleden his fluhtes brecon þa strenges þe he mid strahte and he feol to folde þe king wes feie vppen are stouwe þe i lundene stod temple þe wes þe tirfulle feond þe king feol on þene rof þat he al todraf þus wes þas kineriche of heora kinge biræued tuenti winter hafde bladud þas kinelond an hond æfter his fader þe leil sune þes riche kinges wes bladud hafde enne sune wes ihaten efter his fader daie he heold þis drihliche lond somed an his liue sixti winter he makede ane riche burh þurh radfulle his crafte and he heo lette nemnen efter himseoluan kaer hehte þe burh leof heo wes þan kinge þa we an ure leodquide leirchestre clepiaþ ȝeare a þan holde dawen heo wes swiþe aþel burh and seoþþen þer seh toward swiþe muchel seorwe þat heo wes al forfaren þurh þere leodene uæl sixti winter hefde þis lond al to welden þe king hefde þreo dohtren bi his drihliche quen nefde he nenne sune þerfore he warþ sari his manscipe to halden buten þa þreo dohtren þa ældeste dohter haihte þa oþer ragau þa þridde heo wes þa ȝungeste suster a wliten alre vairest heo wes hire fader al swa leof swa his aȝene lif þa ældede þe king and wakede an aþelan and he hine biþohte wet he don mahte of his kineriche æfter his deie he seide to himsuluen þat þat vuel wes ic wlle mine riche todon allen minen dohtren and ȝeuen hem mine kineþeode and twemen mine bearnen ac ærst ic wille fondien whulchere beo mi beste freond and heo scal habbe þat beste del of mine drihlichen lond þus þe king þohte and þeræfter he worhte he clepede hes guþfulle dohter vt of hire bure to hire fader deore and þeus spac þe alde king þer he on æþelen seat sei me soþere worden swiþe dure þeo eart me hu leof æm ich þe hu mochel worȝ leste þu me to walden kineriche was swiþe wær swa beoþ wifmen wel ihwær and seide ane lesinge heore fædere þon king leofe fæder dure swa bide ich godes are swa helpe me for min ilæfe is al on him þat leuere þeo ært me æne þane þis world al clane and ȝet ic þe wlle speken wit þeou ært leouere þene mi lif and þis ich sucge þe to seoþe þu mith me wel ileue þe king ilefde his doster læisinge and þas ænsware ȝef þat waes þe olde king ich þe seuge leoue dohter dure god scal beon þi meda for þira gretinge ic eam for mire ælde swþe vnbalded and þou me leuoste swþe mare þan is on liue ich wille mi dirhliche lond a þroe al todalen þin is þat beste deal þu ært mi dohter deore and scalt habben to lauerd min alre beste þein þeo ich mai uinden in mine kinnelonde æfter spac þe olde kinge wit his oþer dohter leoue dohter regau waet seist tu me to ræide seie þu bifore mire duȝþen heo dure ich am þe an herten þa answærde mid rætfulle worden al þat is on liue nis me swa dure swa me is þin an lime forþe min ahȝene lif ah heo ne seide naþing soþ no more þenne hiire suster alle hire lesinge hire uader ilefede þa answarede þe king hiis doȝter him icwemde þea þridde del of mine londe ich bitake þe an honde þu scalt nime louerd þer þe is alre leowost þa ȝet nolde þe leodking his sothscipe bilæuen he hehte cumen him biforen his dohter heo was alre ȝungest of soþe ȝærwitelest and þe king heo louede more þanne ba tueie þe oþre iherde þa lasinge þe hire sustren seiden þon kinge nom hire leaffulne huie þat heo liȝen nolden hire fader heo wolde suge seoþ were him lef were him laþ þeo queþ þe alde king vnrad him fulede iheren ich wlle of þe sua þe helpe hu deore þe beo lif min þa answarede lude and nowiht stille mid gomene and mid lehtre to hire fader leue þeo art me leof also mi fæder and ich þe also þi dohter ich habbe to þe sohfaste loue for we buoþ swiþe isibbe and swa ich ibide are ich wille þe suge mare al swa muchel þu bist woruh swa þu velden ært and al swa muchel swa þu hauest men þe wllet luuien for sone heo biþ ilaȝed þe mon þe lutel ah þus seide þe mæiden and seoþþen set swþe stille þa iwarþe þe king wærþ for he nes þeo noht iquemed and wende on is þonke þat hit weren for vnþeawe þat he hire weore swa unwourþ þat heo hine nold iwurþi swa hire twa sustren þe ba somed læsinge speken þe king iwerþe swa blac swlch hit a blac cloþ weoren iwærþ his hude and his heowe for he was suþe ihærmed mid þere wræþþe he wes isweued þat he feol iswowen late þeo he up fusde þat mæiden wes afeared þa hit alles up brac hit wes vuel þat he spac hærne ich þe telle wlle mine wille of mine dohtren þu were me durest nu þu eært me arle læþest ne scalt þu halden dale of mine lande ah mine dohtren ich wlle delen mine riche and þu scalt worþen warchen and wonien in wansiþe for nauere ich ne wende þat þu me woldes þus scanden þarfore þu scalt beon dæd ich wene fliȝ ut of min eæhsene þine sustren scullen habben mi kinelond and þis me is iqueme þe duc of cornwaile scal habbe and þe scottene king regau þat scone and ic hem ȝeue al þa winne þe ich æm waldinge ouer and al þe alde king dude swa he hafuede idemed ofte wes þen mæidene wa and næure wors þenne þa wa hire wes on mode for hire fader wærþe heo uende into hire boure þar heo ofte sætte sare for heo nolde liȝen hire fadder leoue þat maide wes swþen swomefest for hire fader heo scunede and dude þene beste red in hire bure heo abed and þolede þene modkare and mornede swþe and þus ane stonde hit stod æ þon ilka in france wes a king riche and swiþe kene wes ihaten hæleþen he wes ældere he wes a ȝenge king ah quene nauede he nane he sende hiis sande into þisse lande to þan king and leofliche hine gret he bæd hine don is iwille ȝeuen him and he heo wolde habben hæȝe to are quene and æfter hire don ærest þat hire were alre leofust feor haueden liþende men ispeken of þan mæidene feiȝernesse and freoscipe atforen þan frensce kinge of hire mucla fæira wlita of hire muchela monschipe hu heo wes þolemod of fæire hire þeæwen þat nes on kinges lond nan wifman al swa hende and þe king igrette kin þus kin hine biþohte wat he don mohte he letten writen a writ and wel hit lette dihten and sende hit bi his sonde in frauncene londe þus spec þes kinges writ hit wes widen icuþ þe kinge of bruttaine þe is haten greteþ þene aldere of fraunce worþschepe haue þu þire weldeda and þire feire sonde þat grete þu me woldest ac ich do þe wel to witene hær bi mine writ rith þat mi drihliche lond atwa ich habbe ideled iȝeuen hit mine twam dohtren þe me beoh swiþe deore dohter ich habbe þa þridda ac ne ræcche ich wær heo libbe for heo me forhuste and heo hold me for hæne and for mire halde heo me unælede heo makede me swa swiþe wraþ þe worse hire scal iwurþen of alle mine londe ne of alle mine leode þe ich auere biȝeat oþer biȝete mæie ich þe sucge soþriht na scal heo habbe nawiht ac ȝef þu heo wult habben for mæide heo is hende ich heo wulle þe biwiten and senden ha þe in ane scipe mid seoluen hire claþen of me nafþ heo na more ȝif þu heo wult underfon al þis ilka ich wulle don iseid ich habbe þene grund and þu seolf wurþ al hisund þis writ com to fraunce to þan freo kinge he hit lette raden leof him weren þa runen þa wende þe kinge þat hit were for vuele þat kinge hire fæder heo him wolde atleden and he a þa wodeloker wilnede þeos mæidenes and seide to is bornen þat wes þa bisie king ich eam riche mon inoh þat na mare ich ne recche ne scal neuere king þat mæiden me attlede ac ich heo wulle habben to hæhȝere are quene habben heore fader al is lond al hiis seoluer and is gold ne bidde ich nanne maþmes me seolf ich habben inoȝe bute þat mæiden þenne hæbbe ich mine wille mid writ and mid worde he sende eft to þisse londe and bad king him sende his dohter þe wæs hende and he wolde wel don mid muchele worþescipe heo underfon þa nom þa olde king æþele his meiden mid seoluen hire claþes and lette heo forþe liþen ofer þa stremes hire fader hire wes sturne þe frennsce king vnderfeng þis meiden child al hiis folc hit wes iqueme and makeden heo to quene and þus heo þer bilefde leof heo wes þon leoden and king hire fæder luuede i þisse
