king and þe duk speken togaþere mid heore stil rune nome hem to reda þat heo wolden al þis lond habben on heora hond and feden þane king þe while þe he leouede dæies and nihtes mid feowerti hiredcnihtes and heo him wolden finden hauekes and hundes þat he mihte riden ȝeond alle þanne þeoden and libben on lisse þe while þe he leouede þus heo þa ispeken and eft hit tobreken and king hit iherde and eft him wes þe worsse and gan liþe to scottenæ leoda mid his aþume and mid þere eldre dohtre me vnderfenge þene king mid mochele feirnusse and wel me him dihte mid feowerti hiredcnihtes mid horsen and mid hundes mid al þet him biheovede þa hilomp hit seoþþen seone þerafter þe biþohte whet heo don mihte heore þuhte swiþe eille of æþelene hire fædere and heo hit bigan to mainen to hire louerde and seide him ibedde þer heo leiin iueore seie me mi lauerd monne þu ert me leouest me þuncheþ þat mi fæder nis nowhit felle no he wurhscipe ne can his wit he hauet bileued me þuncheþ þe alde mon wole dotie nou nan he halt here fauwerti cnihtes daies and nihtes he haueht her þas þeines and alle heore swaines hundes and hauekes þeruore we habbet harmes and nowher heo ne spedet and auere heo spenet and al þat goud þat we hem doþ heo hit bluþeliche vnderfoþ and cunnen us vnþonc for ure weldede heo doþ muchel bisemære ure men hi tobetet mi fader hauet to monie of idele manne ale þa feorþe dale lete we forþ fuse inoh he hauet on þirti to þirngen to borde vs selve we habbet cokes to quecchen to cuchene vs sulue we habbet bermen and birles inowe lete we sum þis mochele folc fare wher ha wulleþ swa ich æuere ibiden are iþolien nulle ich hit mare þis iherde þat is quene spilede þus and he hire andswarede mid aþelere spiche leiuedi þu haues mochel wouh nauest þu richdom inoh ah hald þine fæder on lisse ne luueþe he nowiht longe for ȝef ferrene kinges hiherde þa tidinde þe we swa takede him on heo us wolden tælen ah late we hine welden his folc on his willen and þis min aȝe ræd is for sone heræfter he beþ dead and ac we habben in ure hond al half is kinelond þa seide lauerd beo þeu stille let me al iwurþen and ich ham wulle atwailden heo sende mid hire ginne to þare cnihtene inne heo hahte hem faren here wæi for heo nolden hem no more feden moni of þen þeinen monie of þen sweinen þe þider weren icumene mid þanne kinge þis iherde king þarfore he wes swuþe wrah þa iȝedede þe king mid ȝemeliche worden and þus seide þe kinge sorhful on mode wa worþe þan monne þe lond haueþe mid menske and bitachet hit is childe þe while þe he mai hit walden for ofte hit ilimpþ þat eft hit him ofpincheþ nu ich wulle hunne faren forþrihte to cornwalen ȝernen ich wulle rædes to regau mire dohter þe hauede hemeri þe duc and mi drihliche lond forhd þe king wende into þan suþ ende to regau is dochter for rædes him trukeden þa he to cornwale com he wes feire þer vnderfon swa al þet halue ȝer mid al his hirede he wes þer þa saide regau to hire duc hemeri lauerd herne þu me to fulle soþe ich sucge hit þe we habbet idon unwisdom þat we mine fader habbet vnderfon mid þirtti cnihten hit nis me noht iqueme do we awai þane twenti a tene beoþ inohȝe for al heo dringket and eteþ and na god heo ne biȝeteþ þa seide hemeri þe duc þe his alde fader biswake swa ich eæuere beo on liue ne scal he habben beote fiue for þer he hauet hirde hinoh for he nauyt no doþ and ȝef he wille henne faren fuse we hine sone al heo ispedden ase heo ispeken hafden binomen him is doȝeþe and al his drihliche folc nolden heo him bileafuen cnihtes beoten fiue þis iseh þe king wa wes him on liue his mod him gon mengen he morȝnede swiþe and þas worde seide mid seorhfulle laichen wela weolla wella hu þu biswikest monine mon þenne he þe treoweþe alre best on þenne biswikes tu heom nis hit nowit ȝare noht fulle twa ȝere þat ich was a riche king and held mine cnihtes nu ich habben ibiden þat ich bare sitte wunnen biræued wa is me on liue ich wes at mire godfulle dohter wuneden on hire leoden mid þritti cnihtes þe ȝet ich mihte libben ah þenne igonne liþen ich wende swiþe wel to don ac wurse ich habbe vnderfon aȝen ich wulle to scotte to scone mire docter ȝernen hira milcea þat heo me nele wurdea bidden heo me vnderfon mid mine fif cnihten þer ich wulle wunie and þolie þeos wænen ane lutele stunde for ne libbe ich nowiht longe þe king wende forh to is dohter wunede norþ fulle þre nihtes heo hærabarewude hine and is cnihtes heo swor a þane ferþe dæi bi al heuenliche main þat ne sculde he habben mare bute enne kincte þere and ȝef he þet nolde ferde wuder he wolde wel oft wes wa and neuere wurs þanne þa þa seide þe alde king æruu was on herten wallan dæþ wela deaþ þat þu me nelt fordemen seoþ seide for cuþ hit is me nouþe mi ȝengestte dohter heo was me wel dure seoþþen heo me wes leaþest for heo me seiden alre sohust þat me biþ vnworþ and lah þe mon þe litul ah and ihc nas na wurdra þenne ich nes weldinde ouer soh seiden þat ȝunge vifmon hire folweþ mochel wisdom þa wile þe ich hæuede mi kinelond luueden me mine leoden for mine londe and for mine feo mine eorles fulle to mine cneo nu ich æm a wrecche mon ne leouet me no mon for þan ah mi dohter me seide seoh for nou ich hire ileue inoh and ba twa hire susteren lasinge me seiden þat ich ham wes swa leof leuere þenne hire aȝe lif and mi dohter dohȝeþe me seide þat heo me leouede swa feire swa monnes fader scolde wet wold ich bidde mare of mire dohter dure nu ich wullen faren feorþ and ouer sæ fusen ihiren of wat beon hire wille hire seohþe word ich nam to grame þarfore ich habbe nu muchele scame for nu ich mot bisecchen þat þing þat ich ær forhowede nule heo me do na wurse þanne hire lond forwurnen ferde to þere sæ mid ane alpie swein into ane schipe he bicom ne icnwo hine no mon ouer sea icomen hauene sone anomen forþ wende þe king nauede he bute enne swein hi axeden þa quene þat heo comen hire a neweste tahten heom leode wer wes þes londes quene king wende on anne feld and reste hine on folden and is swein he forþ sende þe wes iradmon hende to þere quene and seide hire wel stille hail wurþ þu feire quene ich eam þines fader sweine and þi uader is hider ikimen for al is lond is him binomen beoþ ba þine sustren touward him forsworene he cumeþ for neode into þisse leode and help him nu for þu miht he is þi fader alse hit is riht þe quene seæt longe swþe stille heo iward reode on hire benche swilche hit were of winescenche and þe swain sæt at hire fæit sone þerafter him wes þe bet þa alles vppe abræc hit wes god þet heo spæc mi lauerd ich þankie þe þat mi fæder is icumme to me tidinge ic ihire leoue þat mi fader on liue is of me he habben scal goudne reæd bute ich beo þe raþer ded seie me nuþe leof swein and harne mine lare ich þe wulle bitache a male riche peniȝes þer buoþ an sunda to iwisse an hundrad punda ich bitæche þe anne hængest godna and strongna to læden þis garisume to leuene mine fadere and seie him þat ich hine gret godere gretinge and hatine fare swiþe to hare feire burȝe and rumen him herberia i summe riche burie and bugge him alre errust þat him wes alre leouust metes and drinches and hende claþes hundes and hauekes and durewurþe horses halde in is heose feuwerti hiredcnihtes heȝe and riche bihongen mid ræue makie him god baid and ofte hine baþie and him blod lete lutlen and ofte wenne þu wult more suluer sæche hit at me suluen and ich him wulle senden inoh of þisse ende swa neuer he ne cuþe of his alde cuþþe cnihte ne sweine ne nauer nanne þeine þenne feowerti dawes beoþ agan þenne cuþe he anan to leue mine lauerd þat is an is londe icume ouer sæstreme to isen is eastresse and ich hit wulle swa nimen alse ich hine nusten liþen him toȝænes mid mine lauerde fainen mines lauerdes and is fæirliche cume nute hit neuere nane gume buten he beo neowene icume and þus hit writen sende to mine lauerd kinge and þu þas æhte onfo and loca þat þu wel do and ȝef þu heo þus dalest to godere þire hæle and þe swein onfeng þas ahte and to is louerd ferde to þon kinge and seide þas tidinge þer he læi on felde and reste hine on folde sone werþ þe alde king wunliche iæþeled and þas wuord seide mid soþere stefuene after vuele cumeþ god wel is him þe hit habbe mot heo ferden to hare æȝene burh ase þe quene hæhte and al heo iduden efter hire lare þa forþ wuren agan feuwerti daȝene þon nom þe king is leouste cnihtes and gret þat was his leue aþum and seide him bi his sond þet icume he wes to is londe to speken wit his dohter þe wes him swuþe dure wes bliþe þet wes cumen liþen ferde him toȝenes mid alle his þeines and þa quene þa hauede is wille heo comen togadere and ofte heo custen heo uenden to burȝe blisse wes an hirede þer wes bemene song þere ȝeden pipen among al weren þe hællen bihongen mid pellen alle þa meteburdes ibrusted mid golde ringes of golde ælc mon hafte on honde mid fiþelen and mid harpen hæleþes þer sungen lette þe king gan awal and lude clepien oueral and seide þat kin icume wes to londen nu hateþ þe is þe heȝest ouer us þat ȝe king alle wurþe liþe and scal beon eouwer lauerd inne þissere leoden al swa fele ȝere swa he wonien wulle here and ure king scal beon is vnderling whaswa wulle libba alde þas sibba and ȝef o man hit wille breken on ueste it biþ iwreken and wite he alle is mon þat he here haldet on þa answareda þa duȝeþa don we hit wullet lude and stille al þes kinges wille þurþout al þat ulke ȝer heo duden al þus þer mid muchelere sibba mid mocheleære seahte þa þeos ȝer wes agon þa wold king fare ham to þisse londe liþen and ȝernde þeos kinges leue þe king answerede him þus ne scalt þu neuere þider faren bute mochelure ferde ah ich þe wulle lanen of mine leodefolc fif hundred schipes ifulled mid cnihten and al þat heom bihoueþ to habben on fore and þine dohter þa is þisse londes quene heo scall mid mochelure ferde faren mid þe an liþen to þen londen þer þu were leodene king and ȝef þu miht æine finden þe þe wulle aȝenstonde binimen þe þine rihte and þine kineriche þu ahliche ueht and fel heo to grunde and irum al þat lond and sete hit an hond þat heo hit al habbe efter þine daie þas wordes seide and king dude þus and al he iworhte swa his freond him tahte to þisse londen he com liþen mih leoue his dohter he higreþede mid þane beste þe him buwen wolden and alle he ham fulde þe him wit feohten and he al þis kinelond biwon to his aȝere hande and ȝef hit þe wes francene quene and hit ane stunde stod a þissene ilke king one leoden þreo ȝer leouede þæ com his endedæi þat þe king ded læi inne leirchestre his dohter hine leide inne ianies temple al swa þe boc tellet and heold þis lond mid hæȝere strenþe fulle fif ȝere quene wes here þa while francene king fæisiþe makede and com þat wourd þat heo was iworþen widewe þa come þa tidende to scottlondes kinge þat was dead king idæied he sende þurh brittaine into cornwaile and hehte þane duc stronge heriȝen in suþ londe and he wolde bi norþen iahnien þa londa for hit was swuþe mouchel scome and ec swiþe muchel grame þat scholde a quene beon king in þisse londe and heora sunen beon buten þa weren hire beteren of þan aldre sustren þa þa æþelen sulden habben nulle we hit namore iþolien al þat lond we wulleþ habben heo bigunnen werre wanne com on west and þere quene suster sunen sumneden ferde heore nomen weren ihaten þus and ofte heo ledden ferde ofte heo fuhten ofte heo weren buuenne and ofte binoþen þat com at þan laste þat heo wes alre leofust þe bruttes heo sloȝen heo nomen heo duden heo in quarterne in ane qualehuse heo werþede heore moddri mare þene heo sulden þat þe wimman was swa wroþ þat hire sculuen heo was laþ heo nom enne longne cnif and binom seoluen þat lif þat wes an uuel ræd þat hire suluen makede dead þeo wes al þis kinelond an and heond heo fengen to þissen lond and mid fuhten hit biwunnen þa dælden þa broþeran al þis drihtliche lond bi þare hauede al þet west hauede norþ and est and swa heo heolden al þis lond ale þe twa ȝere on heore heond þa þe twa ȝer weren agon þa twineden here þonkes wes in scottlond þene norþ ende he hauede ane honde inne cornwale he hauede moni god hus hafte on hirede swiþe monie cnihtes þeo ne luuede noht þas leoden ah laiþ heo hem weoren he taleden wiþ and is cnihtscipe tælden and þus him to seiden þa vnselie mon lauerd whi nult þu faren and fusen þine ferden and faren ȝend al brutlond and nimen hit to þire heonde þerof we habbeþ sceome and at oure herte muche grame þat þu dalest þis lond þe sculde beon o þire hond þu eært a swa hende gome and þere eældre suster sone delest þine lond wiþ þine mæi þi monscipe is þa lasse þus speken þeos swiken and spileden mid worde swa long heo hine lærde þat he heom ileuede he gaderede ferde þe wes feondliche stor he ferde ouer þe and hermes he worhte he herȝede he brande folc he amærde heo sloȝen heo nomen al þat heo aneh comen þat word com sone suþ for hit wes widen cuþ þet ledde muchele here and hærmes dude þas leoden þa ihurde þat is mæi ferde þus þa iwerþ he swiþe wraþ and þas word seide ȝetsinge a wurþe þe wa monie mon þu bicherrest þurh þe haueþ mi mæi is monschipe afallet ah he scall hit abuggen ȝif ich mot libben þa nom and send ȝeond his cuþþe and gaderede muchel folc and ȝeærwede his ferde he fusede mid monschipe toward his mæie þa heo sculden fehten þa fleh awaie from londe to londe and he him after liþde into wales he flæh he him after ferde þer he oftoc mid muchele strengþe and sloh he him of þat hæued his hap wes þa wurse and al his men slowen þat heo neh comen buten wuhlc wræcche swa cwic cuahte to holde heo nomen liche and leide hit on vrþen wel heo hine buriden þe wes þes wales lauerd wes þet lond þurh ihæten heuede al þis lond þerof he wes lauerd þro and þritti wintere he welde þas riche inne griþe and in friþe his frenden to blisse a dawe þe king wes on leode remus and rome iwrohten beine iweren ibroþeren ah þe an sloh þene oþren after þritti wintere com þe dæi þat deæd læi he hefte anne sune ræhne wes ihaten he wes wis he wes fæir he welde þat riche hær al hit hine luuede þat liuede in londe an þan ilke time hær com a selkeþ taken sulche hare nere eær ne com ne neuer seoþþen hiderto from heouene her com a sulcuþ flod þre dæȝes hit rinde blod þreo dæies and þreo niȝt þat wæs swuþe mochel pliht þa þe rein wes agan her com hider taken anan her comen blake fleȝen and fluȝen in mone eȝene in here muþ in heore neose heore lif heom eode al to leose swulc fare of fleoȝen her was þat heo freten þet corn and þat græs wo wes al þen folke þe wuneden an folden þærafter com swulke monqualm þat lute hær cwike læfden seoþþen her com a strong ræd þat kinge iwerþ dead king hafuede anne sune ihaten his lond he huld half ȝer and suþþen he adun halde þerefter com he wes sone her deæd suþþen com lago þa æhte wike liuede suoþen com king marke he wes þritti wiken king þeo com he wes fif ȝere god king þe king hauede tweie sunen beiene vniselie þe eldere heȝte fereus þe ȝengere hehte þas breþren weren swa wode and swa wiþerwarde þat al heo weren vnsahte and al heo weren vnsome and eiþer hateden oþer swa ne sulde nawiht breoþer and beien mid onde heo weoren in þisse londe þat heore fader of his sunen wes afered for ofte biforen himsuluen heo bigunnen to fuhten þe aldre seide þat al þis lond he wolde halden on is aȝere hond þe ȝengere him ȝef swuh enswere ær ich þe slæ mid mine spere ar þu hit sule aȝen þa while ich beon on liue hauede þe heorte swa luþer and swa loþ him wes his broþer þat swiken he him wolde a summes kinnes wisen fereus hit iherde suggen þorh soþfaste worden þat his broþer hine wolde slæn þerfore he wes ful sari he ferde awæi ouer sæ þat him þuhte selest he funde inne francene eærd þene king þe hehte sward he bad him herdsumnesse heren þat he him wolde beon him for hold cniht ba bi dæie and bi niht þe king wes gled for his kime and for þen cnihtes þet come mid hine and heold hine on erde and hæhliche hine clepede ful soue ȝere mid þon kinge he wunede þere þat king he hauede iquemed and alswa þere quene þa seoue ȝer weoren aliþene þa bad he leue færren þat he wolde into þisse lond þe king him lende ane ferd of his kennest folke himseolf he sende sonde wide ȝen þat londe after alle þen cnihten þe he biȝete mihte and he toclipede muchelen his ferde and al mid isunde come to þisse londe anan heo bigunne fuhte and falde þas leoden and is broþer ferde him toȝenes mid þon stronge fæhte fereus he felden and alle his ferde he leiden to folde hæhte here moder þe riche was and onmære swiþe heo was sari for sorehfulle þan slehte þat heore sune ȝeongere sloh þene eldere þe deæde heore wæs leouere þe quike here wes leoþere þe quike hire wes swa swiþe leoþ þat binimen heo him þohte his lif lai on bure þer him muchel plihte ilomp þer he læi softe and he siker slepte com is moder liþen mid leoþlichen creæften mid oþer six wiuen mid six longe cniuen þeo uniseli moder þus hire sune murþde heo cærf him þene swure atwa a wurþe hire wa þe uniselie moder mid sexe hine to snæde and al todælde lim from oþere þa wes þe muchele speche ȝend þat kineriche of þere quene þa heore sone acualde and of þare seoreȝe þe isiȝe wes to londe þa weas dæd fereus alswa wes binumen wes þere moder monschipe on leode þa nes þer noht of þen kunne þe mihte þis kinelond walden wepmon ne wifmon bute þa seorhfulle gumen heom igadereden and wurpen heo to sagrunde þa aræste here vnfriþe oueral me brac þene griþ sterce weren þe reæmes mid stronge raflake elc mon ræuede oþer þeah hit weren his broþer wrake wes on londe wa wes þone vnstronge her wes hunger and hete her wes alre hærmene mest her wes muchel monqualm þat lut her quike bilefden feowere here weren riche þe haueden ferden muchele þeo nedden al þæ oþere and heom neþþer sætten and speken heom togadere and speleden þa hæȝe þat heo wuolden al þis lond dælen heom bitwenen þus heo hit idemden and þeræfter swa duden in scotlond wes king stater i logres wes king piner cloten hafte cornwale rudæuc hauede norh wales ah cloten hæfde mest riht to aȝen þas riche ah þa oþere weoren ræhere and eke heo weoren richere of golde and of garisume and of gode londe cloten heo oscuneden and his færedene forhowede cloten hauede cornwale þat he heold wel one griþe cloten hauede enne sune þe sel wes on eorþe he wes feir he wes muchel to feahten he wes mære cniht he wes kene and he wes ȝeua custi monie þewes gode he haueda on his moda his nome wes ihote þus þis wes þe feiruste mon þe æuere æhte ær þisne kinedom þa he mihte beren wepnen and his hors wel awilden he liþde ȝeon þeos leoden sulch hit an liun were he sloh piner þene king his folc he al aqualde þa him wihstoden he felde heom to his foten and al logres þat lond he æȝenede to his æȝere hond suþþen he turnde his fare and ferd feorhriht to wales þer he funde rudac king þe reh wes to fehte toȝeines him he funde þer scotlondes king stater heo speken þer to sæhte to sibbe and to some aiþes heo sworen swiken þat heo nolden þus heo makeden heore fære aȝen ferde dunwale and his mochele ferde to cornwale his eærde þa iherde stater þat dunwale wes swiþe fer mid muchele scotferde he scraþ to þisse londe rudauc mid his welscen þat wæl wes þe more into þisse londe heo comen þis floc heo hær slowe wide heo ærnde tuones heo forbarnden mochel dal heo iwesten mid harmen þan mesten þat word com to dunwale þer he wes i cornwale wet ruwak king dude her and þe king stater þa seide dunwale þat was þe duȝende mon nu heo beþ forsworne mid heore swikedome bi ære ne ileue ich hem neueremare nu we sculle ræmen and ræisen togadere vnder þissen luften leten riht scuften sendeþ mine sonden ȝend alle mine londe and biddeh alne godne mon þe griþ wulle halden and alle þe me of haldeh cumen ær sone and sendeþ liþinde men æfter oþere leoden to folien me in mine londe for seoluer and for golde and ich wulle mine rihte faren to stalfehte toȝene þene swerd broþeren þe beiene beoh forsworene for wel often he beoþ awald þe stondeþ o þen woȝe ne mai neuere monsware monscipe longe aȝen þe dunwale hauede isæd al his folc luuede þene ræd he somenede færd swulc nes næuere eær on erde swoþþen wes þa time þe bruttes come hær liþen heo fulde his ferde and for a mucla costa toȝenes þan twam kingen þer he hem funde on walde heo heolden togædere and hardeliche fuhten feollen þa fæie falewede nebbes weoren al þa feldes ifayed mid blode þer wes moni hard gume mid sworde tohewen dunwal i þan fæhte wes feondliche kene þat fæht wes swuþe strong and swuþe stærc and swuþe longe dunwal i þan fahte hauede swuþe gode cnihtes wise and wære monie heo afelden dunwale him biþohte wat he don mihte he nom of his ferde six hundred cnihtes of þan aldre hexten to wiȝe alre hardest and þus heo heom seide on his somrunan nime we þis wepnen þe bi þisse walle liggeþ and halden biforen bresten sceldes þa brade and fare we bihalues alse we of heoren weoren þe wille sullen ore ferden fæhten biliue þenne stateres floc iseoþ ore fæire sculdes cumen on feste hit buh heom wel iqueme for þan wepnen heo wullet wenen þat þeo beon heore iferen we scullen ous biredien and slen rudauc þane king and feorhrihtes þære slen þane king statere mid strengþe we sullen wenden þurh ure wiþeriwinnen and fellen ure feondes for alle heo buh fæi þus spac dunwale þat was þe duȝenede mon and al he iworhte swa his word tahte heo nomen þa seeldes þa leien in þan feldes brade and gode ihelede mid golde heo wenden to þan kingen þer heo weren on kompen þe kingges weren bliþe heo wenden bi þan bordden heo wenden bi þen scelden þat hit heore scalkes weoren sone so dunwale heom næh com swa he hæhte slæn heom slæþ heom mid sweorde for alle heo beoþ forsworne rudac heo slowen and stater heo nomen and al hene toliþeden lim from þen oþere heoræ sceaftes weoren strake of his flæsces heo makeden here marce anan heo ferden towærd heore iueren þa heo togaderen comen somed heo onsloȝen þa kingges weoren deædde heore duȝeþe todealde twinseden cnihtes here tir wes atfallen dunwales men sloȝen al þat heo aneh comen al þa ferde heo falden to grunde buten swulc forwonde man þe mid sorwe atwand þa hauede dunwale þis lond al biȝeten to his hond suþþen he wes heh king coþ hit wes wide of him beoþ on beoken feolefeld bisnen þet wes þa eæraste mon þe guldene crune dude him on here inne bruttaine seoþþen bruttes hit ieode he makede swulc griþ he makede swulc friþ monien laȝen gode þe long souþþen stode heo makeden ane sætnesse and mid aȝe heo semde þe ælc cheorl eæt his sulche hæfde griþ alswa þe king sulf alken farinde mon ȝef slaht oþer þeofþe hæfde idon and he ætsturte into are burie þat heo weren iborȝen þenne and aueremare heo swulden habben are to fuse into hame and habben his æhte and ȝef æi mon him liþere dude he sculde dom þolien and þus ælkene forme gult þe king sulf hine forȝef þe king makede monie laȝen þa ȝet beoþ on londe and alle laȝen gode bi his daȝen stode feowerti wintre he walde þes leode a blisse hit stod on his hand seoþþen dæide þe king wa wes his duȝeþe togadere come his eorles and brohten hine to eorþe inne lundene burh feire hine leiden in are riche temple mid golde heo hine bitunden þe king hauede bi his wiue twene sonen on liue þe ældre hæhte þe ȝeonggere brenne þas breþren iwurþen heom swahte þurh sele monne rede ȝef his leue broþer anne dal of his londe biȝende þere mid monscipe to halden norþ into þare sæ sel þat heo iworþe þerfore his mon he bicom and hærdsumnesse him solde don heold þis suþlond and cornwale on his hond and wales þer forþ mid and faire hit dihte fif ȝer heo heolden þus þis lond and leoue heom wes bitwune þet æuere eiþer oþer luuede alse is broþer ah hauede vuele men his æþelene heo amerden þeo ælche dæie hine larden luþere craftes þat he sculde wih his broþer forewarde breken anne hirdcniht he hauede þe æht wes on þen weorede þe þane balew mæinde and þus spec wih brenne seie me mi lauerd leouest alre monne whi þolest þu þat þe is þin aȝene broþer hauet swa mochel of þisse lande and þu hauest swa lutel nefde ȝe ba enne fader and beie enne moder beiene of ane cunne cuþ hit is on folke nu stond al þis muchele lond a bailenes aȝere hond and þu eært his mon and is cniht þat is woh and nawiht riht eært þu þenne cheuesboren þat þu wult beon forloren oþer þu eart swa eærȝh cniht þat of londe ne rehchest nawiht oþer þu þenchest beo raþe dead and þine duȝeþen al bilaiuen bileæf þe treuweþe bilef þene æþ for al þis folc is swiþe wraþ hercne þine herdes ræd and heo þe wullet helpen hit us þinchet wunder ȝef þu hine nelt awalden þu eært muchele betere cniht to halden comp and ifiht and þu eært muchele ahtere and ec mare hærdere cheflon þu ouercome and scotlond him binome of muraine he wes king and he wiht þe othliche fæht eærst þu hine ouercome and seoþþen þu hine slowe and al his ferde þe he brohte to þan eærde ah wel ich hit ileuen þat we þe sunden loþe þat þu þi þanc al forhele wih þine hiredmonnen ah for nauer nare teonen nulle we þe trukien neuer ane siþen bi ure quike liuen and fær bi ure ræden and mid þe þu læden tweolue of þine witiȝen of þine wisuste monnen and fær forh nu toniht into norewaieȝe forhriht to alfinge kinge þu bist him cume deore and gret þu londes king and al his leode þe king haueþ ane dohter þe him is swuþe dure bide heo to þire bihoue to habben to are quene þenne he siþ þe swa hende cniht he þe ȝeueþ heo forþriht seoþþen ȝern to þan kinge þat he þe læne ferde to lede to þine londe to balden þine leoden bide auerælcne cniht þet þu þer biȝeten miht for seluere and for gold cume mid þe to þisse londe and we sullen þe wile biwiten þine riche derneliche þu scalt don þeos ilka deda þat hit nute þe is þin aȝene broþer ah fær swiþe and cum raþe for þus we þe radeþ þenne þu cumes faren ham we swulleþ beon al fuse mid mochelen ure ferde to færen ȝeon þan eærde to owreken þe uppon þe þe bismar haueþ idon þus spec swike he wes ful god þe oþere him radden al swa þerfore hem wroþe wide wa þa hauede ihirde his hirdemanne lare þa gladede is mod þe rad him þuhte swiþe god and seide hem þis answare after eore rade ich wulle færen he greiþede his cnihtes and feorh færde bi nihttes swa longe þat he bicom to kinge þonne king heo igrette and his gumen alle and þe king him answerede swiþeliche fæire þa spec and his ærnde abed he ȝirnde þeos kinges dohter to habben to are quene and þe king him ȝette al þat he ȝirnde gold and gærsume feoh and færde þa wes swiþe bald on heorte he wes bliþe þat mæiden he weddede and nom heo to his bedde seoueniht he wes þære hit þutte him seoue ȝere ær he aȝen come to fæhten wih his broþer of witten heo weoren amadde þe him swa rædden wes in norwæye in þisse londe ihærde sugge þurh summe sæg treowe of his broþer wifþinge and for wulche þinge and for wulchere neode he to norwæiȝe færde hine biþohte of swulchere dede and þas worde seide þe sæg wes itreouwe wa wurþe a þon broþer þe biswikeþ þene oþer whær beo ȝe mine cnihtes whar beo ȝe mine kempen whar beo ȝe mine leoue men nu we scullen liþen heo ferden to humberlonde þer weoren castles stronge þe castles heo nomen alle and strangede þe walles he lette blauwen bemen and nam al þa burhwes þa weoren on his broþer londe þe he hafde an heonde he dude þerinne mæte inoh and wepmen unifoh þat me mihte heom walden wih anwalde his cnihtes mid himseoluen to þare sæ færden þar laien bi þan brimme and bisilichen hit wisten wes in norweȝe and noht herof nuste he wende þat his broþer nuste noht of his fære leaf he nom at ælfing þe wes norweine king and he him ȝef answere a mote þu wel færen and delgan mi dohter þe me is swþe deore þis understod þe ȝeonge quene faren þat heo scolde heo hauede enne leouemon þa heo swuþe ileoued hæfde þene king of denemark þe leof hire weis on mode he wes swiþe god cniht he hahte þa sende dalgan þa quene into denemarke and guþde þa wes hire gome deore stille bocrunen heo senden him to ræden and seiden him þat a king of britaine hauede heo biwedded and ihaued heo to bedde al hire vnþonkes þerfore hire wes uneþe and heo he wolden læiden toward his leoden næuede heo bute þreo nihte feorst faren þat heo scolde sone hit mæi ilimpen þanne ihc hunnen liþe þah þu habben blisse and griþ ne speke ich þe naueremore wiþ and ihc sende þe gretinge of mine gold ringe þa isæh þis wa him wes ful iwis stille he wes iswoȝen on his kinestole me warp on his nebbe cold wellewatere þa þe king wes awaht he wes swuþe idraht he seide forþrihtes whar beoþ mine cnihtes fare we swiþe to þare sæ sele mine dranches king on ueste mid gudfulle folke to þere sæ wenden scipen þer heo funden makede muchul sæflot and ferden mid streme toȝenes þare hauene þer from halde þa com i wide sæ he imette his wiþeriwinne scip ærne toȝen scip þa hit al towonde to scifren horn aȝen horne halde þe wacre þer wes moni breoste mid brade spere iþurlud helmes þer gullen beornes þer fullen balluw þer wes riue flæh bliue and hæld æfter monie scipen he þer cahte he iseh a scip þar hit laþ sulkene wes þat seilclæþ he clupede to his dringes nu forh nu niþinges þet is þere quene scip þe us biforen queccheþ haldeþ alle þerto and ȝif ȝe hit mawen ifon æueremare ich æu leouie þa wile þa ich liouie mid strengþe heo halden to schipen and þa quene heo igripen sloh þa scipgumen and alle heo nom þat garsume and ladde þa quene delgan toward denemarke anan he þoþte heo to habben to his awere bihoue and oþer weis hit sæht forh geinde glad he wes on heorte he þohte to habben delgan to quene of denemarke ah him com muchel lætting swa him wes alre laþest æft aras a ladlich weder þeostrede þa wolcne þe wind com on weþere and þa sæ he wraþede vþen þer urnen alse tunes þer burnen rapes þer braken balu wes fulle riue scipen þer sunken þer þreo and fifti scipen feollen to grunde in þa teonfulle sæ torneden sæiles hauede a god scip ne gomede him towiht he hine biþohte weht he don mihten he igrap ane wiæxe muchele and swiþe scærpe he forheow þænne mæst atwo riht amidden he lette seil and þane meæst liþen mid vþen þus seide sære him gromede æuerælc æhte mon help þat we libben þat we comen to londe ne recche we on wulche leoden heo ferden mid þon wedere nusten heo nauere whudere vnder fif dawene ȝeong heo comen to þisse londe comen þes kinges cnihtes þe þæ sæ wusten and nomen þene king and delgan þæ quene heo seiden heom enne strongne ræd nu ȝe beon alle dead ah ȝef ȝe wullen us seuggen ȝet ȝe mawen libben whonene ȝe beþ icumene and whet ȝe her sohten answerede mid godlichen worden we beoh sæwerie men and we wullet soþ sucgen ah nuten næuere þæs gumen into whuche londe heo beoþ icume ne þas strond we ne cnoweþ þe we isoht habbeþ þis lon ne þas leoden ne wha her lauerd is ne we nuten na þe ma þat we ne speken wit ure ifæn ah ich eow bidde leoue men leddeþ us to þæn kinge and ich him wulle suggen of blissen and of sorwen and þa cnihtes heom lædden to heore leodkinge and þa quene heore æhte and his iferen and seiden him þat he wes i brutaine i kinges londe sone swa he to þan king com wisliche he clupede him an hail wurh þu king is þi broþer and ich hatte gumenen ich wes lauerd denemarkene king þeos wifman hatte delcan com to norhweie to kinge þe king him ȝef delcan þe ȝare wes mi leouemon sonden commen bitwenen þe soþe word me seiden whennen wolde liþen and mine leouemon leden toȝenes ich him ferde mid feowerti scipen gode and mid al swa fele cnihtes swa þa scipen beren mihten and ich wulle suggen þe an wunder he haueden scipen seouen hundred and ich bigon strong fæht and to flenne his men ich awelde and monie ich aquelde and þer ich nom delgan þe ær wes mi leouemon and ich sugge þe to soþe þat ȝet leoueþ þi broþer for he hald to þen londe and wel com to hauene and ich isæh þare quene scip quecchen mid vþen and ich ferden þeræfter and biwan hit mid fæhte þa wes ich bliþe on mine quike liue þa ich wes i wide sæ wiþer com toȝenes þet weder wes swa wilde and þa sæ wrædde and draf me to þisse londe into þire leode and me do þine milce for þu eart mihti ouer me þe king heom lette halden in swiþe feire benden in ane stronge castle þer he heom wel biwiste nes hit buten feower wiken þat þas þinge ifaren weoren riden into scottelonde mid feower hundred schipen folc þer wes fæie he sende his boden to his broþer and bad hine quicliche aȝeuen him his quene and þane kinge þe his gumen hauede afalled and ȝef he hit nolle him sal beon þa wurse in his londen ich wulle gon and slæn al þat ich finde mid fehte and mid fure þis feoreward ich him halde bute he me wullen ȝeuen þat ich him toȝeurne and mi londe rume and fare to his riche and aȝeue me mine burȝes and mine buri gode castles and toures þe he me halt a teonen forþ ferde þas sonde to king and seide him þeos ibeod from brenne his broþer and him warde al þat he ȝernde þat ne sulde he nauere ibiden þe while þe he mihte riden þe sonde aȝan ferde and seide hit brenne brenne wes swiþe wraþ and bannede is ferde scheldede his scalken alse heo to wiȝe solden folkede his cnihtes alsa heo scolden fehten an halue hæiȝede him toȝeines muchel æie wes þære vnder þan wude of kalatere þer heo heom imetten and vuele hem igretten togædere heo comen heo graneden sone feondliche heo feohten bi þeosende heo fellen swiþe faht king swa duden his bruttes heo weoren swiþe ohte men þat æþel heo biwunnen heom from bæh and mid his folke he fleh al toward þare sæ mid muchele vnsælþe and heom æfter and heo adun leide sixti þusende he leide to þen gronde a schip funde bi þon brimme stonden he bicom þerinne mid his twelf monnen ne leædde he na ma isunde of alle his monnen ouer sæ he ferden in toward france and þeo forwundede men wende into holte þa al þis wes ifarren and wes awæi ifloȝen in euerewic huld eorlene husting he bed þat his riche men rihtne read radden whet him weore to donne bi þon ilke monne and bi kinge þe he huold i bende for him sende word bi ane wise monne þat if he him wold leoþien of laþe his benden þat he wolde his mon beon mid alle his monueorde and he him wolde ȝeuen al þat gold þe he haueden i denemark lond and ælcche ȝere him senden þreo þusund punden herto him wolden finden ȝisel of his gilde wih þon þe he lette sckere hine and his ifere and his leouemen swa deore to denemark leoden king him ȝette þat forward þat he ȝerde and freoliche hine lette faren and alle his iueren hauede þeo ȝeseles and þa ȝeuen gode and his monræidene mid monschipe biwunnen and ledde forh þa wifmon swiþe fæire and he heo bohte swiþe deore bruken he heo þohte huld þas riche wel feole ȝere and he swiþe freolic al his folc he ladde he makede swiþe god griþ his gumen hit wel heolden þa weoren i þissere leode laȝen swiþe gode and al leouede þeone king þe quic wes an londe þa hauede an heond al brutteines lond he ferde ȝeond al and lawen sette he scawede þa wuodes and þa wildernes meduwen and mores and þa hæȝe muntes burwes and tunes and al hit ȝeorne bihold þe king hine biþohte whet he don mihte he bigon ane stræte muchele and swiþe græte feiȝer and swiþe long þurhut al þis kinelond and þe king and his folc fosse heo clupeden heo liþ hut of toteneis a þet cume to toteneis is in cornwale in scotdale anoþer stret he makede swiþe hendi from suþhamtone to seint deuwi seoþþe he makede þe þridde þe kærf þis lond amidde þa þeos stræt weoren idon þa leide þa king heom laȝen on þat whaswa i þen stræten breken griþ þe king him wolde binimen his lif ah whaswa oþerne imette þer fæire hine igrætte þis weoren þeos kinges strætte þe ich ikenned habbe i frænce wes þe wes þeos kinges broþer on his heorte he hauede grome on his mode muchele scome þat he hæuede iloren his kinelond and his quene þe he leouede and him swiþe scomede þat he swa iscend wes he wunede inne france mid his tweolfe iferen he herde þon king and wel him iquemde and al þa frensce leoden swiþe heo loueden brenne for biȝet muchel feoh and feire hit dælde nes he noht ȝælpinde ah he wes ȝeuecusti he wes þer swiþe oht mon and æþele weore hid deden and him þer ofte wel ilomp þerfore he wes þe leofere þa he wes þere wel cuþ and oueral icnawen and þe king hine leouede and al his leoden þa nom he his iferen and bisohte þeos folkes king þat he him sculde fulste mid his gode folke his lond to biȝetene of his breoþer þe king him bihette and wel hit him ȝette þa bead he leaue and he furþer laþ to seguine duc þe lauerd wes of burguine and of þen brutlonde þe is biȝeonde sæstronde feire he igrette þeone duc þa he his griþ sohte he seide þat he him wolden hæren and halden hine for herra leofliche him buwen and halden hine for lauerd þe duc þerfore fain wes and hine fæire onfeng wes swiþe hende his hap wes þe betere cuþe on hundes cuþe an hauekes he cuþe mid his honden hanlie þa harpe þurh his hændecraftes hiredmen hine leouede and his lauerd alse wilcume swa he weoren his aȝene sune þe duc hauede æne dohter þe him wes swiþe deore ah he neuede nenne sune þerfore he wes sari þe duc bisæh a brenne þe hauede bodi hende and him to seide mid sohfeste huȝe þu ært hende and þu ært hæh iboren and þu eært cniht swiþe god and þu eært me iqueme þu come ouer streme þu eart kinges istreonne þu eært me swiþe iliþe and ich þe leouie swiþe al þat ich þe bihate ich hit þe wulle halden ich wulle ȝeuen þe mine dohter þa me is swiþe deore and æfter mine dæie al mi drihliche lond for wel hit luuieþ alle mine burnes þat hit þus beo idon and þat þu þis vnderfon þa answerede mid beienliche worden ich hit þankie þe and alle þine þeode for eouwer muchele wurhchipe wel þat ȝe me vnnen al þis wes idon alse þe duc demde blisse was on hirede þeo þis mæide nom mid muchelere wurhschipe he wunede mid þan ducke þa þat forme ȝer wharþ forþ igan þa wes þe duc dead and hauede his duweþe al þon folk he wes leof ase heore aȝene lif for he heold swiþe god griþ and glæd wes wiþ his monnen he hauede swiþe mucchel lond þat al stod an his hond and he hæfde a swiþe god wif and he heo leouede alse his lif wiþinnen a lut ȝeren hine biþohte an his broþer þe his lond binom him he sende his sonde ȝeond burguine londe þe ferde wes swa muchel þat heo wes vnimete into normandie he com and þer he þa sæ nom and he ferde mid sunde into þisse londe bæh a þat lond mid his leodeferde sonde com to þa him soþ sæide þat his broþer hefde isoht his riche mid vnimete ferde icommen to his eærde lette beoden ȝeond al his londe and bæd al þa kempen þe wiþinne sæ wuneden þat heo comen to his neode to driuen vt þa vnleoden ȝeærwe wes þat ferde and forþward ifusede heo comen swa næh þere twam ferden þa ȝet leouede þa ælde quene a wifmon wis and kene heo wes ihaten ho iber and þat heo wel cudde heo nom hire on anne curtel þe wes swiþe totoren hire hem heo up itæh hire cneon he wes swiþe neh heo eode on hire bare foten al heo hit dude for gode heo com to þere ferde þe icumen wes to þissere eærde heo axede æfter brenne þer he wes bi ferde þer he hine wepnede alse he to fihte þeohte and alle his burnes duden on heore burnen swa leonge me hire tahte þat heo him to com vfenen heo him orn bitwixen hire ærmes heo hine nom ofte heo hine clupte and ofte heo hine custe a whet wult þu brenne whet wult þu balwe menge ȝif þu sleast þine broþer ne bistz þu neuer oþer ne beon ȝit bute tweien mine sunen ȝit be beien biþenc o þire monschipe biþenc o þire moder biþenc a mire lare þu eært mi bærn deore loka her þa tittes þat þu suke mid þine lippes lou war hire þa wifmon þa þe a þas weoreld ibær leo wær here þa wombe þe þu læie inne swa longe leo war here þa ilke likame ne do þu me neuere þane scome þat ich for þine þinge mid sæxe me ofstinge nu hit is vmbe seoue ȝere þat þu weren here and al forewarde þu breke toward þine breoþer þu weore his mon bicumen and he þe leouede also his sone aþes þu him swore swiken þat þu noldest þu hauest woh and he haueþ riht þat is þe swiþe muchel pliht and ouer sæ þu liþe al buten læue to alfinge kinge and nome his dohter ȝeonge swa þu woldest mid ferde faren to þissen eærde and don þe seoluen bisemar fehten wit þine broþer ȝif denemarkene king idrecched þe neuede and suþþen þu come and herm her iuore and æft wendest ouer sæ and nu þu ært sel icumen nu þu eært londes weldent and us scal beon þe wurse mid uncuþe mannen þu wlt þi cun quelle ne sculde na cniht hærȝien þær he hauede hames iwald no eæft on his cuhþe quedschipe wurchen ah leoue sune bei þi starke þonc leie adun þin hærescrud and þinne rede sceld and þi sper longe and þi swerd stronge and ilef þire moder and leoue þinne broþer vrnen ire teares ouer hire leores þat isæh and sorȝeden on his heorte let cliden his gare þat hit grund sohte he scæt his riche sceld feor ut in þene feld awei he warp his gode breond and of mid þere burne and his moder mildelichen ferden in ænne bradne feld and him toȝennes þa weop þe breoþer al swa dede þe oþer þa spec þe moder milde mid muþe ȝit buþ mine leoue sunen liþeþ tosomne and iwurþeþ sæhte and euer on blisse cusseþ and cluppeþ cuþie meies cnihtes ȝit beoþ boþe kene while ich wes quene nis hit noht unhuhtlic incker moder inc hateþ þer heo hom custen þe weren kinges bearn bifeoren þa twam ferden freondscipe makeden bemen þer bleowen blisse wes on folke þer weore segge songe þer were pipen imagge þer wes swa muchel murehþe þat ne mihte heo beon namare þus iweraþ sæht whit his broþer þa makeden heo ane laþunge of heore leoue folke þat al comen to lundene uppe wite of feowerti punden to þan hustingge biforen kinge þa weoren al þas leoden at lundene isomed þer wes þe king and al his kineriche bruttes and scottes and moni scone þein þer wes þe duc of burgoine ihaten weoren þa broþerne bliþe on here mode and al þa twa ferden of moni ane eærde þe kingges nomen to ræde at riche heore monnen þat heo wolden mid ferde faren into france in france weore læwen sulkuþe a þan dawen and selcuþe tidende for þer were feower kinges seide to brenne fare we bliue in touwarde france and mid fehte hit biwinnen heo bleuwen heore bemen and buden here ferde and to þere sæ wenden and wel ouer commen mid nihen hundred scipene heo commen into hauene heo commen into þen lond and neoþereden þa leoden com þa tiþende to þan feouwer kinggen þat king wes icumen and þe duc brenne mid unimete ferde to biwinne france togadere þe kinges come and æþes heo sweoren þat heo wolde libben togadere oþer liggen and euerælc oþer halden for broþer mid aþen heo hit bihæten and ful wel hit heolden heo sommeneden heore ferde þe wes feondliche stor and heo ferden bliue toward mid his ferde wes biforen togædere come þeos kinges mid heore hereþringes ferde whit ferde feonliche feuþten scottes and bruttes beiene togaderes here læuerd heom biforen wende bisides mid his folke of burguine heo smiten togædere helmes þere gullen breken brade sperren bordes þer scænden redde blod scede rinkas feollen þer wes muchel gristbat þer wes cumene fæl weoren þa hulles and þa dæles iwriȝen mid þe dæden ibræid up his helm and clipede to ne isihst þu leoue broþer heou breoþeþ þa frensce and þa ferde of unker londe isund ȝet stondet greiþe we us seoluen mid grimme oure ræsen and heom on ileggen mid orde and mid egge wes swiþe bald and þis wel bileouede al heo heom slowen þe heo aneh comen and þas feower kinges heo leiden to þan grunde whulc riche mon þer atfleh into castle he abeh and heo him after ferden mid spere and mid swerde nes þer nan oþer liþ ȝif heo nalden ȝernen griþ þene castel heo nomen hine seulfne and his folke sloȝen þus heo þurheoden francene þeode in þan ilcan ȝere wes kaisere and his broþer beiene togaderes for heo hauede france mid fehte biwunnen and alle þa fre londes þe leien into france þa hauede heo muche riche irumed to honde þeo speken heo togadere þa sele ibroþeren and seide þat heo wolden halden hustinge of allen þat leoden þe heore læwen leoueden and of al þan londen þe stoden on heore heonden and þurh heore alre dome heo wolden fære to rome to wreken o þon folke remus þene feire þe his broþer in rome ofsloh þer biforen fele ȝere for al þat monkun wes þa ȝet þere al þa kinges þus duden swa heomself demmeden heo gaderede heore ferde in francene eærde þa þat folc wes icumen sone heo fusden for þer wes swa mochel folc and swa vnimete þat a neuere nane walde ne mihte hit al halde heo ferden ouer mungiu mid muchelen here ferden seoþþen heo ferden ful iwis þer me clipþ munt senis heo nomen al taurins and iuorie and alle þe burȝewes of lumbardie versæus and pauie and cremuinne plæucence and buluine þet wæter heo ouerferden of taurim and seoþþen heo ferden ouer bardun tuscan heo habbeþ al biwunnen i heo slowe monie þusend monnen swa heo nehlehte toward rome to late heom þuste are heo þer comen and þat romeanisce floc swiþe wes offered for heom comen stronge tidinge from þon kinge haueden al þa reuen þe wunede in rome and alle þa riche gumen þa rome burwe walden iloked tweiene eorles i þon ilka ȝeære þe sculden witen þat lond and wissien þa leoden and læden here ferde wher hit neod weore for heore beire nome ich þe wulle telle þe an hehte þe oþer þeos ilke eorles weren kene ohte men and wel idone and al þat romanisce folc ferde bi heore ræde þeos eorles comen to rome to þan redfulle monen axeden heom ræddes of swulchere neode wheþer heo boden ferde whit to fehten þe heo speken him wit and seoþþe axeden his griþ þa weoren in rome wise men on dome and þohten bipechen mid heore prætwrenchen heo nomen heom to ræde and to somrune þat noht heo nolden fehten no heore ferd leade ah we wullet gan a leoþe and leoue we wulleþ wurchen we wulleþ setten heom an hond al þis romanisce lond and wurþien heom in leoden al swa mon lauerd scal ȝeuen heom seluer and gold and bitechen heom al þis lond ȝeuen heom garisum swa heo wulleþ kepe vre childre to ȝisle ȝef heo swa wulleþ ælcches barunes sune þe i þissere burh wuneþ þeo scullen beon icorne and swiþe wel iborne childre swiþe hendi ȝisles feor and twenti and ælche ȝer of golde ten hundred punde þa kingges buh stronge and of ferrene lond heo habbeþ swa muche folc swa nes næuer eær on ferde þe kinges beoþ ȝunge of æhte ȝissinge sone swa heo ihurden swulch worde don heo hit wulleþ for heo ne mawen bidde mare buten þat we ȝernen heore ære and ȝif we mawen swa wel don þat heo þis wullen vnderfon and bileuen oure leoden and faren to heore londe seoþþen we sculleþ biginnen to don ure wille for betere is þat we leosen leoue oure children þanne we nimen swulne ræd þat we allen beo deade and al rome burh mid fure forberned and al þat liggende lond þat liþ into rome beo al biræiued þe nu stondeþ riche for ȝif hit wulleþ þe is oure god of þisse lond hermid we sculleþ heom bicharren and seoþþen heom amarren þat ne sculleþ heo nauere isunde cumen to heore londe þa seiden heo in halle þisne read halde we alle þeos eorles heom gereden mid godliche scruden and nomen mid heom cnihtes swa feole swa heom þuhte ha leopen an heore feire hors biwriȝen mid fæire palle ælc mon nom an honde ane scale of rede golde feouwer daies fulle forþward heo wenden þat heo comen to þon eærde þer wes mid his ferde and his broþer beiene tosomne heo axeden aþelinges wer leye þa kinges me heom tahte þa feldes þer weoren þare kingene tælddes heo ferden biliue þat þider heo comen liþe heom þuhte muchel ferlich of al þeon folke wher hit al inumen weore þat heo iseiȝen þere heo iseiȝen king buȝen ut of telde and heo lihten adun and leofliche on cneowen forn at þan kinge heo fullen to folde læuerd þine ære for þu ært leodene king we þe aȝeueþ rome and al þa riche and al þa londes þe liggeþ into rome and alle þe madmes þat we on horde habbeþ and swa muchel garsumme swa þine gumen kepeþ and æþes we sulleþ þe swerien þat we þe nulleþ swiken uppen ure godd wel idon þe is icliped we swullen þine men bicomen and þine monscipe heien mid allen oure mihten daies and nihtes and we þe wulleþ bitechen ut of þissere riche feur and twenti ȝunge riche monne childere þe scullen beon alle icorne and swiþe heiȝe iborne we scullen of þissere þeode cumen to þire neode and whuder þu hatest for þu ært ure hærre and to swulche forward we beoþ hidere isende and we biddeþ þine ære nu and aueremare þe king wes stille and þa swiken speken ille he weonden þat hit weoren soþ þat heo iseid haueden ah al heo þohten oþer to slæn king and his broþer þeo hit up bræc hit wes god þat he spec wel ȝe me bihatet halde ȝeif ȝe wulleþ eow swal beon þe betere to swuche forewarde fon ich hit wulle and ȝe scullen of me halden and habben me for harre and habben freoliche eoure lond and we freond iwurþen todaie a seouennihte bringeþ me her rihtte gold and gersume ȝeoue and eower ȝisles and cumen her on fore þe hæxete of rome and swerie me æþes þat æþ heom scel iwurþen and bicumen nu mine men and mine monscipe hæien and ȝif ȝe þis nulleþ alle ich ȝeow aquelle ah swiþe ham rideþ leou wer here ich eow abide ȝif ȝe spekeþ mid rihte comeþ todæi a seouennihte and ȝif ȝe spekeþ wowe bilæuet inne rome and ich eou wullen to faren and bringen eou sorwen an kare þeos swiken gunnen ride ham into rome and ȝarekeden heore ȝeouen and alle heore ȝisles and to heore dæie brohten to kinge and he heom faire vnderfeng and freondscipe bihehte ȝisles heo him ȝeouen sone and his men bicome and he mid þan ilke foreward fusde eft aȝenward and þa swiken sone ferden to rome and brenne beie tosomne nomen heom to ræde and to somrune þat heo wolden liþen þurhout lumbardie and faren to alemainne and þa aþelene biwinnen þa almainnisce men weoren of here cume warre and heo gadereden heom toȝeines strongliche ferden of alle þeon londe þon keiser hæfde an honde and þa romanisce men ful ȝære hit iseȝen þat and beiene weoren ifarenne heo ȝærkeden ræhþen twa þusend rideres and swiþe an hiȝende senden heom efter heo letten forþ bisiden anoþer folc riden ten þusend kempen alle icudde þat heo biforen comen þan kaiser to helpe þe wolde aȝen king feht ihalden and þat romanisce floc riden heom bihinden heo þohten heom beon onfest þer þe hulles weore mest and senden heom arewen i þon weie narewe slean heore lauerd and his broþer mid him heo forȝeten here ȝisles and þat griþ þat heo ȝurden æþes and þa treuþen þerfore heo hauede teonen and his broþer beien weoren warre of þon swikedome þe heom com of rome þa haueden heo þa mære æie of þan alemainnisce kaisere þa speken heo mid ræde for heo haueden neode þat and his ferde aȝen faren sculde fehten wih þat romanisce folc and fellen ȝef heo mihten and bæh ouer munt mid muclen his strengþe to feahten wiþ þon keisere and wih þon alemainisce here fondien on fehte ȝif he hine ouercumen mæhte and wheþer heore of þen broþeren þe ærht his fæht ouercome come onȝean sonen to helpen þon oþer þe folc of burguine ferde aȝan mid brenne of france and peitou sworen him and plicten of þan maine and of þan turuine treuliche him hærden of normandie and of flaundres freoliche him fulsten and of lohærenne heo liþe to mid strengþe and þat folc of cascuine þe noht nælden griþien and folc of fele leode þe liþe forþ mid brennen to þan romanisce men þe heom æfter uoren brenne and his folc heom to comen anan swa heo iseiȝen buȝe heom toȝennes swa þat romainnisce folc sohte to flæinde and heo heom æfter foren and monie þer fullen and swiþe monie þer fluwen and ferden to rome and þe riche softe heom beh æfter mid starkere fore ferde toward rome and þe aþel king wes in alemainne ferde he hauede inoh muchel and vnifeie bruttes and wailsce scottes and densce þer wes þe king þe god wes to neode þa iherden tellen þe ten þusend cnihtes þe weoren icumen of rome þan keisere to fulsten þat þe riche ferde touward rome and summe heore men islæȝene and summe todriuene nomen heom ræde þat þeonenen heo wolden riden riht touward rome eære þider come þat word com to of his broþer heo he hauede itaken on and al whet he haueden idon and oþer sonde þer com þe sone him talde þat tweie þusend cnihtes þe werren i þon alemainnesce fehte wolden aȝen sone faren into rome and al makeden heore faren alse ha wolden a þare niht faren wes swiþe wis and warscipe him folweden he hauede monie alemains mid agge toheowen and monie he ledde isunde mid him ibunden he hauede tweine wisse men i þon fuhte biwunnen þeo cuþe þes londen lawen and speken whit þon leoden king heom to spæc and þus heom wiþ spilede ihere ȝe cnihtes whet ich eow wulle cuþen ic inc habbe beiene an inne mine benden ȝif ȝet wulleþ after ræde faren ich inc wulle freoiȝen mid gode ræue bihon and makien inc riche faren mid me suluen and ich inckere freond wurþe ȝif ȝit me wulleþ laden þe cunne þas leoden riht to þan weie þe ȝit witen ful wel þar þis romanisce folc forþ wulleþ riden and we heom sculleþ fon on and heom wiþ fahten feollen oure feondes and faren after brenne and liþen mid ræde and rome biliggen and þis ich inc biseche þat al we wurþen sele þa cnihtes weoren wise and ful ȝerewitele and al ham iwurden þe heom toȝernde and heom markede forþ touward muntgiu heo ferden into ane mucele bæche þa munte bihalues þer heo forþ sculden cumen þa weoren þa gumen feie wes bi hullen swiþeliche stille þa comen liþen þa weore romleoden heom to leop biforen and bihinden þeo cnihtes weoren vnwepned þa þe wæne heom wes ȝeueþe heo wenden to beon sikere þeo heom on sohte ne nomen heo nonne cniht quic ah alle heo heom aqualden for nauede nan cnihte þet he næs þere god kimppe ne neauere nenne herdswein þat he ne fahte alse þein ne næuer nænne hirdcnaue þat he nas wod on his laȝe þat faht bigon at midniht and laste þat hit wes dæiliht and swa þene dæi longe heo wenden seoþþen þa muntes and qualden alle þa ilke þe aniht weoren atcropene a þene mærȝen letten blawen his bemen and beonnede his ferde hahte forþrihtes riden þenne ilke wæi þe forþ into rome læi æfter brenne his broþer þe heom biforen wes hit hirde suggen and his broþer abad forþ heo buȝen beiene þat heo come to rome buri þa burh heo bileien mid heore leodferden þet folc þer wiþinnen heom ohtliche wiþ fehten and brenne heo bileien al abeoten and þa oþere hem scuten to scærpe gares ofte heo letten grundhat læd gliden heom an heore hæfd stockes and stanes and strales hate and swiþe wel heo wereden þa walles of rome þer fore alle þan cræften þe heo uten cuþþen ne for alle þen fuhte þe heore ferde makede ne mihten heo romewal nawiht onwalden ah heo loseden monie þusend godere monnen and tuwen heom fram þan walle wa wes heore herten þe king him biþohten whet heo don mihten and seiden heom bitwenen leteþ comen sonen þa feouwer and twenti children þe we habbeþ to ȝislen and doþ up an waritreo þeron heo scullen winden and wreken þan siþes and ure wiþeriwinnen for ȝet we scullen heom to liþen swa heom biþ ælre læþest þe furken weoren aræred heo teuwen up þa ȝisles and heom þer hengen biforen heore eldren wa wes heore faderen þeo heo iseiȝen heore beærn hangen mid muþen heo seiden mid aþen heo hit sworen þerfore hit sculden iwurþen muchele þa wurse swa þat for deaþe ne for lif nalden heo nauere makien griþ for þat weoren þa richcheste and þa alre hæhȝeste and þa radfulleste þe wuneden in rome þat biforen heore eȝenen bihulden and iseȝen þat heore bern me onheng on heȝe trouwen þa orles weorne iwende swiþe for þeonne þe heom wite solden and into lumbardie into þon leode efter monkunne þe heom sculden fulsten to helpene heore monne aȝen and brenne þa com þer a mon irnen from þan twam eorlen þe brohte writrunen into þere burh of rome þat seide heom to soþe þat þa eorles comen in þer ilke nihte mid ten þusend cnihten and mid ferde vnimete of monnen on foten þe sculden cumen bihalues and king aquellen and his broþer beiene togadere ȝif ȝe me wulleþ ileuen anan swa hit beoþ auen sendeþ ut cnihtes and biginneþ to fihten ær hit beo midniht ich sugge eow hit soþriht comeþ mid heore mannen and þe sculleþ eow wurþliche wreken on eower wiþeriwinnen anan swa þe dæi wes agan swa heo ȝeten openeden letten ut cnihtes bigunnnen muchele fihtes swa heo fehten al niht þat hit wes dæiliht þa com þer fusen vnimete ferde an mid muchele monkinne ut of lumbardie and liþen touward brenne and he heom faht wiþ feondliche swiþe and him resde to to þan romanisce folke and heo fusden swiþe þe faht wes unimete þer wes ballu riue bruttes þer fullen and burstes þare hæfden and þa romanisce men remden heom uuenen whet wolde ȝe her niþinges mid þe bruttisce kinge wende ȝe mid ginnen romen biwinnen wenden ȝe mid fehten to fellen uren leoden and beon eow seluen riche and welden al rome ȝe scullen drinken eowre blod balu eow is ȝeueþe ȝe beoþ ure bernenne bone þerfore ȝe sculleþ breoþen fallen and ure leoden swa eow biþ alre læþust and buȝen heom fram þan fuhte wihinnen are muchele dic þe heo hæfden ilet dælfen þat heore folc mihten swiþe wel wunien wiþinnen þerinnen heo speken þerinne heo runden ane lutle while ne leaste hit nawiht ane mile and þus heo seiden heom bitwune ȝif we hennen fareþ þus alle heo wulleþ æfter us and ȝif hit swa ilimppeþ þat we ham cumen liþen heorten we haueden sare and ure cun ædwit aueremare ah ga we heom on mid sweorde for al heo beoþ forlorne and ureke ue ure winemæies for leouere us is here mid manscipe to fallen þanne we heonne isunde farren ure frenden to scare þe while þe heo þus speken and spileden mid worden wende þa þeodisce men þat wolden þenne and seiden heom bitwenen in þere burh of rome nu heo wulleþ heonnen nulleþ heo namare fehten ah and his broþer al heo þoþten oþer heo senden ut of rome cnihtes wel idone feowerti hundred to hæȝen ane castele to kepen king and his broþer and baldeliche whiþ fehten and þa oþere of rome riden heom bihinden and slæn heom bitwenen and wreken ore tounen þe cnihtes weoren on fore fer ut of rome þa hehte and his broþer lihteþ of eowre blanken and stondeþ on eowre sconken and kerueþ eowre spere longe and makiet heom scorte and stronge scradieþ eower sceldes al of þe smal enden and we eow wulleþ biforen libben oþer liggen and aueralc god mon harde hine sulue for her scullen þe wædlen alle iwurþen riche blawen ore bemen and banneþ ore ferde and maken we of ure uæren fihtie ferden and on aueralche hæpe hertoȝe stæpne þa heom makie balde and togadere halde and wenden to þen walle on æuerælchere halue hiȝendliche fo we on for alle we scullen wel don þeo blewen heo here bemen þat heo of rome hit sculden iheren and heo ut iwenden ohte kempen þa iseȝen heo of rome and his broþere þa clupeden heo lude ȝeond þare leoden nu fleþ ure ifan nu we sculleþ heom to gan mid þe forwarde monnen ut wenden him com æfter mid fifti hundred cnihtes mid alle heore wepnen þe weoren vniwælde þa oþere weoren swifte heore wepnen weoren lihte heo leiden togadere and feonliche fuhten weoren heo of rome alle ridinde þa oþere afoten and fengen heom toȝæines and slowen alle heore hors here hæp wes þe lættere heo slowe heo nomen heo duden heore wille of þan rommonen alle heo slowen þat heom aȝen stoden heo breken þa romwalles on auerache halue and binnen heo iwenden and þa burh awelden biwunnen heo rome þe riche burh wel idone þer heo funden michel gold and gærsume unimete heo unbunde þa locun drowen ut þa baiȝes þa palles and þa purpres þe iworht weore in puill alle þa maþemes þe weoren monie kunnes þer wes moni wrehche sone iworþen riche al þa seouen nihte his iwil þar hefde ælc cniht of seoluere and of golde inoh of þon londe letten þa kinges don fæire þinges timbrien þa hallen bæten þa walles þe þer weoren tobrokene mid þeon balu fehte letten heo climben on hæh cleopien to þon folke þat þe kinges heom speken wiþ and þer setten heore griþ þat ne wurþe na man swa wod þat of oþere falle his blod ne of his æhte ȝerne buten he hit ȝeuen him wulle and alle þe flæmen þe iflowe buþ of rome þe aȝan wulleþ cumen þes kinges griþ wilniæn and bicumen þes kinges mon alse we hit ær cuþden cumen al mid sibben and her heore lif libben and habben þa ilke læȝen þe stoden bi heore ældre dæwen and ure hæȝe king hit bitæcheþ brenne þe scæl bilæuen here and beon eower kæisere and himseolf wule liþen and eower læue habben nen he wule buȝen into bruttæine wælle muchel wes þa wop þæ þeonne wende ah heo weoren ifrouuerd sone for þan richedom of rome þer boȝede king of lumbardie and gon wenden into þisse londe lette he ȝeond his castles makie kinewurþe werkes rihten alle þæ hallen and stronginen þæ walles bulden þa bures hæien þa toures and swa þis wunliche lond mid wurþscipe wælden and walde rome fulle fiftene ȝere þa endede wel wes romanisce folc þæs heo seolf nomen heore lond and heolden on heore hond burh and heore blissæ seoþþen wes deæd and i þisse londe makede læȝen stronge and laȝen swiþe gode þe bi his liue stoden ferde to wales and anne burh makede he heo makeda æþþele uppen uske þan wætere of þon ilke flode þe king hire nome funde þan king heo wes deore kæir usch heo næmde and seoþþen heo wes ihæten kair lion ich wullen seggen þe for wan vmbe feole ȝere æfter forþfare herden þe men of rome of deaþe and seiden heom bitwenen while he dude us tuone nu is þe king iburied wrake we us on bruttes and into þan londen we sullen faren bringen þer sorwen and kare hider heo gunnen senden of romanisce ende feower ferrædene þa we clipieþ ferden þe weoren on þan ilke dæȝen legiuns ihaten werren on alche legiun þus feole leodkempen six þusend and six hundred and sixti iferen þeos comen bi wateren of weorren heo weoren wise heo duden i þisse londe alle leode sorwen and auer o þon ende heomseoluen weoren isunde and aueralche wintre inne wales heo wuneden heo iwunne þe burh kair uske and þerinne heo wuneden a þat her com liþen ma of heore leoden for ilke legiuns heo clupeden kair usc kaer liun seoþþen her com oþer moncun þe heo cleopeden kaerliun nu ich þe habben iseid hu hit is igan of kaerliun bi glommargan fo we ȝet to to þan blisfulle kinge þa he hæuede imaked þas burh and heo inemned kaer usc þa þe burh wes strong and hende þeo gon he þonnen wenden he wende riht to lundene þe burh he leouede swiþe he bigon þer ane ture þe strengeste of al þe tune and mid muchele ginne a ȝæt þervnder makede þeo clupede men hit belȝæsȝate nu and aueremare þe nome stondeþ þare leouede þe king in alre blisse and alle his leoden leoueden hine swiþe an his dæies wes swa mochel mæte þat hit wes vnimete þat folc þurh heore drunken moni þusend swulten þe king leouede longe þat hit com touward his ende þat i lundene he wes dæd sari wes his duȝeþe wa wes heom on liue for þæs kinges dæþe heo ferden to his horde and nome þer muche deal goldes heo makeden ane tunne of golde and of ȝimme þene king heo duden þerinne þat wes here louerd vp heo hine duden heȝe an ufenmeste þan turre þat me mihte hine bihalden wide ȝeon þeon londe þat heo duden for muchelere luue for he wes here dure læuerd þus iuor al king seoþþen com his sune hehte his sune wellen æþele wes þe gume welle witer wes þer a mon and wisliche heold his cunedom sæhte and sibbe he luuede unstronge monnen he leoþede griþ he heolde alse his fæder god mid þon bezste bute þat þa densce men dunriht atsoken þat heo to brutlonde nolden maren senden gold ne garsume ne gauel of þon londe hine biþohte what he don mæhte he seonde his sonde wide ȝen his londe he beonnede his folc and ȝærekede ferde muchele and grete mid monnen vnimete he to scipe wende and fram þan londe hælde ofer þane saltne strem sel hit him þuhte a þene oþerne dæi he com to denemarke he iwende uppe þat lond æfter his iwille he axede gauel of þan londe þe his fader hauede an honde þe king him ȝaf mid godene iwille þa seide sune mid gromiende speche ȝif mi fæder dude his wille nulle ich hit naht iwurþen ah fare he ut of mine londe ȝif he wulle libbe þat word com to þe wes brutlondes king wher beoþ mine þeines wher beoþ mine sweines wher beoþ mine kempes and mine kene men eorneþ and eærne and al þis lond bearneþ and alle þa men slæþ þe ȝe cumeþ neh and heore children and heore wif werpeþ into þe wæteren and brekeþ heore walles and berneþ heore halles seælleþ heore tures and swaleþ heore bures and swa heo sculden understonden þat ich am king of brutlonde and þat heo aȝen me to ȝelden alse heo duden kinge forþ iwende þat hired swa þæ king hæhte heo dude þer muchele hermes mid hæhȝere strengþe þe king of þan londe mid muchelere genge com toȝeines mid godliche strengþe heo fuhten wunderliche inoh and denemarkene king ofsloh and his densce ferde he felden to þan grunde he ferden to þan burȝen and him alle onbuȝen and alle he awælde betere and wurse his men heo bicomen and æþes him sworen and æfter cure heo him ȝeuen þreo hundred ȝisles and al swa muchel gærsume swa king bihehte þa inne freode and alle his iueren and þa iuende aȝæn into þisse londe ase he ferden on his wæi bi þan ende of orcanai þa fonde he i sæflod þritti scipe gode of wapmen and of wifmen þe schipe wel afulled mid fele cunne wepnen swiþe ibone þuhte þon kinge hærof swiþe sællic þing whet þat scipen weoren þe he ifunde þere he sende ane sonde him to and hæhte heom suggen wannen heo weoren and whet heo þer sohten and ȝif heo wolden speken him wih and ȝernen þes kinges griþ þa enswerede heore alre lauerd we wulleþ speken him wiþ and ȝeornen his griþ heo togaderen come and griþ heo nomen sone þa queþ wiþ he speke þus we beoþ sæwerie men mid wedere bidriuene ich hæhte and þu art læuerd ouer us we beoþ a þine londe bicumen þine laȝen we biluuieþ and us alle þu miht walden æftere þine iwille of spaine ich wes ut idriuen and al mi drihtliche folc swiþe muchel we habbeoþ isoht bi þisse særime a lond þe us were liþe þe we mihten on libben ne maȝe we hit ifinden for næuer næne þinge lond to ure leoden þer we maȝen to liþen we habbeþ ihaued moni burst moni hunger and moni þurst moni walc moni wind bi wilde þisse watere nu we biddeþ þin ære ne maȝe we drien hit namare and ȝif hit weoren þin iwille and þu hit don woldest to ȝifuen us an ende i þine kinnelonde we wulleþ þine men beon þine monscipe herien and þe leofuen wiþ a to ure liue þa enswærde þat wes brutlondes king nulle ich na so don ah eower monradene ic wulle fon and ich eow wulle senden into ane londe for ich nat whet ȝe beoþ ne whannen ȝe icume beoþ ah ȝe scullen habben lædesmen and forþ ȝe scullen liþen and ich eow wullen lanen of nan man seoþþen noes flod hit hauede ouergan and forþ wende into þisse londe and þer ȝeonde wunde wel mid þon beste and lette hine clepie king and his wif quene and he sette stronge lawen to steowien his folke for heo haueden inne sæ seorwen ibidene fulle seouen ȝere heo misliche foren heore claþes weoren iwerede and vuele heo weoren igærede nakede heo weoren and naþing ne rohten wha heore leome mærcene laȝe ah þet i þe sugge þurh alle þing ne makede heo noht ærst king ah heo makede þa quene þe me cleopede and heo seide on englisc þis is seoþ ful iwis hæfde þas wise quene bi hire weoreldkinge forh laþ to norþhumberlonde þer he gon bulde castel swiþe strongne al abuten him þat londe he nom to his aȝere hond þe balde iwærþ him abolwen and sende ȝeond þæs ærde and sommnede ferde and com to he heom lette quic flan mid muþe heo hit seiden þeo þat hit iseȝen þat mid his honden þurh hæhȝere strengþe seouen hundred ofsloh and swende mid wepnen he lette makien ane dich þe wes long and swiþe deop and he lette al þat wel weorpen þer an innen þa huld he ane stunde his lond mid isunde inn griþe and inne friþe and freoliche on folke wnder þon hær com tidinde salcuþ to londe and hit wes sone icuþ morpidun þan king þat wes icumen of þare sæ a deor swiþe sellich frommard irlonde com hider liþen and bi þon særime rasde to þon folke oft an one dæie hit makede an hundred fæie and æft to þare sæ wende þe wældscæþe luþere þenne hit æft wende aȝan wærþe hit heom grætte þus hit to londe bæh and werede þeos leoden þat folc hit agaste tunes hit aweste þat folc awai hald an aulchere halue þe king hit harde seggen and særi wes an hurten þiþerward wende þe king himseolue to wæine toward þon deore þer he dæþ fæhte þa he com suþ swa feor þer þe feond wunede þa hahte he al his hirdfolc faren to are burȝe and hæhte heom þer abiden and ane he gon riden þa he forþ wende wapnen he ladde þat wes a kene sweord and enne koker fulne flan enne boȝe swiþe strong and a spere swiþe long æt his sadele an æx and æt þe oþer hælue an hondsæx and forþ he gon wenden towarde þan ende þer he herde suggen þat þe feond wonede swa longe he ferde þat he hit ifunde and he lette fuse him to flan swuþe kene and he ærde to þon deore and smat hit a þan sweore þat þe deor feol abac and þe scæft al tobrac and þat deor up astod and ræsde o þene stede and forbat him þa breste ban and þa senuwen þat þa lihte and þa liuere feollen on eorþen and þe king droh his sweord þe him wes itase and þet deor he smat anan uppe þat hæuedbæn þat þet sweord in deæf and þa hilt on his hand bræc and þat deor todede his chæfles and to þan kinge weoþede and forbat hine amidden a twa þat wes þat fiht idon þus ferde þe king for he wes to kene for þe mon is muchel sot þe nimeþ to himseoluen mare þonne he maȝen walden he sæl halden þe raþer for vnræd is swiþe ræh his lauerd he let reosen and auer vmbe stunde felleþ hine to þe grunde þet folc wes swiþe særi for sorwen þes kinges and hit wes bliþe for dæþþen of þon deore þe king hæfden fif sunen bi feire his quene þe aldest hehte welle æþel wes þere a mon hæhte þe oþer þe wes broþer þe þridde hæhte þe feorþe ingenes þe fifte þe ældeste broþer he iwærþ king in þisse londe he wes swiþe soþfest and swiþe wel iþæwed radful and rihtwis and a mete runhende he heold þis lond stille al æfter his iwille mid treouscipe gode þe while his tir læste and þus he hine huld an hæfne þat com his liues ende inne lundene he liþ særi weoren his leode þeræfter com þe oþer his broþer þe wes next him iboren seoþþen he wes king icorn þis wes þe forcuþþeste mon þe æfre hedde kinedom vnriht him wes leof and rihtwisnesse him wes laþ whatse hæfde richedom he hine makede wræcche mon his gode men he hatede þa uuele he hæhȝede al his motinge was ful of ȝitsinge he somnede togædere mid hæhere wraþþe plihten mid honden þat heo wel hulden þurh alle þing flemen heore king and ut heo hine flemden feor of þissen earde and nomen þene oþer his broþer þis wes þe þridde heo afengen hine mid sibbe and makeden hine to kinge þe cniht wes swiþe kene he wes of his speche ælche monne imete wiþ þa goden he wes duhti and sturne wiþ þa dusie þe wes idriuen ut drof him wes on heorte he ferde feor ȝeond moni lond and fondede þan leoden he bisoþte monienne king and monienne keiser monienne richene þein monienne baldne swein he bisohte al þat folc þer he forþ ferde þat heo him solde helpen to muchelure neode mid strengþe oþer mid ginne his lond to biwinne ne mihte he neuere finden mon þe him wolde ȝette beon þe him oht wolde fulsten þat he hider fore ne naþing him bihæten þat heo him wolden helpen þa wes þe king ærm on his mode seorhful on heorte for his muchele burste hine biþohte whet he don mihte þat he wolde aȝen fare and fondien his broþer and war he mihte of his monnen æie milce ifinden hit wes vmbe fif winter seoþþe he heonne ferde seoþþen he þas seorȝe himseolfen hæfde itimbred þa lette he hine atlichen and wende to þissen londe wiþ his aȝene kun he hine vncuþ makede ne icneow hine nauere na man þe hine ær iseȝen hæfden he fræinede þis leodfolc æfter heore kineleouerde and heo him þene king tahten þer he huntede on comelan wiþ his hirdiferen i þon wude of kalatere þeone king he imette and mildeliche hine igrætte læuerd king quaþ hæil wurþ þu an isunde þu ært mi broþer eædi beo þu æuere ne der ich noht kennen for þisses londes monnen þat ich her king weore leste heo me icneowen ah ich bidde þine ære nu and æueremare þa quaþ þe king þi cume me is iqueme to his broþer he com and leofliche hine custe þer þe king weop mid his eȝenen and mid muchelen ædmeden æþelede his broþer and lette hine læden leofliche and stille into ane castle clud wes ihaten and lette hine baþien and beddien feire and duȝeliche hine biwitten and his namen dærnen what iherden auere suggen a sæȝen oþer a spelle þat æuere æni broþer dude þus for oþer þat þe king dude for þe king hine braeid sæc alse þeah hit seoþ weore þe king læi on bure særiliche on beadde he sende his sonde ȝeond his kinelonde lette laþien him to al his leodþeines mid wurden and mid writen þe dude heom wel to witen þat ne mihte he no lengere libben on eærþe ah of heom þe king wolde habben read for hiȝenliche he weoren dæd and heo him redden wher his lich mihte bezst leggen þet word wes cuþ ȝeond þis lond and come þeos cnihtes to burh þis kinges to muchelen hustinge þe king and his broþer weoren in ane bure þeær heo hæfden wel iȝeten and seoþþen idrunken þe king eoden to bedde and his broþer hiine hudde and mid him his leoueste men þe he wuste on liue feowerti gode cnihtes mid burnen wel idihten mid sweorden and mid schelden alse heo to fehte sculden þe king læi in his bædde alse þæh he ne mihte libben in þære burh he sende word bi his beste wikeneren and hæhten his drihliche folc stilleluker dremen for his hæhued oc sæ sweþen þat he ne mihte idriȝen to ihæren þene muchele drem of swa feole mannen þe king lette witen his durren þat ne moste þer na mon in cumen ne wiþinne þon castelburi na quic mon iboren bute þe king mid his seonden æfter him sende þe king aras of bedde and burne he warp on rigge and nam onne his honde ane wiæxe stronge and cluppede into bure his broþer and nomen heore sonde and into þere burh senden æfter þon hehste þringe þat he comen to þen kinge seone swa he to bure com þe king hine inom and he him wræþ to ase he hine wolde anho and him abuten urnen cnihtes swiþe sturne alse heo wolden mid heonden al hine toheowen þus seiden þe king nu ich þe wulle quellen bute þu beo stille and don al mine wille þus andswerde þe þein ich hit wulle don fæin bicum her mines broþer mon ȝif þu þi lif wult habbe þis is þe king þe of eærde wes iflemed þe is nu hider icumen and eower king scal iwurþen þe þein swiþe stille dude al þes kinges wille and seoþþen þe king hine lette don into ane derne bure and lette enne cniht eærne æfter an oþer eorle and swa he þer agon ase þe oþer hæfde idon þus dude þe king bi allen þeos eorlen bi ane and bi ane þat he heom hæfde al clane þa dude he anoþer nom he his broþer mid muchelere blisse to eowrwik hine brohte þer weoren þeos leoden iliþenned togadere atforen al his folke he his kinehelm onfeng and sette hit on his broþer hæfd and hæf hine to kinge æuer seoþþen iwarþ aþelest ærle kingen þat vuel he al forlette þat gode he imette iwærþ he swiþe milde þan ȝunge and þan alden and wiþ alle monnen ful iwis iwærþ þe king rihtwis þis lond wes istaþeled and stod i þon ilke fulle ten ȝere þa iwærþ þe king vnfere swa þe king seoc læi þreo wiken and enne dæi ne mihte he þerof beon hæl ah dæd wes þe king þa comen al þeos leoden liþen tosomne and nomen eft and duden hine to his aþþelen heuen hine to kinge mid hæȝere blisse and hit ane stunde stod on himseolue and wes æþelest of alle his moncunne iuienes and iseȝen þat wes eft iwurþen leodking ouer þisse londe heo somneden muchel folke of feole cunne monnen and ledden here ferde wide ȝeond þissen ærde togædere com ingenes and særliche heo feohte and fælden heore cnihtes þa sette i þon fuhte to flænne and his broþeren him æfter mid alle here mæhte ingenes and nomen þene king heo hine lædde to lundene særi weoren his leoden in are swiþe stronge tur heo duden þene king moni ȝer and moni dæi þe king in þære ture læi and his broþeren gunnen liþen wide ȝeond þeos leoden iuienes hæfde half þis londe riht bi þere al þesne suþ ende he heold an his heonde and hæfde norþ al bi þere forþ and seoþþen þeræfter al togæderen he hit ahte for ingenes ne leouede buten seouen ȝeren þa nom al þis lond and sette an his aȝere hond and he iwarþ him swuþe luþer and læh al his folke þæ com þe færliche dæd and falde hine to grunde swa vuele he luuede his lif þat þe scucke hine ifenge þæ somnede al þis leodfolc into lundene ferden and nomen ut þer he læi in are tur and duden þer a selcuþ þing makeden hine þridde chærre king þa iwarþ he swa duhti swa þe dæi feire alle folc he dude riht wel wes þisse londe idiht inne blisse leouede his leode to murhþe and þa he sculde of liue wende he hæfde feiren ende þa com his broþer sune þe wes þe formeste of þæn fif broþeren þe cniht wes ihaten lador he wes þisse londes king ah lador ne luuede buten ane lutle wile æfter him com sune a ȝer he hulde þas leoden and seoþþen he dun læi ænmaunus hæhte þe oþer þe wes broþer þeos weoren mannes sunes þeos ær weoren kinges þes ilke heold his kinelond þus þat nas na þein in þissen londe þat nalde hine fæin slæn mid his honden and al his folc he hatede and al he hit hænde wiþ al folc he wes wiþerward þe wurse hine leouede and his aȝene heredmen hine to deaþe hateden neoþeles on ende þat folc of þissen londen fusden hine and flæmden feor of þissen ærde for he wes swa wiþerward heo driuen hine of þis ærde mid seorwen and mid seore ne com he her nauermare togadere commen þe hæhste eorles of þissen londe and curen heom enne king of ane cnihte þe wes kene he wes inienes sune of kunne icume iwallo hæhte þe king he wes god þurh alle þing wel he braid on deade efter his alderen of alre godnesse þe gume wes ilæred he hæfde gode þæwes his þeode wes þæ betere ac hit wes ladlich burst þat he ne moste libben na lengere þene seouen ȝere ne mosten he luuien here dæd wes iwallo þe king his duȝeþe he bilæfde seoþþen her rixlede a king rime wes ihaten he wes bæren he wes broþer seoþþen com sune seoþþen wes his fæder hæhte seoþþen com his broþer hæhte seoþþen com king he wes of þeon kunne seoþþen com cherin he wes cun ah cherin leouede longe inne þisse londe ah þa oþer six kinges þe ær weoren on londe ne leouede nan here fulle æhte ȝere ah longe leouede here cherin muchel he dronk mede and win weoren al his duȝeþen bilefed oppe drenche and al he leas his wurþscipe for þon winscenche ne dude nauer oþer god ne greiþe on his þeode ah selliche þinges weoren of þissen kinge swa he leoueden here wel feole ȝere swa næuere vnleoden þis lond ne iseoþten ah þis lond wes on griþe and ifulled mid gode þa com þe ilke dæi þat þe king deæd læi þa hæfde he þreo sunen bi hæȝere his quene þe aldeste hæhte fulgenius aldus and andragus ah ful lutle wile liuede þas ilke ælc of heom an stunde wes king in þissen londe ac wiþinne feouwer ȝere alle heo weoren dæde her þe ȝungeste of þan breþeren þe wes þe bezste andragus he hæhte enne sune he hehde urrian hæhte þat childe þe iwærþ þisse leodes king a ȝer he leouede and seoþþen he dæd þolede æfter þon kinge vrian wes his kunnesmon þa com doten and þeos ilka þreo kinges heolden þas þeode an efter ane þæt dæd heo weoren alle ah nawiht heo her ne duden nouþer god ne ufel seoþþen com merian þes wes a swiþe hende mon hundes and hauekes he hæuede vnimete þat æuereelche dæi he pleuwede mid his deoren ah he wes swa feir mon þat wifmen hine luueden þerof he nom ȝemen ah hit nes him noht iqueme ah he luuede his quene æuere bi his liue seoþþen wes bledon his sune and blæþfest king he hæfde inoh god and hit his gumen dælde nes neuer seoþþen næ king swa custi þurh alle þinge seoþþen wes his sune king cap wes ihæten æfter cap oein for elchen vuele he wes fein seoþþen com sillius þe wes sune seoþþe sone æfter þet com a king blæþgabreat seoþþen þeos worle wes astolled ne cuþe na mon swa muchel of song of harpe and of salteriun of fiþele and of coriun of timpe and of lire gleomen him weoren deore he cuþen al þeos songes and þat gleo of ilcche londe of him wes muchel speche ȝeond þas woruldriche swa þat al þis moncun þat of him iherden tellen seiden þat he wes god of alle gleocræften æuer wes þe king glad and æuere he gomen luueden and þus he lædde his lif þe while þe hit ilæste seoþþen wes his broþer king ihæten he hit heolde seouen ȝeore i griþe he wunede here seoþþen wes his sune king þe vniseliche luuede men cleopeden þene king his deden weoren forcuþe nes nan swa god wif i þon londe þe he walde ȝif heo wes a wiht hende þat he ne makede hore þæh hit weoren an eorles wif he binom hire al hire æþelen þe ȝunge wifmen and þe ælde he makeden to sconde for þisse vniwærste laȝe his leode hine hateden into þan bare dæþe nalde he for þon hit bileæfue seoþþen com redion and rædden þissen þeoden half ȝer and seouen niht þa wes he dæd forhriht seoþþen redært his broþer lasse while þenne þe oþer seoþþen com an þe leouede wel he hæhte famulpenicel on his liue he wes swa riche alle þon oþere vniliche seoþþen com a king þe hæhte pir his hæd wes swulc swa beoþ gold wir þet al folc wundreden on wheonene
