com swa feir mon æfter him com þe king wes on þeode æfter him com eligille þe heold þis lond ful stille þes wes a swiþe wis mon and of alle þinge wel idon mid blisse he luuede here fif and twenti ȝere seoþþen wes king his sune heli ȝeres fulle feouwerti oþer wile he heold griþ and oþer while me fæht him wiþ he wes a swiþe æht gume and he streonde þreo snelle sunen lud wes ihaten þe an he wes a swiþe æht mon þe midlest þe ȝungeste hehte nennius æfter heli king æhte þis lond lud his sune wel longe þes wes swiþe oht king and vnimete kene and he wes swiþe riche for rædes he luuede he ferde ȝeond al þis kinelond and ælche burh he makede strong castles makede lud þe king and lundenne he luuede þurh alle king þe ȝeht þe lud king ahte þis lond hehte lundene trinouant and of castles ner þer naþing bute þat tur þe makede king al swa þes boc her telleþ biuore a þissen spelle lud king lette legge þane wal abuten þe burh of lundene al þe auere ȝet haueþ ilast and swa he wule ȝet wel longe he letten bulden þe hallen swiþe muchele mid alle he hehte ilchene riche mon þat he dælde his æhte atwam and nome þa hæluendale and hæh bold him makede and alle þæ vnstronge men þere burh he duden wiþuten and heȝede þæ burh and makede heo swiþe hende he leide adun þere burhȝe nome and nemnede hire æfter himseoluen and hehten heo kaer lud and oueral hit let cuþen þat he duden al for þon þat seoþþen sculden moni mon þennen þe king weoren dæd demen of his weorken seoþþen her com vncuþ folc faren in þessere þeode and nemneden þa burh lundin an heore leodewisen seoþþen comen sæxisce men and lundene heo cleopeden þe nome ileste longe inne þisse londe seoþþen comen normans mid heore niþcraften and nemneden heo lundres þeos leodes heo amærden swa is al þis lond iuaren for uncuþe leoden þeo þis londe hæbbeþ biwunnen and eft beoþ idriuen hennene and eft hit biȝetten oþeræ þe uncuþe weoren and falden þene ælden nomen æfter heore wille of gode þe burȝen and wenden heore nomen swa þat nis her burh nan in þissere bruttene þat habbe hire nome æld þe me arst hire onstalde þa gon þis lond wenden þat com þis kinges ende lud king iwarþ dæd in lundene me hine leide þer weoren eorles swiþe whæte and leiden þene king bi ane ȝate þat ȝet me cleopeþ ful iwis port lud a bruttisce seoþþen comen ænglisce men wel waht and cleupeden hit ludesȝate and swa hit haueþ wel longe o þon nome istonde þa weoren þer twa children ludes sunen kinges þe ældre hæhte þe oþer temelcinus þas children uueren lutle þa here fader deȝede þa com heore fader broþer and iwærþ himsulf to kinge and biwuste þas children and leofliche heom fedde for luue of his broþer þes wes þisses londes king þe leodes hine luueden for his laȝen weoren gode he sette feire þeauwes in þissen þeoden and he wes swiþe god king and god cniht þurh alle þing þeos children weoxen an hond þat heo mihten halden lond þe king heom ȝef gode tweien eorldomes him wes leouere and he him lundene ȝæf and þermid he ȝæf him al kent for he him wolde iquemen and he hehte to cornwale temen and freoliche þas twein broþerne heolden þas eorldomes buten þat heo icneowen þene king for heore herre for he wes heore lauerd and al þissere leodene þa wile þa heo weoren sæhte and heore men on some þis lond ferde swiþe wel mid sibbe heo hulden ah seoþþen heo iwærþen wærþe and hit iwærþ þa weorse swa þat romleode comen to þissen þeoden and sette ȝeld a þisse londe æiþer seluer and gold þe næuer eær on liue ne dursten hider liþen axien king of þissen londe þat he ȝefue ȝeld into rome þa wes hit ilumpen o þan daȝen ase we soþ suggen maȝen þat scezar wes iuaren mid vnimete ferde from rome into france þe feond wes iwraþþed al þa londes he biwon þe he mid eȝene lokede on he þohte to biwinnen mid strengþen and mid ginnen al middeleærdes lond and halde þat worlde in his hond ah he ne mihte hit don al þas wurlde under fote ah þa þreo dale he biwon of þissere wurlderiche fif and fifti kinelond he biwon to his aȝere hond wiþuten his riche þe ær læi to rome cniht he wes kene ȝeond al middelærde cuþ he wes þe wisseste mon of al þe worulderiche he makede þane kalender þe dihteþ þane moneþ and þe ȝer he dihte feole domes þe ȝet stondeþ ine rome wale þat eæuere ei sucche mon into helle sculde gan wende of rome mid folke wel idone he ferde ouer lumbardie swa he dude ouer muntgiwe he biwon loherne and gascunne peytou normandie and brittaine and luueine and alemaine seoþþen he hæfde iwunnen gascunne he charde aȝen into burgunne into flandres he ferde and makede his schipfærde hit wes an ane time þat þe dæi wes liht and þe sunne wes swiþe briht and cezar rad ȝeond flaundre lond an scewede þære sæstrond þat weder wes swiþe liþe and he þis lond ikende þa freinede and wiþ þon folke he spec þus wat his þat ilke æitlond þat ich mid æȝen iseo feor ouer sæstram feir hit me þuncheþ a wis mon þus quaþ and mid þæne kæisere spæc þæt is a muchel æitlond of alche gode hit is strong þet bruttes ærest ifeng þer beoþ duhtie men brutaine hit hatte þat lond þe þu bihaldest þa spæc cezar he wes wis and swiþe iwar wel ich hit wæt what bruttis wæs for mine bæc hit me suggeþ alle we comen of ane kunne alse þe bæc hit us cuþþeþ vre aldren weoren i troie þer heo teone þoleden æt þon muchele fæhte moni þeosend þer weoren fæie þa heo weoren ouercumen þæ quahten heo wide and ferde sichinde lond þer heo mihten on libben þer bicom and to his liue he wunede þeran þeonnenen come þa kinges þe weoren wunder kene and þe rome biwunnen heo forferde rome þa burh wel idone heo nomen of romanisce londe muchel seoluer and gold heore ȝisles heo letten anhon heore folc heo letten fordon þet dude and his broþer ah nou þer is anoþer ich hahte cezar þerfore is min herte sær þet me mine ældre dude scome ær ich weore mon ibore ah nu ich wulle sende into þon lond to iwiten at þon bezste ȝif heo me wulleþ buȝen and ȝif heo me wulleþ senden gauel of heore londe for ȝif heo wulleþ ȝirne griþ nulle ich heom noht fehten wiþ findeþ me tweien wise men þe wel cunnen a speche he bitæhten heom forþriht a writ þe wes al idiht and grætte þene king of bruttaine þus seide þat writ þe wel bar þe ernde ich æm scesar þe of rome em icumen her ȝif þu wult ȝirne griþ nele ic þe noht fehten wiþ and hiȝendliche me sende gauel of þine londe þu sulf mi mon bicumen and for kaisere me halden for al hit is min aȝen þat ic iseo mid min æȝen iseh þat writ þerfore he wes abolȝen he wes wunderliche wrah for þes tidinde him wes læþ a writ he lette makien mid muchere wraþþe al wiþute grætinge sende hit cesar þon kinge þat writ to þon keisere com þeos wordes weoren þeron idon sillich us þuncheþ cezar þu ært swa wis and swa war þat þu þenchest to beon keisere of alle quike monne þu ært icumen of rome þine word beoþ swiþe store of ure londe þu axest ȝeld and ne scelt þu þerfore ȝælpen þu sulf ært swiþe gripel þine gumen sunden ȝefere þu þenchest to setten o þin hond al middelærdes lond we beoþ in ane æitlonde at þere worldes ende atstonde þe bruttes biwunne and we wunieþ þeron and freoliche we hit haldeþ wiþ alle weoruldkingen and þe nulle we næuere sende gauel of ure londe for ȝif þu weore al swa wis swa ich wende þat þu weore þenne woldest þu vnderstonde þæt we beoþ in ure londe freo and swa scone swa þi folc is of rome for ure ældere ut of troye fluȝen and of anne kunne we beoþ icumen þine aldren and ure at troye wuren ifeire ȝif þu me wult ilæiuen boten þu us wullen bilæiuen þu scalt of brutten muchel balu habben þu and þine iferen ȝif þu auere cumest here for ure aldren weoren kinges inne þisse londe and brenne beiene tosomne heo biȝeten rome mid richere strengþe and hit is ore irihte þat þu an rixlest and forþi þu ahtest me to ȝulden gauel of þine londe and þu hit halst on unriht þerfore þu scalt habben pliht for þu waldest beon min hærre and þu me sculdest buȝen cezar iseh þis writ and he hit wraþliche biheold abolȝen he wes on mode he weorp hit to his foten wær beo ȝe mine cnihtes þe gode beoþ to fihte leteþ ȝarkni mine scipen for nu we scullen wende and forþ we scullen buȝen into bruttaine and nimen þer þis londes king and quic hine forbærnen and biȝutten al þat lond to ure aȝere hond sixti scipen heo makeden vnimete muchele þeos weoren al neowe stronge and wel itreowe of lasse scipen þar weoren swa feole þat nuste na man þe tale þeo com heom a wedere wunderliche feire heo ferden from stronde touward þisse londe heo turnden to hauene inne þare temese þer þa temese and þa sæ heomseoleuen imetteþ sone come þa tiþende to þisse londes kinge and he hit letten cuþen wide ȝeonde þissere þeode þat cezar wes hider icomen and wraþ he hafde þis lond inumen þe king wes war þurh alle þing he wuste wel of heore cume þat hauen of douere he hauede inumen þer lai mid his ferde þe king of þissen earde þider com tiþende þat him wæs sær þat icumen wes cezar moni wes þe kempe þe wes mid þe king and he hafde enne stiwarde þene wisseste mon of al þis ærde belan he wes ihaten bæȝes he dælde he wes cniht swiþe ræh to ræden ane kinge vnder þen kinge he heolde þis lond and þas leoden him hereden þe king hehden his broþer sune beiene tosomne þe aldre hæhte þe ȝungere þeos weoren beien him biforen eorles swiþe balde nennius wes þeos kinges broþer næfde he nenne oþer he ferde ut of cantuarieburie mid balden his ferden of lundene mid kentisce leoden of cornwale his kempen weore kene æridius þe king his scottes he lædde and britael com to neode norþ walene king and guærtaæt þe mode mid þon suþ walscen com of galwæie æssel þe gode com of muriene moni spere kene of alle þissen þeoden come to þære neode to kinge of þissen londe and þene king lærde al þas leodcnihtes þat he his freoscipe mid fehte biwunne and he heom an hond salde swa þat he wolde þat fehten he wolde wiþ cezar þe axede longauel her forþward heo wenden and his folke fusde to þere sæ heo wenden and cezar þer funden of heore cume wes war cezar he cleopede on his cnihtes ȝarewieþ eow to fihte for nu is mid ferde icumen heo liþede togadere mid heore speren longe mid axen mid sweorden mid scærpe speres orde hardliche heo heowen hælmes þer gollen feonliche heo feohten hafdes þer feollen and cesar þe keisere wes vnimete kene his longe sweord he adroh and moni mon þermide asloþ he swonc i þon fehte þat al he lauede asweote he sloh þa him neh weoren alle buten iferen he dude þer muchelne wunder he sloh þer an hundred of ahtere monnen þe feond mid his mæche þat iseh and cleopede his fader nennius and beiene þa eorles buȝen heom togaderes mid swiþe muchele folke togæderen stoden faste iseȝen heo cesar fæhten al swa a wilde bar and heo him to fusden mid ladliche fehte and monie of heore feonden heo fælden to þon grunde þa iseh nennius wær fæht cesar and he him to rasde mid ræhæm his sweorde vppen þene helm he hine smat þat þet sweord in bat selkuþ hit þuþte moni cnihte þat he durste cumen him næh for þa þe keisere wes swa hæh cesar ne queþ nan word ah he bræid ut his sweord and nennium he smat þa uppen þene helm swa þat þe helm tohælde and þat hæfde bledde ah he ne blakede no for he wes cniht wel idon and nefde na bræþ ah his brond he up ahæf and nennius hæf vp his sceld scilde hine sulue adun smat and þat sweord a þene scelde bat hit wraste and þat sweord stikede feste þat sweord heold and nennius þene sceld and þus heo hit longe bituȝen ne mihte he þat sweord ut draȝen þat isæh hu uerden cesar and nennius and heo hem to fusde monie to fulste þa isæh cesar tiþend þat him wes sær he forlette þene brand þa nefde he noht on his hond æ he þa feondliche turnde to flæme nennius wende i þane felde and he turnde his sceld droh ut þene brande þa wes þe eorl swiþe bald monie romanisce men mid þon sweorde he leide adun he wes moniennes monnes bone and monianne he dude scome ah þat he mid þan sweorde smat þerriht hit iwat al þat he þermid atran weore hit flæs weore hit ban þurh þeos sweordes wunde heo fullen to þon grunde alle dæi wes þat fihte a þet com þe þestere niht þe kaisere mid alle þan romanisce here dalden from þan fihte al bi þustere nihte to hærberȝe heo wenden uppen þare sæstronde heo bilefden biæften twenti hundred cnihten þeo leien under scelden islæȝen ȝeond þon felden cesar iwende to his bedde his men weoren ofdredde inne biwakeden in þere nihte þritti hundred cnihten mid helmen and mid burnen and mid stelene sweorden cesar he wes ȝep and swuþe iwær he isæh his muchele lure and of mære he hæfde kare he aras to þan midnihte and bannede his cnihtes and seide heom þat heo wolden faren and fleon of þissen londe faren into flandre and beo þer wuniende a þat he iseȝen his time þat he mihten æft cumen liþen heo ferden forhrihte to scipe al bi nihte heo hæfden swiþe fair weder and wenden into flandre amarȝen þa hit dæi wes þe king mid his duȝeþe ȝarekede his ferde and wende to þan fihte þeo was romanisce folc iuaren from here londe þat ne funden heo nauer enne of cesares monnen þa weoren bruttes bliþe an heore mode muchel wes þa blisse þat heo makeden mid iwisse and sone þeræfter særi heo wurþen and þe king iwarþ særi þurh alle þing for nennius his broþer ne mihte finden bote of his hæfuedwunde þe smat mid honde ne þurh nenne læchecræfte ne mihte he lif habben nes þer nan oþer ræd buten nennius iwarþ dæd and nennius was ilæid at þon norþ ȝæte i lundene þe king næm enne marmestan and lette hine mid golde bigon mid golde and mid ȝimme his broþer he leide þerinne mid richedome þa bruttes nennium biburden nu þu miht iheren sulkeþ word þe king nom þat ilke sweorde þat nennius his broþer biwan of cesare and læide hit bi his broþer þat hit his bone weore wæs þe stelene brond swiþe brad and swiþe long þeron weoren igrauen feole cunne bocstauen æ þere hilte wes igrauen þat þa sweord wes icleoped inne rome crocia mors swa þat sweord hæhte for hit hauede muchele mahte þermide þe keisere þrætede ælches londes here for nas næuere þe ilke bern þe auere iboren weoren þat of þen ilke sweorde enne swipe hefde þat he of his likame lette ænne drope blod þat he nes sone dæd neore he noht swa dohti mid his ferde læi inne flandre þat word com to france heou he iuaren hæfde and hu he wæs mid his færde iflæmde of þissen earde þa weoren þa frensce men þerfore swiþe uæine for toward heo hæfden grome and for þi weoren fæin of his scome ælc frenscmon þe wes aht hæfþ hine selfne biþoht and seide to his iuere ne wurþe he nauere isæle þe nu and aueremare buȝe to cesare þe bruttes habbeþ ouercumen and of heore londe idriuen nulle we him nauere hæren ne hælde for ure hærre ac wih him we scullen ure freoscipe mid fehte bitellen for ne sunde we na bliþere þenne beoþ þa bruttes þe hine habbeoþ ut idriuen and his cnihtes islæȝen þis ihærden segge þat þa frenscen speken þus and þat heo speken of þrætte and of prute ibeote he wende into france mid muchelen his ferde alse heo noht ne cuþe þat heo him vuel walden and sende ȝeond al france æfter his freo monnen þat heo comen him to alswa heo sculden to heore herre don alle heo comen him to and alle hine custen and alle hine grætten and heore grame dærnden wes swiþe wis and war on his þonke he lette bringen muchel gold and gærsume store ærst he ȝæf þæn hæhste þe eoden him næxte ȝefuen swiþe riche of ræden his golde auerelcne cnihte he ȝef ȝeoue brihte mid þere ȝeue he heom ouercom þat wes þa þat bezste iwan and freoliche him bihæhte habben þat heo scolden þa weoren heo his freond þe ær weoren his fulle fon whær is þe ilke mon þat me ne mæi mid mede ouergan þurh þa luue of þan feo feondscipe aleggen makien feolle ifreond þæh heo weoren iuæiede nu spac cesar he wes wis and swiþe iwar ihereþ mine frensce men mine freo cnihtes ich wulle sende to rome to mine monnen wel idone þat heo me sende forþrihtes fif hundred cnihtes for ȝet ich wulle wenden into brutlonde and ȝe me scullen uæren mid mid muchelere strengþe and þat lond ich wulle biwinnen and þa bet eow scel iwurþen for eowre muchele wurþscipe weole ȝe scullen habben alle eowre flemede men mid mire freondscipen cumen aȝæn for ȝifuen ich wulle witen and þe wræcchen makien richen freo ȝe scullen iwurþen and mine freondscipe habben þa answarede þat hired mid hæhȝere stefne mid þe we wulleþ libben and mid þe we wulleþ liggen and wurþscipe þe biwinnen mid strengþe and mid ginnen and mid þe we wulleþ buȝen mid baldere strengþe ouer sæ to brutlonde to þa kinge and wiþ him we scullen fihten and wærken þine cnihtes and iwinnen al þat lond and setten hit in þire hond and þer moste mare to ær þis weoren al idon for al heo weoren særi ær hit soþ weore þa cesar hæfde þis idon and his gærsume idæled and æc hæfde freondscipe mid his feo biwunnen þa ferde he into buluine þer him bezst þuþte he hehte wurchen ane tur wunderliche fæier þe tur wes muchel and hæh and þere sæ heo stod wel neh þe kæisere hire ȝæf nome and oþeres heo cleopede in þare tur stronge kæisere wunede longe þreottene monþes wunede in oþeres and þider he lette al cumen gold and his gærsume næs næuere na tur þe swa weore itimbred mid crafte swa gode swa þa tur of oþeres þer mihten sitten in þon grunde cnihtes sixti hundred and þa turres cop mihte wreon a cniht mid his capen þa þe tur wes al ȝaru þa hæfde cesar þe lasse kare into france he wende and sette his wike ȝeond al he sette reuwen stronge and hæȝen þe fengen þa londgauel and mid þan feo sculden faren æueralcne ȝere to oþres þeon ture þa lette he wurchen wunderliche muchele six hundred scipen and sette heo to hauene þa þat wærc wes idon and al þat þer bihouede to þa seide þe keisere þat to brutlonde he wolde faren forþ bi his quike liue nalde he heom swa bilæuen six hundred scipe gode he fusde i sæflode and nuste na mon þat itel of þan scipen þat seileden after and forþriht heo wenden into þere temese nu þohte cezar ah þer he wes to vnwar he þohte swa forþ teon æfter þere temese rouwen swa longe þat he come to londen and þær heo wolden up faren and fehten wiþ bruttes and iwinnen al þis lond to his aȝere hond ah nas hit noht swa iloten for lettinge com on ueste for sæliþende men seiden þon brutten þat þe kaisere wolde i temese cume þus faren forþ to lunden and fehten wiþ þan leoden and þa bruttes iwurþen war and wisdom biþoþten and nomen longen ræftres stronge and rihte mid stronge irene heo weoren iscod and setten heom i temese flod þer weoren fifti hundred faste i þon grunde and þa herre endes ihodede mid irene bendes toȝænes heom heolden inne þere hauene and swa heo þer stoden biwriȝen mid þon flode þa com cesar and hæræf næs nawiht war þæt weder heom strongliche drof stermen þer sungen weder heom stod on wille heo wenden wel to speden heo urnen touward hauene scipen gunnen helden bosmes þer rendden water in wende seiles þer helfden aþeles adrunken and þa romleoden rameden ȝeond uþen þa scipen wenden to wundre oþer half hundred þerafter com cesar on his hurte him wæs sær heo scuuen ut heore lof and læiden to þon londe and þeo þeræfter comen weoren war sone and heom sælliche ilomp þæt mesten dæl com a lond heo sloȝen heoren teldes wide ȝeond þa feldes and sære menden heoren wines þe adrunken weoren þa wæs þe king war þat þe kæisere wes a lundene mid his hære þa ȝeddede þe king welle broþer nennius þat ich þe quic nabbe and þat sweord crocea mors þe þu biwunne a compe and þe bi mire side isund seȝe riden an oþer half and his broþer sikerlichen we sculden uaren and fehten wiþ þon kæisere and forþ we sculen liþen and fellen his leoden bruttene king wes god cniht þurh alle þing he somnede vnimete here and ferde touward þon kæisere and pus spec wiþ his folke and luueliche spilede biþencheþ eow ohte cnihtes to bitellen eoweore rihtes biþencheþ a þone king and his broþer hu heo biȝeten rome mid riche here ferde and biwunnen al þa richen þe læien into rome and swa heo hit walden wel feole wintre and swa heo þer boȝeden þe wile þe heo luueden and ich hit sugge eow cnihtes rome is eowre irihte nu hit halt cesar þe is tweien icumen her and halt þer eower icunde and her eow wule driuen of londe and hateþ eow swa swiþe þat awei he wule eow driue ȝif ȝe leoseþ þis lond oueral ȝe wurþeþ laþe ah heo ȝe swiþe bisie for we beoþ ohte bruttes cesar is in ure londe and liþ her bi sæstronde ohliche liþe we him to swa him alre laþest beo and awalde we þe keisere and al his romanisce here and aredden ure lond of þan romleodene þa andswereden þa ferde varen we biliue for is fæie mid al his romfolke forþ heo ifusden and ferden biliue þat heo þidir comen þer læi þat folk of rome and heo heom to ræsden mid ræhere strengþe laþliche heo feohten and romware feollen þer cesar folk folden isohten noht bi tene no bi twenti ah bi twenti þusende swa heo fehten al dæi monie þer weoren fæie þet hit com to þere nihte ne mihte cesar namare fihte cesar wes swa swiþe wa and biþohte hine þa þat he wolde a þere nihte fleon awæi mid his cnihten cezar of his lure wes þer war he lette blawen his bemen and bannen his ferden and lette leode cleopien and oueral cuþen þat heo comen to heore innes and ȝarekeden heore ginnes and fæȝeden heoren wepnen amarwen heo fusden to fehte þis ihærden þa bisie þe weoren þer bihælues forþriht heo comen to and seiden him þat cesar wulde þe ȝet wunnien þar and amarwe he weolde fehten mid alle his cnihten and fallen þa bruttes oþer himsulf beo fæie for þus heo letten cleopien and cuþen ȝeond his ferde ah wa la wa and wala wa þat nær iwar þa he wende swiþe wel don ah ne dude he hit no he droh in ane hælue and toc þan herberwe and alle þa nihte greiþeden his cnihtes heore scæftes and heore sceldes þa scælkes weoren bischærred for cesar of his hærme wæs wær abuten midnihte he warnede alle his cnihtes and to scipen ferden and fusden an veste heo hafden swiþe god weder and wenden mid vþen heo ledden in heore scipen æiþer deade men and quiken moni sorhfulne sæg sare iwunded monienne deadne cniht of cesares duhȝeþe swa heo wenden mid þon flode to þon tur of oþres þer wes cezar an heorte he hafde sorȝe and sar amarȝen þa hit wes dæiliht hit wes cuþ forþriht and æc iseid þon kinge hu þe kæisere wes from þissen londe ifaren and al hu he fusde and flæh mid þon vþen þat næs þer bilæued nan of romleoden þa wes þon kinge wa and þus ȝeddede þa wale wale vnræd mani cniht þu makest dæd welle þat ich nas ær war þat wolde wenden ful soh seide þe seg þe þeos saȝe talde ȝif þu ileuest ælcne mon selde þu sælt wel don swa ic wende wel þat þe sæȝe soþ weoren þe me wes toniht itald bi an eorl swicful and bald þat cesar wolde nu todæi brutlond biwinnen oþer her mid sweorde liggen toswungen and al his iuere þe mid him comen here nu wes þis ilke iseid me to biswiken wæila wæi wæila wæi þat he is þus ifaren awæi and naþeles ich em bliþe for auere to ure liue we maȝen ouersitten þis lond ær he us æft isechen for æueremore he mai imunnen þat he him her imunten for her liggeþ toȝere ten þusend of his iferen wiþuten his drihtliche scipen þe i sæ idrunken ah wel ich þonkie mine gode for wurþscipe ich habbe ibiden and twien iflemed þene keisere mid alle his romanisce leode and nu ich wulle to lundene þa burh ich luuie swuþe and þer ich wulle halinesse to mine goden halden and swiþe heom wurþen for heore weldæde þe king lette blawen and bonnien his ferden and hehten heom alle faren heom and hiredmen beon bliþe and fæien heore steden and græiþen heore iweden and þas dæies æn þreom wiken wenden to lundene mid wif and mid bernen blisse to makien eorles and þeines cnihtes and sweines and al þat freoliche folc of brutlondes ærde þene dæie heo vndernomen and to lundene heo comen mid swulche richedome al swa hit weoren i rome þe king bigon seruise on ælches cunnes wise æfter þan heþene laȝen þe stoden o þen ilkæ daȝen þer stoden in þere temple ten þusend monnen þet wes þe bezste cure of al brutlonde biforen heore þe heom þuhte mære wes ihaten heo heolden hine for hæhe godd ælc beorn hæfde on heonde ane þechene bærninde wæs ælc bald beorn iboned mid golde þe king hafde his kinehelm hæhliche on hæfde wæs atforen þan wæfde imaked an wunlic fur þe king warp riches þerin and alle his hæhste men mid him seoþþen heo þer offreden aþþeles madmes and þonkede his gode þe þa muchele wurþscipe uþen him þa þe seruuinge wes idon þat hit to þe mete com þerof ich wulle þe tellen selcuþe spelles weoren in þeos kinges cuchene twa hundred cokes and ne mæi na man tellen for alle þa bermannen islaȝene weoren to þon mele twælf þusend ruþeren sele and þritti hundred hærtes and al swa feole hinden of þan fohȝelcunne ne mai hit na mon kennen and al þat wæl and al þat gold þe wes ȝeond al þeos kinges lond hit wes al isomned at þere sereuunge nes hit nauer mid soþ itald seoþþen þeos weoruld wes astald þat weore on ane stude swulc ȝifueþe istured ne of alche þinge swulc richedom iȝiuen and underfon muri wes þe dæi and liht and þa sonne wes swiþe briht weoren þa bernes iscængte mid beore and þa drihliche gumen weoren windrunken heo ferden ȝeond þa feldes mid scæftes and mid sceldes summe heo gunnen ærnen and somme heo gunnen eornen and summe heo gunnen pleien pliht com on ueste summen pleoden on tæuelbrede and summen ærnden heore stede þa weoren þer tweiene prute heo weoren beien herigal hehte þe an æueling þe oþer herigal wes þes kinges mæi þet wes hærm a þen ilke dæi ahte cniht wes auelin wes is hem þeos tweien cnihtes bigunnen mid sceldes to scurmen ærst heo pleoweden and seoþþe pliht makeden þer herigal smat æuelin swiþe vuele a þane chin heo bigunnen to chiden cnihtes come riden euelin wes swiþe wraþ and mid þan stæue todraf and smat herigal a þon ribben þat þe stæf tobræc amidden þa queþ þe cniht herigal euelin þat is swiþe sar þu me smite bi þon rugge ah sare þu hit slat abuggen for nu þi stæf is tobroken balu þe scal beon ȝifueþe wes swiþe sari þat him wes swa ilumpen þe oþer wolde him habben dæd hit þuhte him swiþe hærd ræd and he hine biþohte wæt he don mihte nefde he noht on his hond bute enne luttelne sceld isæh he enne hendlicne mon þe þer stod bihaluen þe wes þudere icumen for to iseon þare cnihte gomen þe ȝunge mon heold on his hond enne stelene brond þene brond igrap mid grimliche lechen and braid hine of þere scæþe þa wes his hurte æþe he ræsde to herigale and smat hine swiþe sare þat his neb and his neose niþer ba heolden æft he him to sweinde and þa hond him ofswipte dunt he him ȝef þane þridde and forsmat hine amidde swa endede þæ pleowe þat herigal læi ofsloȝen and euelin þonene wende his sweord he bar on honde ne funde he nonne swa kene mon þat hond him durste leggen on al þat folc he bibæh to inne he flæh þet iherde þe king icud hit wes him sone hu hit al wes ifaren and hu herigal læi ofslæwen þe king nom þreo aldere men and sende to and hehte hine bringen his mæi to þon kinge to þolie þes kinges dom for þan slæhte þe he hafde idon and ȝif he swa nolde he hine flæme wolde þa answerede and toward þan kinge he spæc þus nulle ich hine bringen for nauer nane þinge þat me euelin fordo noþer slæ ne na aho ah ich habbe freo lond þat freoliche stont a mire honde and ich habbe min hired heh vnder þon kinge ȝif her is æni cniht þe of eueline axeþ riht come to mine herede and þer he hit scal habben and ich sugge eow to soþe nis þer ræd nan oþer þis wes sone icuþ to þe king iwarþ him swiþe wraþ swulc he weore of witte and þeos ilkæ word him seide ut of min æhsenen and his iueren and ȝif ich hine mai eower ifon in þon stude he beþ fordon forþrihtes nom alle his cnihtes and anan gon liþen ut of lundenne and iwenden into kent to his ane castle and hine strongede wel mid mete and mid wepnen and þe king nom lundene and þat lond to his aȝere hond and seoþþen fusde into kent mid muchelere ferde mid here and mid fure þat lond forferde swiþe nom tweie cnihtes and sende to þon kinge and þus þe cnihtes him spæken wiþ king ȝeornneþ þi griþ is þin aȝene mon al þine wille he wule don wiþ þon þe þu him ȝeue griþ and late hine sæhtne þe wiþ and leten bileuen þine brune his lond þe þu forbærnest iþench þat he wes ludes sune of þine broþer he is icumen and his fader ahte al þat lond þat nu stondeþ a þire hond and al hit þuncþ him wel idon ȝif þu his sæhtnesse wult vnderfon bute nele he þe nauere euelin mid ærhþe bitæchen þat þu him sculle oþer don oþer slæn oþer ahon þa þe king iherde þis þa wes he wræþ ful iwis and þus seide þe king whar beo ȝe mine kemppen mine drihtliche men wrekeþ me of his lond ich wulle forbærnen and his bone iwurþen þis iherden suggen and he answerede þus whilen hit wes iseid inne soþ spelle þat moni mon deþ muchel vuel al his vnþankes swa ich moht nu neode for muchere neode þe mon þe þoleþ þat me hine wule fordon þat ich telle vnwisdom þe while he mæi þurh æni cræft i compe hine werien ælc cniht ah an uuel to don ær he wurse vnderfon and swa ich æuere bere sceld and spere sende ich wulle to þon kæisere and græten cesare and mænen to him mi sar and bedden þat he me ræde for nu ich habbe neode þe riche cnihte makede a writ wel idiht and nom erendrake godne and sende him to oþres to þon kæisere mid al his romanisce here and þus wes þat writ idiht and þus hit spæc forþriht hail beo þu mid þine here þe keisere þu hattes cezar to þe ich mæne mi sær þin aȝene mon þis nis nan swikedom for þat weord þat ich þe sende bi mine liue ich hit halde and þu hit nult ileuen beoten hit læssingge beo ich hit wulle trousien þurh minne tirfulne godd þurh mine lauerd þe leof me is on heorte for ofte hit is ilumpen inne feole leoden þet æfter muchele hatinge hehȝe men heom luuede and æfter muchel weorldscome wurþscipe wurhten twien þu hafuest ibeon ouercummen and þine men we habbeþ islæn and inome and idriuen þe of brutlonde mid feht swiþe stronge mid us þu hæfuest bileued moni þeosend kempen þat nes noht þurh ure kinge ah hit wes þurh me seolfne and þurh sele mine folke for ich lædde mid me lundene uerde and eke al þa kentwærre þe kempen weoren gode and þerwiþute monienne þe bald wes to fehten seoþþen we þe hafden ouercomen and þi folke islaȝen an iinomen nu is and his men swa modi iwurþen þet mid fehte heo wulleþ me sende ut of brutlonde fleme me from leoden feor from londe mi lond heo habbeoþ me al iwest and lundene me biræued and me sulfne heo þencheþ quellen and alle mine kempen ȝif þu þis writ iheren wult hit wule þe suggen minne gult þa þu weoren from us iliþe at þa latere cherre þa wes þa king swa bliþe swa he nas nauer ære on his liue and on oþer halue he hæfde kare for he nusten þat þu woldest faren noþeles he seide atforen al his duȝeþe nu is awei ifloȝen tweien he is aflemed tweien he com to bruttene þer him wes balu ȝeueþe ne þurfe we nu nauermare iseon hine cumen here for her beoþ his bezste cnihtes islæȝen in ure fehte and nu we sulleþ for heore beone bliþe iwurþen scullen alle mine bruttes mid baldere prute liþen to lundene and þer lof makien vre lauerde and alle ure goden mid him for þere muchele wurþescipe þe ich nu walde þus liþden to lundene alle brutleoden cnihtes and þringes mid wifue and mid children and mid alle þe wurþscipe þe heo weoren wældinde ouer þa we þus comen to lundene we gunnen lof makien ure lauerd and alle ure goden mid him seoþþen þeos weorld wes astalled nes hit nowher itald þat weore nowhar swa muchel mete iuorþþed to ane mele ne swa muchel god dringe folke ideled muchel wes þa gladscipe þa gunnen heo to pleien summe mid foten ueire igerede summe an heorse hehliche iscrudde þa weoren þar tweien scalkes and ifengen here sceldes scriþen under bordes and skirmden mid mæine þe oþer wes mire suster sune euelin hehte þe gume þe oþer herigal heh he wes on hirede of þes kinges kunne icomen he wes his hæluesuster sune he wes þon kinge arle deorest of alle his drihtfolke herigal smat euelin swiþe vfele i þene chin and euelin iwarþ him wraþ and werede hine sulue a þere side he smat herigal þat þe dunt him þuhte sar herigal þa seide and mid muþe hit sweor þat euelin i þon dæi dæd sculde þolien euelin wes swiþe ofdred for me him dead bihæhte and smat on herigales sceld þat his stæf atwaie wond ofte wes euelin wa and næuere wurs þene þa scilde him mid his scelde nefde he elles noht an honde and herigal him soþte on mid hehære strengþe euelin iseh enne gume ȝungen him bihalfues and bar an his riht hond ænne stelene brond euelin him ræsde to and hine ræhliche græp an hiȝinge he þat sweord adroh and herigal ofsloh þat iherde þe king þat herigal wes ofslaȝen and euelin awæi ifloȝen to me he sende his seonde wiþuten gretinge hehte me bringe to him mine mæi euelin swiþe bringe hine him to to þolien his hirdes dom for an of þon he weolden him don oþer slan oþer anhon and ȝif ich þat nalde ich scolde fleon of his onwalde and ȝif he mihte me seoluen ifon he me walden slæn oþer anhon ich ȝirnde þes kinges griþ and walde sæhtnen him wiþ and riht him don i mine hirde for ich wes his eorl þe hehste ah nolde ich him neuere euelin to ærmþen him bitache and he me aflemde sone from hirede lundene he hæfueþ me binome and mine cnihtes ofslaȝen naþeles ich habbe an hirede twa and fifti hundred and ȝet ich habbe an honde twenti castles stronge and miseolf ich wunie inne kent mid kene mine beornnen and þe king me fehteþ wiþ and nule me ȝeuen na griþ nu þu hauest iherd mi sær lauerd cesar al mid soþe worden alse þis writ þe telleþ a þisse write ich habbe idon þat ich wulle bicumen þin mon and halden þe for herre for hehne mine lauerd wiþ þan þe þu me helpe at heȝere neode and aredde me of þon kinge þas weord ich wulle þe treosien þurh mine tirfulne god þat ich hit wulle soþien ase ich hit bi write suggen and cum hiȝendliche to britteine þat lond ich þe biteche þurh me þu hit bilæfdes and þurh me þu hit scalt habben þis writ iherde þe him hafde isend þa enswerede þe keisere nulle ich him ileuen þurh alle leodene aþ bute he me sende anan his feire sune cenan and þritti oþere ȝisles to oþres me sende þeo beon alle icornne and hæȝe ibornne ȝif he þis wule don his bod ic wulle afon and cumen him to helpe mid hæȝere strengþe þas word sende mid write to forþriht anan sende his sune cenan and þritti ȝisles oþere he sende him to oþeres and þe sele to þere sa iwende mid alle his folke fusde touward burttene anan swa hit daȝede he com up at douere þat word him herde and sone þider wende and þas wordes seide wulcume ært þu swiþe leof þu ært me þis lond ich þe bitæche heo speken tosomne and spileden mid sehte þeo while hefede þe king ȝeond al his kinelond isomned ferde stronge to lundene he wolde liþen and enne castel biliggen þe þe stronge hafde þa ȝet an honde þa þe ferde wes al igadered þa com an gume ærnen and anan he þus cleopede to hal seo þu ure king ich þe bringe tiþende of þon romleoden þe laþe þe beoþ an heorten alle heo beoþ i doure þine dædliche iuan and þer is to speken wiþ þeos word beoþ soþe þe ich her sugge and þench mid wulche deden þu miht werien þine leoden þa wes særi þe king and lette biliue blawen his beme cuþen his kempen þa tiþende neowcumene þat þe kæisere mid his romanisce here wes þerriht icumen and þa hauene at doure hafde inomen þa sæide þe king lundene we mote bilæuen and to doure liþen bonnieþ ure ferde and fare we biliue forþ ferde þe king mid vnimete folke riht towarde doure to his muchelen vnbihoue þat iherde cesar he wes wis and swiþe iwar þat þuderward com on ueste þa wes bliþe for þe tiþende leofue he ferde ut of doure bi þe sæoure into ane muchele slæde and slahliche his folc hudde and wende into ane oþere ende to ane wilderne into ane wude muchele and þus spec and wiþ his folke spilede þus ne wurþe nan cniht swa wod ne kempe swa wilde þat he æuere speke worde furþer þene his speres ord ne from his ifere ride for tosomnen we scullen gliden faste togadere and ure ifan fællen and ȝif here is æi heredring þe maȝen nimen þene king nime hine mid isunde and ne ȝefue him nane wunde for he is mi lauerd and mi cun nulle ich hine quellen ah we scullen al his folk feollen to grunde and ȝemen þes fehtes and nawiht þes fenges fællen þa ræȝe and læten þa ræf liggen and al swa lerde leoue his cnihtes hæfde to iueren þritti hundred riderne cnihtes icorene kenewurþ kempen and hæfde to iueren ten þusend rideren alswa heo þus leien stille and bidiemden heore wille þer com þe king riden mid vnimete ferde mid vnimete folke and com heom bitweonen þer heo þoleden teonen him wes biforen bihinden ah ær awoc and ut of wude wende and al þat folc þe he lædde lude hit grædde bleowen here bemen belden heore beornes and heom toward wenden on euereelchen ende þis iherde þe king iherde he þene muchelne dræm and þene dune muchelne he seide forþrihtes wepneþ eow cnihtes þes kinges heorte wes ful sær he wende þat hit weore cesar ah cesær mid his ginne biuoren wes ful stille and ihærde þane dræm wel of folke and wes al rædi alse he to wolde ræsen and þe king nuste herof naþing ah he wepnede his cnihtes and ȝarewede heom to fehten ær heo weoren hælf ȝaru þer com faren and he fusde heom to mid feondliche strengþe þe cnihtes þe weoren igarede bigunnen to fæhten and heom to mid aþelere strengþe æt þon frumræsen he feolde of þon folke feowerti hundred þat folke wes þæ læsse þa wolde þat folke fleon þer com teon forn aȝæien heore hæued and heom to heolde of þon folke he sloh muchel and unifoh þa fleh bruttene king wel ofte him wes wa neuer wurse þene þa him wes biforen him bæften and on ælche side siȝen to his hærme þe king hine biþohte isæh him bihælues ænne holt hæhne bi ænnes wudes ende þider he gon wenden and muchel of his folke floȝen mid þon kinge and astiȝen uppe þen hul mid muchele modsorȝe naþeles þer up þurngen fiftene þusunde wes þe munt swiþe hæh hasles þer greowen swiþe wes þe hul biclused mid cludes of stane heo bigunnen þene wude feollen and heo biforen leggen mid stocken and mid stanen and mid stelene orden heo gunnen heom to werien wiþ heore wiþeriwinnen þene hul makede þe king to strongge enne castle an are nihte firste þat worc wes iforþed for þer worhten sweines þer worþten þeines and þe king mid his honden wurhte ful swiþe to burȝen his liue þa þet work wes up iset heom wes alles þa bet and cesar bilai heom abute þer a þen hulle wes þe king þer he þolede muchelne burst nes þer neouþer win ne must þreo daȝes and þreo niht ne æt þer næuer na cniht heo weoren swiþe uuele ilæd for þe king heom hauede al forrad þe nold sæhtnesse afon at his mæie þerfore he læi on hulle hunger him derfde nearew wes þe king ilæd nuste he nenne ræd for nuste he a nare halue helpen þat him mahte isæh alle dæi biforen his fulle iuan alle icoren þene kæisere mid alle þan romanisce here mid alle þan romleoden to þes kinges unneoden and alle dæi þus cleopeden to nu þu scalt adreden for þine ærdæden hit þe likede wel þat þu us adun læidest mid þine fehte and ure kun feldest nu is icumen þin wadæi for dæþ þu scalt þolien mid hungere and mid hæte and mid sceome muchele þa wes wa þeon kinge and nom him enne ræd for him wes muchel neod he nom enne wisne cniht and sende hine forþriht vt to þon folke þer weoren his iuan and grette mid griþfulle worden bed hine cuþen þat he his cun weoren and þa bet æt þære neode for he wes his broþer sune for nabbe ich þe noht swa uuele idon þat sculde þerforen dæd onfon for þat is muchel unriht ȝif æuere æi god cniht wule his godliche cun bute gulte aquellen æt heȝere neode nu þu must me ræden sæhtnien me wiþ þene kæisere and wiþ þon romanisce here and seoþþen ich wullen þe speken wiþ and makien æfter þine wille griþ togaderen wit scullen libben togadere wit scullen liggen þenc of mire neode and sæhtne me wiþ romlede for ȝif ihc her forwurþe auerst þe beoþ þa wurse for ȝet heo wurþþeþ þe laþe þe me fulsteþ nu to dæþe þa answerede and wiþ þene cnihte he spec þus heu ȝare wes hit iwurþen inne worlderiche þat mines æmes muchele mod swa milde is iwurþen and swa swiþe ræh mon rihtes icnawen ȝet ne beoþ fif dæiȝes allunge iurede þat he me nolde vt driuen binimen me æt þan liue þærto he duden al his mahte he biræuede mine æhte and al þat me wes leof him wes wunderliche læþ þe king dude vnwisdom þat he swulc mod him droh on for he fæht wiþ cesare þan romanisce keisere and he hine twien ouercom and his folk sloh and nom ne dude hit noht þe king ane ah we alle clane þer ich wes o þon fihte mid alle mine cnihten hærde biþrungen i wel feole stunden ah ich miseolf neore and mine gode cnihtes inumen weoren ure king and his bruttes alle aqualde ah we biforen þon kinge fuhte ful swiþe and driuen ut þene kæisere mid his romanisce here ne dude hit noht þe king ane ah duden we alle clæne þa we hafden swa idon and muchele wurscipe anfon þa iwarþ þe king on mode prut ah ne draf he hine noht ane ut seoþþen hit is nu herto ibroht nu is min eam wel biþoht mid mildliche worden he ȝerneþ mine milcne for itemed is þe wode nu beoþ his word gode nu ich wulle wende mi mod aȝenes uuel ich wule don god and lutlien ich wulle his kare and sæhtnien him wiþ cesare ær cumen þe ende of þisse dæi helpen him ȝif ich mai wes swa god sone he dude hine barfot and alle his bezste cnihtes þe mid him weoren an fuhte and eoden to þon kaisere þer he wes i þon here and feollen to his foten and folden and isohten mildeliche spæc þus þe treowe cniht lauerd þin are nu and æuermære lett me speken þe wiþ ich ȝerne mildce and þi griþ þu hauest ouercumen minne æm inne þine fehte he nam flem i þissen hulle he liþ and ȝeorneþ þe lifgriþ for al þu hauest ouercumen and muchel of his folke iualled to grunde and þene kinge and al his lond biȝiten to þire aȝere hond ȝif him nu lifues griþ and let hine speken þe wiþ ær he wes freo king nu þu ært iwreken him on let hine bicumen þin aȝene mon and ælche ȝer þe sende þat gauel of brutlonde madmes and muchel feoh þe monscipe is þin aȝen þis iherde cesar of þissere specche he wes wær aweiward he halde and nolde hit iheren makede hine swulc he weore wraþ for þon wurde þe he iherde wes wis and war þæne kæisere he eode neor and græten worden þæne keisere igrætte and þus queþ hærcne hiderward wiþ me ne beo þu noht wiþerward ilæst ich habbe þe min foreward and al þat ich þe bihehte biforen vnkere cnihte ich bihæhte þe al brutlond to setten a þire aȝere hond and swa ich habben nu idon and þu hit hauest al underfon ah ne bihæhte ich þe nauere to slæn minne æm mid nane rihte ne mai ich hine fordon for ich eam his mæi and his mon ne scal he næuere dæd þolien þe while þe ich mai him freoien ah ȝif mine eame lifues griþ and let hine sæhtnie þe wiþ þi mon he sæl bicumen to ȝisle biteche þe his sune and ælche ȝere senden þreo þusend punden and þat ich þe wullen swerien uppen mine sweorden ȝif þu þis nult iwurþen þe wurs þeo scælt iwurþen ne scalt þu nauere mid þine here isund of brutlonde faren þa wes adrad þe keisere mid his romanisce here leouere him weore þane al his lond þene al his seoluer þæne al his gold þat he weore in oþeres in his castel gode for þa hefde swiþe muchel care þon kæisere þe wende þat swiken hine wolde wes wis and war þat he wel cudde þær þus seide þa to þan eorle mi leofue mon al þine wille ic wulle don don ich wulle þin ræd for þu me hulpe þa me wes neod for ne funde ich nauere treoure mon bitweonen þis and latran þis wes sone icud to þa wes he swa bliþe swa he nes neuere on his liue vt wende þe king adun of þan hulle bliþe on his mode ah þer dude wel and wurþscipen muchele he hine lette ueden he hine lette scruden he hine lette baþien ær he him biuoren come þa hit wes al igreiþed þa comen heo togæderes griþ þer heo astalleden and wel hit wes ihalden heo makeden heore foreward biforen heore duȝeþe bicom aȝene mon and ælche ȝere him sende þreo þusend punden æþes þer weoren isworene and neoren heo nauere forlorne for treowe men heom astalden and alswa heo gunnen heom halden neoþeles wes þæ ærste mon þe dude þis lond inne þeowdom seoþþen noe and his sunen of þære arche weoren icumen þeo al þis wes iuaren þa todælde þa verden and þe keisere and his iueren al þat winter heo wuneden here mid sæhte and mid sibbe mid selcuþe murȝeþe touward þan sumere heo ouer sæ wende and lædde mid him þe wes his deoreste mon and walde al þat he wolde heonene into rome hit stod on dome ne com he naueremare here ne nan of his iuere ne leouede he neuer seoþþen buten seouen ȝere þe wes þisse londes king þa his endedæie com in eouerwicke heo dæide ær þe king were dæd dæide his quene þe king wes al bærnles bruttes weoren særi þis iherde þe i cornwale wes dux þat his eam wes idæied and his aþelene ætfallen and his broþer iuaren uorþ mid and muchel of his cunne quehten mid himseolue hine biþoþte hu he faren mihte and hu he mihte gan on þat he hafde þisne kinedom þe lud king his fader walde wel longe nom his sonde and sende into brutlonde bad heom buȝen him to þa bet heom sculde iwurþen hebben hine to kinge al buten compe bitachen him al þat lond þe lud his fader hafde an hond and he heom wolde luuien þa while þat he luuede and ȝif heo þis wolde habben he hit wolde oþer he wolde mid fehte fallen heom to grunde bruttes ferden heom to lundene to muchele hustinge þat heom þuhte þe bezste ræd to don þat heom bæd æfter him heo senden and heouen hine to kinge þa weoren inne bruttene blissen inouwe tou and twenti wintre þis lond he iwalde seoþþen com þe ilke dæi þat þe king dæd læi inne lundene he liþ særi weoren his leoden þeos kinge hæfde enne sune ihaten he wes iuaren mid his æme forþ into rome augustus cesar hine makede cniht þat wes swiþe muchel riht for seoþþen wes dæd and duȝeþen bilæfden ne bilæfde he næuer nænne of cunne þat heold feht and iwin swa dude and weorede romeþeode wiþ vncuþe leode þis iherde bruttes þe weoren swiþe bisie þat þe kene wunede inne rome þe wes sone and of lud kinge icume tweien cnihtes heo nomen sone and senden to rome and þeo cudden þat his fader wes of liue and beden hine stilleliche iuaren of þere riche nes hit noht longe þat he ne com hider sone and bruttes hine onfengen and heouen hine to kinge on dæie þe king wes inne bruttene com a þissen middelærde anes maidenes sune iboren wes in beþleem of bezste alre burden he is ihaten þurh þene halie gost alre worulde wunne walden englenne fæder he is on heuenen froure moncunnes sune he is on eorþen of sele þon mæidene and þene halie gost haldeþ mid himseoluen þene gast he wel daleþ to þan þe him beoþ leoue alswa he dude peture þe wes a wræche fiscære þe makede hine an mancunne hehst of alre manne bruttene king wes god mon þurh alle þing and he luuede here twa and twenti ȝere an his dæie her luuede a mon inne þisse leoden feorliche þing fuleden him he wes ihaten teilesin heo heolten hine for witie þurh his witfulne cræfte and al heo hit ilæfden þat teilesin heom seide he seide heom seolkuþ inoh and al heo hit funden soþ he seide heom ælche ȝere wæt heom to cumen weore þe king him sende æfter wise twalf cnihtes bad hine comen him to þat he nan oþer seolden don and heo hine broþten sone biforen þen folkekinge anan swa þe king hine imette fæire he hine igrette swa me helpen min hefde and mi chin welcume ært þu teilesin and leouere me is þine isunden þenne a þusend punden þa andswerede teilesin and þus seide to swa ich mote gode iþeon al þu hit sælt wel biteon þa wes glad and þus seide to teilesin her beoþ to þisse londe icumen seolcuþe leodronen and fromward þeon londe of ierusalem iwurþen heo beoþ in beþleem þer is iboren an luttel child inne þere leoden muchele is and stor þe eiȝe tacnen þer beoþ on sterren an monen and on seonnen eie is on moncunnen þis is widen icuþ and þa writen me beoþ to icume and ic wolde iwiten æt þe þu ært mi wine deore to whan þis tocne wule ten to wulche þinge temen for herfore is alches londes folc lædliche afered þa answerede teilesin and þus seide to hit wes ȝare iqueþen þa quides beoþ nu soþe þat scolden beon a child iboren of alle folke icoren and þat scolde beon ihaten hælend and helpen his freondes alesen his leofue wines of læþe heore bendes of helle bringen adam noe and and samiel and symeon þene alde an and alle his broþeres mid him and eliseon asor and naason and his broþer and monienne oþer moni hundred þusend þe iþud beoþ to hellen and for swulchere neode he is icumen to þere þeoden þeos word seide teilesin and alle heo weoren soþe þa þan kinge wes icudde þas quides þa weoren soþe þa weoren þa tiþinde cuþe ȝeond his kineriche bruttes herof ȝemden and noht hit ne forȝeten wes god king and griþful þurh alle þing and þa romleoden swiþe hine luueden and ȝif þe king wolde wiþ heom wiþerheolden he miþte æthalden heore feoh þe her fætte ah æueremære bi his liue he hit heom leofliche ȝeaf seoþþe him comen þæ tiþinde of godes childe ne leouede þe king mære buten ten ȝere seoþþen þe king bilæfden his lif inne eowuerwike he ȝet liþ her he bilæfden tweien sunen wiþer and aruiragune wiþer wes þa ældere aruiragun þe ȝungere ah þe king biqueþ wiþer al his kineriche and he dihte and delde æfter his fader dæie he wes swiþe god cniht and hæfde ihælden moni fiht ah he wes swiþe sturne and stærc wiþ þeon folke he nalde for nane dome mare heren to rome ne na gauel heom senden vt of þissen londe ah whæreswa he fonde enne gume þe of rome weore hider icumen he lette smiten him of þat hæfde biræiuie hine at liue and þus he heom græiþeden mid grimme his gomene an kæisere wes in rome ihaten iherden þa tiþende of wiþer þon kinge whulcne scome he him hæfden idon and mare him bihehte þe kæisere hine wrædden þe wurs him wes on heorte and swor bi his rigge þat wiþer hit scolde abiggen he bigon to senden ȝeond al þan romleoden he hætte al þa ræiȝe and alle þa radfulle alle his hæȝe men his hustigge isechen and heo togædere comen i þere burh of rome heo buden heore ferden wide ȝeond þon ærde mid unimete dome heo ferden vt of rome heo ferden swa longe þat heo comen to þisse londe þe kæisere and al his romanisce here at portchæstre heo comen alond and stepen up a sæstrond and bilæien anan portchæstre mid heore folke swiþe faste heo letten deluen diches vnimete deope and al abuten oueral he makede stænene wal þa wes portchestre burh mid þan bezste ah mid þan windræsen al heo gunnen toreosen mid fure and mid fehte foruaren þurh þan kæisere þis iherde wiþer þe wes bruttene king her þat icumen wes i þisse lond þat wes swa strong þe king gæderede uerde wide ȝeond his eærde and aruiragus his broþer gæderede anoþer and ferden toward þære sæ mid selkuþe folke þat heo comen mid heore here to þan kæisere feondliche heo feohten fullen þa fæie and þe eorl aruiragus mid æþele help his broþer hæfde enne richene mon þe wes icleoped he redde þæn kæisere and al þan romanisce here hamund biheold wiþer and his wiþerhappes and heu ladliche i þon fihten he sloh þa romcnihtes and al þat him biforen stod he falden to his foten hamun hine biþohte whet he don mihte hv he mihte þene king wiþer aquelle hamun ferde ȝeon þat wæl and wende þa deden funde þer enne cniht þe islæȝen wes þerriht nom he his burne and his goldileired bord leoup he an his stede and bihælues he gon riden þer he isæh wiþer king þe wiþer wes an compe hamun þe ridere smat his aȝene ifere and warþ him swiþe bisi swulc he weore wende þe king wiþer þat he weore his iuere ah þer he na ne come ȝif hit nere for swikedome hamun arnde upward and oþer while adunward þenne he isæh romanisce mon he rasden him ouenan his speche wes al brutisc swulc he weoren swa longe he gon riden þat he wes bi þæs kinges side and fæht þan kinge biforen swulc he weoren his mon iboren and sloh is haȝen iueren muchel swikedom wes þere þe king him treousede on for he wes swa æht mon and wende for soþ riht þat he weore his aȝen cniht þe king wende forþrihtes bihælues þan fihte he wes swiþe ofhæt þat al his burne wes biswæt he lette his burne of his rugge eorne and hamun him to strac mid toȝen his mæine mid his spere he wes wæht þes kinges breosten he tobræc þane king wiþer he ofsloh þer wes swikedom inoh and seoþþen rehliche fleh to his romleode kudde hit his kæisere whet he dude mid his spere þis isæh aruiragus þat his broþer islæȝe wes þus mid muchelen hiȝinge he leup to þan dæde kinge igrap his stede and alle his iwede and sturede i þon compe alse hit þe king weore mest alle þa bruttes þe weoren þere wenden þat hit weoren wiþer heo ræsden to romleoden and heo remden to flonne heo sloȝen forþrihtes cnihtes niȝen þusende heo læiden to þon grunde þe kæisere sad wes of þon compe his folc flah into scipen and from þæn londe iwenden forþ mid þon vþen feondes heom uereden fif þusend heo lefden uppen þon londe þat ne mithte no to scipe cumen þat heo neoren islæȝen oþer inomen wunderliche awei heo riden touward ane muchele wude aruiragus heom æfter mid twenti þusend cnihtes heo sloȝen heo nomen mid honden heo todrowen hamun þurh þene wude flæh riht touward þere sæ he ærnde to are hæuene he wenden scipen habben þe sæ wes iȝeonged þe scipen stoden a londe þæ wile þe he þa scipen vt scæf aruiragus him to draf nefde hamun to iueren bute þritti rideren aruiragus heom alle sloh and hamun mid heorsen todroh for his broþer dæþe him wes swiþe unneþe and an oþer halue he wes glæd þat his ifon weoren dæd for hamundes dæþe hamton heo hit hæhte nu and aueremare þe nome stondeþ þere nu þu iherest of wuche gomen aras þer þe tonome swa doþ a feole wise tonome ariseþ and ofte of lutle þinge þe longe ilasteþ for his nauere nan oþer gomen þat cleouieþ alswa ueste þa hamun and is iueren weoren dæd aruiragus wes swiþe glad ah sone þeræfter him com særinesse he and his cnihtes þeonene forþrihtes tuo winchestre wenden wæne com on ueste heo wende to soþe þat heo siker weoren þe keisere mid alle his romanisce here ouer sæ wende al mid isunde nes he þer buten enne niht þe wind wende forþriht fromward þan stronde into þissen londe wenden aȝan weder him stod an wille hiȝenliche sone to portchestre heo comen up iwende þe kæisere mid al his romanisce here iwepned wel alle heo wenden to þan walle to heo eoden alle afoten and swiþe freche weoren ouer þene wal heo clumben and binnen heo þrungen þat folc heo al slowen þa æhte heo nomen al þa wunliche burh heo barnden to duste þus portchæstre toræs and nauere seoþþen heo ne aras þat heo swulc weore swa heo wes eare þe keisere mid wunderliche here ferde to winchæstre and bilæi þa burh swiþe feste þer binnen wes aruiragus ærmliche biþrungen and muchel dæl of his cunne of bruttisce monnen wa wes þon kinge aruiragus and to his cnihtes seide þus suggeþ me gode men godfulle kempen wulle ȝe me helpen mid hæhȝere strengþe her to biwinne wurþscipe minne þa answereden aþele cnihtes nulle we þe bilæuen for liue ne for dæþen on heo duden heore iweden and leopen on heore steden cnihtes þer weoren swiþe iwhæte heo duden up þere burhȝæten heo makeden heore sceldtrome þa scalkes weoren gode weoren alle þa cnihtes ȝærewe to þon fihte þa somnede alle þa alde þe to fehte heom scolde halden bi are halue heo riden and spileden of ræde and nomen tweien cnihtes and senden to þon kæisere and axeden wheþer he wolde griþ þe he wolde vnfrih ær þer come mare lure hefde he þene cure þa andswerede and wiþ þan cnihten he spec þus wel is þe man nut þe sæhtnesse wurcheþ ich æm ræh mon inoh rome is min riche and alle þa londes stondeþ a mire honde þa biȝet me biuoren þe kæisere and æfter mine dome hæreþ into rome buten þes ilke kinedom nulle me noht icnawen na þissere leodes folke for lauerd me halden and me pugcheþ muche scome at mire heorte ic habbe grome ȝif rome scæl forleosen þa while þe ich leouie heore muchele wurhscipe þat mine ældere hire biwunnen for nare ȝitsunge for nare ȝiuernesse ne com ich to þissen londe to halden fiht stronge ne for nane plihte buten to biȝiten mine rihte and ic heo wulle biwinnen oþer an wæle liggen æc cnihtes ȝit beoþ hider icumen from þon kinge aruiragune fareþ swiþe aȝen to þan folckinge suggeþ him to soþe for hit cumeþ him to cuþe þat ȝif he wule a leoþ gan and halden me for lauerde and he me wulle buȝen þa bet him scal iwurþen ȝif he me wule sende mine rihten of his londe ic hine wulle wurþien mid wurhscipe muclen and suggeþ him ful iwis ich ȝifuen mine dohter to sibben and to some þe bet wit mawen libben and ȝif he þis nule don he scal wurs vnderfon faren wit swullen tosomne and mid fehten hit todælen makien wænslæhtes þænne beoþ þe wurse þa cnihtes wenden forþriht to þan folckinge cudden him soþ quides from þæn kæisere þe king isæh þe neode and droh to his ræde and he mid wurþscipe þas cnihtes awurþede þat he of his kinedome wulde heren into rome and seoþþe wurþscipe him don his dohter to quene vnderfon togædere heo comen and sæhten heo weoren sone and seoþþen heo alle iwenden into winchæstren þa weoren in þissen londe blisfulle songes heo wuneden inne winchæstre an and twenti wikene and senden to rome ful iwis æfter þan maidene þat maiden mid isunde com to þisse londe and þe kæisere ȝæf heo þisse kinge ȝet hit is isene þat heo wes her quene þat þe king aruiragus to quene hæfde þes þinges weoren idone and hæuede isend to rome þa while iwende and þe king aruiragus into orcaneiȝe and þat lond al bilæien ah muchel lond þerabuten al heo hit biȝeten two and þritti æitlond heo setten on heore aȝere heond heore griþ heo setten fæste and wenden to winchæstre from rome wes icumen ful iwis þat fæire maide isund and hire iuæren sixti rideren þat maiden wes iwedded þe king heo hafde to bedde muchel wes þa blisse þe wes þanne i bruttene mid þan kinge aruiragus and þæn kæisere þa wes þis folk swa bliþe heo nære nauer ær on liue for þere muchele blisse heo arærden enne burȝe an enne swiþe feire stude uppe sæuerne þa þe burh wes al imaked mid muchelere strengþe þa burh ȝæf aruiragus þæn kaisere and þat lond þerabuten muchel and noht lutel he hæhte setten hire on nome þe hire mihte isemen hu þe king aruiragus nam to quene and þer þe king heo ȝef þan romanisce kæisere þe heȝe kairclou heo hehte ac nas hit noht longe þat þe nome moste stonden ac for wurþscipe swa wes þe nome iqueþþen ah þa ærest in þissen londe com he funde enne feire wimman heo wes witer heo wes wis heo wes maiden ful iwis cnihtes heo biwunnen i þon fihte inne portchæstre and heolden heo wel fæste and ȝeuen heo hit wes him swiþe iqueme and he hire rædde and forþ mid him ladde and leouede þe wimman leofliche swiþe þe wifman iwarþ mid childe bi þan balde þa þet child wes iboren wel wes þerforen þa þe time wes ifulled þat hit fulleht sculde habben æfter þan haþene laȝen þat stoden o þen ilke dæȝen nome heo him aræhten and gloi þat child hahten þis child wæx and wel iþæh and muchel folc him to bah and him bitæhte þa burh þe he ahte and sette heo mid cnihten þe gode weoren to fehten and hæhte heo wite wel faste and heoten heo gloichestre al for his sune luuen þe leof him wes an heorten þe seoþþe biȝæt al walisc lond to his aȝere hond and þerof he wes deme and duc feole ȝere þis child me biwuste inne gloichæstre and þa þeos þinges weoren idone ferde to rome and ladde þes childes moder for quene nauede he oþer þa com to rome tiþende him com sone þat þer wes cumen liþende into þere leode an swiþe selcuþ gume of he wes icome he wes ihaten he dude þer feole teonen he uerde ȝeond al þat lond and turnde hit to godes hond heonene wes iuaren þis lond heold aruiragus and his quene þe wifmon wel idone þa isæh þisses ledes king þat him ne derede naþing þus he wunede here mid blisse twenti ȝere vnder þan comen tiþende to aruiragus þan kinge næs þer nan oþer ræd bute inne rome wes dæd wa wes þisse kinge swa wes þere quene swa wes alle þon bezsten þe wuneden an bruttene an þan timen hit wes þat gloi wes swiþe god cniht þa þeo tiþende weoren comen to londe of þen kæisere and hu hit wes al iuaren þa seide þe king aruiragus and wiþ his duȝeþe he spac þus swa ich auere ibiden are nulle ich naueremare þurh nane dome heren into rome næ naueremare heom senden gauel of mine londe ah ȝif heo hider cumeþ liþen leoden to biwinnen her heo sculeþ ibiden bitterest alre baluwen næ biȝeten nan oþer god buten here ȝeoten heore blod scullen alle heore wif widewen iwurþen þus seide þe king þeh hit soþ neore þer he sæt mid his scenche an his kinebenche ah al oþer hit iwarþ inne þan twam wintren for þa romleoden sende to þissere þeoden hæhte heom senden here gauel of þissen londe and þe king aruiragus wradliche heom answerede hehten heom mucle eiȝe ut of his æhseone fleon of þissen londe ær heo fæiȝe iwurþen forþ heo iwenden into romlonde þa wes i þon ȝere vaspasien kæisere þes tiþende him wes læþ and herfore he was wraþ he clupede to ræde alle romleode and seide bi his liue þat he wolde to bruttlonde bitelen his irihten þat ær ahte and ȝif heo nolden gan an griþ he wolden fehten heom wiþ and al romleoden þis him gon ræden vaspasien him forþ wende þat he com to france þa ȝet hit wes al his aȝen þat he isæh mid his aȝene ladde he þere leodene king þe hine for lauerd icneou vorþ mid imseoluen touward þissen londen to þere sæ he wende scipen he þer funde þat toȝenes him weoren ibonned þe ȝet þe he wes i rome he ibad þes wederes wind com on oueste in he wende at witsond and æt doure he þohte nimen lond aruiragus þerof wes war and atliche him biuore uerde and draf hine ut mid strengþe forþ mid sæstrame mid him hafde vaspasien swiþe gode sæmen strahten vt here lof and leiden æfter vþen forþ bi sæside seileden swiþe an hiȝende ful sone to tottenas heo come strahten scipen to þan londe and eoden uppen stranden heo nomen heore wepnen and forþ gunnen wenden tosomnen heo riden uaste þat heo comen to he wenden wel to bistelene into þare burhȝe ah þet burhfolc wes war and wel hine wusten wel heo closden heore ȝeten and ȝareweden heom to fehten and þa burh biwusten wel mid þan bezsten seouen daȝes fulle vaspasien mid his monnen læiȝe at exchæstre and bilaie heom swiþe ueste þat iherde aruiragus þat he wes icume þus he nom al þa ferde of brutlondes ærde and sone he gon faren in toward cornwalen into exchæstre þa burh wes þa fæstre aruiragus wes þerinnen mid bruttisce mennen vaspasien þervte þa burh bilæi abute amarȝen þa hit dæi wes duren heo vntunden cnihtes heom gereden grundliche feire blewen þa bemen heornes gunnen dremen heondleden scæftes and goldfaȝe sceldes riden ut tosome ræȝe brutes þritti þusend þe þræt wes þa mare þerute wes heom toȝæn þe kæisere togadere heo tuhten and laþliche fuhten hardeliche heuwen helmes þer gullen stercliche tostopen mid steles egge alle dæi þer ilæste fæht mid þan mæste a þet þat þustere niht todælde heore muchele fiht læien a ba halue cnihtes toheouwen þær wes hærm mid þon meste biuoren exchæstre þat biheold þa quene ihaten særi wes hire heorte mid hermen afulled cleopede to hire lauerde þe leof hire wes on heorte to þon kinge aruiragus þæ quene spac wiþ him þus lauerd biþenc þe þine þeowes beoþ gode þu hauest mucle treowscipe treowþe staþeluæste þat beoþ þa þingges þe biriseþ to ælche kinge riche men and hæne ȝif wiþ seoumen he wule beon clænen biþenc þu a þine quides þe þu sulf quiddest wiþ minne fader þe wes þi cudliche freond þe dude þe þa wurhscipe bitahte me þe to wiue and þu ært me swa leof swa mi kinelauerd mi cun is her wiþvten and þi kun her wiþinnen ȝif þu brekest þine quides and mi cun quellest soþ ich þe habbe iseid wiþ þine sune þu beost iuæid and ȝif mi cun clembeþ and bineoþen þe ibringeþ and þe seoluen and þin folc falleþ to grunde ȝif þu and þine þer wurþeþ dæd þeonne beo ich wiþ mine sune iued betere weore sæhte þene swulc vnisibbe and biþenc þe of þan fore hu þu mine fader swore to lasten alche ȝere al to þine liue gauel into rome of þine kinedome and ȝet ilæsteþ þi lif swa hit do longe for þi þu most holden þat þu ær bihæhtest al þa heredcnihtes heolden mid þere quene þe king and alle his cnihtes wakeden alle nihte al niht heo runden whæt heom weoren to ræde ne mihte heo finde nænne ræd þe heom þuhte al swa god swa heom þuhte þe soþe quides of þere quene amarwe þa hit dæi wes duȝeþen heom gereden togædereward heo uusden alswa heo wolden fehten forþ com þa quene and rad heom bitweonen ærst heo nom griþ and seoþþen heo heom spac wiþ sette sæhtnesse somnede cnihtes þa ær weoren ifeonde makede heom to fronde and þe king heom bihehten his foreward to haldene and swa he hit ilæste þe while þe he luuede þus heo weoren sahte and þus heo weoren some þa wes þeos bruttene swiþe iblissed and vaspasiæn and his iueren al þat winter wuneden here from burie to burie ferden mid blisse anan swa seomer come þa ferden heo to rome brutlond wes bliþe a to þeos kinges liue nu hauede þe king aruiragus enne sune þe hehte he wes isende to rome to leornien in scole þer him wes swa wel idiht he wes clærc and god cniht þider him com sonde ut of þissen londe þæt her nes nan rad for þe king his fader wes dæd and he mosten cume sone to his kinedome swa wes þat writ idiht and he hit dude forþriht to þisse londe he com and underfeng þene kinedom wel riche wes aruiragus and mucle ricchere a þisse londe he heold griþ a þisse londe he hulde friþ her wes blisse her wes mete and alre godene mast a þissen ilken hit stod þet com ouer sæflod an king þe hæhte elche oþer unilic he com ut of scice elches londes vniliche he brohte mid him þe peohtes folc of muchele mahte seoþþen wes ærst mon and he mihte uuel don a he ferde bi sæflod and dude he uuel and næuere god monie hundreþ buriȝe he hæfde imakede blæþe he ferde bi sæstronde into scotlonde þat lond he al wæste mid hermen þan meste þurh þat lond he ærnde and hærȝede and hærmde comen þa tiþende to þon kinge hu þe king his ræflac makede sone he sende sonde ȝeond alle þisse kinelonde hæhte æuerælcne mon þa his monscipe uþe þat he wel iwepned comen to hirede þis folc wes isomned and þe king fusde ferde into scotlonde þere he king fond heo fuhten swiþe feondliche and feollen þa peohtes and þer wes ofslaȝen and seoþþen mid heorsen todraȝen þer dude þe king a wel swuþe sællech þing uppen þen ilke stude þer he uordude he lette aræren anan enne swuþe sælcuþ stan he lette þeron grauen sælcuþe runstauen hu he ofsloh and hine mid horsen todroh and hu he þa peohtes ouercom mid his fæhtes vp he sette þæne stan ȝet he þer stondeþ swa he deþ al swa longe swa þa woreld stondeþ nome him scupte þe king and hehte þene stan westmering a muchel dæl londes þe þer liþ abuten nom þe king to his hond and hæhte hit westmerelinge lond nu þu hafuest soþ iherd for wham hit swa hatte þa þe þeo peohtes weoren ouercumne i þon fehte and wes dæd and his iueren fordemed þa fluȝen þer bihælues fiftene hundred þat weoren þa feirest men þe weoren i þon fehte hæfden he to heretoȝe enne hæhiborene mon þeos weolden heom iburȝen and bihalues fleon and buȝen vt of londe to helpen heore liue þat isehȝen þreo eorles þe i þeon fehte weoren ohte whudereward þa ferde heore flæm makeden þe eorles heom siȝen to mid selen heore cnihtes driuen heom into ænne hæhne wude þer heo heærm þoleden stod þe wundliche wude amidden ane wælde biuoren na bihinden ne mihten þær nan atwinden ah alle hi heom nomen and nane heo ne asloȝen fæste heom heo bunden and brohten to þen kinge þat þe king heom sculden don oþer slan oþer hon anan swa þe king heom spec wiþ swa heo ȝeornden his griþ ȝeorne heo hine beden þurh his ædmeden þat he nomen heom to þrallen and heo him wolden þiwien and heo him wolden beon liþe a to heore liue al þe king weorhte also heo bisohten and heom an heond sælde muchel dæl of londe al abuten þer heo caþel wrohten þat lond wes swiþe god ah seoþþen wes þe muchel flod nes hit neuere itiled þurh nænne eorþeitilie no nauere þer ne wuneden on nanes cunnes quic mon sonen heo gunnen to ærien þat lond wes swiþe æþele heo tileden heo seowen heo repen heo meowen wiþinnen þan þrom ȝeren þa nomen heo twælf iueren and heo uerden sone þat heo to þisse londe comen bruttes heo gretten mid græiþlichen worden beden heom beon on sele and alle isunde we eow toȝerneþ ȝeue swiþe deore þet ȝe us ȝiuen wifmen to habben to wiue þenne maȝe we heolden luue to þissen leodfolke þa þis iherden bruttes heokerliche heom þuhte and hehten heom faren awæi and fleon of heore londe for nolde heo heom ȝetten þa þinges þe heo ȝernden peohtes weoren iscende and heore wæi forþ wende ham to heore cunne and cudden heom heore erende heo nomen heore sonde and sende to irlonde to þes londes kinge gille caor ihaten and biden hine heom senden wifmen of his londe and þe king heom ȝette al þat heo ȝeorenden þurh þa ilke wifmen þa þer wuneden longe þat folc gan to spelien irlondes speche and auer seoþþen þa laȝen wunieþ a þan londe swa heo beoþ þere nu and æueremare hæfde þe king god griþ ȝeond his lond a to his liue his leoden weoren bliþe þa com þe ilke dæi þat þe king dæd læi forþ com þes kinges sune wes ihaten þes wes ræh þes wes strong þes wes stiþ an þonke þes cuþe alle þa domes þe stoden inne rome ah he ne luuede noht longe þat wes his leodene hærm ah þa while þe he luuede his lond he huld a blisse hæfde þe king þe wes bruttene aþel enne leofue sune ihaten þes wes þe bezste mon þe auere hæfde kinedom seoþþen to brutlonde com bruttes þe hit biwan wes kineboren wes wel itoȝen and he wes swiþe blæþfæst bruttes hine luueden moni wes þat gode þing þat cuþe þe king nes þa na man vnder lufte þe cuþe betere cræftes þurh þisne ilke æþele mon vnderfeng þis lond cristindom þe mon þe wule lusten hu hit ærest ilomp þeos boc him wulle suggen soþþere wordes hu þe king ærst luuede men wel idone comen ut of rome comen to þan kinge and talden him tiþende of alle þere fore þe dude in rome and whulcne martirdom hauede vnderfon and þa oþere halȝen þe mid godde hah weoren þa longede swuþe þon kinge ære he mare wuste of þan lauerd þa weoren inne rome men wel idone and an hali mon þer wes pape wes ihaten nom þe king of his leofuste monnen sende to þa papen and feire hine gon greten and bed hine on godes nomen þat him god uþe þet he senden him anan sumne godcunde mon for þe king wolde wel don and laȝen vnderfon libben mid rihte and luuien his drihte he an alle his leoden þe wuneden inne þissere þeoden þa þuhte þat tiþende swiþe murie nes na mon on liue þat weore alswa bliþe alse wes þe hali man þa he þis iheren gon þe pape hafden tweien biscopes þe luueden godes rihten hiderwardes he heom senden þa biscopes forþ wenden þat comen þa godes sonden into þissen londe to þon kingen and to al his hereþringen þa spac dunian and þe oþer biscop fagan seiden þan kinge larspel and he hit hærcnede wel ær þat lærspel weoren idon þe king ȝeornde cristindom and alle his duȝeþecnihtes hit ȝeorde forþrihtes þe king fulluht vnderfeng and alle his gode men mid him and alle his bruttes þe him buȝen wolden and þa fulluht nulden vnderfon þe king heom letten fordon þa þis wes al idon þa token heo oþer weise on beiene þa biscopes ferden ȝeond þas bruttene alle þa templen þe þa heþene hafden itimbrid heo letten alle þa scrud at þere dure werpen vt wascen þa waȝes wel mid þan bezsten þa nomen anlicnes þe weoren ihatene heo letten heom draȝen vt oþer bi hondes oþer bi fot heo heom letten swalen inne swærte fure þa þis wes al idon þa token heo oþer weiis on heo ferde forþrihtes þurh godes mihten from stouwe to stouwe and stureden heomseoluen hælȝeden alle þa templen a þes helindes nomen þa þet wes all idon þo token heo oþer weis on þa setten heo biscopes þan folken to dihten þerouer ærchebiscopes þat clærcscipe to rihten chirchen he letten areren monie and wel iwhare preostes heo þer setten ase þerto mihte semen þa þis wes al idon þa token heo oþer weis on þa com þe king and lond þerto leide and sette þeron godes friþ and freoden alle þe chirchen and þa laȝen beoþ a monie studen alswa heom on dude naþeles heo weoren soþþen swiþe awæmmed ladliche iniþered þurh niþfulne craft and eft heo weoren irihte swa hit weolde drihten þa alle þas þinges weoren idone þa ferden þa biscopes to rome and bileæfden in þisse londe þat folc a godes heonde and heore lauerd þe leof heom was an heorte þus hit ferde here wel feole ȝere þe leodking leouuede wel longe twa and feowerti wintre mid muchere winne her wes mete her wes drænc men þerof dræmden her wes unimete fare a þissere folc riche þus heo gunnen driuen and forȝeten to swiþe þat heom tæhte þe hehȝe mon þe gode biscop dunian and fagan his iuære þe while þe heo weoren here inne griþe þurh alle þing wunede þe king þat com þe ilke dæi þat þe king dæd læi leof him wes griþ and ræd inne gleochæstre he wes dæd þær hehȝe bruttes þene king bureden þa wes þe weorlde swa uorþ iuaren seoþþen ure drihte wes iboren an hundred ȝere and sixti þa þe king sah to grunde seoþþen king wes dæd her wunede a swiþe strong red ne bilæfde he her neouþer suster ne broþer ne quene ne næh cun þe his caþel mihte heolden to rome comen tiþende of þon kinge hu þe king wæs hære dæd and i þisse londe nas na ræd heo makeden heore uerde and senden to þissen ærde seuarus wes heore hæretoȝe inne rome he wes ibore þe ferde wes swiþe strong þeo comen heo to þisse lond wende anan to hæbbene þisne kinedom ah bruttes weoren bisie and ofte hine abæileden ofte heo him wiþ fuhten a feole cunne wisen seuarus hine biþoþte whet he don miþte in his herede he makede griþ and lette awæi þat vniriht þat na man ne wurþe swa wod ne witte bidæled þat in his hirede breke griþ uppe leome and uppe lif of nauere nane þinge þat come to his cleopinge þis iseȝen bruttes þe weoren swiþe bisie þat seuarus in his hirede hæfde hehliche griþ and mong heomseoluen vnimete seorȝen bruttes siȝen togæderes fulle seoue þusend and speken wiþ and ȝirden his hiredes griþ and he heom ȝette and ȝef ȝiues swiþe gode þa wes seuarus hired selcuþliche istronged alle þe ær weoren buuen he heom sette bineoþen and muchele luue heold wiþ alle þat ȝirnden his griþ he uærde to lunden and heo hine vnderfengen he uerde þurh þis kinelond and sette hit in his aȝere hond and æuere heo fluȝen him biuoren þe his feond weoren swa swiþe he heom hænde þat heo fluwen ouer heo fluȝen forþrihtes þat heo comen to þan peohtes and heo heom vnderfengen and nomen heom to iuaren heo makeden enne hehne cniht heore heretoȝe forþriht fæier cniht and hende fulgenes wes ihaten he heom scolde læden and he heom sculde ræden enne ende of scotlonde nom fulgenes to his honde þe ende him wes deore he hæhte dæire sæuarus from scottewærd seoþþe aȝæn wende and his folc lædde into lundene and fulgenes vt of scotlen muchel scaþe makede he leop into brutlond mid muchele baluræssen æhte he nom men he sloh he duden seorȝen inoh and þus he uerde longe inne scotlonde þis iherde seuarus þe inne rome wes kæisere and seoþþen hider al þa lond stod an his aȝere heond þe kæisere sende his seonde ȝeond feole londe lette him to beoden swa monie of weorcmonnen þat he lette makien ænne dic þe wæs wunderliche deop muche and swiþe stronge bisides scotlonde from sæ to sæ eode þæ dich ælche oþere vnilich þervfenen he makede scid wal wunder ane cræftie seoþþen he sette cnihtes to witen hit dæies and nihtes þat neuere poht þerouer ne com ne næuere nan oþer mon bute whaswa walden ȝernen griþ and speken þan kæisere wiþ and wunien forþ here mid seuare þan kæisere þat iherde fulgenes þat þis weorc iuorþed wes þat he into þisse londe ne mihte ne dæies ne nihtes nuste he þa nænne ræd þe him æuere þuhte god he cleopede alle his dringches þat heo comen to hustinge heore kinge to ræden of his muchele neode heo him rædden to faren riht into cise færliche he þider com and fæire wes underfon he spac wiþ þan peohtes and swa muchel heom bihæhte þat heo gædereden in þan ærde mucle scipferde and ferden bi sæstronde into þissen londe he uerde riht to euerwicke brutten þutte sellic þa burh he anan bilæi mid baldere strengþe seoþþen he dude to witen þurh worde and þurh writen alle his freonden þe weoren in þissen londe þat heo scolden wel don and alle comen him to he heom wolden mucle wele and wurþscipe itæchen and æuere to his liue heo sculden beon him leoue þis iherden bruttes þerfore heo weoren balde and wenden from þan romænisce kæisere moni þusend bruttes to fulgenes and he heom faire onfeng and muche feoh bihæhte þat iherde sæuarus þat fulgenes dude þus he somnede uerde of folke of þissen ærde he uusde touwærd euerwic to his fæisiþe þa he to euerwic com fulgenes him wes aforen on heo bigunnen fehten feondliche swiþe a ba hælue þer ful folc unimete sæuare þer wes ofslæȝen and feole his romwæren fulgenes wes iwunde wunderliche sære þat i þan þridden dæie he sarne dæd þolede of sæueres dæþe þer demden sæiden heom bitweonen þa þat tir ahten seuarus wes god cniht and he heold us swiþe riht þæ while þe we him walden heren ær we turnden to fulgene þurh heore vuele ræde beien heo beoþ dædde nime we sæuarusses lic and lede we hit into eouuerwic and þær we hit sculleþ biburien mid muchelere blisse and forþ ȝelden þa duȝeþe þe he us dude whilen al weoren þa dæden alse heo idemden sæuarus bilefde here tweien sunen þus hæhten heore nomen þe ældere hehte basian þe ȝungere hahte gezan þe beiene heo weoren ibroþeren ah noht of are moder basianes moder wes of brutlondes ærd and gezanes moder of romanisce monnen bruttes nomen basian and bitahten him þisne kinedom and þa romanisce men to kinge makede gezan bruttes weoren bisie and basian heo luueden and þa romanisce men luueden swiþe gezan þær aras muchel ballu bitwenen þissen broþeren heo nomen here uerden and comen to stalfehte and þer þe king basian sloh his broþer gezan and þat romanisce folc fleh of þissen londe ac monie þer weoren ifalled i þan muchele fehte i þisse londe wes a ȝung mon vnder þon kinge basian carrais wes ihaten his nome þes wes a sellich gume his fader wes an unstrong cniht ah þe sune wes swiþe sturne þat wes þe bisegæste mon þe wunede inne bruttene of nane quike monne næuede he care nænne wa wes him þurh alle þing þat basian wes bruttene king basian wes griþful king and carrais ne likede hit naþing þa a þan ilke time verden bi særime vtlaȝen to iwiten fulle sixti scipen carrais hine biþohte of ane hindere cræfte þat he wolde sone faren into rome forþ he iuusde and into rome ferde and spac wiþ þane kæisere and wiþ þan romanisce here and þus seide carrais he wes swike fuliwis hæil seo þu cyrian þe king þe græteþ basian and dæþ þe ful wel to witen ba bi worden and bi writen þat ne mæi he þe no mare senden þat gauel of bruttlonde for twien haueþ bigunnen to senden hit bi his monnen i sæ heo funden vtlaȝen and habbeoþ alle his men islaȝen and iræued al þat gærsume þe scolde þe to cume þa vtlaȝes beoþ swa stronge bi watere and bi londe þat ne mæi na man ouer sæ uaren bute mid swiþe mucle care ah ȝif þi wille weore þat þu woldest me ihere and bitachen me þine writen and senden me twælf scipen and hælden me to munde a þire aȝere hond into sæ ic wolde faren and slæn alle þa utlaȝen and þi gauel þe sende ut of brutlonde for ich æm ennes cnihtes sune and cun ich habbe iwide haueþ mi fader bi þære sæ castel swiþe sæle and cnihtes inowe and men unifoȝe alle heo wulleþ to me draȝen to quellen þa utlaȝen and þus ich wulle þurh mire hond witen þi feh and þi lond þis ihærde cyrian speken þene swikeful mon and al he ȝette him þat he him to ȝirde writen he him bitehten and wapnen him aræhte and forþ hine senden touward þissen londe forþ he ferde carrais þat he com to france æuere his writen he vnfeold þer he forþ ferde and seiden al þan monnen what he i rome hæhde biwunnen and folc him wende an æuerælche ende carrais com to sæ mid selcuþe uolke he hafde to iueren fif hundred rideren and folc he hafde a foten muchel and vnnimete al þa scipen bi sæstronde he nom to his honde he uerde forþ in sæ uerden hine vþen and he sone bicom into brutlonde and anan bigon ræuinge uppen basian þene kinge carrais nom his sonde and sende ȝeond þisse londe bad ælcne ȝungne mon þe weorces nalde ȝeomen and æuereælcne utlaȝe þe his lond hadde biboȝen and auerælcne cnihtes sune þat his main wolde cuþen and ælcne wiþerfulne mon þe god wolde biwinnnen þat him to scolden comen for golde and gæirsume þas weoren cuþe wunder ane wide and þa wiþerwarde sumnede uerde heo comen to carrais þritti þusend fuliwis and heo uorþ iwenden bi þan sæstronde heo rupten heo ræfden noht heo ne bilæfden castles heo nomen bruttes heo sloȝen monie heo forbarnden aþele heo uerden norh heo uerden æst al þat lond heo makeden west heo ferden into scotlon þer heo scaþe worhten and aȝan to þisse londe þas leoden heo foruerden he nom ænne bisine mon and sende to brutten and þas word heom sæde þe carrais heom sende carrais þe stronge wunieþ inne comela and send her bihalues and grætet wel bruttes ȝe buþ godliche gumen and ich eow wulle griþien and freoscipe eow ȝiuen and freondscipe halden ȝif ȝe on eowre cuþþe king me wulleþ makien and andswereden for heo weoren aþele men and seiden þurh alle þing þat heo nalden swiken heore king for næuere quicne mon swiken þene king basian and þis word aȝæn com to carrais þon stronge
