carrais hine biþohte whæt he don mæhte bi twam wittre cnihten he sende to þan pohtes þa pohtes weoren on londe next basiane þan kinge to heom com þa sonde from carrais þon stronge and muchel heom bihæhte of worliche æhte þa pohtes weoren uuele he leoseden heore aþele heo sworen forþrihtes and treoþen heo plihten þat heo wolden basian inne fehte biswiken þis word com to carrais þa wes he glad ful iwis forþriht he nom his sonde and sende to þan kinge and seide him forþrihtes þat wiþ him he wolde fehte buten he him wolde rumen and bilæuen þæs riche þa seide þe king basian ær ih wulle dæd beon wiþinnen seouen nihte heo comen to þan fihte biforen þere burh eouerwic þat feht wes swiþe storlic þa heo scolden bezst fehten þa fluȝen al þa pohtes and heo basian þe king mid alle bilæfden and carrais him on þrong and mid spere him ofstong bruttes heo sloȝen and moni hundred þer nomen þa stod al þis lond a carrais aȝere hond þa nom he al þa peohtes and sende into scotte and ȝaf heom þere muchel lond inne scotlonden and heore cun wunede þære seoþþen aueremare þis word com to rome heræfter ful sone hu carrais hæfde iuaren and basian þene king ofslæȝen heo somneden twa ferden of romanisce ærden and nomen tweien eorles þe weoren swiþe aþele allec hæhte þe an wes wis and strong mon þe oþer wes icleoped þus gallus heo ferden of rome and to þisse londe comen þat heo bicomen to carrais þan kinge carrais heo ofsloȝen his cnihtes heo nomen þus þa romanisce men ræsden to leoden and allec nom to his honde muchel of þisse londe þa ȝet þer weoren monie bihælues þe castles heolden stronge burhȝes brade and longe heo lætten hiȝendliche varen seoþ into cornwalen æfter þe wes i cornwale duc he com an hiȝenge and heo hine heouen to kinge þa somneden sele þeines hehte alle þa cnihtes cumen to þan kinge and æuerælcne ohte mon biwinnen his aþelen heo buden heore uerde uppe niþinges bærde þa wes allec þe king iliþen into lunden and bruttene king sone him bæh æfter hit wes an anne hæhȝe dæie halȝeden leoden wes allec þe king in are temple in lundenne mid his romleoden þa iherde þe king mucle ludinge in lundene stureden þa leoden allec him ut leop and his wepnen he igrap and al his romleoden þa i lundene weoren and comen ut of þere burh and iseȝen heom bihæluen iseȝen heom bisiden sillic heom þuhte wha hæfde al þa monuerede þidere isende bruttes heom buȝen to mid bittere ræsen allec heo sloȝen muche folc heo nomen and sum on uæste bæh into þere burh and þe eorl into lundenne flæh lette luken þa ȝeten and himseolf læþ to walle and bruttes þa burȝen gunnen biriden and bileien þa burh wel mid þe bezsten þe king þe wes cniht swiþe god sende his sonde into scotlonde into muriane æfter monweorede and æc into west wales æfter wælbrutten and swa he lette sone uaren soþ into cornwalen hæhte ælcne mon of þan ærd þe hæfde on his chinne bærd uppe leome and vppen lif to lundene liþen inne seouen nihte isomned heo weoren heo heolden to walle mid wunderliche strengþe and gallus godliche werede bruttes a þan ende breken þa walles and iwenden binnen þa wes þa burh biwunnen and gallus gæinde to anne castle and þer binen him ræsde mid his romanisce uolke and bruttene king bæh to þæn castle and lætte to læpen alle þa brutleoden þa isæh gallus þat his help wes swiþe wac þa leonede he ouer wal and lude gon cleopien þene king þu ært swiþe kene ich wullen þe speken wiþ and ȝirne þe liues griþ þat þu mid griþe me leten uaren forþ touward rome and mid me mine leoden þe ȝet beoþ an liue and ich þe wulle swerien vppen mine sweorde þat nulle ic naueremare aȝen cumen here iherde þat þeos word him þuhte god and al him iȝette þat gallus þer ȝerde of þan castle heo ut foren and aþes heo sworen and swa heo gunnen wenden uorþ ut of londen þa com scottene king scriþen to hirede and imætte gallus and his gumen alle sone cleopede þe wes scottene king whar beo ȝe mine gumen vt of galwæiþa whar beo ȝe mine men ut of mureine whar beo ȝe mine scottes scriþeþ me biside her we sculleþ wel whreken ure wines deore and ure uulle iuan fallen to þan grunde ȝif þe king þe is cniht swiþe god haueþ heom speken wiþ and iȝefuen heom liues griþ nes ich noht þere ne nan of mine iuaren ne we hit nulleþ halden for ure freond heo habbeoþ aqualde heo leiden heom bitweonen heore speren longe and ladlichen swiþe feolen romleoden and gallus heo nomen and þat hafd him of sloȝen and wurpen hine in ænne broc þe þer heom bi stod and al þæt wal heo brohten into þan broke þer gallus i þan broke at grunde was biburied þa wes þas þeode iclansed of romleode and bruttes þan broke nome bitæhten for gallus wes islaȝen þerbi hæhte hine nemni galli and a þere ænglisce boc he is ihaten walebroc nu ich habbe þe iraht hu he hauede þene nome icaht for nu and aueremare is þe nome þere þa wes king þe wes cniht swiþe god fulle ten ȝere mid brutten heo luuede here seoþþen his ende bicom þat was uuele idon þat he sculden swa raþe uaren of þissen lifdaȝen for he wes swiþe læfful alle luueden i glouchæstre wes an eorl of aþelene moncunne þe alre hæheste iborne mon þe wunede inne bruttene wes ihaten hæhst of þan brutten he wæs of gloies cunne þe glochæstre ahte swa þat mid alle heore mihte heo comen to ane fihte eorl i þan fihte stod and sloh þene king imong þissen imonge com reouþe to þisse londe swa þat þe kæisere sende to þisse londe hider he com faren mid muchelere ferde þa he com to londe he uunde mid compe hæfde biuunnen þat he king was himseolue and cuþliche speken and freondscipe makeden iuastened mid treoþen þa seide mi broþer haueþ me al þa londes bitaht a mire honde bitwixe muntgiu and scotlonde þat ic heo scal þurhscriþen and alle þa ilke men fordon þat luuieþ þene cristindom þa wes wa þe king wæs on bruttene þat isæhtnesse mid treoþe hafde isemed heold hine stille and dude his wille elcne cristine mon at þan hefde he binom and þa wiþsaken wolde cristindom he dude his marken him on þus ferde he martrede seint alban and seint and seint and tweien ancres of kærlion næs nan biscop næs nan clærk ne cniht neore he swa sterc bute he wiþsoke cristindom þat he nes anan fordon þa þis wes al idon þa uerde forþ and bilæfde king inne bruttene þes king hæfuede enne dohter þe wes him swiþe deore and he al kinelond bitahte þan maidene an hond for næfde he nan oþer child þe mihte i þissen londe beon king þat mæide hehte elene seoþþen heo wes quene i þan londe of ierusalem leoden to blissen þis maiden wes wel itæht on bocken heo cuþe godne cræft and wunede in þisse londe mid hire fader stronge heræfter sone þat word com to rome þat hæfden iquald þene king þa weoren romleoden bliþe on heore mode for he hæfde an his daȝen muchel of heore cunne islaȝen ȝet ne com neuere to rome aȝen þa nom ænne eorl wel idon þat wes þe ræhȝeste mon þe wuneden inne rome and hæfde moni lond ilæid under his hond nas na man in his dæȝen þat dursten him derf makien þe kæisere hine sende into þissen londe into þissen ærde mid vnimete uærde hehte þe eorl æþelest alre cnihten þis iherde þat icumen wæs adræd he wes swiþe of his ahȝene liue he nom forþrihtes six wise cnihtes to heom sende and wilcumede hine to londe and he seolf him wolden specken wiþ ȝef he him wolden ȝifuen griþ and him sende æfter þat he come mid twalf cnihten tosomne heo comen togædere heo speken sone þa queþ þe kin lust me nu wel ich sugge þe þurh alle þing ich sloh þene king þe hæfde þurh his wiþerlaȝen muchel of þine cunne ofslaȝen and mid strengþe eow atholden wolde þat gauel of þissen londe and muchelne scome he eow dude þe ræþer he dæd þolede for ich wes an of þan hæhste þat swore eow hersumnesce to romen þat we sculden senden þat gauel of þissen londe þas aþþes þe king bræc þerfore he is nu dæd ah aswike wit vnker fihtes and lokien we to þan rihten and ich wullen halden to and halden þe for hærre and beon þe ful liþe and halden þe for lauerd and ælche ȝere þe senden þat gauel of brutlonde þa answerede riche mon and swiþe bald þu ært wis mon and wisdom þe folleweþ beo nu godful king and gumene þu beo lauerd and al ich þe ȝette swa hit ȝirnest and ich wulle mid monscipe þine monradene onfon for þu us dedest monscipe and god þa þu sloȝe mid muchelere wurscipe sæht heo iwurþen mid muchelere blisce heo wuneden in burȝen ah nes hit buten ane while þat þer anoþer time neoren noht feouwerti daȝen allunge iuæreden þat þe king seoc lai an comlen his hæfde swiþe oc and þe king wes wunderliche seoc seouen niht and ænne dæi þe king swiþe seoc lai hit heold hine bi þan ribben þat ne mihte he na leng libben and he cleopede him to riche his þeines þat heo him sculden ræden at swulchere neode hu he mihte dihten ælene his dohter þa heo hafden al iseid þat wes þe utemæste raþ þat heo ȝeue ælene to are quene and al his kineliche lond sette in hond and him dude swa þe king wes inne bruttene þa nes þer nan oþer rad bute iwarþ dæd and hauede ælene biwedded to quene þet wes þa wiseste wifman þa wunede a bruttene hauede his quene a child heom wes imene þa þat child wes iboren god sulf hit hauede icoren þerfore wes al bliþe þat wunede inne bruttene þa comen tosomne weorldseli men heo funden þat child nome swiþe hende heo luueden his licame and ȝeuen him his fader nome hæhte þe king and hæhte þat child þe lef wes on heorten alle brutlonden his moder elene wæs þisses londes quene þat child wæx and wel iþæh godes mildce him wes neh bruttes him weoren liþe and he hom luuede swiþe heo weoren his moder cunnesmen icomen heo wes of brutten and his fader inne rome wes iuostred al þat þet child mid æȝen isæh al hit to bæh þeo þat child wes uorþ iuæred and wes of twealf ȝere nes na man i þis ærd þat weore of heorten swa hærd þene wes wraþ ne dursten na mon speken him wiþ and þenne he wes bliþe he wes uule liþe swiþe he luuede alcne cniht þe wæs leof to deme riht and his bruttisce cun swiþe hine bihoȝeden and his romanisce cun wurþliche him radde þa þat child wes of þrittene ȝere þa iwærþ his fader vnueren þat wes þe utemesten ræd þat þe king iwærþ dæd and nome þat child and makeden heom þerof anne king and þe ȝunge king mid wisdome heold þis lond swulc he weore an æld kingen alre baldest þa wes a þen ilke time a kæisere inne rome he wes ihæten þe wurse hine luuede þat wes þe forcuþþeste mon þe quic wes on liue al rome he fordude þurh his muchele misbode alle þa heȝe men he hatede to dæþe and alle þa hæne mid harme he igrætte þer weoren monie i rome riche and wel idone þe bilæfden al þat leoden and fluȝen of þan londe for þan scamen and for þan bisemare þe heom dude þe kæisere and comen to þissen londe to þan kinge and menden to him heore sær and heore sorhsiþes and þan vnimete scome and þenne muche grome þe heom hæuede idon and idriuen of heore londe for nusten heo nenne king þe heo mihten to kennen swa heo mihten to for he wes of heore cunne ȝeorne heo hine beden þat he heom scolden ræden hu heo mihten awræken heore wansiþes vppe þe heore monscipe hæfde auælled swa longe heo ræd ȝeornden þat he heom ræd ȝette þat he wolde riden wiþ ræiȝere strengþe forþ into rome and þa riche biwinnen and wreken heom on þe his cun hæfde iscænd and þe king gode gaderede uærde vnimete folc monianes cunnes þe king gon to riden touward romleoden þat he com to rome mid ræȝere strengþe þe king wes swiþe god cniht and he ȝarkede his fiht and he ofsloh þer wes blisse inoh þa weoren romleoden bliþen on heore þeoden þa wes þe king kæisere of rome and þer wes elene þe halie quene and hire þreo æmmes þe ældeste hæhte leonin and marin þe eorles weoren wel idone heom bitæhte rome to ræden þa leden to dihten þere þeoden and þa læuedi ælene þa halie quene to ierusalem wende mid richere genge and spæc wiþ þan elde of þan iudean þe weoren balde and heo heom bihehte swiþe muche æhte þat heo hire scolden ræden to vinden þa rode þe ure lauerd alisden on þes middelærd þeo heo sohten and þere quene heo itæhten þa wes heo swa bliþe swa heo nes neuere ær on liue and heo vele ȝere þurh þan wunede þere þe while hire æem leonin wes in rome mid of þan broþeren he wes ældest of wisdome alre selest nomen þa romwisen and wimman him ȝeuen of þan hehste cunne of romanisce monnen þa wifman wes biwedded and leonin heo hæfde to his bedde he dude alse hit is wune he streonede hire on enne sone þa þat child wes iboren þa funden heo him hehne nome heo hehten hine forþriht anan þene hæȝe and þe king luuede swiþe þat child þus hit ferde þære wurs hit ferde here þa wes inne walsce londe a duc þe wes swiþe strong he hehte he wes of heȝe cunne he cleopede to brutlonde þat hit wes his icunde and al þat þe sæ bigæþ wes swiþe mah he nom muchele uærde and wenden ȝeond þissen ærde ærst he sloh þæ eorles and þrallede þæ chærles he heomelede þa reuen nalde he nænne bilefuen al þis kineliche lond nom to his hond þis word com to in rome þer he wunede in hu hauede idon his folc islaȝen and ihon særi wes þa and sorhful an heorte for he ne mihte nanes weies cumen to þissere kineriche for he hauede al romelond þe stod an his aȝere hond and his moder elene him hafde isend æfter þa nom he traher his æm and tæhte hine to rade and þis lond him bitahte biwinnen ȝef he hit mahte for himseolf ne com he naueremare herin ah he nom folc and æhte and traher bitehte mid muchelere uerde sende hine to þissen ærde and for he wes his moder æm ȝef he mihte slæn and he mihte swa wel don halde himseolf þisne dom traher forþ wende toward þissen londe mid ferde mid þan mæste he com to portchæstre þa bruttes weoren swiþe whæte and heolden fæsten heore ȝæte and traher heom fæht wiþ and þæne þridde dæi heo ȝerden griþ and traher ferde binnen and portchæstre wes biwunne and þonnene he gon wende riht to winchæstre and wes icumen biuoren into þære burhȝe togædere heo comen heo fæhten and sloȝen þat slæht ne mihte na mare beon i fihte he isæh his muchelne lure and nom him oþerne cure and ferde bi nihte to þære sæ rihte ær bruttes hit mihten iwiten his ferde wes al iscipen and forþ heo gunnen wenden i scotlonde and he al scotlond iwon to his aȝere hond and he wende ouer mid hæhȝere strengþe and in þissere bruttene burȝes he aweste þat iherde þe king wes an ærde and he mid his folke þiderward fusde togadere heo comen and fuhten ful sone nu hæfde traher swiþe muchel folc þer scottes and peohtes and romanisce cnihtes traher feht wiþ and he hine sone ouercom scottes huuen up muchelne ræm and folc nam flem and romanisce beornes sloȝen þa bruttes þa wes wa and he wende to þere sæ bi þere sæstronde þer he scipen funde into þane scipen he laþ and into norwæiȝe he draf nafde he of his fihte bute an and þritti cnihtes and alle þa oþere weoren inomen and traheres men bicumen and fiftene þusend islæȝen and idon of heore lifdaȝen þa wes in norweoȝen ærd a king þe hæhte him spæc wiþ and ȝernde mildeliche his griþ and seide him hu traher mid teone hine hauede iflæmed and ȝif þu me wult wlsten mid muchele þine ferden þat ich maȝen aȝæn cumen to mine kineriche ich þe wulle luuien and halden þe for lauerd mid sæhte and mid sibbe þa while þat ich libbe and after mine dæiȝen mine duȝeþe þe bitachen þa ænswærede þe king wes of þan ærd þu sælt in þisse ȝere beon mid me hære and deornliche sende into brutlonde mid weorden and mid writen bi monnen þe heom cunnen witen and senden þine sonden to þine bezste freonden bihæten seoluer and gold muchel æhte and lond ȝif ai mon mihte traher king tuhten to dæþe mid drenche oþer mid dweomerlace oþer mid steles bite oþer mid æie crafte biwinnen him his mahte þenne mihtes þu aȝen faren mucle þe lasse weoren þi kare þenne wlle i þe aȝan bringen and makien þe to kingen al dude lare sende his sonde into þisse londe þurh þan ilke crafte þe king him tæhte and traher wes on bruttene king swiþe bliþe næfde he of caræ næuer nane na mare þeh he nære iboren oþer i watere forloren traher wes i lundene bliþe mid his leoden fulle seouen nihte bliþe mid his cnihten þa wes i kent an eorl ihaten feond he wes þes kinges for þingen ofte he ferde to þan kinge and hernede tiþinge chæpmen bunden heore ware þa wolde þe king faren ferde him biforen mid feower hundred cnihten and leop ut of ane wude wunder wel iwepned traher king he þer fond and mid spere hine stong and his muchele uerde sette to fleonde and heom after droh and muchel folc he þer ofsloh and seþþen he uerde into kent into ane stronge castle and sende an hiȝinge after þan kinge and he anan com to þissere kineriche to kinge he wes vnderfon þa þuhte hit him wel idon heo ferde ȝeond þas þeoden and sloh þa romleoden þa hæhne and þa riche alle heo sloh iliche wharswa he mihte hine kennen ne læuede he nauer ænne and twa and twenti ȝere he wuneden seoþþen here inne griþe and inne friþe mid freondscipe of brutten þa þe he wes wel ald mon þa com him uuel on þat vuel hine heold stronge ah he þreowede longe þe king hine biþohte what he don mihte wham he mihte bitæchen al his kineriche and al his duȝeþe æfter his dæie mid carte he for to lundene and sette his hustinge eorles þer comen riche and wel idone and alle þa wise þe wuneden on bruttene þa þe king heom hauede isæid and bæd heom ræden him ræd whæm he mihte bitæche al his kineriche for nefde he nenne sune þe his land mihte halden ne child bute ane dohter þe him wes swiþe deore and hire he wolde bitachen al his kineriche and ȝefuen hire lauerd þene hæhste mon of þis ærd summe him ræden anan þat heo ȝeuen þan eorle he wes wis and riche him heo mihte bitæche oþere þer weoren þe þis nalden ihæren i cornwale wes an eorl god þe wes ihaten cradoc he stod up i þan hustinge and þus spæc wiþ þan kinge hercne me hercne me kinelauerd no here ich nenne godne ræd þe þe ȝet beo isæd ȝif þu bitachest þine kineriche þat word comeþ sone vorþ into rome for nu is ælene ierusalem quene and þe king and alle his cnihtes mid him and dæd his þe riche leonin and his broþer marin and þe ȝunge cniht i rome haldeþ muchel fiht and traher i þisse londe mid spere wes ofstungen and ælche dæi inne rome þe wel idone haldeþ swiþe muchel iwin wiþ and wiþ valantin and þe king of us ne þencheþ naþing and þus we beoþ of bruttene freonden biræued bute þu wisliche bitæche þine kineriche wulleþ romleode cumen to þissere þeode and foruaren vs mid fehte and ure freond ivallen and maken vnsæhte and binimen us ure irihten þenne þu beost forþfaren ne beon we næuere buten caren ah send into rome æfter þan wel idone he is swiþe hende gume and he wes leonines sune his fader wes ælenen æm he is of aþele cunne and ȝif him þine dohter þa þe is swiþe deore and make hine to kinge and þine dohter to quene þenne maȝe we libben mid sæhte and mid sibben and a to ure liue witen ure leoden mid winne and mid wurþscipe mid muchele wisdome þa aras and stod biuoren þan kinge he wes wunderliche wraþ for þeos speche him wes laþ he spæc aȝen cradoc alse he hine wolde fordon ah ne rohte næuere cradoc of al þat eorl spæc for al þat hustinge þe wes biuoren þan kinge biluueden cradockes ræd for heo iseȝen þat hit wes neod þa cleopede brutlondes lauerd hail seo þu caradoc herfore þu scælt habben wurhscipe muchele læn me þinne sune þe is a swiþe wis gume to uaren a mire neode into romþeode æfter þane richen and þane kene þæt he cume swiþe þe while þe ich beo on liue and ich him wulle bitæchen mine kineriche and mine dohter orien to habben to quene and ic wulle mede bitæchen ich ȝeue him norhhumberlond here mid mire aȝere hond þis ich him bitæchen of mine kineriche wiþ þan þe he me bringe þæ hende al swa þe king ȝirde hit him ȝette he ferde uorþrihtes mid þreom wise cnihtes þat he com to rome to þer wes muchel vnfriþ in al þan londe nas na griþ ah mid vnfriþe þer wes muchel win mid and mid heo duden vnimete teone muchel lond heo hæfden binomen ære þider come þe gume sone swa isæh swa he him to bæh and fæire hine igrætte mid guþfulle worden and he iradliche lædde hine to ræde and he þus spæc wunderliche feire hercne þu ært of muche cunne þu weore elene æmes sune of hæhȝe cunne þu ært icumen ær ich hider uore nis nawhit ȝære ure king i lundene heold his husting þat hustinge wes god hit wes witeneimot vnhæle and ælde hæueþ þene king vnbalded þer wes moni cniht god and þe king heom æxede ræd wham he mihte bitæchen his dohter and his riche and alle his doȝeþe æfter his dæie þreo eorles anan icure þe eorl canaan þat me sculde him brutlond bitachen al on his hond and þa fæire oriene þes kinges dohter to quene eorldom kent is ihaten and mi fader is an icorren eorl cornwalen lauerd he is ihaten caradoc he is of þine cunne and ich hatte þe mæste of his childeren þa heo hæfden anan þus icoren þa lep mi fader up swulc hit an liun weore and wiþseide þene cure biforen ure kinge þer wes swiþe muchel dune þeines þer dremden and mi fader makede lust and þus spæc while wes elene quene ælene hæfde enne æm þe æþele wes on londe he wes ihaten leonin uorþ he ferde mid traher hæhte his broþer and marin þe oþer traher i þissen londe wes islæȝen mid wornge fader hine sloh þat wes swiþe muchel woh for traher king wende þat heo weoren ifreonde lusteþ wel bruttes þe her beoþ bihælues leonin hadde ænne sune and inne rome he wuneþ he hatte of þan aþele cunne sende we to rome and haten hine cumen some and in ure hustinge hæhuen hine to kinge and þa feire oriene bithæchen him to quene þenne maȝen we libben mid sæhten and mid sibben þus spæc mi fader caradoc biforen þan folke þa andswerede þe king hit wes him swiþe iqueme and alle his beornen þe wunieþ on brutene bute wes swiþe wræþ for þe cure him wes læþ cleope nu to ræde þine rædȝiuen gode and sæie me her of andswere for nu tomarwen ich wulle faren þa wes for þisse worde swiþe fæin he cleopede his rædȝiuen and eoden to rune þe ræd wes sone iræd al swa hit bad stille iwende sone of rome i þan seouennihte mid alle his cnihten wenden þa romleoden þat he wolde to heore vnneode þat he wolden fehten aȝan valentin and for a heo weoren auared of and of his hirede ah anan heo wende toward þissen londe and swa he gon liþen into londenne fairlac he gon bringe þan kingen and þe king him forȝef his dohter to quene þa wes king hit þuhte bruttes idon wel and eorl mid wraþþen wende to scotten and monie scottes him buȝen to and ane burh bigunnen næs þa in al þan ende burh al swa hende þa þeo burh wes al imaked mid muchelere strengþe he sette hire æne nome æfter himseoluen ofte he ræd hire þurh and þurh and hehte heo cuningesburh nu and æueremare þe nome stondeþ þere ledde ferde in þan norþ ærde he hatede þat abohte moni mon þa wise men of þisse londe þe luueden þas leoden makeden hustinge bitwexen and þan kinge þer heo iwurþen sæhte and þer heo iwurþen somme and makede i þissen londe griþ god mid þan bezste and þe king him bihæhte anan to makiene riche mon swa he dude seoþþen þet abohte moni mon mid griþe he wuneden here fulle fif ȝere þa hefde gærsume vnimete for he næfde of his londe na gauel isende to rome þa þe fif ȝer weoren agan þa sæide þat he wolde ouer sæ uaren and fehten wiþ þan frenscen and ȝif he þere mihte speden toward rome he wolde riden to wreken his teone on and on valentin þe monie him hæfden idone teonen inne rome þus spæc uor him wes to murie for þis lond wes þa swiþe god and he hit hæfde al vnder fot and him ne stod æie to naþing for dæd wes þe king bæd ferde feorliche store þe king hafde kene men and vnimete gærsume forþ he gon wenden ut of þissen londen forþ he gon liþen ut þissen leoden he makede himseluen muchel clond ne isæh he nauere æft þis lond ouer sæ he wende and wel com to londe in ane londe swiþe riche þe hehte armoriche þa scipen urnen a þen lond þat folc wenden uppe strond heo bigunnen ænne castel god mid þan bæzsten heo riden ȝeond þæn leode and nomen þer muchele prude heo funden herrefeng inoh and lædden to heore ferde and æc heo nomen wummen wunder ane monie and duden þat heo wolden ȝeond ærmoriche londe þis iherde þe wes lauerd i þa lond hu þe king amerde his riche sende sonde ȝeond al þan londen þer he æine freond hæfde þe him helpen wolde and þohte þat he wælde heom driuen of his londe heo comen bi dæielihte to ane stronge fihte bruttes heom ouercomen and heo sloȝen and fiftene þusende þer weoren islaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen þa þis feht wes idon þa wende aȝen into herberȝe to resten hine seolue amarȝen þa hit dæi wes duȝeþen heom gereden heo wenden to þere heȝe burh þe nantes is ihaten ne funden heo þerinne noht of moncunne þe heom wiþ wolde stonden and þa burh heolden al hit wæs awæi ifloȝen and of þan londe iboȝen buten a lute wifmen þe weoren þer wiþinnen þa burh nom and sette mid his monnen þeo cleopede to þan eorle þu ært god cniht þu hæfuest ihalden wel mi fiht and ich þe wulle mede muchele bitæche for þu hæfdest al brutlond i þire aȝere hond ȝif ich hit nere þu weore king þere and þe eorl þe is of mine cunne ȝet hit mai ilimpe hit is þe an vnþonke ah loke wulche wætres and wunliche londes whulche wurþliche wude whulche wilde deores whulche liþe londe on to libbenne þis lond hehten armoriche þis ich þe bitæche and muchele mare herto ȝif ich hit mæi ifo herof þu scalt beon king and þas riche aȝen vt ich wullen driuen al þat ich finde on liue ȝungen and alde vt of þisse londe and wulcne swa ich mai here ifon i þan stude he beoþ fordon and sende ich wulle to þe is min aȝene stiward eorl he is treowe for æuer he is aþneowe for him ich habbe wel bitæht brutlond to witene and he me scal senden into þisse londe wapmen and wifmen of wel feole cræften cnihtes and þeines and al heore sweines sixti hundred cnihten þe gode beon to fihten ten hundred þeines seoue þusend sweines seoue þusend burhmen þe sæle beon on æhte þritti þusend wifmen þe wel beon ifunden þenne þis folc biþ hider icumen and heo stude habbeþ inumen þenne biþ al þis fæire lond iset brutten an hond æfter þine leoden bitæche heom name brutlond þat lasse nu and aueremare þe nome stondeþ þere and þus armoriche nome niþer wes auælled swa þat næueremare ne biþ he aræred þeos ȝeue afeng and iwraþ þeos kinges freond mid muchelere wurþscipe and wel heo hit heolden and þe king sende into þisse londe and hæhte þe biwuste brutlondes ærd þat he him swiþe sende þat folc of brutlonde and folc of ælche cræfte sundri scipen bitæhte and mong þan wifmonnen wepmon næuer enne buten þa seoluen scipmen þe heom scullen læden al eoden þeos ræd swa þe king hæfde iseid and þer heold to mid hæhȝere strengþe and þe king ferde uorþ toward france and biȝæt al þat kinelond and sette hit on his aȝere hond and þeonne he gon liþen into lohernne al þat lond he biȝæt swa he dude liuieine æc swa he gon liþe into lumbardie al þat lond he biȝæt þær wes caradoc dæd þa hauede his sune sorȝen inowe nes þer nan oþer ræd buten þe mavric iwærþ dæd to rome wende uppe valentin and vppen i fehte he nom þene oþer þa ȝirnde griþ þa oþer cnihtes heo weoren hende þe king heom dude i bende and he anan sone ahnede al rome þat word com to hu iuaren hafde and þat caradoc wes dæd inne lumbardie and alswa his sune for muchele sarinesse þa nom þe eorl ænne swiþe wisne mon and sende to þissen londe to þan stronge þe wes stiward swiþe bisi inne þisse bruttene to me brohten writ þat dæd wes his broþer caradoc þe mære and his sune deore þa næfde caradoc i þis ærd broþer bute and he forþriht nom an his hond al caradokes lond þa iherden þa frence men þat at rome wes and cradoc wes dæd þa nomen þa frence ænne ræd þat heo wolden flæme þene kene vt of þan londe þe him ȝæf an honde þe is bihalues france and bruttaine is ihaten and ne ȝirnde na griþ ah festliche heom feht wiþ and wel he makede his castles treowe and swiþe uæste and alle his beornen he wes leof þe comen of þissen londe for alle he hæfde þa cnihtes þe him bihehte and ec þa eorles and þa sweines and þa cheorles and alle þa burhmen þa him bihehte wifmen neuede he noht feole buten fiftene hundred for wifmen nolden noht liþen vt of þissen londe buten þe eorl þe wes þe hæhste i þis ærd walde heore borh beon þat heo scolden heore while wel biteon þa hæhuede ænne dohter swiþe deore heo hæfde al þat hæreword of þan maidenen of þis ærd þeo wimman wes on sele heo hæhte vrsele sende to þis ærd to þan eorle and bed þat he him ȝeue his dohter to quene ȝæf andswere wurþscipe habbe he þerfore monscipe habbe þat he mire dohter wel on nu todæi a seouen nihten ich heo senden him bi mine cnihten and alle þa wimmen þe him ȝef mi lauerd þider heo scullen liþen ȝif heo wulleþ libben oþer ich heom wullen alle fordon and bi þan titten anhon þa ȝarkede þisses londes lauerd his dohter þe wimman wes wel sæle he þohte heo to sende ouer sæstrames into bruttaine londe to þan stronge þa iherden þa wimmen wide ȝeond þas bruttene þat me wolde senden vrsele to þan londe hire comen to inoȝe monie and vnifoȝe þat wolden mid hire uaren to þan kinge swiþe feole heo bisohte ma þeone heo rohten þa þe dæi wes icumen þe hafde inumen þat forþ scolde uaren þat mæiden vresele þa hafden to iwiten seouen and twenti scepen alle heo weoren isunde i þere burh of lunden inne þere temese heo teuhten heore seiles wind heo hæfden wunsum weder mid þan bezsten and heo seileden forþ þat inne sæ heo comen þa vmbe stunde ne sæȝe heo noht of londe þa aras heom a wind a þere wiþer side swurken vnder sunnen sweorte weolcnen haȝel and ræin þer aræs þe hit iseh him agras vþen þer urnen tunes swulche þer burnen bordes þer breken vimmen gunnen wepen þa scipen þa urnen biuoren twelue þer weoren forloren þa oþere weoren al todriuen and forþ mid þere sæ iliþen nes þer na steoresmon þat æuere aht cuþe þeron nes næuere na mon iboren ne of nane londe icoren þat hæleþ weore swa stærc ne swa hærdiheorted þe iherde þesne weop and þisne wunderliche ræm and cleopien to þan halhȝen mid hæhȝere steuene þat his heorte neore særi for þan vnimete sorhȝen seoþþen þis world wes astald and monnen an honde isælde ne com nauere wurse hap to nane wummannen summe þe scipen wunden forþ mid þan wederen fulle fiftene i þan ane wes vrsele þe sæ wes wunder ane wod and ladliche iwraþþed and þa scipen i þere wildere sæ æuere norþ forþriht þreo dæies and þreo niht þa weoren ut of norweiȝen tweien eorles iuaren and heo weoren kene ful iwis of denemarke and of norweiȝe heo weoren iqueþen vtlaȝen and heo ferden bi sæsiden vnimete wide heo icneowen wel a þan wolcnen þas wederes custes heo droȝen to ane aitlonde þer heo leoþe hafueden wes in hungrie þer he harm worhte wes inne scise þer he scaþe makede þat he ne mihte i þan londe na lengere atstonde and of norweiȝe iflemed þer heo fiht þoleden and inne sæ heo weoren iuaren uulle seoue ȝeren and swa heo leien i þan æitlonde and iseȝen þat weder stronge iseȝen scipen an and an while ma while nan þeonne feowere þenne fiue sellic heom þuhten a þissen liue whæt weoren þa ȝemere scipen þa ȝeond þa sæ weolken þe wind gon aliþen and þat weder leoþede and isæh i þere sæ þa scipen wandrien and þus spæc þere wiþ his iuere forþ wit nu swuþe and after heom biliue mid gode fiftene scipen faren we heom æfter mid ure bezste cnihten þe gode beon to fihten and leten ælle ure oþere scipen ure herberwe biwiten for þis is sum riche king rædes bidæled þe wolde mid his folke uaren to summe londe and haueþ þeos wind and þeos weder awider him istonden þat wa is him aliue nu wende we him to biliue and ȝif hit wule þat is deore lauerd min þat we maȝen mid fihte biwinnen hine and his cnihtes and heo ne beon of ure laȝen we scullen him don of lifdæȝen and swa we scullen nimen a hond heore seoluer and heore gold and faren to ure inne and ȝeolpen for þere winne forþ heo wenden mid flode fiftene scipen gode þe strengeste þe weoren a þan dæȝen and fulled mid utlaȝen and anan oftoken fif scipen of wimmonnen afulled seolcuþ heom þuhte what hit beon mahte and heo cleopeden heom on nes þer nan ændswere for al weoren þa wimmen awald to þan deþe to heom heo droȝen and þas fif scipen nomen and furþer heo iwenden and niȝene heo iuengen and heo mid þan feowertene scipen ferden to þan londe seoþþen þis worlde wes astald nes hit neowhær itald on songe no on spelle ne miþte hit na mon telle þat weoren æi wimman swa wræcchelichen atoȝene ne swa reoliche inne sæ forradde nom vrsele þa scolden beon quene and scome hire bihedde and ladde heo to his bedde þa þe heþene mon hæfuede on hire his wille idon he ȝæf heo his hiredmonnen sone to makien to heore and summe heo heom salden for seoluer and for gold and monie and vnifoȝe heo þer ofsloȝen and summe heo heom drengte in þere sæ deope and summe heo godd wiþsoken and to haþenescipe token and þus heo weoren forradde mid reowþe þan mæste and ihurden suggen ful iwis þat þas bruttene wes of cnihte bidæled for hauede swiþe monie ilæd to armoriche and ladde to rome monie and wel idone swa wes þis kinelond of folke swiþe vnstrong and iwenden into scotten þat lond heo þurh arnden and herȝeden and barnden þa ahte heo nomen þat folc heo ofsloȝen and swa heo wenden hiderward ouer þere hermes heo worhten and hene lond makeden þis iherden bruttes and weoren þerfore særi heore sonde heo nomen sone and senden touward rome heo grætten and talden him of and of his iuere whet heo duden here and beden hine heom ræden oþer ælles heo weoren dæde wes sari for swulche tiþende and anan dude ut of bende þene hende anan swa he him to com þus he cleopede him on bicum mi mon and þu scelt seoþþen wel don and ich þe wullen senden into brutlonde ich wulle al þat kinelond bitechen þe a þire hond and þu scalt beon mi stiward swa wes þe eorl and ȝif þu wult wel don ich wulle þe makien riche mon and driuen of mire þeoden vncuþe leoden þa andswerede mid griþfulle worden al ich wulle wurchen after þine willen liþen wuderswa þu wult and halden þe for lauerd þe aþes weoren isworene and æft heo weoren forlorene þe keisere bæd swiþe muchelne here and he chæs of þan iwihte ten þusend cnihten and makede gumene ælder and swa heo gunnen wenden into þissen londe and her he fæht ful iwis wiþ and wiþ þat wes swiþe wel idon þat he heo æt compe ouercom and draf heom ouer sæstronde into yrlonde and seoþþen ferde ȝeond þis lond swa him wes alre leofuest and þe kæisere inne rome wes hæh mon and hæuede valentin wel uaste biclused in ane castle þa hefde valentin and inne rome muchel cun and iseȝen þene enne broþer idæled from þen oþer heo senden heore sonde into puille londe and heo senden to gradie þan duc of lumbardie and into alemaine to aþelen þan folke and into feole londe þæ læien þerabeoten and beden of heore ærde alle gaderen værde and to ane isette dæie sone cumen abeoten rome and wreken uppen valentin and gratien herof nuste naþing þe riche king ah he wunede inne rome mid muchele richedome vmbe lutle virste þa comen þa uerden al abeoten rome riden seouen kinges heo tobreken rome wal and eoden in oueral rome burh heo nomen and heo sloȝen and duden vt valentin and alle his iueren mid him of þan stronge castle and keiser hine makede and nomen heore sonde and senden to þisse londe and senden gratien word whæt þer wes iwurþen and gratien forþriht anan ahnede þisne kinedom þisne kinedom haueden gratien þe ær ahte and valentin of rome ahte þa riche þus riht þurh swulne ræd wes dæd and wes king her þat wes cuþ wel iwar wiþinnen ane ȝere nes þer first namare iwraþ þe king gumene forcuþest al he foruerde þis lond þa leoden him weoren laþe þa riche he foruerde þa wræcche he drof of ærde ne durste þa riche þeines nowhær him cumen toȝeines ah alle heo hine fluȝen and alle heo hine bibuȝen þa weoren in æst ængle aþele iborene cheorles twene ibroþeren itwinnes heo weoren þe oþer hehte and þe oþer heo isehȝen on feole studen hou þe king þis lond fordude þas cheorles heom biþohten whæt heo don mihten and speken heom ful stille þat þene king heo walden quellen and senden in æst ængle wide ȝeond þan londe and sumnede on ærde seouen hundred cheorles and seiden þurh alle þing þat heo walden bisechen þene king and bidden hine mildce þurh þene milde godd þat he þurh his mihte heolde heom to rihte ah and his broþer al heo þuhten oþer heo uerden swiþe warliche mid wunsumme lades and ælc bær an honde ænne saȝel stronge and bisiden heo gunnen heongen cniues swiþe longe vnder heore barme to scilden heom wiþ hærme and swa heo forþ ferden alle isunde and vmben are mile heo ræsten ane while and auerælcne hiredgume feire heo igrætten and mildeliche þurh alle þing fræineden whær weoren þe king and hiredmen heom tahten whær heo hine finden mæhten whær he wes in anne wude in ane wilderne and æfter ane bare he hine abohte ful sære þa cheorles wenden to þan wuden and warliche heom hudden alle bute tweien toward þan kinge heo weoren beien and iuunden þene king þær he wes an slæting and him to cleopeden quickere stæuene hiderward lauerd king we þe wulleþ cuþen a wunderlic þing of ane swulche bare þe her is bihalues vnder ane berhȝe þer he burh hafueþ ichosen ne iherde we næuere on liue tellen of swulche swine ȝif þu þider wult riden þer he þe abideþ þerfore wes þe king glad and þiderwærd wes swiþe ræd and þa cheorles him biuoren beien togædere þa cheorles up þreowen þene king heo icneowen and heo hine niþer setten and al hine toheowen þus gratien þe king for ut an slæting sone hit wes oueral iseid þat þe luþere king wes dæd þa weoren inne bruttene blissen inowe ah sone þeræfter sorȝen heom weoren ȝiueþen þa wes æuerælc cheorl al swa bald alse an eorl and alle þa gadelinges alse heo weoren sunen kinges þis word com to wel iwhare hu þe king wes iuaren comen sæliþende men uorþ into irlonde and funden þer ful iwis and and talden heom tiþende al of þissen londe hu hit al wes iuaren and þat cheorles næfden nane kare and hefden al þis kinelond iset a cheorlene hond þa weoren glade ful iwis and and seiden þat heo walden toward þissen londe mid muchelere uerde heo comen to þissen ærde heo hæfden of gutlonde utlaȝen stronge of neorewæi and of denemarke men swiþe starke and of yrlonde þene stronge of scottene heo hafden alle þa hæhsten and of galeweoþe gumen swiþe kene and swa heo gunnen wenden ut to norþhumberlonde ahten heo nomen folc heo þer sloȝen castles heo ararden and ahneden þa arde þa burhȝen heo nomen and al þat heo neh comen þa iseȝen bruttes þat balu wes on londe nusten heo nænne ræd heo wenden alle wurþen dæd sonden heo nomen sone and senden toward rome and beden heore are þa and aueremære ȝif heo heom wolde helpen to hæȝere neode a to heore liue heo walden heom liþe and luue to heom halden ȝif heo heom helpen wolden þis word wes isend bi write swiþe deore and þat writ wes irad imæng þan romleden þa speken sone þæ wisseste of rome bi vfelen iwurhten sculden we heom to wenden for gratien heo sloȝen his men heo forforen and neoþeles we heom scullen senden ferde of þissen ærde of þissen ænde ænne ælpi verde vt heo senden of rome cnihtes wel idone fif and twenti hundred comen into lunden and buden al þa ferde of brutlondes ærde and ferden forþ ful iwis to and and heo fehten heom wiþ and sloȝen heore uerde and heo sulf mid ærhscipe arnden to heolte and letten slæn heore folc heore vnimete uerde and heo seolf liþden forþ biuoren scotlonde and heom æfter mid his romanisce cnihten ah heo ne mihten for nane þingen iuinden and heo bigunnen feorlic ane swiþe deope dich and þerouenon oueral ænne strongne stanene wal bi þere sæstronde biside scotlonde þer weoren æuere iwuned þe vtlaȝen to londen cumen and seoþþe heo heom dihten to biwiten þa dich mid cnihten þa dic and þa wal weoren ȝare þa næfde bruttes nane kare aȝan heo gunnen wenden to þare burh of lunden and of rome hustinge bad sone þer com moni riche mon to þan hustinge anan moni cniht moni eorl moni þein moni cheorl moni riche burhmon þer wende beon bliþe anan þa sorhfulle weoren an heorten ær þe dæi weoren agan þe feire cniht lette beoden his ferde uorþriht þat heo comen to hustinge mid alle heore þringe and þa sweines at hærberwen letten heore hors wel ȝærwen and makien þa heors al swa ȝare swa heo sculden forþ faren and al þat folc duden þus swa hit hæhte and swa heo gunnen wenden to heore hustinge þa þat folc wes al icumen and ælc his stude hafde inomen þa hehte me lusten inne lundenne þa stod him up þe riche cniht and seide þus lusteþ me nu bruttes þe her beoþ bihalues ich habbe eow to suggen soþ word of rome ȝe us sende sonde into ure londe of þare sorhȝe ful iwis þe eow duden and and ich mid mire ferde com to þissen ærde and ich habbe eower iuan iualled to þan grunde and iflemed ut of ærde buten uærde nu ȝe maȝen toȝere careles wunien here of þare ilke uerde þe islaȝen is on ærde ȝe us habbeþ ofte imaked wraþ þeruore inne rome ȝe beoþ laþ for ofte ȝe us habbeþ athalden þat gauel of þissen londe and æc ȝe habbeoþ ufele idon islæȝe þene king gratien and ofte ȝe us bihateþ treoþe to halden and æuere a þan ænde ȝe wakieþ an honde we habbeþ for eower luuen ilosed ure leoden cnihtes i þissen londe an hundred þusende seoþþen cesar ærst bicom her ah swa we ibiden are nulle we no mare ah we wulleþ sone uaren into rome and bitachen eow þis kinelond and haldeþ hit on eowre hond and brukeþ hit mid wunne for nulle we naueremare aȝan comen here we habbeþ of þisse londe ihaued monie þusend punde þa we habbeþ her bisoht ah heo beoþ ful deore aboht we beoþ ofte hider ifaren mid wandreþe and mid care and nu ȝe maȝen wel don bisecheþ eow wepnen anan and werieþ eow seoluen wiþ vncuþe leoden neoren eower ælderen aþelene cæppen heonne to rome al þat lond stod on heore aȝere hond and al þat lond þat heo iseȝen sone heo hit biwunne al heo hit biwunnen mid heore ahte wæpnen ah makieþ in eowre londe castles swiþe stronge and werieþ eowre þeode wiþ vncuþe leode and wunieþ her hal and hæil and habbeþ alle godne dæie þa þeos word weoren isæid þa wes her a strong ræd næs nauere þe mon iboren inne nare burhȝe þe auere mihte tellen þurh nane spellen of þere muchele særinæsse þa isiȝen wes to folke þa weoren inne lundenne laþliche iberen þer wes wop þer wes rop and reoþen vnimete þa þeo romleoden riden toward scipene and bruttes bilafden inne þisse londe mid vnimete reoþe ne cuþe heo ræd nænne þas tiþinde ful iwis iherde and heo hefden ane verde of vnimete folke and heo gunnen wenden into norhhumberlond ȝeond þat lond heo arnden and sloȝen and barnden and swa heo forþ wenden þat heo comen to þan walle þeo þa romleoden hæfden aræred bruttes weoren wiþinnen mid swiþe feole monnen and wiþvten and ȝeorne wes abuten hu he mihte aȝeinnen þat he weoren binnen heo ræsden to þan walle ræiȝe þeines somned alle þa uerde feole cunnen ærde þa dich wes swiþe wid and deop and þa ferde toleop and bruttes weoren igærede and þene wal weoreden heo scuten in heo scuten ut scalkes þer feollen arwen fluȝen ouer wal al abuten oueral swa þicke wes heore uæræ swulc hit haȝel wæren þat for þa arewen ne mihte þa bruttes ȝemen nanes fihtes ah adun of þan walle iwenden heo alle and setten to fleme feondliche swiþe and þa oþer breken þane wal and eoden binnen oueral and after heo droȝen and swuþe heom sloȝen heo sloȝen þer muchel wunder twa and fifti hundred al of brutten seoluen wiþuten þan scotten and wiþutten þan dænscæn þa inne þere dic bilæfden þus iþæh þis kinelond a þere bruttene hond whæren bruttes cnihtes icorene ah nu heo weoren alle swiþe forlorene ne beoþ heo neuere hæȝe buten heo hælp habben of oþere moncunne for heo seolf ne cunne þus ferde ful iwis and þa bruttes of lundene to rome sende sone beden heom swiþe cumen and don alse heo ær weoren iwuned þat heo arædde þis lond and nomen hit al to heore hond for heom heo hit vþen bet þane þan vncuþen þa ȝeuen heo þus answære nulle we nauere þider faren to þolien þat swinc and þat iwin aȝæn þat heþene cun for þat is goddes wiþersake ihaten and his iuere nulle we nauere cumen þere þat is al þe ende nulle we þuder wende anoþer halue we habbeoþ mare þene we maȝen anhebben nes þer nan oþer andswere and þas sonden gunnen aȝæn faren þa heo aȝan comen þa bruttes from rome þa tiþende talden þe romleoden heom salden þa wes lundene folc mid sorȝen ibunden þa wes þer an ærchebiscop þat wes hali mon and god and mid godde swiþe hæh ihaten he sende his sonde ȝeond alle brutlonde æfter alle þan clæreken þe godes lare cuþen alle þaie ihadede gumen hiȝendliche him to comen and heo ful sone to lundene comen þus heom spæc wiþ mid us wunien godes griþ þat is on latin ful iwis þat me sæiþ vobis and heo him seiden forn to et cum tuo þa bigon he larspæl and of gode spæc swiþe wel a þan daȝen at seint wes þe ærchebiscop stol and wel feole ȝere þe ærchebiscopes weoren þere ah seoþþen þa seint com hit wes to cantuareburi idon nu seide þa wes þa heolie mon lusteþ lauerdinges of ure tiþendes þa þes haþene mon þe is ihaten and and heore uerde habbeþ ibroht wa to þissen ærde and wulleþ þesne cristindom al forfaren and fordon and ich wulle habben leue forþ ich wulle liþen and ouer sæ wenden to summe hæȝe kinge and bidde þane hæȝe king þat hæ us hælpen þurh alle þing and ȝif ich mai iuinden to speken wiþ swulche kinge þenne wulle ich wel fain cumen hidere aȝæin oþer ælles næueremare nulle ich cummen here and ȝe bidden for me on eower bare cneowen and habbeþ alle godne dæi cumen ich wulle ȝif ich mai þa wes þat folc særi and sorhful on heorte ne biden nauere brutware an heore liue swulche care forþ wende and his clærkes mid him riht forþ to þere sæ þær heom sæl þuhten scipen heo þer funden and sone in wenden and heo ful sone ouer sæ comen into bruttaine þerforen heo weoren faine þa þe king ȝæf þan eorle ah dæd wes þa swa wes þe king ah hæhte his sune þe wes of icumen brutaine þat lond he hafde al in his hond armoriche hæhte þat lond ah þene nome hit losede an hond wes þer king vnder him wes moni hæh dring to þan kinge com and he hine lette wel afon þe ærchebiscop feol to þes kinges fot and bæd hine biþenche uppen godd lauerd king ofte þe wurþe godd fæin iþenc þat þu weore sune of brutten þu ært al icumen ich æm icumen to speken þe wiþ and ȝeornnen þe liues griþ into ure londe beoþ icumen twæine hæþene gumen and muchel ufel heo doh us heo habbeoþ of ure londe al þene norþ ende and swiþe we beoþ auæred þat heo nu habben mare and ȝet heo þencheþ ufele don to fallen þæne cristindom and turne to heþenesse þa hæȝe and þa læsse for þi fader nom of brutlonde alle þa cnihtes stronge and moni þusend ladde to rome þe wel idone and nu liggeþ ofslaȝen þa heo bilæfden an ure daȝen and þus is brutlonddes ærd of folke bidæled sonde we sende to rome and beden þat heo comen and heo us habbeoþ word isend bi vre sondmonnen þat we don þat bezste þat we muȝen for nulleþ heo nauermare cumen ah hateþ us biwinnen hælp ȝif we cunnen and habbeþ iqueþen us scere nu and aueremare ah wel mæi don hu hit ga for wræcches we beoþ æuerema whilen weoren bruttes þa bezste men of londe al þat heo bigunnen al heo hit biwunnen nu heo beoþ ouercumen æiþer islaȝen and inomen and awæi ivaren mid and mid þi uader þat nis þer bileued wel neh nan þat auere beo æi tale on ah þu ært of ure cunne of us naue þu nane sunne help us nu for þu miht ælles we habbeoþ muchel pliht þus spæc þe ærchebiscop þat king hit vnderstod þe king gon siche sare him gunnen glide teores and urnen his æȝene þat his hiredmen hit iseȝen þa ȝæf þe king andswære and wiþ he spæc þus þere ich eow wulle helpen mid hæȝere strengþe ich þe wullen bitæchen twa þusend cnihtes þat scullen beon þa bezste þæ wunieþ inne brutene and minne broþer swulcne nat ich nænne oþer swa wid swa is pes dæiliht nat ich nenne betere cnihte ne nat ich a wærulderiche cniht his iliche makieþ hine lauerd ouer al brutlondes ærd þa axede þe king his deore broþer and he forþrihtes bitahte him þa cnihtes forþ ferde and þe ærchebiscop mid him and þe king himseolf walde uaren ah of frensce monnen he hæfde kare hiderward wende þe hende and al his uerde isund at totteneis heo comen a lond þeder com þe ohte mon wælla wel wes he ibon and mid him twa þusend cnihten swulche na king ne æhte forþ heo gunnen liþen into lundenne and senden æfter cnihten ȝeond þat kineriche and æuerælc oht mon þat hiȝenliche come anan þet iherde bruttes þer heo wuneden i þan puttes inne eorþen and inne stockes heo hudden heom alse brockes i wude i wilderne inne hæþe and inne uærne þat ne mihte wel neh na man nenne iuinden buten heo weoren in castle oþer y burhȝe iclused uaste þa heo iherden of þissen worde þat wes an ærde þa comen ut of munten moni þusend monnen heo leopen ut of þan wuden swulc hit deor weoren liþen toward lundenne moni hundred þusend bi straten and bi walden al hit forþ hælden and þa æhte wifmen wæpmonnes claþes duden heom on and heo forþ wenden towward þere uerde þa isæh þe eorl al þis folc cumen to him þa wes he swa bliþe swa he nes næuer ær an liue forþ heo nomen heore wæi twa niht and enne dæi þat heo comen ful iwis to and togadere heo ræsden mid ræȝe strengþe fuhten feondliche feollen þa uæie ær þe dæi weoren agan islaȝen wes and and peohtes inowe and scottes vnifohȝe densce and norenisce galewaȝes and irreisce þa while þat þe dæi wes liht ilæste auere þis slæht þa com hit to þan æuentime þa cleopeden þe æorl and bad þa wæiwitere forærnen þa wateres and snelle men toward þære sæ þet þer heom sculden sechen þe mon þe iseȝen þat gomen hu forþ gengden þa quenen ȝeond wudes and ȝend feldes ȝeond hulles and ȝeond heldes whærswa heo funden æine mon atwunden þe weore mid þan hæþene kinga þa quenen lude loȝen and al hine todroȝen and beden for þere seole þat hire neuere sæl nere þus þa bruttisce quenen moni þusend aqualden and þus heo areden þæsne kinedom of and and þe ohte ferde to selechæstre and heold his hustinge of alle his þringen alle þa bruttes buȝen to þan mote and nomen aþeling and makeden hine bruttene king muchel wes þa murþe þat wæs a mancunne and seoþþen heo him ȝefuen wif wunder ane hende iboren of þan hæsten of bruttene þan alre bezsten of þissen hæȝe wiue hæfuede inne þissere leode þreo sunen lutle hæfde þe æreste sune wel neh his fader nome hæhte þe king and hæhte þat child þa þis child wes iwaxen þat hit cuþe riden þa lette his fader hit munekien þurh luþere monnene ræde and þat child munec wes inne winchæstre after him wes iboren anoþer þe wes þe midleste broþer he wes ihaten his tonome hæhte þa wes alre last iboren a child wes wel icoren he wes ihaten vther his aþelen weore store he wes þe ȝungeste broþer ah he leouede lengere þane þa oþere þe ærchebiscop þe toward gode wes ful god he biwuste þa twa childere for luue of þan kinge ah wale þat heore fader na lengere ne moste libben for he hafde gode laȝen þa while þe he luuede ah he nes king here buten twælf ȝere and seoþþen wæs þæ king dæd hercne nu þurh wulcne ræd he hafde in his huse ænne poht hende cniht and swiþe aht he uerde mid þan kinge and mid alle his dringen nanes weies oþer bute alswa his broþer þa iwarþ he swa riche al his iferen vniliche þa þohten he to swiken þene richen he com biuoren þan kinge and feol an his cneowen and þus leh þa leodswike biuoren his lauerd lauerd king cum uorþriht and spec wiþ þinne cniht and ic þe wulle tællen of uncuþe spællen swulc þu næuere ære an ærde ne herdest þa aras þe king and eode forþ ut mid him ah wale þat hit nusten cnihtes heo eoden swa longe forþward þat heo comen in ænne orchærd þa seide þa swike þere lauerd beon wit here þe swike set adun alse he wolde holden run and he bah to þan kinge alse mon dæþ of runinge he igrap ænne cnif swiþe long and þene king þermid ofstong into þere heorte and he himseolf atsterte þer þe king dæd læi and þe swike fleh awæi þat word com to herede hu þe king iuaren hafde þa wes muchel reoþe and rumede to folke þa weoren bruttes bisie an þonke heo nusten þurh nane þinge whet heo mihten to kinge for þas kinges sunen tweien lutlen heo weoren beien neþe riden an horse and vther his broþer þa ȝæt sæc his moder and þe aldeste wes i winchæstre munecclaþes he hauede an alse an of his iueren þa comen to lundenne al þis leodisce folc to heore hustinge and to ræden heom of kinge wulche weis heo mihten don and heu heo mihten taken on and wulc an of þissen children heo mihten habben to kinge þa curen þas leoden to habben to kinge ouer heom þat iherde ȝæp mon and swiþe war imong þan eorlen he stod and fastliche hit wiþsoc and he þus sæide soþ þæh hit nære ich eow wulle ræden ræd mid þan bezsten abideþ feouwertene niht and cumen we æft her riht and ich eow wullen suggen soþþere wordes þat mid eower eȝenen ȝe scullen iseon and eowre while wel biteon þis ilke we scullen ibiden and to ure londe þa while riden and halden griþ and halden vriþ freoliche on ærde al duden þat hird swa demde and he himseolf wende alse he walde to his londe and turnde riht þene wæi þe into winchæstre lai vortiger hafde walisc lond þat haluendæl an his hond feouwerti cnihtes gode he hauede on his hirede he wende to winchæstre þer he funde and spæc wiþ þæne abbod þe þat munster biwat þer wes munec þas kinges sune of bruttene he wende into þan munestre mid mildere speche he sæide þat he wolde speken wiþ þe abbed hit him uþe and he hine ladde to spæchuse þus spæc vortiger wiþ þene munec þa þær hærcne minne ræd for nu is þi fader dæd þer is þi broþer and vther þe oþer nu habbeþ þa ælde þa aþeleste an londe icoren his tonome is ȝif heo maȝen þurh alle þing heo wulleþ makien hine king and vþer þi broþer sukeþ ȝet his moder ah ic heom habbe wiþsæid and forsake þenche for ich habben ibeon stiward of al brutlondes ærd and eorl ich æm riche mine iueren vniliche and ich habbe walsce lond haluendæl in mire hond mare ich habbe ane þane þa oþere al clæne ich æm icome to þe for monne leofuest ært tu me ȝif þu wult me swærie aþes ich wulle don of þe þas claþes ȝif þu wult æchen mi lond and þin ræd don in mire hond and makien me þinne stiward ouer al brutlondes ærd and þurh mine ræde don al þine dæde and þu wulle me an hond plihten þat ich hit scal al dihten ich þe wulle þurh alle þing makien brutlondes king þes munec sæt wel stille þa spæche him eode an wille þa andswarede þe munec mid muchelere liste wel wurþe þe vortiger þat þu ært icumen her ȝif aueremare cumeþ þæ dæi þat ich king beon mæi al mi ræd and al mi lond ich wulle don i þire hond and al þat þu wult don mine men hit scullen vnderuon and aþes ich þe swerie þat þis ich wulle uorien þus seide þe munec he murnede swiþe hu hit al weore þat he munec neore for him weoren blake claþes wunder ane laþe vortiger wes ȝæp and war þat he cuþde wel iwar he nom ane cape of his ane cnihte on þene munec he heo dude and ladde hine ut of þan stude he nom ænne swein anan and þa blake claþes dude him on and heold rune wiþ þane swæin swulc hit þe munec weore munekes eoden vpward munekes eoden dunward iseȝen bi þan weien þane swein mid munecclaþen þe hod hongede adun alse he hudde his crune wende æche oþer þat hit weore heore broþer þe þer sæt swa sære i þa spæchuse a þan dæilihte imong alle þan cnihten heo comen to heore abbede and hine gretten þurh gode lauerd we beoþ icumen biuoren þe for sellic us þencheþ whet vortiger þencheþ in ure spæchuse þer he spel haldeþ þurhut þesne dæi na munec þerin cumen ne maie buten ane and þa cnihtes al clane sære we adredeþ þat heo him misræden þa answerede þe abbed næi ac heo him radeþ god biddeþ hine halden his hod for nu is his fader dæd vortiger þer abed þe while awæi rad vortiger up aras of þan munstere vt laþ and alle his cnihtes ut wenden forþrihtes munekes þer urnen þider anan wenden to uinde þa iseȝen heo þa claþes liggen bi þan waȝes þa ælcan to oþer mænden of heore broþer þe abbed an horse leop and æfter rad and sone gon ofærne þe eorl þus seide þe abbed to vortigerne þer he rad seie me þu wode cniht whi dest þu swa muchel vnriht þu binimest us ure broþer let hine and nim þene oþer nim þat child and make of him ænne king and ne wraþ þu noht sæint ne do þu him nan vnriht þis iherde he wes ȝæp and swiþe iwar sone he aȝan com and þe abbed he nom and swor bi his honden þat he hine wolde anhongen buten he him plihte þat he wolden vorþrihtes vnhadien þas kinges sone of þis londe and for swulchere neode he sculden beon king of þissere þeode þe abbed ne durste nan oþer þar he vnhadede his broþer and þat child ȝef þan abbede an hond twenti sulhene lond and seoþþen heo liþeden forþ into lundenne vortiger þe hæȝe forbad his hiredmonnen þet heo nane manne ne tælden whæt heo hæfden vortiger i lundene læi þat com þe ilke isæte dæi þat sculden to hustinge cumen þa cnihtes of þissen to þan dæie heo comen monie and vniuoȝe heo redden heo runden ræiȝe þa beornes þat heo wolden habben and to kinge hæbben for vther wes to lutel þa ȝet he moste suken and munec wes þe ældest wes of heom and heo nalden for nane þinge munec makien to kinge þis iherde vortiger þe wes ȝæp and swuþe iwar and an uoten leop swulc hit an liun weore nusten þa bruttes na whon whæt vortiger hæfde idon he hæfde in ane bure þene deore wel ibaþþed and iscrud and seoþþen mid twælf cnihten ihud þa spæc þus vortiger he wes of ȝæpscipe war lusteþ lauerdlinges þe while þe ich speke of kinges ich wes i winchæstre þer ich wel spedde ich spæc wiþ þene abbed þat is hali mon and god and seiden him þa neode þe icumen is to þissere þeode of dæþe þerfore him is vnneþe and of þan childe þe he hæfde ihalden and ich bad hine for gode don þat child of hade and for swulchere neode king he scolde beon on þeode and þe abbed nom his ræd and dude al þat ich hine bed and here ich habbe his munekes þe gode beoþ and mære þat sculleþ witnesse beren eowe alle biuoren leo wær here is þat ilke child makien we herof enne king and her ich halde crune þa þerto bihoueþ and þat þis wule wiþsuggen he hit scal abuggen vortiger wes swiþe strong þe hæhste mon of brutlond nes þer nauer nan swa hæh þat his quides durste halsien wes i þere ilke wike þe ærchebiscop forþ iwiten nes þer nan biscop þat forþ on his wæi ne scoc na munec ne nan abbed þat he an his wæi ne rad for heo ne dursten for gode don þer þa misbode nime þane munec child and makien brutlondes king þis isæh vortiger of ufele he wes wel iwar up he gon stonden þe crune he nom an honden he setten heo vppe þat him wes on þonke nes næuere na man þat don þer mihte cristindom þat mihte blessinge don in þan kinge bute vortiger ane hit dude for alle clane þe frume wes vnhende and alswa wes þe ænde he forlette goddes had þerfore he sorȝen ibad þus wes king and vortiger wes his stiward al his kinelond sette i vortigeres hond and al he dude an londe swa himsulf wolde þa isæh of muclen vfele he wes wær þat þe king ne cuþe of londe naþing for he nefde ileorned nauer nane lare buten in his munstre þat munec scolde drigen vortiger þat isæh þe wurse him wes ful neh ofte he hine biþohte wæht he don mahte hu he mihte mid læsinge iquemen þan kinge nu þu miht iheren hu þes swiken him gon uaren weoren of brutlonde þa bezste alle dæde nu weoren þas kinges broþeren beien ful lutle and ærchebiscop þer biforen wes dæd and himsulf þisses londes king of þare laȝe ne cuþe naþing vortiger þis isah and he to þan kinge bæh mid mildere spæche his lauerd he gon greten hal seo þu brutlondes lauerd ich æm icumen þe þus næh for muchelere neode for suggen þe tiþende þe beoþ icume to londe of swiþe muchele plihte nu þe bihoueþ mihte nu þe bihoueþ wepnen to werie þine þeoden her beoþ chæpmen icumen of oþere londen alse hit is iwune heo habbeoþ ibroht to me tol for heore æhte and heo habbeoþ me itald and treowþen iplihte þat þe king of norewæiȝe neowenliche wule hider uaren and þere densemonne king þas denen wulle atsechen and þe king of rusie ræhȝest alre cnihten and þe king of gutlonde mid ferde swiþe stronge and þe king of frise þeruore me agriseþ þa tiþende beoþ stronge þe icumen beoþ to londe heruore ich æm swiþe adred for ne con ich nenne godne ræd buten we moten mid mihten senden æfter cnihten þat beon gode and stronge and þat wel cunnen a londe and setten þine castles mid kene monnen and swa þu miht þi kinelond werien wiþ vnleoden and þinne wurhscipe halden mid hæȝere strenþe for nis nan kinelond na swa brad næ swa long þat ne biþ sone inomen ȝif þær biþ to lute gumen þenne answerede þe king of londe ne cuþe he naþing vortiger þu ært stiward ouer al brutlondes ærd and þu hit scalt walden after þine willen send after cnihten þe gode beon to fihten and nim al i þire hond mine castles and mi lond and do al þine iwille and ich wulle beon stille bute þe anlæpi þing ich wulle beon icleoped king þa loh he wes of vfele swiþe iwær nes he nauere swa bliþe ær on his liue nam læue and forþ he gon liþe and swa he uorþ ferde al þat lond he sette an his aȝere hond and þe monraddene he nom æuere æwher he com and swa he nom his sonde and sende to scotlonde and hæhte þa pohtes þa alre bezste cnihtes þreo hundred him cumen to and he heom wolde wel don and þa cnihtes him to come þeræfter wel sone þus spæc þe swikefulle gume cnihtes ȝe beoþ wulcume ich habbe i mire hond al þis kinewurþe lond mid me ȝe scullen liþen for ich eow wullen luuien and ich eow wullen bringe biuoren ure kinge ȝe scullen habbe seoluer and gold þe bezste hors of þis lond claþes and fæire wif eore wille ich wulle driȝen ȝe sculleþ beon me leofue for þa bruttes me beoþ laþe lude and stille ich wulle don eore wille ȝif ȝe wulleþ in londe halden me for lauerd þa forþrihtes answarede þa cnihtes al we wulleþ don þine iwille and heo gunnen wenden to þan kinge to þan kinge com of ufele he wes wel war and seide him of his dæde hu he idon hæuede and her ich habbe peohtes þa scullen beon hiredcnihtes and alle ich habbe þine casles swiþe wel bitæht and þas uncuþe cnihtes biuoren us scullen fihten al þe king bilufde swa hoȝede ah wale þat nuste þa king of his þohte naþing ne of his swikedome þe he dude þeræfter sone þas cnihtes weoren an hirede hæhliche iwurþed fulle twa ȝere mid þan kinge heo wuneden þere and þe stiward wes heore alre lauerd a he seide þat bruttes neoren noht to nuttes ah he seide þat þa peohtes weoren gode cnihtes a weoren bruttes godes bidaled and þa peohtes walden al þat heo wolden heo hafden drænc heo hafden mete heo hafden muchel blisse æke vortiger heom salde al þat heo wolden and heom wes al swa leof swa heore aȝene lif swa þat heo al speken þer heo heore mete æten þat weoren wurþe to walden þas þeode þurhut alle þinges bæt þene swulche þreo kinges vortiger ȝef þissen gumen swiþe muchele gærsume þa ilomp hit on ane dæie þa at his inne laie he nom his tweiene cnihtes and sende æfter þan peohtes hæhten heom cumen for for alle heo sculden æten þer to him comen þa cnihtes to his inne forþrihtes he uondede heom mid worde alse heo seten at borde he lette heom bringen schenches of feole cunne drenches heo drunken heo dremden dæi þer forþ eode þa heo weore swa drunken þat wakeden heore sconken þa spæc þat he hæfde iþoht ær hercneþ nu me cnihtes ich wulle suggen eow uorþrihtes of mire muchele sorȝen þat ich fore habbe imurned þe king me bitahte þis ard for to beon his stiward ȝe beoþ me on liue alre monnen leofest ah nabbe ich æhten to ȝiue mine cnihten for þes king æh al þis lond and he is ȝung and þæh strong and al ic him mot ȝelden þat ich nime of his londe and ȝif ich his forleose ich sal laȝe þolien and mine ahten ich habbe ispend for ich eo wulle iquemen and nu ich mot heonene uaren feor to summe kinge heren him mid sæhte and biwinnen mid him ahte ne mæi i noht for muchele scome habben here þesne wone ah forþ ich mot liþen to uncuþe leoden and ȝif auere cumeþ þe dæi þat ich æhten biȝiten mæi and ich maȝen swa wel iþeon þat ȝe cumen a londe þer ich beon ich eow wulle wel biwiten mid muchelere wurþscipe and habbeoþ alle godne dæi toniht ich wulle faren awæi hit biþ a muchele wæne whær ȝe iseon me aueremare nusten noht þas cnihtes wæt þe swike þohte vortiger wes fæc for her he his lauerd biswæc and þe cnihtes heolden hit for soh þat þe swike sæide hæhte his sweines sadeli his blonken and nemnede twælf scalkes to laden mid himseoluen to horsen heo eoden swulc heo wolden of þeoden þat iseoȝen þa peohtes þa fordrunkene cnihtes hu vortiger wolde uaren heruore heo hæfden muchelne kare heo eoden to ræden heo eoden to rune alle heo menden heore lif for vortiger heom wes swa leof and þus seiden þa peohtes þa drunkene cnihtes whæt maȝe we nu to rade whæ scal us nu ræden wha scal us feden wha scal us scruden wha scal an hirede beon ure lauerd nu vortiger is iuaren alle we mote fusen nulle we for nane þinge munec habbe to kinge ah wulle we wel don forþriht faren we him to diȝelliche and stille and don al ure iwille into his bure and drincken of his beore þenne we habbeþ idrunken dreme we lude and summe sculleþ to þere dure mid sweorden stonden þer biuoren and summe forþrihtes nimen þene king and his cnihtes and slæn of þa hafden and we seolf hired haben and leten sone ofærnen uræ lauerd and seoþþen þurh alle þinge hæbben hine to kinge þenne mah we libben swa us biþ alre leofuest wenden þa cnihtes to þan kinge forþrihtes eoden heo alle þurhut þære halle into þas kinges bure þer he sæt bi fure nes þer nan þat word spæc bute gille callæt þus he wiþ þæne kinge spæc swiken he þohte þet lust me nu leodkinge nulle ich þe liȝen naþing we habbeoþ ibeon an hirede hæhliche iwurþed þurh þinne stiwærd þe haueþ iwiten al þis ærd he us haueþ wel iued he us haueþ wel iscrud and to soþe ich sugge þe mai mid him we æten nu todæi ah sare us ofþuncheþ nefden we noht to drinken and nu we beoþ in þine bure ȝef us drinken of þine beore þa ȝæf þe king answare þat scal beon eowre laste kare for ȝe sculleþ habben to drinken þa while þe eow god þunche me heom brohte drinken and heo gunnen dremen þus sæide gille calæt to þere dure he wes ful wæt whær beo ȝe cnihtes sturieþ eow forþrihtes and heo þene king igripen and his hæfde of smiten and alle his cnihtes heo sloȝen forþrihtes and nomen ænne sondesmon and senden toward lunden þat he swiþe sculde ærne æfter þat he swiþe comen and þene kinedom nome for þat wuste he þurh alle þing islæȝen wes þe king þet iharde þe swike wes ful derne þus he hæhte þene sondesmon aȝan forþriht anan and hat heom wel biwiten al ure wurþscipen þat nauer anne wende ut of þan ænde ah alle me abiden a þat ich cume riden and swa ich wulle dele þis lond us alle imæne forþ wende þe sondesmon and vortiger nom anan and sende ȝeond lunden and to hustinge hehte heom ræþen and ful sone þat heo alle comen icumen weoren þa burmen þe swiþe balde weoren þa spæc vortigerne þe swike wes ful deorne swiþe he gon to wepnen and særiliche siken ah hit wes an hafde and noht an his heorte þa axeden hine þa burhmen þe swiþe balde weoren lauerd vortigerne whæht is þat þu murnest nert þu na wimman swa sære to wepen þa answarede vortigerne þe wes swike ful deorne ich eow wulle telle for reoliche spelle of muche særnesse þe isiȝen is to londe ich habbe i þis ærd ibeon eower kinges stiwærd and ispæken him wiþ and iluued hine swa mi lif ah nalde he at þan ende nænne ræd luuien he luuede þa peohtes þa vncuþe cnihtes and us nalde he god don ne neower feire vnderfon ah heom he wes liþe a to heore liue ne mihte ic of þan kinge habben scipinge ich spende mine ahte þa wile þa heo ilaste and seoþþen ich nam leue to mine londe liþe and þenne ich hæfde mine gauel cumen aȝan to hirede þa isæhȝen þa peohtes þat þe king nefde nane cnihtes neo nauere nænne cunesmon þe heo wolden oht fore don heo nomen heore uore into þas kinges bure ich suggen eow þurh alle þing islæȝen heo habbeoþ þæne king and þencheþ þisne kinedom and us alle fordon and wulleþ forþrihte makien king of ane peohte ah ich wes his stiward wræken ich wulle minne lauerd and æueræche oht mon hælpen me þat to don on ich wulle mid mine gæren and forþriht ich wulle uaren wenden ut of lunden cnihtes þritti hundred heo riden and heo arnden forþ mid vortigerne þat heo nehlæhten þer weoren þa peohtes and he nom enne of his cnihtes and sende to þan peohten and seide heom þat he com ȝif heo hine wolden vnderuon þa peohtes weoren bliþe for heore fæisiþe and heo nomen heore gode gæren nes þer neowþer sceld ne spære vortiger forþrihtes wepnede alle his cnihtes and comen þa peohtes and bruhten hæued þas kinges þa vortiger þis hæued isæh þa hælde he to grunde ful neh swulc he hafuede modkare mest of alre monne mid his lechen he gon liȝen his heorte wes ful bliþe þa seide vortigerne þe swike wes ful deorne auerælc oht mon mid sweorde leggeþ heom on and wrækeþ wel an ærde þe seorȝe of ure lauerd nænne heo ne nomen ah alle heo heom sloȝen and to þan inne wende into winchæstre and sloȝen heore sweines and heore burhþeines heore cokes and heore cnaues alle heo duden of lifdæȝen þus ferden þa tiþinde of þan kinge and þa weorldewis mon þa oþere childre biwusten for heo hafden care of vortiger heo nomen and vþer and ladden heom ouer sæ into þere lasse brutene and fæire heom bitahten budiz þan kinge and he heom feire vnderfeng he wes heore cun and heore freond and mid muchelere liste þa childere he biwuste and swa wel fele ȝere mid him heo weoren þere vortiger a þissen londe wes ihoue to kinge alle þa bruttes stronge stoden an his honde fif and twenti ȝeren he wes king here he wes wod he wes wild he wes ræh he wes bald of alle þinge he hæfde his iwille bute þa peohtes neoren næuere stille ah eouere heo wenden ȝeond þene norh enden and henden þis kinelond mid hærmen vnimete and wreken heore cun inoh þat vortiger here ofsloh vnder þan comen tiþende into þissen londe þat wes cniht þe wes ihæten and alswa wes vther god cniht and swiþe iwar and wolden comen to þissen londe and leden here swiþe stronge þis wes feole siþe iqueþe ofte iquidded ofte comen tiþinde to vortiger þan kinge þerfore him ofte scomede and his heorte gromede for men hit sæiden wel iwhær nu cumeþ and vther and wulleþ wræken þene king of þis lond nis þer cost nan oþer wærken heo wulleþ heore broþer and slæn vortigerne and to duste hine forberne þus heo wulleþ al þis lond setten an heore aȝere hond swa quiddeden ælche dæi al þat verden æfter wæi hine biþohte whæt he don mihte and þohte sende sonde into oþere londe æfter vncuþe cnihten þa hine biwiten mihten and þohte to beon wær wiþ and wiþ vther vnder þan comen tiþende to vortiger þan kinge þat ouer sæ weoren icumen swiþe selcuþe gumen inne þere temese to londe heo weoren icummen þreo scipen gode comen mid þan flode þreo hundred cnihten alse hit weoren kinges wiþuten þan scipenmonnen þe weoren þer wiþinnen þis weoren þa færeste men þat auere her comen ah heo weore hæþene þat wes hærm þa mare heom sende to and axede hu heo weoren idon ȝif heo griþ sohten and of his freondscipe rohten heo wisliche andswerden swa heo wel cuþen and seiden þat heo walden speken wiþ þan kinge and leofliche him heren and hælden hine for hærre and swa heo gunnen wenden forþ to þan kinge þa wes þa king in cantuarieburi þer he mid his hirede hæhliche spilede þer þas cnihtes comen biforen þan folckinge sone swa heo hine imetten fæire heo hine igrætten and seiden þat heo him wolden hæren i þisse londe ȝif he heom wolde mid rihten athalden þa andswerede vortiger of elchen vuele he wes war an alle mine iliue þe ich iluued habbe bi dæie no bi nihtes ne sæh ich nauere ær swulche cnihtes for eouwer cumen ich æm bliþe and mid me ȝe scullen bilæfuen and eouwer wille ich wulle driȝen bi mine quicke liuen ah of eou ich wulle iwiten þurh soþen eouwer wurþscipen whæt cnihten ȝe seon and whænnenen ȝe icumen beon and whar ȝe wullen beon treowe alde and æc neowe þa answerede þe oþer þat wes þe aldeste broþer lust me nu lauerd king and ich þe wullen cuþen what cnihtes we beoþ and whanene we icumen seoþ ich hatte henges hors is mi broþer we beoþ of alemainne aþelest alre londe of þat ilken ænde þe angles is ihaten beoþ in ure londe selcuþe tiþende vmbe fiftene ȝer þat folc his isomned al ure iledene folc and heore loten werpeþ vppen þan þe hit faleþ he scal uaren of londe bilæuen scullen þa fiue þa sexte scal forþ liþe ut of þan leode to uncuþe londe ne beo he na swa leof mon uorþ he scal liþen for þer is folc swiþe muchel mære þene heo walden þa wif fareþ mid childe swa þe deor wilde æueralche ȝere heo bereþ child þere þat beoþ an us feole þat we færen scolden ne mihte we bilæue for liue ne for dæþe ne for nauer nane þinge for þan folckinge þus we uerden þere and for þi beoþ nu here to sechen vnder lufte lond and godne lauerd nu þu hæfuest iherd lauerd king soþ of us þurh alle þing þa answærede vortiger of alc an vfele he wes war ich ileue þe cniht þat þu me sugge soþriht and wulche beoþ æoure ileuen þat ȝe on ileueþ and eoure leofue godd þe ȝe to luteþ þa andswarede hænges cnihtene alre fæirest nis in al þis kinelond cniht swa muchel ne swa strong we habbeþ godes gode þe we luuieþ an ure mode þa we habbeþ hope to and heoreþ heom mid mihte þe an hæhte phebus þe oþer þe þridde hæhte woden þat is an weoli godd þe feorþe hæhte iupiter of alle þinge he is whar þe fifte hæhte þat is þe hæhste ouer us þæ sæxte hæhte þat is a godd wel idon þe seoueþe hatte an hæh godd in ure lond ȝet we habbeþ anne læuedi þe hæh is and mæhti heh heo is and hali hiredmen heo luuieþ for þi heo is ihate frææ wel heo heom dihteþ ah for alle ure goden deore þa we scullen hæren woden hehde þa hæhste laȝe an ure ælderne dæȝen he heom wes leof æfne alswa heore lif he wes heore walden and heom wurþscipe duden þene feorþe dæi i þere wike heo ȝifuen him to wurþscipe þa þunre heo ȝiuen þunresdæi for þi þat heo heom helpen mæi freon heore læfdi heo ȝiuen hire fridæi heo ȝiuen sætterdæi þene sunne heo ȝiuen sonedæi monen heo ȝifuen monedæi tidea heo ȝeuen tisdæi þus seide hængest cnihten alre hendest þa answerede vortiger of ælchen vfel he wæs wær cnihtes ȝe beoþ me leofue ah þas tiþende me beoþ laþe eouwer ileuen beoþ vnwraste ȝe ne ileoueþ noht an ah ȝe ileoueþ a þene wurse þe godd seolf awariede eoure godes ne beoþ nohtes in helle heo niþer liggeþ ah neoþeles ich wulle eou athælde an mine anwalde for norþ beoþ þa peohtes swiþe ohte cnihtes þe ofte ledeþ in mine londe ferde swiþe stronge and ofte doþ me muchele scome and þerfore ich habbe grome and ȝif ȝe me wulleþ wræken and heore hæfden me biȝeten ich eou wullen ȝeuen lond muchel seoluer and gold þa andswerede hængest cnihtene alre feirest ȝif hit wulle al hit scal iwurþe þus and woden ure lauerd þe we on biliueþ hengest nom læue and to scipen gon liþe þer wes moni cniht strong heo droȝen heore scipen uppe þe lond forþ wenden dringches to vortigerne þan kenge biuoren wende hengest and hors him alre hændest seoþþen þa alemainisce men þa aþele weoren an deden and seoþþen heo senden him to heore sæxisce cnihtes wel idon hengestes cunnesmen of his aldene cuþþen heo comen into halle hændeliche alle bett weoren iscrudde and bed weoren iuædde hængest swaine þene vortigernes þeines þa wes vortigernes hired for hehne ihalden bruttes weoren særi for swulchere isihþe nes hit nawiht longe þat ne comen to þan kinge cnihtes sunen uiue þa ifaren hafden biliue heo sæiden to þan kinge neowe tiþenden nu forþrihtes icumen þa peohtes þurh þi lond heo ærneþ and hærȝieþ and berneþ and al þene norþ ænde iuæld to þan grunde herof þu most ræden oþer alle we beoþ dæden þe king hine biþohte whæt he don mihte he sende to þan innen after al his monnen þer com hengest þer com hors þer com moni mon ful oht þer comen þa saxisce men hengestes cunnesmen and þa alemainisce cnihtes þe beoþ gode to fihte þis isæh þe king vortiger bliþe wes he þa þer þa peohtes duden heore iwune a þas hælf þere heo weoren icume and þe king vortiger of heore cume wes ful war togadere heo comen and feole þer ofsloȝen þer wes feht swiþe strong comp swiþe sturne þe peohtes weoren ofte iwuned vortigene to ouercumen and þa heo þohten alswa ah hit ilomp anoþer þa for hit wes heom al hele þat hængest wes þere and þa cnihtes stronge þe comen of saxelonde and þa ohte alemanisce þe þider comen mid horse swiþe monie peohtes heo sloȝen i þan fehte feondliche heo fuhten feollen þa fæie þa þe non wes icumen þa weoren peohtes ouercumen and swuþe heo awæi floȝen an ælche helue heo forþ fluȝen and alle dai heo fluȝen monie and vnnifoȝe þe king vortigerne wende to herberwe and æuere him weoren on uast hors and hængest hængest wes þan kinge leof and him lindesaȝe ȝef and he ȝæf horse madmes inoȝe and alle heore cnihtes he swiþe wel dihte and hit gode stunde stod a þan ilke ne durste nauere peohtes cumen i þan londes no ræueres no utlaȝen þat heo neoren sone ofslæȝen and hængest swiþe fæire herede þane king þa ilomp hit in ane time þat þe king wes swiþe bliþe an ane hæȝe dæie imong his duȝeþe monnen hengest hine biþohte what he don mihte for he wolde wiþ þan kinge holden runinge þan kinge he eode toforen and fæire hine gon greten þe king sone up stod and sætte hine bi himseoluen heo drunken heo dremden blisse wes among heom þa queþ hengest to þan kinge lauerd hærcne tiþende and ich þe wulle ræcchen deorne runen ȝif þu mine lare wel wult lusten and noht halden to wraþþe þat ich wel leare þe king answarede swa henges hit wolde þa sæide hængest cnihten alre fæirest lauerd ich habbe moni a dæi þine monscipe ihæȝed and þin holde mon ibeon i richen þine hirede and in ælche fæhte hæhst of þine cnihten and ich habbe ofte ihærd hohfulle ronen imong þine hiredmonnen heo hatieþ þe swiþe into þan bare dæþe ȝif heo hit dursten cuþe ofte heo stilleliche spækeþ and spilieþ mid runen of twam ȝunge monnen þat feor wunieþ hennen þe an hæhte vther þe oþer þe þridde hæhte þe wes king i þisse lond and he her wes ofslaȝen þurh swicfulle laȝen nu wulleþ cume þa oþere and wræken heore broþer al forbærnen þi lond and slæn þine leoden þe seoluen and þine duȝeþen driuen ut of londe and þus suggeþ þine men þer heo somned sitteþ for þa twene broþere beoþ beyne kineborne of kunne þas aþele bruttes and þus þine duȝeþe stille þe fordemeþ ah ich þe wulle ræde of muchele þire neode þat þu biȝite cnihtes þa gode beoþ to fihte and bitache me ænne castel oþer ane kineliche burh þat ich mai inne ligge þa while þa ich libbe ic am uor þe iuaid þærfore ic wene beon dæd fare þer ic auer fare næm ich næuere bute care buten ich ligge faste biclused inne castle ȝif þu þis me wult don ich hit wulle mid luue afon and ich wulle biliue senden after mine wiue þat is a sexisc wimmon of wisdome wel idon and after rouwenne mire dohter þe me is swiþe deore þenne ich habbe mi wif and mine winemaies and ich beo i þine londe fulliche atstonde þa bet ich wullen hiren þe ȝif þu þis ȝettest me þa answarede vortiger of ælchen vuele he wes war nim cnihtes biliue and send æfter þine wiue and æfter þine children þan ȝungen and þan olden and æfter þine cunnen and afeoh heom mid wunne þenne heo to þe cumeþ þu scalt habben gærsume hæhliche heom to ueden and wurþliche scruden ah nulle ich castel na burh nane þe bitechen for men me wolden scenden i mine kinelonde for ȝe haldeþ þa hæþene laȝe þat stod on eoure ælderen dæȝe and we haldeþ laȝe and wulleþ auere an ure dæȝe þa ȝet spæc hængest cnihten alre hendest lauerd ich wulle þin iwil driȝen her and oueral and don al mine dæde æfter þine ræde nu ic wulle biliue sende after mine wiue and æfter mire dohter þe me is swa deore and æfter ohte monnen þa bezste of mine cunne and þu ȝif me swa muchel lond to stonden a mire aȝere hond swa wule anes bule hude ælches weies ouerspræden feor from ælche castle amidden ane ualde þenne ne mai þe atwite þe hæne ne þe riche þat þu æi hæhne burhȝe hæþene monne habbe bitæht þe king him iȝette swa hengest ȝirnde hengest nom læue and forþ he gon liþe and æfter his wiue sende sonde to his aȝene londe and he seolf wende ȝeond þis lond to sechen ænne brædne fæld þer he mihte wel spræde on his feire hude he com æn enne ende in enne fæire uelde he hafde ane hude biȝite to his neode of ane wilde bule þe wes wunder ane strong he hæfden ænne wisne mon þe wel cuþe a craften þe nom þas hude and a bord leide and whætte his sæxes alse he schæren wolde of þere hude he kærf enne þwong swiþe smal and swiþe long nes þe þwong noht swiþe bræd buten swulc a twines þræd þa al islit wes þe þong he wes wunder ane long abuten he bilæde muche del of londe he bigon to deluen dic swiþe muchele þeruppe stenene wal þe wes strong oueral ane burh he arerde muchele and mare þa þe burh wes al ȝare þa scop he hire nome he hæhte heo ful iwis kaer carrai an bruttisc and ænglisce cnihtes heo cleopeden þwongchastre nu and aueremare þe nome stondeþ þere and for nan oþere gome næueden þæ burh þene nome a þet come densce men and driuen ut þa bruttes þene þridde nome heo þer sætte and lanecastel hine hæhten and for swulche gomen þæ tun hafde þas þreo nomen vnder þan com liþen hider hengestes wif mid hire scipen heo hæfde to iueren fiftene hundred ridern mid hire
