comen to iwiten muchele æhtene scipen þer comen inne muchel of hengestes cunne and rouwen his dohter þe him wes swiþe deore hit wes umbe while þat com þe ilke time þat iȝarked wes þa burh mid þan alre bezste hengest com to þan kinge and bad him gistninge and seide þat he hafde an in iȝarked toȝeines him and bad þat he come þerto and he scolde beon fæire underfon and þe king him ȝette swa hengest hit wolde hit com to þan time þat þe king gon forþ liþe mid þan deoreste monnen of alle his duȝeþe forþ he gon buȝen þat he to burh com he biheold þene wal up and dun oueral al him wel likede þat he on lokede he wende into halle and his heleþes mid him alle bemen heo bleowen gomen men gunnen cleopien bord heo hetten breden cnihtes setten þerto heo æten heo drunken dræm wes i burhȝen þa þe duȝeþe hafde iȝeten þa wes heom þa bet iloten hængest eode into þan inne þer wunede rouwenne he heo lette scruden mid vnimete prude al þat scrud þe heo hafde on heo weoren swiþe wel ibon heo weoren mid þan bezste ibrusted mid golde heo bar an hire honde ane guldene bolle iuulled mid wine þe wes wunder ane god hæȝe iborenne men heo lædden to hallen biuoren þan kinge fairest alre þinge reowen sæt a cneowe and cleopede to þan kinge and þus ærest sæide in ænglene londe lauerd king wæs hæil for þine kime ich æm uæin þe king þis ihærde and nuste what heo seide þe king vortigerne fræinede his cnihtes sone what weoren þat speche þe þat maide spilede þa andswarede a cniht swiþe sellic he wes þe bezste latimer þat ær com her lust me nu lauerd king and ich þe wulle cuþen whæt seiþ rouwenne fæirest wimmonnen hit beoþ tiþende inne sæxelonde whærswa æi duȝeþe gladieþ of drenche þat freond sæiþe to freonde mid fæire loten hende leofue freond wæs hail þe oþer sæiþ drinc hail þe ilke þat halt þene nap he hine drinkeþ up oþer uuel me þider fareþ and bithecheþ his iueren þenne þat uul beoþ icumen þenne cusseoþ heo þreoien þis beoþ sele laȝen inne saxelonde and inne alemaine heo beoþ ihalden aþele þis iherde of alchen uuele he wes war and seide hit an bruttisc ne cuþe he nan ænglisc maiden rouwenne drinc bluþeliche þenne þat maide dronc up þat win and lette don oþer þerin and bitæhten þan kinge and þrien hine custe and þurh þa ilke leoden þa laȝen comen to þissen londe wæshail and drinchæil moni mon þerof is fain rouwenne þe hende sat bi þan kinge þe king heo ȝeorne biheold heo was him an heorte leof ofte he heo custe ofte he heo clupte al his mod and his main hælde to þan mæidene þe wurse wes þer ful neh þe in ælche gomene is ful ræh þe wurse ne dude næuere god he mæingde þas kinges mod he murnede ful swiþe to habben þat mæidene to wiue þat wes swiþe ladlic þing þat þe cristine king luuede þat haþene maide leoden to hærme þat maiden wes þan kinge leof æfne alse his aȝene lif he bad hengest his dring ȝiuen him þat maidechild hengest funde an his ræd to don þat þe king him bed he ȝef him rouwenne wimmon swiþe hende þan kinge hit was icweme he imakede heo to quene al after þan laȝen þe stoden an hæþene dæȝen nes þer nan cristindom þer þe king þat maide nom ne preost ne na biscop ne nauere ihandled godes boc ah an heþene wune he heo wedde and brohte heo to his bedde maiden he heo hæfde and mærȝeue hire bitahte þa he hine an hire hafde iscend he hire ȝef londen and kent þe king hafde þreo sunen þe weoren swiþe hende gumen þe ældeste hehte vortimer and garengan wes an eorl þe kent ohte longe and his fader biuoren him and seoþþen he þurh his cun þa he bezst wende to halden his lond þa hafde hengest hit an his hond sellic þuhte þan cnihte whæt þe king þohte þe king luuede þa hæþene and henede þa cristine þe hæþene hæfden al þis lond to walden under heore hond and þes kinges þreo sunen ofte þoleden sorȝen and kare heore moder wes þa dæd þeruore heo hafden þe lasse ræd here moder wes swiþe god wif and ladde swiþe cristin lif and heore steopmoder hæþene hengestes dohter nes hit noht longe buten ane stunde þat þe king makede ueorme swiþe store þe hæþene he laþede þarto he wende swiþe wel to don þider comen þæines cnihtes and sweines and alle þe cuþe a boken þa feorme forsoken for þa hæþene weoren hæhst an hireden and þæt cristine hired for hæne wes ihalden þa hæþene weoren bliþe for þe king heom luueden swiþe hengest hine biþohte what he don mahte he com to þan kinge mid are hailinge and dronc to þan kinge þa spæc þus hængest cnihtene alre hændest þat of hæþene laȝen leouede a þan dæȝen hærcne me lauerd king þu ært me leof þurh alle þing þu hæuest mine dohter þæ me is swiþe deore and ich æm þe an folke swa ich þi fader weore hærcne mine lare heo sculleþ þe wurþen leofue for ich wulle hæhliche to helpen þe ræden þin hired þe hateþ for me and ich æm iuæid for þe and þe hatieþ kinges eorles and þringes heo uareþ in þine londe mid hære swiþe stronge ȝif þu wult þe awraken mid wurþscipe muchen and don þine vniwinen wa send after mine sune and æfter enne oþer ebissa his wedbroþer þis beoþ þa hæhste men þe æuere hired lædden and i þan norþ ende ȝif heom of þine londe heo beoþ of muchele mæhte and stronge i fæhte heo wulleþ biwiten þi lond wel mid þan bezsten þenne mihte þu mid winne þi lif al uorwerien mid haueken and mid hunden hiredplæie luuien ne þræt þu nauere habben kare of uncuþe leoden þa answarede vortiger of ælchen uuele he wes war send þine sonde into sexlonde after þine sune and after þine freonden ma do him wel to iwiten þat he sende his writen æfter al þan cnihten þe gode beoþ to fihten ȝeond alle sæxþeoden þat heo cumen to mire neoden and þeh he bringen ten þusend gumen alle heo beoþ me wel icumen þis ihærde hengest cnihten alre henddest þa wes he swa bliþe swa he nes næuere an his liue hengest sende his sonde into saxlonde hehte cumen and his wedbroþer ebissa and al of heore cunne þat heo mihten iwinnen and alle þa cnihtes þæ heo biȝiten mihten sende sonde ȝeond þreom kinelonde and bad ælchene ohte gume hiȝenliche him to cume þe wolden biȝiten lond oþer seoluer oþer gold heo comen to hirede alse haȝel þe ualleþ þat was to iwitene mid þreo hundred scipene forþ wenden mid þritti þusend and æc ma ohte men and kene and ebissa his iuere æfter com liþen mid unimete leoden and he ladde to iwiten oþer half hundred scipen þeræfter comen liþe fiue and fife bi sixe bi seoue bi tene and bi ælleuene and þus heo comen liþen toward þissen londe hæþene hæregumen to hirede þis kinges þat þis lond wes swa vul of uncuþe leoden þat nes nan swa wis mon no swa ȝerwitele þat mihte todæle þa cristine and þa hæþene for þa hæþene weoren swa riue and auere heo comen biliue þa iseȝen bruttes þat balu wes an londe þeruore heo weoren særi and an heorte druri and ferden to þan kinge þe hæhste of þissen londe and þus him to sæiden mid sorhfule steuene lust us nu lauerd king of ure leodrunen þu ært þurh us bald king inne þissen brutene and þu hafuest þe biwunnen hærm and muchele sunnen ibroht heþene folc ȝet hit þe ihærmeþ and þu letest godes laȝen uor uncuþe leoden and nult ne ihæren ure drihten for þissen hæþene cnihten and we þe wulleþ bidden for alle godes sibben þat þu heom bilæuen and of þine londe driuen ȝif þu ælles ne maht we wulleþ makien muchel fæht and driuen heom of londe oþer heom adun fallen oþer we usseoluen ofslaȝen wulleþ liggen and leten haþene uolc hælden þas riche bruken hit mid winne ȝif heo hit maȝen iwinnen and ȝif heo alle beoþ hæþene and þu ane cristine nulleþ heo nauere longe habben þe to kinge buten þu a þine daȝen afo hæþene laȝen and bilæue þe hæhȝe godd and luuie heore þenne scalt þu forwurþen a þissere woruldriche and þi wracche saule siȝen to helle þenne hauest þu aboht þe luue of þire brude þa answærede vortiger of ælc an uuele he wes wær nulle ich heom bilæuen bi mine quike liue for hengest is hider icumen he is mi fader and ich his sune and ich habbe to leofmonne his dohter rouwenne and ich heo habbe biwedded and ihaued a mine bedde and seoþþen ich sende after and after his iueren ma hu mihte ich for scome scunien heom swa sone driuen of londe mine wines deore þa andswarede bruttes mid sorȝen ibunden nulle we naueremare þine iboden here ne to þine hirede cumen ne þe uor king halden ah hatien we wulleþ mid hæhȝere strengþe alle þine hæþene wines and hærme igreten bidden us to fultume þat is godes sune forþ iwenden eorles forþ iwenden beornes forþ iwenden biscopes and þa bocilæred men forþ iwenden þæines forþ iwenden sweines alle brutleoden þat heo comen to lundene þer wes moni hæh at þan hustinge and þeos kinges þreo sunes alle heo weoren þider icumen þer wes and and swiþe monie oþere þat comen mid þan broþere al þat folc þider com þat luueden þene cristtendom alle þa riche nomen heom to ræde and nomen þes kinges ældeste sune þe to þan hustinge wes icumen and mid muchele loftsonge heuen hine to kinge þa wes vortimer cristine king þer and his fader fulede þan hæþenen vortimer þe ȝunge king wes swiþe kene þurh alle þing he sende hengest word and horse his broþer buten heo hiȝenliche uerden of þis riche he heom walde ufel don baþe ablenden and anhon and his aȝene fader he foruaren walde and alle þa hæþene mid hæȝere strengþe þa andswærede hengest cnihtene alre hendest her we wulleþ wunien wintres and sumeres riden and ærnen mid þan kinge vortigerne and alle þa mid vortimere uareþ heo sculleþ habben sorȝen and kare þat iherde vortimer he wes wis and swiþe iwar and lette beoden uerde ȝeond allen þissen ærde þat al þat cristine folc come to hirede vortimer þe ȝunge king i lundene heold his husting þe king hehte ælne mon þe luuede þene cristindom þat heo þa hæþene hatien scolden and þa hæfden bringen to vortimer þan kinge and twalf panewes habben to mede for his weldede vortimer þe ȝunge verde ut of lundene and his broþer and þe oþer heom wes icumen word þat hengest læi at epiford uppen þan watere þe men nemneþ darewente þer comen tosomne sixti þusend monnen an are halue wes and categer and al þat leodliche folc þat luueden ure drihten an oþere halue weoren drenches mid vortigerne þan kinge hengest and his broþer and moni þusend oþer tosomne heo comen and mid mæine onsloȝen þer uellen to þan grunde twa and þritti hundred of hængestes monnen and hors wes forwonded þer com and mid his spere hine þurhnom and hors forþriht þer forwundede and hengest gon to flonnen mid al his drihtmonnen and vortigerne þe king flæh forþ alse þe wind heo floȝen forþ into kent and vortimer heom after went uppen þere sæbrimme þer hengest þolede pine þer heo gunnen atstonden and fuhten swiþe longe fif þusende þer weoren islæȝen and idon of lifdæȝen of vortigernes monnen of þan hæþene cunnen hengest hine biþohte whæt he don mahte iseh he þer bihalues ane hæuene swiþe mære moni scipen gode þer stoden i sæflode heo iseȝen an heore riht hond a swiþe fæier æitlond hit is ihaten tænate þiderward heo weoren whæte þer þa sæxisce men þæ sæ isohten and anan gunnen wenden into þan æitlonde and bruttes heom after mid feole cunne craften and heom toheolden in æchere hælue mid scipen and mid baten heo gunnen smiten and sceoten ofte wes hængest wæ and nauere wurs þene þa buten he dude oþerne ræd þer he sculden wurþen dæd he nom ænne sperescæft þe wes long and swiþe stærc and dude a þene ænde ænne mantel hende and cleopede to þan brutten and bed heom abiden he wold spæcken heom wiþ and ȝirnen þeos kinges griþ and mid griþe sende to londe to makien his forward þat he faren moste wiþuten mare sconde into sæxlonde bruttes wende to londe to vortimere heore kinge and hengest spæc wiþ vortigerne of rune swiþe derne vortigerne wende a þat lond and ber anne ȝerd an his hond þa while þa heo of griþe speken saxes i scipe leopen and droȝen up to coppe hæȝe heore seiles and wenden mid wedere i þere sæ wilde and letten i þissen londe wiues and heore children and vortigerne king þe heom luuede þurh alle þing mid muchele modkære hengest gon awæi uaren swa longe heo ferden þat inne saxlonde heo weoren þa weoren inn bruttene bruttes swiþe balde heo droȝen on heom muchel mod and duden al þat heom þuhte god and vortimer þe ȝunge wes duhti mon þurh alle þing and vortigerne his fader ferde ȝeond þas bruttene ah nes hit nan swa wac mon þat him ne hokerede on and swa he gon wondrien fulle fif wintren and his sune vortimer riche king wuneden her and al þis leodisce folc luueden hine swiþe he wes milde ælche cnafe and tahte þan folke godes læȝe þan ȝungen and þan ælden hu heo cristindom sculden halden writen he sende to rome to þan pape wel idone þe wes ihaten sceint romæin al cristindom he makede fain biscopes he nom twæin hali men heo weoren bæien germain and of ceore and of træis heo uerden ut of rome swa þat heo hider comen þa wes swa bliþe vortimer swa he nes næuere ær her he and alle his cnihtes iwenden uorþrihtes an here bare uoten toȝeines þan biscopen and mid michelere murhþe muþes þer custen nu þu miht iheren of þan kinge vortimere heu he spac wiþ seint germain for heore kume he wes fæin lusteþ me lauerddinges ich æm þissere leodene king ich hatte vortimer mi broþer hatte vortigerne hehte ure fader him uulieþ unrædes he hafþ ibroht i þis lond hæþene leoden ah we heom habbeoþ iflemed al swa ure uulle iuan and mid wepnen ifelled of heom ueole þusen and isend heom ouer sæstram þat heo nauere sel ne cumen aȝan and we scullen an londe luuiæn ure drihten godes folc urofrien and freondliche hit halden wurþen mils liþe wiþ þa londtilien churichen we scullen hæhȝen and hæþenescipe hatien habbe alc god mon his rihte ȝif godd hit an and ælc þrel and ælc wælh wurþe iuroeid and here ich biteche eou an hond al freo ælc chiriclond and ich forȝiue ælchere widewe hire lauerdes quide and þus we scullen an ure daȝen aniþeri hengestes laȝen and hine and his hæþenescipe þæ he hider brohte and minne fader biswak þurh swike his craftes þurh his dohter rouwenne mine uader he uorradde and mi uader swa uuele agon scunede þene cristindom and þa hæþene laȝen luuede to swiþe þa we sculleþ sceonien þa while þa we luuien þa answarede seint germain for swulche worden he wes fain ich þonkie mine drihte þe scop þes daȝes lihte þet he swulche mildce sent to moncunne þas biscopes ferden ȝeond þis lond and setten hit al a godes hond and þene cristindom heo rihten and þat volc þerto dihten and seoþþen þeræfter sone heo iwenden to rome and sæiden þan papen þe roumain wes ihaten hu he hafden her idon iriht þene cristindom and þus hit ane stunde stod a þan ilken vo we ȝet a alre kinge he ærmest he louede rouwen of þan hæþenne cunne hengestes dohter heo þuhten him wel softe rouwenne heo biþohte whæt heo don mahte hu heo mahte hire fader wreken and hire freondene deaþ ofte heo sende sonde to þon kinge heo him sende maþmes moniare cunne of seoluer and of golde þe beste of æie londe heo ȝirnede his ære þat heo moste wonien here mid his fader and foluen his rædes þe king uor his fader bone ȝette hire hir bone buten þat heo sculde wel don luuien þene cristindom al þat þe king ȝirnede al heo hit ȝette ah wale þat of hire þonke næs wær wale þat þe gode king of hire þonke nuste naþing þat he nuste þene swikedom þe þohte þa luþere wimman hit ilomp an are tide heo nom hire to ræde to don bi his ræde alle hire neode and to wlche time heo mihte wel don vnderuongen þene cristindom forþ heo gon riden to þan kinge þa heo hine imette uæire heo hine igrette hal wrþ þu lauerd king bruttene deorling ich æm þe icomen to cristindom ich wulle auon an þan ilke dæie þe þu seolf demest þa wæs þe king bliþe þurh alle þing he wende þat hit weore soþ þat þeo scaþe sæide bemen þer bleowen blisse wes on hirede forþ mon brohte þat water biforen þan kinge heo seten to borde mid muchelure blisse þa þe king hafde iæten þa eoden þeinesmen to mete in halle heo drunken harpen þer dremden þa swicfulle rouuenne eode to are tunne þer wes idon in þes kinges deoreste win nom heo an honde ane bolle of ræde golde and heo gon scenchen on þas kinges benche þa heo isæh hire time heo fulde hir scale of wine and atforen al þan dringe heo eode to þan kinge and þus hailede him on þe swicfulle wimman lauerd king wæs hail uor þe ich am swiþe uæin hercne nu muchel swikedom of þere luþere wimmon hu heo gon swiken þer þene king þe king heo uæire underuæng to his fæiesiþe spæc bruttisc and rouuenne saxisc þan king þuhte gomen inoh for hire spæche he loh hærcne hu heo toc on þis swicfulle wimman in hire bosme heo bar bineoþen hire titten ane guldene ampulle of attere ifulled and þa luþere rouuenne dronc þene bolle þat heo hafde half don after þes kinges dom þa while þe þa king loh þa ampulle heo ut droh þene bolle heo sette to hire chin þat atter heo halde in þat win and seoþen heo þa cuppe bitahte þan kinge þe king dronc al þat win and þat atter þerin þe dæi forþ eode blisse wes on hirede for þe gode king of þan swikedom nuste naþing for he isah rouuenne halden þene bolle and drinken half þat ilke win þat heo heuede idon þerin þa hit com to þare nihte þa todælleden hiredcnihtes and þa ufele rouwenne wende to hire inne and alle hire cnihtes mid hire uorþrihtes þa heihte heo hire sweines and ec þaie þeines þat heo an hiȝinge heore hors sculden sadelien and heo swiþe stille stelen ut of buruwe and wenden al bi nihte to þwoncchestre uorþrihte and þer swiþe vaste biclusen heom in ane castle and luȝen þat his sune hine wolde biliggen and vortigerne þe swikele king ilæfde þare læsing nu vnderȝat his sune þat he hefde atter inomen ne mihte na lechecraft helpen him næ wiht he nom feole sonden and sende ȝeond his londe and hehte alle his cnihtes to him comen forþrihtes þa þat folc was icumen þa wes þe king swiþe untrumed þa ȝirnde þe king heore griþ and þus he spac hem alle wiþ alre cnihten wrþ eow best þe heren æie kinge þer nis nan oþer red buten hiȝendliche ich beo dæd hir ich bitæche eow mi lond al mi seoluer and al mi gold and alle mine maþmes eowre monscipe is þa mare and ȝe forþrihtes senden after cnihtes and ȝeuen heom soluer and gold and hældeþ ȝe seolf eowre lond and wrekeþ eow ȝif ȝe cunnen of sexisce monnen uor weonne so ich beo uorþfaren hengest eow wul makien kare and nimeþ mine likamæ and leggeþ an chæsten and ledeþ me to þare sæstronde þer saxisce men wulleþ cumen a lond anan swa heo me þer witen awæi heo wulleþ wenden nouþer quic ne dead ne durren heo me abiden imong þissen dome dæd iwarþ þe gode king þer wes wop þer wes rop and reuliche iberen heo nomen þes kinges licame and ladden to lundene and bisides bælȝesȝate fæire hine biburȝeden and nawiht hine ne ladden alse þe king heihte þus liuede and þus he endede þar þa iueolen bruttes a balufulle ræde heo nomen anan and bitahten heom þesne kenedom welle reoulich wes þer a þing nu was vortigerne æft king nom his sonde and sende to sexlonde and grette wel hengest cnihten alre væirest and bad hine an hiȝinge comen to þisse londe and mid him brouhte here an hundred ridæren for þat wite þu þuru alle þing þat dead is vortimer þe king and siker þu miht hider comen for dæd is mi sune nis þe non neod to bringen mid þe muchel genge leste ure bruttes æft beon abolȝen þat eow æft seorwen siȝen bitweonen hengest somnede uærde of feole cunne ærde þat he hefde to iwiten seouen hundred scipen and ælc scip he dihte mid þreo hundred cniten i þere temese at lundene hengest com to londe þat word com ful sone to þan kinge þat hengest was in hauene mid seouen hundred scipene ofte was wa neuer wrse þan þæ and bruttes weoren sari and seorhful an heorte nusten heo an worldriche ræd þat heom weore ilike hengest was of ufele war þat he wel cudde þær he nom sone his sonde and sende to þan kinge and grette king mid swiþe uæire worden and seide þat he was icumen swa fader sculde to his sune mid sibbe and mid saihte he wolde on sele wunien griþ he wolde luuien unriht he wolde scunien griþ he wolde habben griþ he wolde holden and al þis leodisce folc luuien he wolde and þene king luuien þurh alle þing ah he hefde ibroht i þis lond ut of sexleoden seouen hundred scipene of hæþene folke þat beoþ þe alre wihteste men þat wunieþ under sunnen and ich wulle quaþ hengest leden heo to þan kinge to an isette dæie atforen al his duȝeþe and þe king scal arisen and of þan cnihten cheosen twa hundred cnihten to leden to his fihten þe sculen biwiten þene king durewurþliche þurh alle þing and seoþþen scullen þa oþere uaren to heore ærde mid sibbe and mid sæle aȝen to sæxlonde and ich wulle bilæuen mid monnen alre selest þat is þe king þe ich luuie þurh alle þing þat word com to brutten hu hengest bihæhte heom þa weoren heo uæine uor uæiren his worden and setten griþ and setten friþ to whulchen ane uirste þe king an ane dæie wolde iseon þas duȝeþe þat iherde hengest cnihten alre uæirest þa wes he swa bliþe swa he nes neuer ær an liue for he þohte swike þene king an his riche her iwraþ hengest cnihte uorcuþest swa biþ æuerælc mon þe biswikeþ þe him wel on wha wolde wenen a þissere weorldriche þat hengest swiken þohte þene king þat hæfde his dohter for nis nauer nan mon þat me ne mai mid swikedome ouergan heo nomen ænne isetne dæi þat scolden þas duȝeþen cumen heom tosomne mid sæhte and mid sibbe an ane uælde þe wæs muri anuast ambresburi þe stude wes ælenge nu hatte hit stanhenge þer hengest þe swike æiþer bi worde and bi write cuþde þan kinge þat he cumen wolde mid his monuerde to wurþscipe þes kinges ah he nalde bringen on drihte buten þreo hundred cnihten þa alre wiseste men þe he mihte uinden and þe king brohte al swa ueole baldere þeinen and þeo weoren þa alre witereste þe wuneden on bruttene mid goden heore iweden al buten wepnen þat heom no towurþen þurh þrist of þan wepnen þus heo hit speken and æft heo hit tobreken for hængest þe leodswike þus he his gon learen þat ælc nome a long sax and læiden bi his sconke wiþinne his hose þer he hit mihte hæle þenne heo comen tosomne sæxes and bruttes þenne queþ hengest cnihten alre swikelest hail seo þu lauerd king ælc þe is þin vnderling ȝif æuere æi of þine gume gære haueþ bisiden send hit mid freondscipe feor from us seoluen and beon we on sele and motegen of sahte nu we maȝen mid sibben ure lif libben þus þe baldefulle mon bispac þer þa bruttes þa andswarede her he wes to vnwar ȝif here is æi cniht swa wod þat wepnen habbe bi siden he scal leosen þa hond þurh his aȝene brand buten he hit sone heonene isende heore wepnen heo awæi senden þa nefden heo noht an honden cnihtes eoden upward cnihtes eoden adonward ælc spac wiþ oþer swulc he weore his broþer þa weoren bruttes imænged wiþ þan saxes þa cleopede hengest cnihtene swikelæst nimeþ eoure sexes sele mine bernes and ohtliche eou sturieþ and nænne ne sparieþ bruttes þer weoren riche ah ne cuþe heo noht þa speche whæt þa saxisce men seiden heom bitweonen heo breoden ut þa sæxes alle bihalues heo smiten an riht half heo smiten an lift half biuoren and bihinden heo leiden heom to grunde alle heo sloȝen þat heo neh comen of þes kinges monnen sone þer feollen feouwer hundred and fife wa wes þan kinge on liue þa hengest hine igrap mid grimmen his gripen and bi þan mantle hine ibræid þat breken þa strenges and sæxes him sette to and wolden þene king fordon and hengest hine gon werien and nalde hit noht iþeuen ah he heold hine ful faste þe while þat feht ilaste þer wes moni riche biræfued þan liue summe heo fluȝen swiþe ofer þene feld brade and wereden heom mid stanen for wepnen næfden heo nane þer wes swiþe hard fiht þer feol moni god cniht þer wes of salesburi an oht bonde icumen ænne muchelne mæin clubbe he bar an his rugge þa wes þer an aþele eorl ihaten cniht mid þan bezste he æhte glochæstre he to þan cheorle leop swulc hit a liun weoren and binom him þe clubbe þa he bar an rugge æuere wulcne swa he smat þer forþrihtes he iwat biforen and bihinden he laide heom to grunde þreo and fifti he þer sloh and seoþþe to ane stede droh he leop uppen stede and swiþe gon him riden he ærde to glochæstre and þe ȝates læc ful feste and anan forþrihtes lette ærmi his cnihtes ȝeond alle þan londe and nomen þat heo funden heo nomen orf heo nomen corn and al þat heo quic funden and brohten to burhȝe vnnimete blisse þa ȝæten heo tunden uaste and wel heom biwusten lete we hit þus stonden and speken of þan kinge sexes him leoppe to and wolde þene king fordo hengest cleopede uorþrihtes aswikeþ mine cnihtes ne sculle ȝe hine noht forfaren for us he haueþ ihaued mucle care and he haueþ to quene mine dohter þa is scone ah alle his burhȝes he scal us bitæchen ȝif he wule his lif broken oþer ælles him is balu ȝiueþe þa wes væste ibunden giues swiþe grete heo duden an his foten ne moste he nauere biten mete ne wiþ nenne freond speken ær he heom hæfden isworen uppen halidom þat wes icoren þat he al þis kinelond wolde bitæchen heom an heond burhȝes and castles and al his comelan and al swa he idode ase hit idemed was and hengest nom an his hond al þis riche kinelond and delde his leoden muchel of þisse londe he ȝæf æne eorle al kent ase hit bi lundene went he ȝæf his stiwarde æstsex and his burþeine middelsax bitahte þa cnihtes hit atfengen and ane while heo heolden þa while ȝeond þis lond ferde and bitahte hengest hæȝen his burhȝes and hengest forþrihtes dude þerin his cnihtes þa while muchel smal folc læi inne suþsæxe and inne middelsæxe muchel of þan kunne and inne æstsaxe heore aþeleste ȝuȝeþe mete heo ferden al þat heo funden heo forlæiȝen þa wif and godes laȝen breken heo duden i þan londe al þat heo wolden þat iseȝen bruttes þat balu wes on londe and hu sæxisce men isiȝen weoren to heom bruttes scupten þan londe nome for sæxisce monnen scome and for þan swikedome þat heo idon hæfden for þan þe heo mid cnifen biræueden heom at liue þa cleopeden heo þat lond al æstsæx and westsæx and þat þridde middelsæx vortigerne þe king bitahte heom al þis lond þat ne bilæfde him an honde a turf of londe and himseolf vortigerne flæh ouer sæuærne feor into wellisce londe and þer he gon atstonde and his hired mid him þe hæne wes iwurþen and he hæfde an horde gersume swiþe stronge he lette his men riden widen and siden and lette him to bonnen of ælches cunnes monnen þe æuere wolden his feoh mid freondscipe ȝirnen þat iherden bruttes þat iherden scottes to him heo comen þerafter ful sone an ælchere side þider heo gunnen riden monies hæȝes monnes sune for golde and for gærsume þa hæfde he tosomne sixti þusend monnen þa sumnede he þa richen þa wel cuþen ræden gode men rædeþ me ræd uor me is swiþe muchel neod whar ich mihte on wilderne wurchen ænne castel þer ic mihte an inne libbe mid mine monnen and halden hine wiþ hengest mid hæȝere strengþe a þat ich mihte bæt burhȝen iwinnen wræken me a mine feonden þa mine wines feolden and habbeþ al mi kinelond awræht ut of mire hond and þus me iflæmed mine fulle ifan þa andswerede a wis mon þe wel cuþe ræden lust me nu lauerd king ich þe cuþe god þing uppen þan munte of reir ich wullen ræden þat þu castel wurche mid stronge stan walle for þer þu miht wunien and libben mid winne and ȝet þu hauest a þire hond muchel seoluer and gold to halden þine hired þa þe helpen scal and swa þu miht on liue libben alræ sælest þa andswerede þe king let hit cuþen an hiȝing ȝeond muchele mire ferde þæt ich faren wulle to þan munte of reir and ræren þer castel forþ ferde þe king and þa ferde mid him þa heo þider comen dic heo bigunnen sone hornes þer bleouwen heowen lim heo gunnen bærnen ȝeond þat lond ærnen and al wæst walsce lond setten a hond al heo hit nomen þat heo neh comen þa þe dic wes idoluen and allunge ideoped þa bigunnen heo wal a þere dic oueral and heo lim and stan leiden tosomne of þer wes wunder fif and twenti hundred a dæi heo leiden þene wal a niht he feol oueral a marwe heo hine arædden a niht he gon toreosen fulle seouen nihte swa heom dihte ælche dæi heo hine aredden and ælche niht he gon reosen þa wes sari þe king and sorhful þurh alle þing swa wes al þa uerde ladliche offæred for æuere heo lokede whænne hengest come anuuenan þe king wes ful særi and sende after witien æfter worldwise monne þa wisdom cuþen and bad heom leoten weorpen and fondien leodrunen fondien þat soþe mid heore siȝecraften whæron hit weore ilong þat þe wal þe wes swa strong ne moste nihtlonges nauere istonden þas weorldewise men þer a twa wenden summe heo wenden to þan wude summe to weienlæten heo gunnen loten weorpen mid heore leodrunen fulle þreo nihten heore craftes heo dihten ne mihten heo nauere finden þurh nauere nane þinge whæron hit weore ilong þat þe wal þat wes swa strong æuereælche nihte toras and þe king his swinc læs buten witie þer wes an he wes ihaten he seide þat he hit afunde ah hit þuhte læsinge he seide ȝif mon funde in auer æi londe æuer æi cniht bærn þe næuere fæder no ibæd and openede his breoste and nomen of his blode and mengde wiþ þan lime and þæne wal læide þenne mihte he stonde to þere worlde longe þat word com to þan kinge of þere læsinge and he hit ilefde þah hit læs weore sone he nom his sonde and sende ȝeond þan londe swa feor swa he for dæþes kare dursten æies weies faren and in ælche tune hercneden þa runen whær heo mihten ifinden speken of swulche childe þas cnihtes forþ ferden widen ȝeond þan ærde tweien uerden ænne wæi þe westriht him læi þe læi forþrihtes in þer nu is kaermerþin bisides þere burh in ane weie brade hefden ænne muchelne plæȝe alle þa burhcnauen þas cnihtes weoren weri and an heorte swiþe særi and seten adun bi þan plaȝe and biheolden þas cnauen vmben ane stunde heo bigunnen striuinge alse hit wes auer laȝe imong childrene plæȝe þe an þe oþerne smat and he þeos duntes abad þa wes swiþe grim touward and þus quaþ þe þene dunt hefde vnwærste man whu hæuest þu me þus idon þu hauest idon me muchel scome þerfore þu scalt habben grome ich æm anes kinges sune and þu ært of noht icumen þv nahtes i nane stude habben freo monnes ibude for swa wes al þa uore þi moder wes an hore for nuste heo næuere þene mon þat þe streonde hire on no þu on moncunne nefdest fader nenne and þu in ure londe makest us to sconde þu ært us imong icumen and nært nænes monnes sune þu scalt i þissen dæie þeruore dæd þolien þis iherden þa cnihtes þer heo weoren bihalues heo arisen up and eoden neor and neodeliche ȝerden of þissere uncuþe talen þe heo iherden of þan cnauen þa wes inne kairmerþin a reue þe hehte þa cnihtes biliue comen to þan reue and þus him to sæiden sone mid muþe we buþ herrihtes cnihtes and habbeoþ her ifunde enne cnaue ȝunge he is ihaten ne icnawe we nawiþt his cunne nim hine an hiȝinge and sende hine to þan kinge alse þu wult libben and þine limen habben and his moder mid him þe hine bar to monnen ȝif þu þis wult don þe king heom wule underfon and ȝif þu hit noht ne ȝemest þerfore þu bist flæme and þas burh al forbard þas leoden al fordemed þa answarede þe reue of kæirmerþin wel ic wat þat al þis lond stunt a vortigernes hond and we beoþ alle his men his monscipe is þe mare and we scullen þis don fain and driȝen his wille forþ wende þe reue and burhmen his iuere and ifunden and his plaȝeiueren mid him heo nomen and his iuæren loȝen þa þa wes ilad þa wes ful glad wende þat he ilad weore limen for to leosen ah al anoþer set þe dom ær hit weoren al idon nu wes moder wunder mere iwurþen in ane haȝe munstre munchene ihaded þider iwende þe reue of kairmerþin and nom him þa lafdie þer heo læi on munstre and uorþ him gon ærne to þan kinge and muchel folc mid him and ladden þa nunne and sone wes þat word cuþ to vortigernes kinges muþ þat icumen wes and brohte þa lauedi and heore sune wes mid hire þer icumen þa wes an liue vortigerne bliþe and þa læuedi aueng mid swiþe uæire læten and he bitahte goden twælf cnihten þa weoren þan kinge holde and hine witen scolden þa sæiden þe king vortiger wiþ þa nunne he spilede þer gode læuedi sæi me sæl þe scal iwurþe whar weoren þu iboren wha streonede þe to bearne þæ andswarede þa nunne and hire fader nemnede þriddendale þis lond stod a mines fader hond of þan londe he wes king cuþ hit wes wide he wes ihaten cnihtene lauerd þa answarede þe king swulc heo his cun weore lauedi sæie þu hit me sæl þe scal iwurþen her is þi sune wha streonede hine who wes him a folke for fader iholden þa heng heo hire hæfued and heolde touward bræsten bi þan kinge heo sæt ful softe and ane lutle while þohte vmbe while heo spac and spilede wiþ þan kinge king ich þe wulle tellen for seolcuþe spellen mi fader þe king luuede me þurh alle þing þa iwarþ ich on vestme wunder ane fæir þa ich wes an uore fiftene ȝere þa wunede ich on bure on wunsele mine maidene mid me wunder ane uæire þenne ich wæs on bedde iswaued mid soft mine slepen þen com biuoren þa fæireste þing þat wes iboren swulc hit weore a muchel cniht al of golde idiht þis ich isæh on sweuene alche niht on slepe þis þing glad me biuoren and glitenede on golde ofte hit me custe ofte hit me clupte ofte hit me tobæh and eode me swiþe neh þa ich an ænde me bisæh selcuþ me þuhte þas mi mæte me wes læþ mine limes uncuþe selcuþ me þuhte what hit beon mihte þa anȝæt ich on ænde þat ich was mid childe þa mi time com þisne cnaue ich hæfuede nat ic on folde what his fader weoren ne wha hine biȝate inne weorlderiche no whaþer hit weore unwiht þe on godes halue idiht la swa ich ibedde are nat ich namare to suggen þe of mine sune hu he to worulde is icume þe nunne beh hire hæfde adun and hire huȝe dihte þe king hine biþohte whæt he don mihte and droh him to ræde redȝiuen gode and heo him radden ræd mid þan bezste þat he ofsende þat wes a selcuþ mon he wes a wis clærc and cuþe of feole cræften he cuþe wel ræden he cuþe feor læden he cuþe of þan crafte þe wuneþ i þan lufte he cuþe tellen of ælche leodspelle com to hirede þar þe king wunede and þene king grætte mid godfulle worde hail seo þu and sund vortigerne þe king ich æm icumen to þe cuþ me þine iwille þa andswærede þe king and talde al þan clærke hu þa nunne hafde isæid and axede hine þer of ræd ord fram þan ende al he him talde þa sæide ich con ful wel heron þer wunieþ in þan lufte feole cunne wihte þa þer scullen bilæfuen þat domesdæi cume liþen summe heo beoþ aþele and summe heo uuel wurcheþ þeron is swiþe muchel cun þa cumeþ imong monnen heo beoþ ihaten ful iwis demones ne doþ heo noht muchel scaþe bute hokerieþ þan folke monine mon on sweuene ofte heo swencheþ and monienne hende wimmon þurh heore cræfte kenneþ anan and monies godes monnes child heo bicharreþ þurh wigeling and þus wes biȝeten and iboren of his moder and þus hit is al igan quaþ þe clærc þa sæide to seolue þan kinge king þine men me habbeoþ inumen and ich æm to þe icumen and ich iwiten wulle what beon þi wille and for wulche þinge ich æm ibroht to kinge þa spilede þe king mid cwikere speche þu ært hider icumen þu nært nanes monnes sune swiþe þe longeþ after laþe spelle iwhiten þu wult þa uore nu þu hit scalt ihere ich habbe bigunnen a weorc mid grundliche strengþe þe haueþ mine gærsume wel swiþe binume fif þusend men wurcheþ þeron ich habbe lim and stan on leode nis betere nan na in nare leode weorcmen al swa gode al þat heo leggeoþ a dæi to soþe ich hit sugge mæi ær dæi amarwen al hit biþ dune ælc stan from oþer iualled to þan grunde nu suggeþ mine wise and mine witie men þat ȝif ich mine þi blod ut of þire breoste and minne wal wurche and do to mine lime þenne mai he stonde to þere worlde longe nu þu hit wost al hu þe iwurþe scal þis ihærde and bælh on his mode and þas word sæide wraþ þeh he weore nulle hit nauere god seolf þe gumenene is lauerd þat þi castel stonde for mine heorte blode ne nauere þi stan wal stille ne ligge for alle þine witien beo swiþe swikele i sæiþ læssinge biforen þæ seolue þat þu scalt afinde a þisses dæies ferste for þis sæde þe is mi fulle ifa þa tiþende me þuncheþ game ich wes iscæpen him to bone let cumen biuoren þine witie and alle his iuere forþrihtes here þa þeos lesinge talden þan kinge and ȝif ich þe sugge soþe mine worde of þine walle and whi he adun falleþ and mid soþe hit bitelle þat heore talen sinde lese ȝef me heore hæfden ȝif ich þi wærc hæle þa andswarede þe king mid quickere steuene swa me helpe min hond þis forwærde ich þe halde to þan kinge was ibroht þe witie and seofue of his iueren alle heo weoren uæie gromede and he grimliche spæc sæie me leodswike laþ me on heorten whi falleþ þes wal uolden to grunde sæie me whæ hit vælleþ þat þe wal reoseþ what mai man uinden at þere dicgrunde wes stille ne cuþe he noht tellen þa seide þas word king hald me forward let deluen þas dich seouen uoten deopere heo scullen uinden ænne stan wunder ane ueire he is ueir and brad volke to bihalden þa dich wes idoluen seoue vet depre þa uunden heo anan þerrihtes þene stan þa sæide þas word king hald me forward sæie me monne me laþest and sæie þisse kinge wulches cunnes þinges vnder þissen stane staþel habbeoþ inumen wes stille ne cuþe he noht telle þa sæide wunder a water her is under doh awai þisne stan þat water ȝe findeþ anan heo duden awæi þene stan atforen þan kinge anon þat water heo funden þa sæide æxe me þe is mi fulle ifa umben ane stunde suggen þe of þan grunde what wuneþ i þan watere wintres and summeres þe king axede ah ne cuþe he nowiht þeron þa ȝet sæide þas word king hald me foreward let alæten þis wæter and wei weorpen þer wunieþ i þan grunde tweien draken stronge þe an is a norþ half þe oþer a suþ half þe oþer is milcwhit ælche deore unnilich þe oþer ræd alse blod wurmen alre baldest ælche middernihte heo biginneþ to fihten and þurh hire fihte feollen þine wurckes þa eorþe gon torusien and þi wal toreosen þurh swulche wundre þi wal is afallen þa iwraþ i þissen flode and noht for mine blode þis wæter wes al ilæde þes kinges men weoren glæde muchel wes þa blisse biuoren þan leodkinge and sone þeræfter sari heo weoren ær þe dæi come to ende heo iherden tiþinde þa þa water wes al ilædden and þe put wes ilær þa comen ut þas tweien draken and muchel dunen makeden and fuhten grimliche dun i þere dich ne isæh nauere na cniht nan ladluker fiht fluȝen of heore muþe fures leomen þis isah þe leodking grimme heore lates þa wes he awundred on þissere wurlderiche what weore þis tacninge þa he isæh þer on grunde and hu hit wuste þat nan oþer mon nuste ærest wes þe white buuen and seoþþen he wes bineoþen and þe drake ræde forwundede hine to dæþe and æiþer wende to his hole ne isæh heom seoþþe na mon iboren þus ferden þeos þing þat isah vortigerne þe king and alle þe weoren mid him luueden swiþe and þe king hatede and his hæfued him binam and his seouene iueren þe mid him weoren þære to telde eode þe king and mid him lædde and seide him mid mucle luue þu ært wilcume and ich þe ȝiuen wulle al þat þu ȝirnest of mine londe of seoluere and of golde he wende þurh þat lond al iwinnen ah al oþer hit wende ær comen þes daies ende þus fræinede þe king his leofe freond sæie me nu monnen me leofuest what bitacnieþ þa draken þe þene dune makeden þe stan and þat water and þat wunderliche fæht sæie me ȝif þi wil is whæt bitacneþ al þis and seoþþen þu most me ræden hu ich scal me læden and hu ich mai biwinne kinedom minne of hengest mines wiues fader þe swiþe me hæfþ iharmed þa andswarede þane kinge þe spac wiþ him king þu ært unwis and vnwiter a ræde þu fræinest of þan draken þe þene dune makeden and whæt tacneþ heore fiht and heore feondliche gripen heo tacneþ kinges þa sunde to cumene and heore fiht and heore uare and heore uæi uolc ah ȝif þu weore swa wis mon and swa witter a þoncke þat þv fræinedest me of feole þine sorȝen of þire mucle kare þa þe is to cumene ich þe wolde suggen of sorȝe þine þa quaþ vortiger þe king leofue freond sæie me of þan þinge þe me to cumen sonden bluþeliche baldere stefne ich þe wulle suggen ah æuere hit wule þe reouwen king king bisiȝ þe sorȝen þe biþ ȝeueþe of cunne his bern þu aqualdest þu lettest slæn þe wes king a þis lond þu lettest þine peohtes hine ladliche biswiken þeruore þu ibidest alre baluwene mæst seoþþen þu tuȝen uuenon þe uncuþe leoden saxes to londe þeruore þu wurþest to sconde nu beoþ of brutaine beornes ariued hit his and vther nu þu ært þærof war heo cumeþ tomærȝen fuliwis i þis lond at tottenæs ich do þe wel to witene mid seouen hundred scipene and nu heo inne sæ seilieþ biliue þu hauest heom muchel uuel idon and nu þu most þat laþ onfon þu hauest a ba halue bone þe þe þencheþ þine ifan þe biuoren and þine ifeond bæften ah flih flih þinne wæi and burh þine life and fleo þider þe þu fleo heo þe wulleþ after teon he hæueþ ærest þisne kinedom ah he þurh atterne drench dæþ scal iþolien and seoþþen scal vther habben þesne kinedom ah þi cun hine scal mid attere aquellen ah ær he dæd þolie he scæl dune makien vther scal habben ænne sune of cornwaille he scal cumen þat beoþ a wilde bar iburstled mid stele þe bar scal forbærnen hæhȝe þa burhȝes he scal alle þa swiken swenien mid eiȝe he scal al þi riche cun mid witen aquellen he biþ swiþe oht mon and aþele an þonke heonenæ into rome rixleþ þeos ilke scal he alle his feond fallen to grunde soþ ich habbe þe isæid ah nis þe na þe softre ah flih mid þine verde þine iuon þe cumeþ to herede þa aswac worden þe wise and þe king lette blawen þreottene bemen and forþ mid his ferde feondliche swiþe nes þer uorþrihtes bute uirst of ane nihte þat comen þa broþere beien tosome to sæstronde ful iwis at dertenemuþe i totenas þis iherden bruttes and weoren bliþe ful iwis heo droȝen ut of þan wuden and of þan wulderne bi sixti and bi sixti and bi seouen hundred bi þritti and bi þritti and bi feole þusend þa heo comen tosomne ful sel hit heo þuhte þa broþeren to þissen ærde brohten vnimete verde and her comen heom biuoren balde þas bruttes vnimete uolc al hit wræh þa wolde þæ ær weoren ȝeond wudes wunderliche todreued þurh þene muchelne æie and þurh þe muclen ærmþe and þurh þene mucle hærm þa hengest heom wrohte and hafde alle heore hæfdmen mid cniuen amurþerd mid sæxen tosnæþde snelle þe þeines bruttes heolden husting mid heȝe wisdome heo nomen þene ældre broþer anan inne hæȝe hustinge and heouen hine to kinge þa weoren bruttes mid blisse auulled bliþe an mode þæ ær weoren murne comen þas tiþende to vortigerne þan kinge þat wes icoren and to kinge iheouen þa wes vortiger wa and æft him wes wurse vortiger uerde ver to ane castle hæhte hæh an ane munte cloard hæhte þe munt and hærgin hahte þat lond onvæst wæie þe is a water hende vortigernes men nomen al þat heo neh comen heo nomen wepnen and mete a moni are wise to þan castle heo brohten swa muchel swa heo rohten þat heo inoh hafden þeh hit lutel hulpe and vther weoren of vortigerne war whær he wes uppen cloward biclused in castlen heo letten blawen bemen bonnien heore uerde volc unimete of moni ane londe ferden to þær læi vortigerne king wes wiþuten king wes wiþinnen cnihtes þer fuhten mid feondliche ræsen æuerælc god mon gurede hine seolfuen þa heo iseȝen þat heo siȝen næfden þa to wude wenden wunder muche uerde heo uelden þæne wude adun and droȝen to þan castle and fulden al þæ dic þe wes wunder ane deop fur heo in sende on æuerælche ende and cleopeden to vortiger nu þu scalt þe warmen þer for þu sloȝe þe wes king of þis lond and seoþþe his sune nu is icumen and vther his broþer þa þe balu sendeþ þe wind wæht þat fur þat hit wunderliche born þe castel gon to bernen bures þer swælden feollen þa hellen floȝen to grunde ne mihten þer na cniht aȝeines þe fure makien fiht þat fur eode oueral and barnde hus and barnde wal and þe king vortigerne þerinne he gon to berne al hit forswælde þat þerinne wunede þus ændede þer mid muchele ærme vortiger þa hafde al þat lond an his hond þer wes þe aþele eorl ihaten he wes of gloucestre cnihten alre glæuest þær i þan ærde makede hine stiwærd þa hæfde and vther his broþer heore ifan auelde and weoren þerfore þe bliþere þis iherden hengest cnihten alre strengest þa wes he auæred feondliche swiþe he fusde his ferde and flæh touward scotten and þe king æfter him uerde an hiȝinge and hengest þuhte þat he walde mid al his monuerde ȝif me onsohte him fleon into scotte þat he mihte mid wiȝele þanene atwinden ȝif he ne mihte i þan londe uor atstonde ferde uorþ and droh his folc riht norþ mid deorling ȝif ich mot ibiden þat ich aȝæn ride and hit wulle drihte þe scop þes daȝes lihte þat ich mote mid isunde biȝite mine ikunde chirchen ich wulle arære and god ich wulle hæren ich wulle alche cnihte ȝeuen his irihte and auerælche beorne þan ælden and þan ȝungen ich wulle milden wurþen ȝif godd me wule ivnnæ min æþel to biwinnen to hengeste comen tidende of þan kinge þa spac hengest cnihten alre swikelest hærcneþ nu mi men monscipe eou is ȝiueþe her cumeþ and vther his broþer eke heo bringeþ swiþe muchel folc ah alle heo beoþ fæie for vnwis is þe king swa beoþ his cnihtes and a cnaue is his broþer þe an alse þe oþer þerfore maȝen bruttes beon muchele þe vnbaldur þenne þat hæfd is unwræst þe hælp is þæ wurse and wel ȝe hit maȝen imunen þat ich wulle mæinen betere beoþ ure fifti þænne heore fif hundred þat heo feole siþen ifonded habbeoþ seoþþen heo an londe fondeden leoden for cuþ hit is wide of ure wiþerdeden þat we beoþ kempen icud mid þan bezsten we scullen aȝen heom stonden and driuen heom of londen and walden þas riche after ure iwille þus bælde hængest cnihten alre hændest balde his ferde þer heo wes an felde ah oþer weies hit was idiht ær come seouen niht forþ comen þa tiþinde to þan kinge whær hengest wunede buuen are munede hafde to iueren þritti þusend rideren baldere brutten þe heore beot makeden and æc he hafde walisce wunder ane monie þa lette he his cnihtes dæies and nihtes æuere beon iwepned alse heo to wiȝe scolden for auere he care hafde of heþene uolke þa iherde hengest þat wes onuast nom he his ferde and fusde him toȝaines þa wes wær þat hengest wolde cumen þær he uærde in ane velde wel iwepned under scelde nom he forþrihtes ten þusend cnihtes þa weoren bezst iboren and of his ferde coren and setten heom a þan felde auoten under scelde ten þusend walisce he to wude sende ten þusend scottes he sende bihalues þe hæþene to imete bi stiȝen and bi straten himseolf he nom his eorles and his aþele kempes and his holdeste men þa he hæfde an londe and makede his sceldtrume swulc hit weoren an hær wude fif þusend þer riden þa sculden al þis folc biwiten þa cleopede eorl of gloucestre ȝif hit me on drihte þe alle domes waldeþ þat ich mote ibide þat hængest cume riden þa is a þissen londe swa longe atstonde and biswac mine leofe freondes mid longe his sæxes bisiden amberesburi mid ærmliche witen ah ȝif ich mihte of þan eorlen þat aþel me biwinnen þenne mihte ich suggen soþ quides mine þat me hafde godd seolf godes iunnen ȝif ich mine ifan fallen to grunde anan and wræken mi deore cun þat heo habbeoþ ilæid adun vnneæþe wes þis spel isæid to þan ende þa iseȝen heo hængest halden ouer dune mid vnimete ferden feondliche heo fusden tosomne heo comen and feondliche heo sloȝen þer þa ræȝe men togæderen heom ræsden helmes gunnen gullen cnihtes þer feollen stel eode wiþ þan ban balu þer wes riue urnen inne strete stremes of blode faȝeden þa feldes and þat gras falewede þa iseh hængest þat his help trukede þa hald he fram fæhte and bihalues flæh and his folc after fusde biliue þa cristine liþen after and heom on læiden and cleopeden godes sone beon heom a fultume and þe heþene leoden æc lude cleopeden ure godd whi trukest þu us an hond þa hengest isæh þa hæþene ibuȝene and þa cristine men cumen heom anufene þa fleh henges þurh and þurh þat he com to kuniggesburh i þare burh he wende burh to brukene and þe king after wende anan and clepede to his leoden ludere stæuene ærneþ æuere vorþ and vorþ hengest is ifaren norþ and heo him after buȝen þat heo to burhȝe comen þa isæh hengest and his sune al þa uerde heom after cumen þa sæide hengest cnihten alre wraþest nulle ich na mare fleon ah nu ich wulle fihten and mi sune and his wedbroþer ebissa and al mi monuerde sturieþ eouwer wepnen and fare we heom toȝænes and makien feondslæhtes and ȝif we hom ne falleþ þænne beon we fæie ilæid on felde and freonde bidælde hengest bah a þene wald and bilæfde al his teld and makede his sceldtrume al of his hæþene gumen þa com þe king and moni þusend mid him and bigunnen þer oþer fæht þe wes feondliche stærc þer wes moni græt dunt idæld i þan compe þer weoren þa cristine wel neh ouercumene þa comen þer uaren fif þusend rideren þa hafde an horse to fihten heo smiten a þan hæþene þat heo adun helden þer wes feht swiþe stor eornest ful sturne i þan fæhte com þe eorl of gloucetre and ifunde hengest cnihten forcuþþest whar he feondliche faht and þa cristine feolde his gode sweord adroh and uppen hengest sloh and hengest warp þene sceld biuoren and ælles weoren his lif forloren and smat i þene sceld þat he atwa toscænde and hengest him leop to swulc hit a liun weore and smat an helm þat he atwa tofeol þa heowen heo mid sweorde þa swipen weoren grimme fur flæh of stele ofte and wel ilome vnder are stunde þa leop to grunde and isæh him þat wæs a kene gume ful iwis of cornwale he wes eorl he wes widene cuþ þa wes þæ beorn muchele þe balder and hæf hæhȝe his sweord and lette hit adun swippen and smat hengest a þan hond þat he forlette his brond an hiȝinge hine igrap mid grimme his læchen bi þere burne hode þa wes an his hafde and mid muchelere strengþe hine adun swipte and seoþþe he hine up bræid swulc he hine tobreken wolde and mid ærmen hine bisprædde and forþ hine lædde nu wes hengest inumen þurh þene æhte gume þæ cleopede þene eorl of gloucestre hengest nis þe noht swa murie swa þe wes bi ambresburie þer þu þa sæxes droȝen and bruttes ofsloȝen mid muchele swikedome þu mi cun sloȝe nu þu scalt læn leosen and losie þine freonden mid reoliche witen an worlde forwurþen hengest eode stille ne isæh he help nenne hine ladde to his leodkinge and grætte þene leodking mid leofliche worden hail seo þu aþeles cunnes her ich bringe þe biuoren þe wes þines cunnes bone hengest þene heþene þe hærm us hafueþ iuræmmed godd hit me iuþe þat ich hine igripen habben nu ich hine ȝiue þe uor monne leofuest ært þu me and let þine hiredchilderen pleien mid þissen hunde scotien mid heore flan and his cun scenden anan þa andswarede þe king quicliche steuene edi seo þu eorlene aþelest þu ært me leof al swa mi lif leoden þu scalt beon alder þer me nom hengest and þer me bond hengest þer wes þa hengest cnihten alre ȝeomerest þis feht wes ouercumen and þa hæþene fluȝen þa iseh þat his fader wes ful wa and ebissa his wedbroþer buȝen heom togadere and fluȝen into eouuerwic mid ærmþen inoȝe and greiþeden walles tohalden þa halles summe þa hæþene to þan wude iwenden þær þat ganninde folc læiden heom to grunde þa wes þe king iquemed wel þurh alle þing he wende into cuningesburh mid his drihtfolke and þankede drihten swulchere mihten þreo dæies and þreo niht þe king wunede þarriht to lechinien þa wunden of leofenen his cnihten and baþien on burȝe heore wærie ban þa þe þridde dæi com and þat folc hafde imaked non þa lette þe king blawen and beonnede his eorles þa heo comen to hustinge to þan kinge þa heo togadere comen þe king heom axede sone whæt heo him radde þat his richemen weoren a wulchere witen hengest scolde forwurþen and hu he mihte bezst wreoken his leofueste freondes þe anfest amberesburi leien biburide þa stod up ældadus and wiþ þene king he spac þus towardes gode he was god he wes an hali biscop eorles broþer nefde he nenne oþer lauerd king lust nu me what ic wullen tellen þe ich wulle makien þene dom hu he scal beon fordon for he is on leode monnen us laþest and haueþ ure kun ofslæȝen and idon of lifdæȝen and he is an hæþene hund helle he scal isechen þer he scal sinke for his swikedome lauerd king hærcne me wat ich þe wulle tællen a king wes in ierusalem saul wes ihaten þe wes in hæþenesse king of muchele mæhte agag wes ihaten ierusalem he hatede he wes king of þe amalæh þe wurse him wes ful nieh auere he hatede ierusalem mid hærmen þan mesten nolde he neouere heom ȝiuen griþ ah auere he heom stod wiþ he heom barnde he heom sloh he dude heom sorȝen inoh hit ilomp in ane time þat þe sunne gon to scine þa sat agag þe king inne his hæh sættele meinde his fæie blod and muneȝede hine to fusen he cleopede his cnihtes anan uorþrihtes swiþe to eouwer steden and forþ we scullen riden we sculleþ bærnen and slæn al ibuten ierusalem forþ wende þe king and muche ferde mid him þat lond heo gunne þurhærnen and þa tunes furbernen þat iseȝen þa men þe wuneden inne ierusalem and heo heom toȝeines cnihtes and sweines and fuhten wiþ þene king and mid fæhte hine ouercomen and al his folc sloȝen and agag heo king nomen and swa heo mid him comen to saul þan kinge þa wes saul þe king bliþe þurh alle þing þe king axeden ræd at his riche anan whæþer he mihte him bet don oþer slæn oþer anhon þa leop up a witiȝe of israel he wes swiþe hali mon hæh touward drihten nuste na mon i þan dæȝen swa heh mon an godes laȝen nom agag þene king and lædde hine a þan cheping and lette hine swiþe sterke to ane stake binde and nom mid his riht hond ænne durewurþe brond and þus cleopede him on þe gode mon þu hattes agag þe king nu þu ært an ærming nu þu scalt fon þat læn þat þu forferdest ierusalem þat þu hauest þas hæȝe burh swa swiþe forworht and monienne godne mon islæȝen and idon of lifdæȝen swa ich ibide are ne scalt þu nauermare þat sweord anhof and hærdeliche adun sloh and al toswadde þene king in ierusalemus chepping and þa stucchen tarueden wide ȝeond þa straten þus tok on and swa þu aȝest hengest don þis iherde þe eorl of glocetere touward hengest he leop swulc hit a liun weore and igrap hine bi þan toppe and hine æfter him halede and ladde hine þurh and þurh and þurhut cuningesburh and wiþuten þere burhȝe he hine lette binden his swored adroh and hengestes hafd ofsloh and þe king hine nom forþrihtes for he wes swa oht cniht and læide hine in eorþe after heþene laȝen and bad for þere sæule þat hire neuere sæl neore and nu þe king lette beode husting and lætte blawen bemen and bonnien his ferde folc þer wes sellic and ferden riht to euerwic and biclusden þer wiþinnen mid his monnen þe king lette deluen ænne dich al abuten eouerwic þat ne mihte þer na man neoþer ute no in gan þæt isæh þerfore him wes wa and his hæþene folc þe he hafde an burȝe heo nomen heom to ræde what heo don mæhten and þus spac wiþ his iuere ebissa nou ich habben me biþoht what ich don wulle ich and mine cnihtes scullen forþrihtes in ure bare brechen gan ut of burȝen ræmen a mine swore ænne raketeȝe and cumen to þan kinge his mildce biddinde ælles we beoþ alle dæde buten we fulien þissen ræde alle heo duden swa swa heom radde duden of claþes karefulle cnihtes and eoden ut of burhȝe blaþe þeines tweiene and tweiene twenti hundred þis biheold aþelest kingen seolcuþ him þuhte of þan nakede cnihten tosomne comen þa ferde þat læi ȝeond þan ærde iseȝen cumen þat wes hengest sune he bar an his honde ænne raketeȝe longe he com to þan kinge and biuoren his hæredringe he feol uppen uolde þas kinges fæt isohte and þas word seide þa hengestes sune imilze mi lauerd king þurh þene milde godd for luue of god almihten haue milce of mine cnihten for alle ure heþenescipe hæne is iwurþen laȝen and ure leoden for laþe we beoþ drihten for us is itruked an hond and woden and and venus and didon frea and and alle ure laue nu us sunde laþe ah we wulleþ ileuen in leofen þine drihten for al hit trukeþ us an hond þat we to temden we ȝeorneþ þine are nu and aueremare ȝif þu me wult griþien and þu me wult friþien we þe wulleþ to teon and þine holde men beon luuien þine leoden and þine laȝen halden ȝif þu þet nulle do þine iwille whaþerswa þu wult don þa us slan þa us anhon and þe king wes mildheorte and heold hine stille he biheold a riht hond he biheold a lift hond wulc of wiisen ærest spæken wolden alle heo weoren stille and swiȝeden mid stæuen nes þer nan swa hæh mon þat durste word sciren and æuere læie æt þes kinges foten swa alle his cnihtes leien him biæften þa spac þe gode biscop and seide þus æuere hit wæs and a hit biþ and ȝet hit us bihoueþ þene we milze ȝeorneþ þat we milze habben wurþe he is milze þe wurþeliche heo biddeþ and þu seolf læuerd king leoden þu ært ælder imilze þu and his iueren alswa ȝif heo wulleþ cristindom mid gode lefuen vnderfon for ȝet hit mai ilimpen i summere leoden þat heo maȝen drihten duȝeþliche hærien nu stont al þis kinelond a þire aȝere hond bitec heom enne stude þer he biþ iqueme and nim of heom ȝisles swulche þu wult ȝirnen and let heom wel halden in irene benden finden þan ȝislen mete and claþ finden al þat heom biþ leof and þenne miht þu wel halden þis moncun i þine londe and let heom tilien þat lond and libben bi heore tilæhþe ȝif hit seoþþen ilimppeþ sone þerafter þat heo trukieþ an hond treouþen to halden and wakieþ mid wærke and þe wiþer haldeþ nu ich þe demen þene dom whæt þu miht seoþþen don let riden heom to ræhliche swiþe and let heom alle fordon spillen and æc anhon þis ich þe deme drihten hit ihere þa andswarede þe king quickere stefne al swa ich wulle don swa þu hauest idemed þus spac þe kingþa aris up þu scalt swiþe wel don vnderuoh cristindom þer wes iuulȝed and his iueren alswa and alle his cnihtes i þan stude uorþrihtes heo nomen heore ȝisles and ȝeuen þan kinge þreo and fifti children heo bitæhten þan kinge and þe king heom sende bisiden scotlonde aþes heo sworen swiken þat heo nalden þe king bitahte heom an hond sixti hidene lond þeron heo wuneden wel feole wintren þe king wes inne eouerwic aþele him þuhte he nom his sonden and sende ȝeond his londe hæhte his biscopes his bocilærede men eorles and þeines cumen him toȝeines to þan kinge to muchele hustinge hit iwærþ sone þat heo gadere comen þe king his folc grætte mid fæire his worden he wilcumede eorles he wilcumede beornes and þa biscopes and þa bocilærede men ich eou wulle suggen mid soþe worden whi ich eou æfter sende and for wulche þingen her ich aȝeuen ælche cnihten is cunden and his rihten and æuerælche eorle and æuerælche beorne þat he mæi biwinnen bruken hit mid wunnen and ælche monnen bi his life ich hate griþ luuien ich hæten eou wurchen and bulden þa chirchen bellen leten ringen godes lof singen heren mid ure mihten leofe ure drihten ælche mon bi his mæhte halden sibbe and sæhten læten tilien þat lond nu hit is al a mire hond þa þis dom wes isæid alle heo leofden þisne ræd þe king heom ȝef leoue þenne to liþe ælc uærde heomward swa heom bezst þuhte seouen niht fulle þe king læi þer stille and seoþþen he gon liþe into lundenne to gladien þat burhfolc þat ofte weoren bisie he letten stronge walles he lette bulden halles and rihte al þa workes þe ær weore tobrokene and aȝef heom alle þa laȝen þe stoden bi heore ælderne dæȝen he makede þer reuen þan uolke to reden and þenenen he gon wenden riht to winchæstre þer he lette wurcchen halles and chirchen þer him þuhte swiþe muri seoþþen he uerde to ambresburi to þan leerstowe of leofuen his freonden þa hengest mid cniuen þer aquald hæfuede he lette axien anan men þat cuþen hæuwen stan and æc gode wurhten þe mid æxe cuþe wurchen he þohte wurche þer a werc wunder ane ueire þat a sculde ilasten þa while men liueden þa wes inne kaerlium a biscop þe hahte tremoriun he wes swiþe wis mon inne weorldrichen mid þan kinge he wes ouenan þæ walde and þus tremorien godes dring spæc þer wiþ þene king lust nu me what ich þe wulle cuþen and ich þe wullen suggen sælest alre ræden ȝif þu hine wult luuien æft he þe likeþ we habbeoþ ænne witeȝe is ihaten ȝif æi mon hine mihte ifinden uppe þissere wælden and to þe ibringen þurh æies cunnes þinge and þu his iwille driȝen woldest he þe wolde runen selest ræden hu þu mihtest þis weorc makien strong and sterk þet a mihte ilæsten þa while men leoueden þa andswarede þe king þas wordes him weoren iqueme leoue freond tremoriun al þis ich wulle don þe king sende his sonde ȝeond al his kinelonde and bad æuerælcne mon axien after and ȝif me hine mihten ifinden bringen hine to þan kinge he him wolde ȝifuen lond boþe seoluer and gold and a weorlrichen driȝen his iwille þa sonden gunnen riden widen and siden summe heo uerden riht norþ and summe heo uerden suþ forþ summe heo uerden riht æst and summe heo uerden riht west summe heo uerden anan þat heo comen to alæban þat is a wælle inne wælsce londe þe walle he lufode and ofte hine þerinne baþede þa cnihtes hine funde þer he sat bi þan stronden sone swa hine imetten fæire heo hine igrætten and þus him to forþrihtes sæiden þa tweien cnihtes hail seo þu monnene wisest bi us þe gon græten þat is a godful king ihaten aþelest alre kingen stont al þis muchele lond in kinges hond faire he þe bisecheþ þat þu him to buȝe and he þe wule ȝiue lond boþe seluer and gold ȝif þu an riche ræde wulle þan kinge andswerede þa þæt cnihten wes ful wa ne recche ich noht his londes his seoluer no his goldes no his claþes no his hors miseolf ich habbe inowe þa sat he stille longe ane stunde þas cnihtes weoren afæred þat he fleon wolde þa hit alles up brac hit wes god þat he spæc ȝif beoþ tweiene cnihtes icumen herrihtes ȝurstendæi ær none ich wuste þat ȝe comen and ȝif ich swa walde ne mihte ȝe me finden ȝe bringeþ me gretinge from þan kinge ich cneou his cnihtes ær he come to londe and ich icneou þene oþer vther his broþer ic icneou beien ær heo iboren weoren þæh ich nauer nouþer mid eȝen ne iseȝe ah walawa walawa þat hit is idiht swa þat þe leodene king leng ne mot liuien ah nu ich wulle fusen and beon eouwer ifere to þan kinge ich faren wulle and driȝen his iwille forþ ferde and þa cnihtes wiþ him swa longe þat heo comen to þan leodkinge komen to þan kinge wiltidende næuer ær an his liue nes þe king swa bliþe for næuere nanes monnes cume þe him to come þe king to his stede and ut him gon ride and alle his cnihtes mid him to wulcumen þe king hine imette and fære hine igratte he hine iclupte he hine custe he hine cuþlæhte muchel wes þe murhȝe i þan monuerede al for cume þe nes nanes monnes sune wale þat an worlde næs nan witie þat auere wuste here whes sune he weore buten drihten ane þe wlæt al clane þe king lædde to bure þe wes deore he hine fræinien gon mid fæire his worden anan þat he dude him to vnderstonde of þan weorldes ȝeongen and of al þan ȝeren þat to cumen weoren for hit weoren him swiþe iwil þat he þerof wuste andswerede þa and to þan kinge seide swa o þe king þu fræinest me a sellic þing loke þat þu na mare swulc þing ne iscire for mi gæst is bæl iwis þa a mire breoste is and ȝef ich among monnen ȝelp wolde makien mid gladscipe mid gomene mid godfulle worden mi gast hine iwarþeþ and wirþ stille and binimeþ me min wit and mine wise word fordut þenne weore ich dumbe of æuerælche dome ah bilef swulche þinges quæd to þan kingen for whanswa cumeþ neode to aueræi þeode and mon me mid mildescipe wulle me bisechen and ich mid mine iwille mote wunien stille þenne mæi ich suggen hu hit seoþþen scal iwurþen ah ich þe wulle ræden of nexte þire neoden and sugen þe herriht what þu hauest an heorten a ueld is bi amberesburi þe is brad and swiþe muri þer wes mid cniuen þi cun idon of liuen þer wes moni bald biswiken to þan deþe and þenchest þene stude mid wurþcipe igraten mid sælcuþe wærcken wurþien þa dæde þat þer scal stonden to þere worlde longe ah nauest þu neuere nenne mon þe cunne awiht þeron þe cunne wærc makien þe nauere nulle trukien ah ic þe wulle ræden to swulchere neode for ich what a wærc mid wundere bistonde for þat weorc stondeþ inne irlonde hit is a swiþe sellic þing þat woerc is of stane swulc ne beoþ oþer nane swa wid swa is weorlderiche nis nan weorc his iliche þa stanes beoþ muchele and mahten heo habbeoþ þa men þe beoþ unhal heo fareþ to þan stane and heo wasceþ þene stan and þermide baþieþ heore ban umbe lutle stunde heo wurþeþ al isunde ah þe stanes beoþ muchele and unimete græte for nis nauere na mon iboren i nauere nare burhȝe þe mihte mid strengþe þa stanes þenne bringe þa andswarede þe king þu sæist sællic þing þe nauere nan iboren mon ne maie heom bringgen þenne no mid nare strengþe of þan stude lade hu mihte ich heom þenne heom bringen þeonne þa andswarede þan kinge þat spac wiþ him ȝuse ȝuse lauerd king hit wes ȝare iqueþen þat betere is liste þene ufel strenþe for mid liste me mai ihalden þat strengþe ne mai iwalden ah somne þine uerde and far to þan ærde and þu mid þe lede gode monne uerde and ich wulle mid þe þi monscipe biþ þe mære ær þu aȝæn wende þine iwille þu scalt habben and þat weorc þu scalt bringen mid þe to þissen londe and swa þu hit scalt leden to þere lichraste and wurþien þene stude þer þine wines liggeþ and þu seolf scalt þerin þine ban resten þenne þi lif endeþ þer þu scalt resten þus seiden and seoþþen he sæt stille alse þeh he wolde of worlden iwiten þe king hine lette bringen into ane fære bure and wunien þerinne æfter his iwille þe king lette beoden husting of alle þan londe þa stod an his honde he bad him ræde to swulchere neode and heo him wel rædden riche his beornes þat he dude þene ræd þat him hauede isæd ah heo nælden leden þene king ut of þis londe ah heo curen heom to ældre vther þene gode and fiftene þusend cnihten fæire iwepned baldere brutten þa þider sculde buȝen þa þas ferde wes al ȝaru þa bigunnen heo to faren mid alle þan bezste scrippen þæ bi þære sæ stoden and ferden swa longe þat heo comen to irlonde and þa hauene nomen þæ cnihtes wel idone heo eoden uppen sæstrond and biheolden irlonde þa spæc and spilede mid worden iseo ȝe nu ohte men þene muchelne hul þe hul swa swiþe hæh þere weolcne he is ful neh þat is þat seolliche þing hit hatte þere eotinde ring elches weorkes unniliche hit com of aufrike slæþ eower teldes ȝeond al þas feldes her we scullen ræsten to þreom dæȝen uirsten i þan feorþe dæiȝe we scullen heonne fusen touward þan hulle þer is ure iwille ah we scullen us ær baþien and bonnien ure beornes græiþien ure wepnen for wel heo us bihoueþ þus hit bilæfde and þer læie þa ferde þeo ahte irlond a king þat wes swiþe strong he hæhte gomenen he wes lauerd him comen þa tiþende þat brutes weoren an londe he lette beoden ferde ȝeond alle irlondes ærde and he gon þretien swiþe þat al he wolde heom todriue þa þat word him com to þat brutes wolden þer don and comen to þan anes to fæchen þa stanes þa þe king makede mucchel hoker and scarn and seide þat heo weoren sotten iueren þat ouer sæ brade þider weoren iliþene to sechen þer stanes ase in heore londe neoren nane and swor a seint brænden ne scullen heo læden ænne stan ah for þan stanen heo scullen ibiden alre baluwenen mæst heore blod ȝeoten ut of heore buken and swa me scal heom tachen stanes to sæchen and seoþþen ich wulle buȝen into brutlonde and suggen þan king þat mine stanes ich wullen werien and buten þe king beon stille and don mine iwille ich wulle in his londe mid fæhte atstonden maken him weste paþes and wildernes monie widewen inoȝe heore weres scullen deȝe þus þe vnwise king plaȝede mid worden ah al an oþer hit iwærþ oþer he iwende ȝaru wes hes ferde and forþ heo gon fusen swa longe þat heo comen þer læien brutes on togaderen heo comen and hærdliche onsloȝen and fuhten feondliche feollen þa fæie þa irisce weoren bare and bruttes iburnede þa irisce fullen and wriȝen al þa feldes and þe king gon him to fleonne þar and flæh forþrihtes mid twenti of his cnihtes into ænne muchele wude wurþscipen biræiued wes his irisce uolc mid stele iualled þus wes þe king iscænd and þus he endede his ȝelp and þus to wude ferde and lette his folc fællen þa bruttes biheolden þa dede ȝeond þan vælden seouen þusend þer leien liues bidæled bruttes ȝeond þan uælden ferden to heore telden and heore gode wepnen wurþliche bihoȝeden and þer heo gunnen ræsten alse heom radde i þan feorþe dæie þa gunnen heo fusen and ferden to þan hulle iwæpned wel alle þer stod þat seolkuþ werc muchel and swiþe sterc cnihtes eoden upward cnihtes eoden dunward cnihtes eoden abuten and ȝeorne biheolden iseȝen þer on londe sellic werc stonden þer weoren a þusend cnihtes mid wepnen wel idihten and alle þa oþer to iwiten biwusten wel heore scipen þa spæc and spileden mid þan cnihten cnihtes ȝe beoþ stronge þas stanes beoþ græte and longe ȝe mote neh gon and neodliche heom fon on ȝe mote uaste heom wriþen mid strongen sæilrapen scuuen and hebben mid hæȝere strenþe treon græte and longe þat beon swiþe stronge and gaþ to ane stane ȝe alle glæne and cumeþ mid strengþe ȝif ȝe hine maȝen sturien wel wuste hu hit sculde iwurþen þa cnihtes tostepen mid muchelere strengþe heo swunken ful swiþe ah næfden heo syȝe þat heo auer æine stan sturien mahten biheold vther þe was þe kinges broþer and þas word sæide þe witeȝe vther tih þe aȝan and bonne þine cnihtes and stondeþ al abuten and ȝeorne bihaldeþ and beoþ alle stille þat na man þer ne sturie ær ich sugge eou nu anan hu we scullen fon on vther droh hine abac and bonnede his cnihtes þat ne bilafden þer nane aneoweste þan stane al swa feor swa a mon mihte werpen ænne stan and eode abuten and ȝeornen gon bihalden þrie he eode abuten wiþinnen and wiþuten and sturede his tunge alse he bede sunge þus dude þer þat cleopede he vþær vther com swiþe and alle þine cnihtes mid þe and winneþ þas stanes alle ne scullen ȝe læuen nænne for nu ȝe maȝen heom hebben swulche veþerene balles and swa ȝe sculleþ heom mid ræde to ure scipen lede þeos stanes heo ladden swa heom radde and duden heom in heore scipen and seileden uorþ to iwiten and swa heo gunnen wenden into þissen londe and ladden heom in ann velde þe is wunder ane brad he is brad and swiþe muri onuæst ambresburie þer hengest biswæc bruttes mid sæxen heom gon ræren alse heo stoden ærer swa næuer nan oþer mon þene craft ne cuþe don ne næuer ær þer biforen nes na mon swa wis iboren þat cuþe þet weorc rihten and þa stanes dihten þat tidende com to þan kinge i þan norþ ende of fore and of vthæres his broþer þat heo weoren mid isunde icumen to þissen londe and þat þat worc wes al idiht and iset upriht þe king wes an breoste wunder ane bliþe and lette beode hustinge swa mid swa wes al his lond þat al his folc swa swiþe muri come to amberesburi al his drihtliche uolc to whitesunedæie þider com þe king and al his folc mid him a whitensunendæie he þer wærf makede alse ich þe wulle telle a þisse bocspelle weoren a þan walde teldes itælded in þan brade uelde niȝe þusend teldes al þan whitensunendæi þe king a þan uelde læi hæt halȝien þe stude þe hæhte stanhenge þreo dæies fulle wunede þe king stille i þan þridde dæie heȝe wurþede his duȝeþe he makede tweie biscopes wunder ane gode seint to kaerliun to eouuerwic seint beien heo iwurþen hali and mid gode haȝe i þan feorþe dæie duȝeþen todælden and swa ane stunde hit stod a þan ilken þa ȝet þer wes a luþer gume vortigernes sune wes þe ilke into wælisc londe iwent and þer a þen ilke daȝen wes bicumen utlaȝe ah ne durste he noht longe wunien þer for and for vther ah he biȝet scipen gode and ferde bi sæflode into alemaine he uerde mid fif hundred monnen and þer he biwon muchel uolc and makeden scipferde and for swa longe þat he com to þisse londe into þere þer he hærmes worhte ah ne durste he noht longe i þan ænde atstonde þe king ferde þiderward and fleh aweiward æfter sæ swa longe þat he com to irlonde sone he þer funde þene king of þan londe his heorte wes swiþe sær he grette þene king hail seo þu gumene ælder ich æm to þe icume ich wes vortigernes sune mi fader wes brutlondes king he luuede þe þurh alle þing and ȝif þu woldest toȝere beon þider min iuare swa wit sculden ispæcken and minne fader wel wreken and wel wreken þi folc þat vther her qualde and þi selcuþe wærc þat heo heonne droȝen and æc ich iherde suggen þer ic ferde inne sæ þat þe king seoc is iwurþen and liþ inne winchæstre a bedde ful faste þu miht ileue me inoh for þis is witerliche soþ and makeden heore forward þar aþes heo sworen monie and unifohȝe þat heo wolden al þis lond sætten on hæore tweire hond þe aþes weoren isworene ah æft heo weoren forlorene þe king gaderede ferde wide ȝeond his ærde to þere sæ beoþ iwende and passen into þan scipen eoden and forþ heom letten gliden forþ heo wenden biliue þat heo comen to meniue þat wes a þan time tun swiþe hende þat mon nu iwitterli clepeþ seint deouwi þer heo nomen hauene mid heȝere blisse scipen eoden a þat strond cnihtes eoden a þat lond þa sæide touward he went seie me king nu we beoþ icumen her nu ich sette þe an hond halfendæl þis kinelond for is of winchastre icume to me anes cnihtes sune and sæiþ me swulne ræd þat wule beon dæd þat ufel is under his ribben þat ne mæi he noht libben her wit scullen wel wreken unker winemæies biwinnen his wunseles swa us biþ alre selest to þan kinge com þat word into winchæstre þat and weoren mid ferde icumen hær þe king cleopede vther þe wes his leoue broþer vther bed uerde ȝeond al þissen ærde and far to ure feonden and drif heom of ærde oþer þu heom fusen oþer þu heom feolle ich wolde faren æc ȝif ich neore swa seoc ah ȝif ich mai beon feore ich þe cumen after sone al dude swa þe king him sæide þer and passen at seint deowi sorȝen iworhte þerbi and þe king muchel sorȝe he dude þær brutlond heo þurharnden hærȝede and barden and vther i þissen ærde sumnede his ferde and hit wes longe uirst ær he mihte fusen ariht and west walisc lond set an his aȝere hond hit wes an ane dæie his duȝeþe weoren bliþe þer com faren appas feondes hine væreden to he quaþ þus cum hidere to us ich þe wulle telle of ane wilspalle ich was at winchæstre at þine wiþeriwinnen þer liþ þe king seoc and sorhful an heorten what scal beon mi mede ȝif ic þider ride and ich þe swa iqueme þat ich hine aquele þa andswarede passen and toward appase went ich bihate þe todæi an hundred pund for ic mæi ȝif þu me iquemest þat þu hine aquelle treoþen he plihten þesne swikedom to dihten appas eode to bure and þesne balu mæinde he wes an hæþene gume ut of saxlonde icume muneckes claþes he nom an he scar his crune ufenen he nom him tweien iueren and forþ he gon fusen and wende anan rihte into winchæstre swulc hit weore an hali mon þe hæþene deouel he wende to þan burhȝate þer þe king on bure lai and gratte þene dureward godes grætinge and bad hine an hiȝinge gan in to þan kinge and suggen him to soþe þat vther his broþer hæfde him þider isend seolne læche þene bezste læche þe wunede an æi londe þe auerælcne sucne mon of ufele bringen con þus læh þe laþe mon leodene kinge for wes ifaren forþ mid his ferde no nauer vther hine ne isæh ne þider hine isende and þe king wende þat hit weore soþ and ilefde him inoh wha wolde wene þat he swike weore for an his bare liche he weorede ane burne þerufenen he hæfde ane ladliche here and seoþþen ane cule of ane blake claþe iblæcched he hæfede his licame swulc ismitte of cole he cneolede to þan kingge his spæche wes ful milde hail seo þu aþelest alre kingen hider me sende vther þe is þin aȝen broþer and ich al for godes luue æm to þe her icume for ich þe wulle helen and al hal makien for leofe godes sune ne ræche ich nane garsume no mede of londe no of seoluere no of golde ah ælche seocken ich hit do for luue of mine drihtene þis iherde þe king hit wes him swiþe iqueme ah whar is æuere æi mon a þisse middelærde þe þis wolde wenen þat he swiken weore he nom his glæsfat anan and þe king mæh þeron anne while after þan þat glæsfat an honden nom and sceoweden hit forþrihttes biforen þas kinges cnihtes and þus sæide anan appas þe haþene mon ȝif ȝe me wulleþ ileuen ær tomarwen eue þes king scal beon al hal ihaled an his willen þa weoren bliþe alle þa weoren i bure appas eoden in ænne bur and þat balu mæinde and dude þerto atter þa scamoiene hatte and com ut forþrihtes imong þa burhcnihtes and þan kinge he gon dæle muchel canele and gingiuere and licoriz he hom lefliche ȝef alle heo nomen þat lac and he heom alle biswac þeos swike feol a cneowe atforen þan leodkinge and þus saide him to lauerd nu þu scalt afon of þissen drinchen ane dæle þat scal beon þin hale and þe king up drong and þer þat atter he dronc anan swa he hafde idrunke þe leche hine adun læide þus seide appas to þan burcnihtes wreoþ nu wel þene king þat he ligge a swæting for ich sugge eou þurh alle þing al hal beoþ aure king and ich wulle to mine inne and speken wiþ mine monnen and to þere midnihte ich cume forþrihtes mid oþer lachecrafte þa sculleþ beon him liþe forþ wende þe swike þe king læi on sweuete appas to his inne and spec wiþ his monnen mid stilleliche rune bistal of þan tune to þere midnihte þa sende þa burhcnihtes sixe of heore monne to appases inne heo wenden hine to finden and longi hine to þan kinge þa wes he ifloȝen and feondes hine uæreden þa men aȝein comen þer þe king wunede and cudden i þan bure of appases fore þa mihte me iseon sorȝen inoȝe beon cnihtes feollen adun and ȝirnden heore dæþes þer wes muchel waning heortne graning þer wes moni reolic spel þer wes gumene iȝel heo leopen to þan bedde and þene king hedden þa ȝet he lai on sweouete and on muchele swate þæ cnihtes mid weope þene king awehten and heo him to cleopeden mid mildere steuene lauerd hu mid þe hu beoþ þine beorste for nu is ure læche ifaren buten laue iliþen ut of hirede for hæne us bilæued þe king heom ȝaf andsware al ic æm toswollen and þer nis nan oþer ræd nu nan ich wurþe dæd and ich bidde forþrihtes ȝe beoþ mine cnihtes þat ȝe græten vther þe is min aȝe broþer and biddeþ hine halden mi lond an onwalde godd seolf þurh alle þing lete hine beon god king and hateþ hine beon kene and æiwær riht deme wærcche uolke for fæder hænen to frouere þenne maie he halde lond an onwalde and nu todai þenne ich beo dæd nimeþ alle anne ræd and leteþ me ilenge riht to stanhenge þer liþ muchel of mine cunne þurh sæxen aqualde and ofsendeþ biscopes and bocilarede men mi gold and mi seoluer deleþ for mire saule and leggeþ me an æst ænde inne stanhenge næs þer nan oþer ræd þer iwarþ þe king dæd and al swa his men duden swa þe king demde inne wæles wes vther and herof næs naþing war neuere þurh nare liste herof naþing nuste naþeles he hafede mid him þene witeȝe aȝeineden þere uerde þe icumen wes to ærde vther lai inne wales in anne wilderne and fundede to uarene wiþ to fehten þa a þan auentime þe mone gon to scine wel neh al swa brihte swa þe sunnelihte þa isehȝen heo feorre ænne selcuþe sterre he wes brad he wes muchel he wes unimete of him comen leomen igastliche scinen þe steorre is ihate a latin comete com of þan steore a leome swiþe sturne at þeos leomen ende wes a drake hende of þes draken muþe leomen comen inohȝe ah tweien þer weoren muchele þere oþere vnimete þe an droh touward france þe oþer touward irlonde þe leome þe toward france droh he wes briht vnifoh to munt giu wæs iseȝen þa seolcuþe takne þe leome þa strehte westriht a seouen bæmen wes idiht þis isah vþer ah nas he noht herof war sær him wes an heorte and seolliche auæred swa wes al þat muchele folc þat wes in þere uerde vþer cleopede and bad hine cume to him and þus seide him to mid swiþe softe worden leoue freond fonde þiseoluen and sæie us of þan tacne þe we isæȝen habbeoþ for nat ich on worlde riche to whan hit scal iwurþen buten þu us raden aȝæn we moten riden sæt him stille longe ane stunde swulc he mid sweuene swunke ful swiþe heo seiden þe hit iseȝen mid heore aȝen æȝen þat ofte he hine wende swulc hit a wurem weore late he gon awakien þa gon he to quakien and þas word seide þa witeȝe wæilawæi wæilawæi a þissere worlderiche muchel is þa sorȝe þe isiȝen is to londe whær ært þu vther siten me biuoren her and ich þe wulle suggen of sorȝen inoȝen dæd is kingene aþelest swa is þe oþer þi broþer þe biswac mid his swikedome nu haueþ vortigernes cun aquald nu þu ært al ane of aþele þine cunne ah ne hope þu to ræde of heom þat liggeþ dede ah þenc of þe seoluen seolþen þe beoþ ȝiueþe for selde he aswint þe to himseolue þencheþ þv scalt wurþen god king and gumenene lauerd and þu to þere midnihte wepne þine cnihtes þat we i þan morȝenliht mæȝen come forþriht forn at meneue þer þu scalt fihten ær þu þenne wende sclæht þu scalt makien þu scalt beien slæ þer and and monie þusend of þan gumen þat beoþ mid heom hider icumen þat taken of þan steorre þe we isaȝen swa feorre soþ hit is leof þat tacnede þines broþer dæd biuoren þa steorre wes þæ drake elcches wurmes vnimake þat taken wes a þire half þat weore þu þiseolf þu scalt habben þis lond and þin æie beon muchel and strong swulche toknen beoþ uncuþe of þas draken muþe eoden tweien leomen wunder ane lihte þe an strehte feor soþ ut ouer france þat is an æiȝesful sune þat of þine licame scal cume þe scal moni kinelond mid compe biwinne and an ende he scal rede moniane þeode þe oþer leome þe strahte west wunder ane lihte þat biþ a dohter þa þe biþ swiþe deore þe leome gon
