striden a ueire seoue strengen þat beoþ seouen uæire sunen þe of þine dohter sculleþ cumen þe scullen moni kinelond biȝiten to heore aȝere hond heo sculleþ beon wel stronge a water and a londe nu þu hauest of me ihærde þe wule halpen swiþe uorþrihtes far to þine fihte and gon to slume swulc he wolde slæpen vp aras vþer nu he wes wis and war and hæhte his cnihtes to horse forþrihtes and hæhte heom biliue faren to meneue and alle heore fare græiþen alle heo scullen fehten i þan flokke biforen he hafde cnihtes wel icoren seouen þusend cnihte ohte men and wihte hafde he amidde cnihtes wel bihedde oþer seoue þusend selere þeinen hæ hede bæfte ohtere cnihten ahtene þusen ohtere kempen and of ganninde uolke swa feole þusend þat a nane spelle ne mihte heom na mon tellen forþ heo wenden biliue þat heo comen to meneue þer isah whar him com vther and hæhde his cnihtes to wepne forþrihtes and heo to biliue and gripen heore cniues and of mid here breches seolcuþe weoren heore leches and igripen an heore hond heore speren longe hengen an heore æxle mucle wiæxe þa sæide þe king a swiþe seollic þing her cumeþ vþer broþer he wule bidden mi griþ and noht fehten me wiþ þa formeste beoþ his sweines faren we heom toȝeines ne þurfen ȝe nauere rehchen þah ȝe slæn þa wrecchen for ȝif vther sune wulle her mi mon bicume and aȝeuen his fader richen ich hine wullen griþien and latten hine liuien and inne fæire benden læden hine to mine londe þe king wordede þus þa while him alomp wurs weoren vtheres cnihtes at þan tune forþrihtes leiden fur a þene tun and fehten biliue mid sweorden heom to rakeden and þa irisce weoren nakede þa iseȝen irisce men þat brutten wes an eornest feondliche heo fuhten and neoþeles heo feollen heo cleopeden on heore king whar ært þu niþing whi nult þu hider wenden þu lezst us her scenden and þin ifere isih us fallen here cumeþ us to halpe mid hahȝere strengþe þis iherde þerforen wes his heorte sær mid his irisce cnihten he com to þan fihte and passend vorþ mid him beien heo weoren uæie þa iseh vþer þat icumen wes þer to him he gon riden and smat hine i þere side þat þat spere þurhrade and þa heorte toglad hiȝendliche he hine biwent and oftoc and þas word sæide vther þe sele þu scalt abiden her cumeþ vther riden he smat hine uuenen þat hæued þat he adun halde and þat sweord putte in his muþ swulc mete him wes uncuþ þat þe ord of þan sworde wod in þere eorþe þa sæide vther liȝ nu þer nu þu hauest brutlond al bitald to þire hond swa þe is nu iræd þeron þu ært ded wikien ȝe scullen here þu and þin ifere and brukeþ wel brutlond for nu ic hit bitæche inc an hond þat ȝit maȝen toȝere mid us wunien here ne þurue ȝe nauere adrede wha eou scullen feden þus sæide vþer and seoþþe he arnde þer and drof irisce men ȝeond wateres and ȝeond fenes and sloh al þa uerde þe mid commen to ærde summe to þere sæ iwiten and leoppen in heore scipen mid wederen and mid wateren þær heo forferden þus heo ispædden her and nu wes þis feht idon and vther aȝen com and forþrihtes wende into winchæstre in are brade strete he igon mete þreo cnihtes and heore sweines cumen him toȝeines anan swa heo ine imette fæire heo hine igrætten hail seo þu vther þeos æþeles beoþ þin æȝen ded is kingene aþelest he þe haueþ iset an hond al his kinewurþe lond he bad þe beon a sele and þenchen on his saule þa weop vþer wunder ane swiþe vþer wende forþriht into winchæstre þa weoren him biforen wiþuten þere burȝe alle þa burhmen mid reouliche iberen sone swa heo hine iseȝen heo him to sæiden vther þin are nu and æueremare ure king we habbeoþ ilore wa is us þerfore þu weore his broþer nafde he nænne oþer no he nefde nenne sune þe mihte king bicumen ah nim þu þene kinehalm he is þe icunde and we þe wulleþ helpen and halden for lauerd mid wapnen and mid æhten and al ure mihte þis iherde vþer he wes wis and he wes war þat þer næs cost nan oþer seoþþen dæd wes his broþer he nom þenne kinehelm þe him bicom swiþe wel and he wurþliche iwarþ him to kinge and heold gode laȝe and his folc lufede imong þat he king wæs and his wikenares chæs him ætwende nuste he nauere whidere no nauere a worlderiche to whan he bicome wa wes þan kinge swa wes al his duȝeþe and alle his hirdmen þeruore murnende weoren þe king lette riden widen and siden he bad gold and gersume ælche farinde gume whaswa mihte finde an londe þerto he læide muchel lof ah ne herde he him nawhit of þa biþohte vther whæt him sæide ær in þan hereȝeonge inne walisc londe þer heo iseȝen þene drake ælches wurmes vnimake and he þohte of þan tacnen þe him tahte þe king wes swiþe særi and sorhful an heorte for ne les he næuere leouere mon seoþþen he wes an liuen neouere nenne oþer ne his broþer þe king lette wurchen tweien imaken tweien guldene draken al for luue swa swiþe he wilnede his cume þa þe draken ȝaru weoren þe oþer wes iuere wharswa he an ærde ladde his ferde he wes heremærke in auerælche happe þene oþerne he wurþliche ȝæf into winchæstre into þan biscopstole þer he stude haldeþ þerto he ȝef his gode spere þermid me sculde þene drake bere þenne me scolde halidom beren to processiun þis iseȝen bruttes þas draken þa weoren imaked þus æuer seoþþen heo cleopeden vther þe to hermærke þene drake bar þene nome heo him laiden on þet wes vþer an brutisc drakenhefd an englisc nu wes vther god king ah of nefde he na þing þis word iherde þer he norþ wunede and ebissa his wedbroþer and osa þe oþer þa sende þider and sette heom þer on his griþe and bitahte heom an honde sixti hiden of londe iherden ful iwis al hu hit ifaren wes of dæþe and of vtheres kinedome him to cleopede his cun þe wes aneoste nomen heom to ræde of heore alde dede þat heo wolden bi heore liue cristindom bilaue heo heolden husting and hæþene bicomen þa comen þer togadere of hengestes cunne fif and sixti hundred of heþene monnen sone wes þat word cuþ an ȝeond þan londe icud þat hengestes sune wes hæþene bicume and þas ilke gumen alle þa igriþed hæfuede sende his sonde into walisce londe after þan irisce þe vþer æturnen and after þan alemainen þe weoren awei idraȝene þa weoren to wude iwende þe while men sloh and huden heom wel iwhar þe while men sloh þat folc ut of wude teh and touward scotlonde beh auer þer comen ma and ma and ferden toward þa heo tosomme weoren iwende þa weoren þer þritti þusend wiþuten þa wifmen of hengestes cunnen heo nomen heore uerde and gunnen to farene and setten al an heore hond biȝeonden þere lond and þat leoden þer heo gunnen liþen ferde þer wes sellic and wenden riht to eouerwic and an ælche side þa burh gunnen biride and þa burh bilæien hæþene leoden and nomen hit al to heore honde forþ into scotlonde al þat heo iseȝen heo talden heore aȝen ah vþeres cnihtes þa weoren i þan castle wereden þene tun wiþinnen þat ne mihten heo næuere binnen ne iherde mon in nane stude lute men þat swa wel duden swa sone swa vþer of þissen þingen iwarþ war færde he bad stronge ȝeond al his kinelonde and he swiþe hiȝendliche ferde touward eouerwic ferde uorþriht anan þer him læi and his ferde fusde heom toȝeines wuruen heom togadere mid grimmere strengþe heowen hardliche hælmes gullen falewede feldes of fæie blode and þa heþene saulen helle isohten þa þes dæies ende bicom þa wes hit swa ufel idon þat þat hæþene uolc þa ufere hond hafeden and mid muchelere strengþe sturmden þa bruttes and driuen heom to ane munte þæ wes unimete stor and vþer mid his monnen teh to þan munte and hæuede iloren in fihte leofe his cnihtes fulle seouen hundred his hælp wes þa wurse þe munt hæhte dunian þe vther wes ufenan wes þe munt þurhwexen mid ane wude feiren þe king wes þer wiþinnen mid swiþe feole monnen and hine bilæi mid hæþene monnen niht and dæi bilæi hine al abuten wa wes þan brutten wa wes þan kinge vþer þat he nes ær wær þat he nefde an londe bet vnderstonde ofte heo eoden to ræde of swucchere neode hu heo mihten ouercumen hengestes sune þer wes an eorl ocht mon fuliwis cniht he wes wel idon he wes vþeres mon eorl of cornwaille cuþ he wes wide he wes swiþe wis mon of alle þinge wel idon to him saide vþer særi an heorten hail seo þu gumenene lauerd þu ært min aȝe mon and swiþe wel ich þe on þu ært cniht wel idon muchel is þi wisdom alle mine leoden ich don in þine ræden and alle we sculle wurchen after þine iwille þa heng his breowen adun þe king vther and stod him ful stille and bad suggen his iwille þa andswarede he wes hende ful iwis sæie me vther whi halst þu þin hafed adun nast þu þat godd ane is betere þene we al clæne he mai whamswa he wule wurþcipe bitachen bihate we him on liue þat we him nulleþ liȝe and leten we us ræden of ure misdeden ælc mon forþriht af alle his sunen nimen scrift ælc mon scriuen oþer swulc hit weoren his broþer and æuerælc god cniht nime on him muchel scrift and godde we scullen bihaten ure sunnen to beten and to þere midnihte ȝarkien us to fihten þeos hæþene hundes tælleþ us al ibunden hengestes sunæ weneþ þat we beon alle inumen heo liggeþ i þissen felden ihæled in heore telden heo beoþ swiþe werie iboren heore wepnen nu nan heo sculleþ slumen and seoþþen slæpen of us nabbeoþ heo nane kare þat we aȝen heom wulleþ faren to þere midnihte we sculleþ forþrihtes swiþelicche stille adun of þissen hulle na wurþe cniht swa god þat he scire æi word ne nauer nan hæleþ þat he horn blawe ac we scullen steppen heom to swa we stelen wolden ær heo wurþen iware we scullen heom amærre we scullen heom to teon and tidende tellen and æuerælc ocht mon sterkliche heom legge on and swa we scullen of londe driuen vnicunde and mid mihte of ure drihten bitellen ure irihten al þas ferde idude swa heom hauede ibede ælc mon forþrihte dude hine vnder scrifte bihehten god to donne and þat ufel to forgonne to þere midnihte wepnede heom cnihtes and auoremeste uerde adun vþer and his cnihtes alle swiþeliche stille and smiten i þa waldes imong alle þa teldes and sloȝen þa hæþene mid hæhȝere strenþe fluȝen ȝeond þan feldes falewe lockes uolken hit wes ærmest heo droȝen heore þermes mid muchele vnisunde heo feollen to þan grunde þer wes forþriht inume hengestes sune and his wedbroþer ebissa and his iuere þe king heom lette binden mid irene bænde and bitahte heom sixti cnihten þe gode weoren to fihten ufennen þan walden uaste to halden and he seolf draf him forþ and muchel dune makede and þe hende uorþ an oþer ende and alle heore cnihtes æuere forþrihtes adunrihtes sloȝen al þat heo neh comen summe heo crupen to þan wude an heore bare cneowen heo weoren amærȝe volken alre ærmest wes ibunden and ilad to lunden and ebissa and nes heom nauere al swa wa þis feht wes idon and þe king wende forþ into norþhumbre mid hæȝere blisse and seoþþen to scotlonde and sette hit al his aȝere hond he sette griþ he sette friþ þat ælc mon mihte faren wiþ from londe to londe þeh he bere gold an honde of griþ he dude swulc þing þat ne mihte næuer ær na king from þan ilke time þat bruttes comen her liþen and seoþþen vmbe stunde he ferde to lunden he wes þere an æstre mid aþele his uolke bliþe wes þe lundenes tun for vthere he sende his sonde ȝeond al his kinelonde he bæd þa eorles he bæd þa cheorles he bæd þa biscopes þa bocilærede men þat heo comen to lunden to vþer þan kingen into lundenes tun to vþer riche men sone to lundene comen heo brohten wif heo brohten child swa hehte vther þe king mid muchele godnæsse þe king iherde mæsse and þe eorl of cornwale and mid him cnihtes uale muche blisse wes i þan tun mid vþer kinge þa þe mæsse wes isungen to halle heo þrungen bemen heo bleowen bordes heo brædden al þat folc æt and dronc and blisse heom wes imong þer sæt vþer þe king an his hæh setle forn aȝan him hende cniht ful iwis þe eorl of cornwale mid aþele his wife þa heo weoren alle iseten eorles to heore mete þe king sende his sonde to þere hende eorles wif wifmone alre hendest ofte he hire lokede on and leitede mid eȝene ofte he his birles sende fron to hire borde ofte he hire loh to and makede hire letes and heo hine leofliche biheold ah inæt whær heo hine luuede næs þe king noht swa wis ne swa ȝærewitele þat imong his duȝeþe his þoht cuþe dernen swa longe þe king þis him droh þat iwærþ him wraþ and him gromede swiþe wiþ þene king for his wife þe eorl and his cnihtes arisen forþrihtes and forþ mid þan wife cnihtes swiþe whraþe vther king þis isah and herefore særi wes and nom him forþrihtes twælf wise cnihtes and sende after gumenene ældere and beden hine an hiȝinge cumen to þan kinge and don þan kinge god riht and beon icnowen of his pliht þat he hafde þene king iscend and from his borde wes iwende he and his cnihtes mid muchele vnrihte for þe king him wæs glad wiþ and for he hailede in his wif and ȝif he nalde aȝein cumen and his gult beon icnawen þe king him wold after and don al his mahten binimen him al his lond and his seoluer and his gold þis iherde gumenene lauerd and he andsware ȝaf eorlene wraþest næi swa me helpe drihte þa iscop þas daȝes lihte nulle ich nauere aȝæn cumen no his griþ ȝirnen ne scal he neuere on liue me scende of mine wife and suggeþ vþer kinge at tintaieol he mai me finden ȝif he þider wule ride þer ich him wulle abiden and þer he scal habbe hærd gome and mucle weorldes scome forþ wende þe eorl ire on his mode he wes wærþ wiþ þene king wunder ane swiþe and þretede vther þene king and alle his þeines mid him ah he nuste whæt com seoþþe sone þeræfter þe eorl anan wende into cornwaille he hafde þer tweie castles biclused swiþe uaste þæ castles aþele weore of his eoldrene istreon to tintaieol he sende his leofmon þa wes hende ihaten wifene aþelest and heo biclusde uæste inne þan castle wes særi and sorhful an heorte þat swa moni mon for hire sculden habben þer lure þe eorl sende sonde ȝeond al brutlonde and bæd alcne ohte gome þat he him sculde to cume for gold and for seolure and for oþere ȝiuen gode þat heo ful sone to tintaieole comen and his aȝene cnihtes comen forþrihtes þa heo togædere weoren sele þeines þa hafde he fulle fiftene þusend and heo tintaieol faste bitunden uppen þere sæstronde tintaieol stondeþ he is mid sæcliuen faste biclused þat ne biþ he biwunne þurh nanes cunnes monnen bute ȝif hunger cumen þer anvnder þe eorl uerde þenne mid seouen þusend monnen and wende to ane oþere castle and biclusde hine ful uæste and bilefde his wif in tintaieol mid ten þusend monnen for ne þurue þa cnihtes dæies na nihtes buten biwiten þat castelȝat and careles liggen slæpen and þe eorl wuste þene oþer and mid him his aȝen broþer þis iherde vther þe king wes swiþe steorc þat his eorl his ferde hafde igadered and wolde halde weorre mid muchelere wraþþe þe king bad his ferde ȝeond al þissen ærde and ȝeond al þan londe þa stoden an his honde monies kinnes leoden liþen heom togæderes and comen to lundene to þan leodkinge ut of lundene tun ferde vþer he and his cnihtes ferde uorþrihtes swa longe þat heo comen into cornwæille and ouer þat water heo tueoȝen þat hatten tambreis riht to þan castle þer heo wusten mid muchelere læþe þene castel heo bilæien ofte heo toræsden mid ræȝere strengþe tosomne heo leopen leoden þer feollen fulle seouen nihte þe king mid his cnihten bilæi þene castel his men þer hafeden sorȝen ne miste he of þan eorle naþing iwinnen and alle þa seouen nihte ilaste þat selliche feoht þa iseh vþer king þat him ne spedde naþing ofte he hine biþohte whæt he don mahte for him wes swa leof æfne alse his aȝen lif and him wes on leoden monnen alre læþest and ælches weies him wes wa a þissere weorlderiche for he ne mihte beon wurþe naþing of his wille þa wes mid þan kinge an ald mon swuþe hende he wes a swiþe riche þein and ræh on ælche dome he wes ihaten vlfin muche wisdom wes mid him þe king bræid up his chin and bisah an vlfin swiþe he murnede his mod wes iderued þa quaþ vþer to ulfin þan cnihte ulfin ræd me sumne ræd oþer ich beo ful raþe dæde swa swiþe me longeþ þat ne mai i noht libben after þere faire þis word halt me derne for ulfin þe leoue aþele þine lare lude and stille don ich heom wulle þa andswarede ulfin þan kinge þet spac wiþ him nu ihere ich muche seollic ænne king suggen þu luuest and halst hit swa deorne þe wifmon is þe to leof and hire lauerd al to laþ his lond þu forbernest and hine blæþ wurchest and þrattest hine to slænne and his cun to fordonne wenest þu mid swulche hærme to biȝeten þenne heo sculde don swa ne deþ na wifman mid æie vnimete halden luue swete ah ȝif þu luuest þu sculdest hit halden derne and senden hire sone of seoluere and of golde and luuien hire mid liste and mid leofliche bihæste þa ȝet hit weore a wene whar þu heo mihtes aȝe for is wel idon a swiþe treowe wimmon swa wes hire moder and ma of þan kunne to soþe ich þe suggen leofest alre kinge þat oþere weies þu most aginnen ȝif þu hire wult awinnen for ȝurstendæi me com to an æremite wel idon and swor bi his chinne þat he wuste whar he ælche nihte resteþ vnder lufte and ofte he him spæc wiþ and spelles him talde and ȝif we mihte mid liste biwinnen þenne mihtest þu þine iwille allunge biwinne þa wes vþer þa softer an his mode and ȝaf andsware red vlfin þu hauest wel isæd ich þe ȝiue an honde þritti solh of londe þat þu biwinne and don mine iwille vlfin ȝeond þat folc wende and sohte al þa uerde and he vmbe stunde þene æremite funde and an hiȝinge brohte hine to þan kinge and þe king him sette an hond seouen sulȝene lond ȝif he mihte bringen to þan kinge þe æremite gon wende in þene west ænde to ane wilderne to ane wude muchele þer he iwuned hafde wel feole wintre and swiþe ofte þerinne sohte sone þe armite com in þa ifunde he vnder ane treo stonden and sære him gon longen þene æremite he isæh cume alse while wes his iwune he orn him toȝænes beiene heo uæineden þas heo clupten heo custen and cuþliche speken þa sæide muchel wisdom wes mid him sæie þu mi leofe freond wi naldest þu me suggen þurh nanes cunnes þinge þat þu wældest to þan kinge ah ful ȝare ich hit wuste anan swa ich þe miste þat þu icumen weore to vþere kinge and what þe king þe wiþ spæc and of his londe þe bæd þat þu me sculdest bringe to vþer kinge and vlfin þe sohte and to þan kinge brohte and vþer forþrihtes anan sette him an honde þritti solh of londe and he sætte þe an honde seoue sulhȝene lond vther is oflonged æfter þere hende wunder ane swiþe after wiue ah longe is æuere þat ne cummeþ nauere þat he heo biwinne bute þurh mine ginne for nis na wimmon treowere in þissere worlderiche and neoþeles he scal aȝe þa hende on hir he scal streonen þat scal wide sturien he scal streonien hire on ænne swiþe sellichne mon longe beoþ æuere dæd ne biþ he næuere þe wile þe þis world stænt ilæsten scal is worþmunt and scal inne rome walden þa þæines al him scal abuȝe þat wuneþ inne bruttene of him scullen gleomen godliche singen of his breosten scullen æten aþele scopes scullen of his blode beornes beon drunke of his eȝene scullen fleon furene gleden ælc finger an his hond scarp stelene brond scullen stan walles biuoren him tofallen beornes scullen rusien reosen heore mærken þus he scal wel longe liþen ȝeond londen leoden biwinnen and his laȝen sette þis beoþ þa tacnen of þan sune þe cumeþ of and of þes speche is ful derne for ȝet næt hit neoþer no þat of vþere scal arisen swilc a sune for ȝet he beoþ unstreoned þa sturieþ al þa þeoden ah lauerd quaþ nu hit is iwille þin þat forþ i scal fusen to uerde þas kinges þi word ich wulle heren and nu ich wulle wende and faren ich wulle for þire lufe to vthere and habben þu scalt þat lond þat he þe sette an hond þus heo þa ispecken þæ æremite gon to weopen deorliche he hine custe þer heo gunnen dælen ferde riht suþ þat lond him wæs ful cuþ forþriht he fusde to þes kinges ferde sone swa vþer hine isæh swa he him toȝeines bæh and þus quaþ vþer þu ært wilcume her ich sette þe an honde al þene ræd of mine londe and þat þu me ræde to muchere neode vther him talde al þat he walde and hu him wes on leoden wimmonnen leofest and hire lauerd monnenen alre laþest and buten ich habbe þinne ræd ful raþe þu isihst me dæad þa andswerede let nu cume in vlfin and bitæc him an honde þritti sulȝene lond and bitæc þan æremite þat þu him bihete for nulle ich aȝæn na lond neouþer seoluer na gold for ich am on rade rihchest alre monnen and ȝif ich wilne æhte þenne wursede ich on crafte ah al þin iwille wel scal iwurþen for ich con swulcne lechecraft þe leof þe scal iwurþen þat al scullen þine cheres iwurþen swulc þas eorles þi speche þi dede imong þere duȝeþe þine hors and þine iwede and al swa þu scalt ride þenne þe scal iseon a mode hire scal wel beon heo liþ inne tintaieol uaste bituned nis nan cniht swa wel iboren of nane londe icoren þe mid strengþe of tintaieol þe ȝeten mihten untunen buten he weoren ibirsted mid hungere and mid þurste þat is þat soþe þat ich þe sugge wulle þurh alle þinge þu scalt beon swulc þu eorl weore and ich wulle beon iwil del swulc him is þat is a cniht swiþe herd he is þeos eorles stiward iurdan is his burcniht he is swiþe wel idiht ich wulle makien anan ulfin swulc is iurdan þenne bist þu lauerd and ich þi stiward and ulfin iurdan þi burcniht and we scullen faren nu toniht faren þu scalt bi ræde wuderswa ich þe læde scullen nu tonihte half hundred cnihten mid speren and mid scelden beon abuten þine telden þat nauere nan quik mon ne cumen þer aneosten and ȝif þer aueræi mon cume þat his hæued him beon binumen for þa cnihtes scullen suggen selen þine beornen þat þu ært ilete blod and restest þe on bædde þas þingges forþrihte þus weoren idihte forþ ferde þe king næs hit cuþ naþing and ferden forþ mid him vlfin and he tuȝen riht þen wæi þa into tintaieol læi heo comen to þas castles ȝæte and cuþliche cleopeden vndo þis ȝætessel þe eorl is icumen here þe læuerd and britael his stiward and iurdan þe burcniht we habbeoþ ifaren al niht þe ȝæteward hit cudde oueral and cnihtes urnen uppen wal and speken wiþ and hine icneowen mid iwis þa cnihtes weoren swiþe whæte and wefden up þa castles ȝæte and letten hine binnen fare þa læsse wes þa heore care heo wenden mid iwisse to habben muchel blisse þa hædden heo mid ginne þer wiþinne and heolden vþer þene king wiþinne heore walding and ledde þer mid him his gode þein ulfin þis tidinde com biliue in to þan wife þæt hire læuerd wes icumen and mid him his þreo gumen vt com forþ to þan eorle and þas word seide mid wunsume wurde wilcume læuerd monne me leofest and wilcume iurdan and britael is alswa beo ȝe mid isunde todæled from þan kinge þa quæþ vþer ful iwis swulc hit weore muchel þat monkun þæt is mid vther and ich æm bi nihte bistole from þan fihte for æfter þe ic wes oflonged wifmonne þu ært me leofuest buþ into bure and let mi bed makien and ich me wulle ræsten to þissere nihte uirste and alle dai tomærwe to blissien mire duȝeþe beh to bure and lætte bed him makien wes þat kinewurþe bed al mid palle ouerbræd þe king hit wel bihedde and eode to his bedde and læi adun bi nu wende ful iwis þat hit weoren þurh neuere nænes cunnes þing no icneou heo vþer þene king þe king hire wende to swa wapmon sculde to wimmon do and hæfde him to done wiþ leofuest wimmonne and he streonede hire on ænne selcuþne mon kingen alre kenest þæ æuere com to monnen and he wes on ærde ihaten nuste noht wha læie on hire ærme for æuere heo wende ful iwis þat it weoren þe eorl næs þer na mære uirst buten þat hit wes dæiliht þer forþrihtes vnderȝeten þa cnihtes þat þe king wes iuaren ut of þere uærde þa sæiden þa cnihtes soþ þæh hit neoren þat þe king wes ifloȝen mid ærhþen afeolled ah al hit wes lessinge þat heo seiden bi þan kinge herof heo heolden muchel run uppen vþer þa seiden þa eorles and þa hæhste beornes nu þenne hit wat hu hit iuaren is þat ure king is ifaren and his ferde bilæiued he wule forþrihtes wepni his cnihtes and ut he wule to fihten and feollen us to grunden mid woden his þeines muchel wæl makien þenne weore us beteren þat we iboren neoren ah leten we blawen bemen and bonnien ure uerde and þe kene scal beren þas kinges marke hæbben haȝe þene drake biforen þissere duȝeþe and faren to þan castle mid kene ure folke and þe eorl scal beon ure aldre and we him scullen here swulc hit þe king weoren and swa we scullen mid rihte wiþ fihten and ȝif he us wule speken wiþ and ȝernen þis kinges griþ setten sæhtnusse mid æþen soþfæste þenne maȝen we mid wurþscipen heonene iwenden þenne nabbeoþ ure æfterlinges nane upbreidinges þat we for ærhscipe heonene atærnden al þat leodliche folc bilufde þesne ilke ræd bemen heo bleowen bonneden uærden up heo hafden þene drake ælches mærken vnimake þer wes moni bald scalc þe sceld weiden on sculdre moni þein kene and wenden to þan castle wes wiþinnen mid kene his monnen he lette blawen beomen and bonnien his ferden leopen an steden cnihtes gunnen riden þæs cnihtes weoren swiþe wate and wenden ut at þan ȝate tosomne heo comen sone fastliche heo onsloȝen feolle fæie men uolden isohten þer wes muche blodgute balu wes on folke imong þan fihte ful iwis mon sloh þene eorl þa gunnen his men fleon and þa oþere after teon heo comen to þan castle and binnen heo þrasten sone hit comen binnen ba twa þa uerden þer ileste þat fiht þurh þene dæiliht ær þe dai weore al asceken wes þe castel biȝeten næs þer nan swa wracche swein þat he nes a wel god þein comen þa tidinde into tintageol an hiȝende forþ into þan castle þer vþer wes inne þat islaȝen wes ful iwis þe eorl heore læuerd and alle his heregumen and his castel inumen þis iherde þe king þer he læi an skentting and leop ut of bure swulc hit an liun weore þa quaþ þe king vþer of þissen tiþende he wes wær beoþ stille beoþ stille cnihtes inne halle here ich æm ful iwis eore læuerd and iurdan mi burward and mi stiward ich and þas tweie cnihtes leopen ut of þan fihte and hider in we beoþ idraȝen neore we noht þere islaȝen ah nu ich wulle fusen and sumnien mine ferde and ich and mine cnihtes scullen al bi nihte faren in ænne tun and imeten vþer and buten he of sæhnesse speken ich wulle me wurþliche awrake and ȝe þesne castel bicluseþ swiþe uaste and hateþ me þat heo noht ne murne nu ich fare forþriht habbeoþ alle gode niht biforen ferde and þe þein vlfin and seoþþen ut of tintageolestun æuere heo uerden alle niht þat hit wes dæiliht þa com he to þan ærde þer læi his ferde hafde a þene king his wlite iset þurh alle þing þa icneowen cnihtes heore kinelauerd þer wes moni oht mid blissen afeolled þa weoren inne bruttene blissen inoȝe hornes þer bleowen gleomen gunnen gleowen glad æuerælch cniht al mid pælle biþæht þreo dæies wes þe king wuniende þere and þan feorþe dæie to tintaieol he wende he sende to þan castle his selest þeines and grætte wifuene aþelest and sende hire taken whæt heo i bedde speken hehte heo þat heo aȝeuen þene castel biliue þer nes nan oþer ræd for hire lauerd wes dæd ȝet wende þat hit soþ weoren þat þe dæde eorl isoht hafede his duȝeþe and al heo ilæfde þat hit læs weore þat þe king vþer æuere weoren icumen her cnihtes eoden to ræde cnihtes eoden to rune radden þat heo nalden þene castel lengere halden heore brugge heo duden adun and bitahte hine vþer þa stod al þis kinelond æft an vtheres hond þer vþer þe king nom to quene wes mid childe bi vþer kinge al þurh wiȝel ær heo biwedded weore þe time com þe wes icoren þa wes iboren sone swa he com an eorþe aluen hine iuengen heo bigolen þat child mid galdere swiþe stronge heo ȝeuen him mihte to beon bezst alre cnihten heo ȝeuen him anoþer þing þat he scolde beon riche king heo ȝiuen him þat þridde þat he scolde longe libben heo ȝifen him þat kinebern custen swiþe gode þat he wes metecusti of alle quike monnen þis þe alue him ȝef and al swa þat child iþæh æfter wes iboren þeo ædie burde heo wes ihaten æne þat ædien maiden and seoþþen heo nom loþ þe leones ahte heo wæs inne leodene læfdi longe liuede vþer mid muchelere blisse her mid gode griþe mid gode friþe freo on kinedome þa þe he wes ald mon þa com him ufel on þat vfel hine læide adun seoc wes vþer swa he wes here seoc seoue ȝere þa iwurþen bruttes swiþe unbalded heo duden ofte unwræste al for æieleste þe ȝet læi ibunden in þe quarterne of lunden hengestes sune þa at eouerwic wes inume and his iueren ebissa and his oþer heom biuusten twælf cnihtes dæies and nihtes þa weoren weri oflæien inne lundenne iherde suggen of seocnesse þas kinges and spac wiþ þa wardesmen þe hine witen scolden hærcneþ me nu cnihtes þat ich eou wulle cuþen we liggeþ here i lundene uaste ibunden and ȝe monienne longne dæi ouer us ilæien habbeoþ bettere us weoren to libben inne sexlonde mid muchele richedome þene þus reouliche here and ȝif ȝe wolden iwurþen and don mine iwille ich eou wolden ȝiuen lond muchel seoluer and gold þat a ȝe mihten riche rixlien in þan londe and eoure lif libben swa eou biþ alre leofuest for no biden ȝe nauere ȝiuen gode of vþer kinge for nu ful raþe he biþ dæd and his duȝeþen al bilæueþ þenne nabben ȝe nouþer þat an no þat oþer ah biþenche eou ohte men and doþ us eoure mildze on and þencheþ whæt eou weoren leof ȝif ȝe þus ibunden leien and mihten in eouwer londe libben inne winne swiþe ofte wiþ þæs cnihtes spac swa cnihtes gunnen runen cnihtes gunnen ræden to heo seiden ful stille we scullen don þine iwille aþes heo sworen swiken þat heo nalden hit wæs in ane nihte þat þe wind wende rihte forþ iwenden cnihtes to þere midnihte and ledden uorþ and ebissa and after þere temese tuhten forþ into þere sæ forþ heo iwenden into sæxlonden heore cun heom com aȝeines mid mucle flockes heo liþen ȝeond þan leoden swa heom wes alre leofuest me heom bitahte lond me ȝæf heom seoluer and gold hine biþohte whæt he don mahte he þohten hider wenden and wræken his fader wunden ferden heo biȝæten of folke vnimete to þere sa heo wenden mid muchele þrætte to scotlonde heo comen sone heo fusden alond and mid fure hit igrætten sæxes weoren ræie scottes heo sloȝen mid fure heo adun læiden þritti hundred tunes scottes heo sloȝen moni and unifoȝen comen þa tidende to vþer kinge vþer wes swiþe wa and wunderliche ihærmed and senden into loæines to leofen his freonden and grette lot his aþum and hehte hine beon an sund and hahte hine nimen an his hond al his kinewurþe lond chihtes and freomen and freoliche heom halden and leden heom to ferde swa laȝen beoþ an ærde and he hæhte his cnihtes leoue beon hærsume loþe mid leofliche læten swulc he weoren leodene king for lot wes swiþe god cniht and hafde ihalden moni fiht and he wes metecusti æueralche monne he bitahten him þa warde of alle þissen ærde heold muche vnfriþ and lot faht him ofte wiþ and ofte he ahte biȝæt and ofte he heom losede bruttes hafden muchel mode and vnimete prute and weoren æielese for þas kinges alde and lætten swiþe hokerliche of lote þan eorle and duden swiþe vnwraste alle his haste and weoren alle twiræde heore teone wes þa mare þis wes isæid sone seocken þan kinge þat his hæȝe men lot al forhoȝeden nu ich þe wulle tellen a þissen bocspællen hv vþer þe king uundede hine seolven he sæide þat he wolde wende to his ferde and mid his eȝene iseon wæ þer wolde wel don he lette makien þere gode horsebere and letten beoden uerde ȝeond al his kineærde þat ælc mon bi his liue comen to him swiþe bi heore liue and bi heore leme to wræken þas kinges scome and ȝif þær is æi gume þæt nulle hiȝenliche cume ich wulle hine hiȝenliche fordon oþer slæn oþer anhon alle ful sone to hirede heo comen no durste þær bilæuen na þæ uatte no þe læne þe king forþrihtes nom alle his cnihtes and ferde him anan to þan tune of verolam abuten uerolames tun com him vþer wes wiþinnen mid alle his monnen þa wes verolam a swiþe kinewurþe hom seint alban wes þer islæȝen and idon of lifdæȝen þe burh wes seoþþe foruaren and muchel folc þer wes islæȝen vþer lai wiþuten and wiþinnen vþeres ferde fusde to wale ræsden to feondliche þeines riche ne mihte heo of þan walle ænne stan falle no mid nare strengþe þene wal amærre wælle bliþe wes þæ hangestes sune þa he isæh bruttes buȝen from walle and sorhful wenden aȝæin to heore telden þa sæide to his iueren ebissa her is icumen to verolam vþer þe lome mon and wulle wiþ us here fihten in his bære he wænde mid his crucche us adun þrucche ah tomærȝe wæne hit dæi buþ duȝeþe scal arisen and oppenien ure castelȝæten þas riche we scullen al biȝeten ne scullen we nauære here liggen for ane lomme monne ut we scullen riden uppen ure steden goden and to fusen and his folc fællen for alle heo beoþ fæie þat hider beoþ iridenen and nimen þene lome mon and leggen in ure benden and halden þene wræcche a þat he forwurþe and sa me scal lacnien his leomes þat beoþ sare and his ban rihten mid bitere stelen þus him ispac wiþ his iuere ebissa ah al hit iwraþ oþer þene heo iwenden amarȝe þa hit daȝede duren heo untunden up aras ebissa and and hehten heore cnihtes ȝarkien heom to fihte vndon her brade ȝæten burȝen untunen him ut ræd and muche folc him after glæd mid balden his beornen þer he bælu funden vþer him þis isæh þat heom to bæh and þohten his ferde feolen to grunde þa cleopede mid quickere stefene þer wær beo ȝe bruttes balde mine þeines nu is icumen þe ilke dæi þe drihten us helpen mai þat scal ifinden þat he þrættede me to binden iþencheþ on eoure aldren hu gode heo weoren to fehten iþencheþ þene wurþscipe þat ich eou habbe wel biwiten ne læten ȝe næuere þas hæþene bruken eoure hames þæs ilke awedde hundes walden eouwere londes and ich wullen bidden drihten þat scop þæs dæies lihten and alle þaie halȝen þa an hæfene hæhȝe sitteþ þar ich on þissen felde mote beon ifroured nu fuseþ heom to swiþe fulste eou drihten þe alwaldinde god biwiten mine þeines cnihtes gunnen riden gæres gunnen gliden breken bræde speren brusleden sceldes helmes þer scenden scalkes feollen þe bruttes weoren balde and bisie to fihten and þa hæþene hundes hælden to grunde þer wes islaȝen ebissa and þer seouentene þusend siȝen into helle feole þer atwenden touward þan norþ enden al þene dæilihte vþeres cnihtes sloȝen and nomen al þat heo neh comen þa hit wes eauen þa wes hit al biwunnen þa sunggen hiredmen mid hæȝere strengþe and þæs word sæiden inne murie heore songen her is vþer icume to verolames tun and he hæfueþ idubbed swa and ebissa and and itah heom a londen laȝen swiþe stronge þat men maȝen tellen heore cun to spelle and þerof wurchen songes inne sæxlonde þa wes vþer bliþe and igladed swuþe and spac wiþ his duȝeþe þe deore him wes an heorte and þas word sæide vþer þe alde sexisce men me habbeoþ for hene ihalden mine unhæle me atwiten mid heore hokerworden for ich wes here ilad inne horsebere and sæiden þat ich wes ded and mi duȝeþe aswunden and nu is muchel sellic isiȝen to þissere riche þat nu haueþ þeos dede king þas quiken aqualden and summe he heom flæmde uorþ mid þan wedere nu iwurþen herafter drihttenes wille fluȝen sæxisce men feondliche swiþe þe weoren bihalues ihalden from þan fihte forþ heo gunnen scriþen into scotlonde and nomen heom to kinge þene hende he wes hængestes mæie and monnen him leofuest and hine lufede þæ while þe he leouede weoren þa saxisce men swiþe iswunten and iscriþen heom tosomne into scotlonde and þene hende heo makeden to kinge and sumneden færde wide ȝeond þan ærde and sæiden þat heo wolden mid heore wiþercraften inne winchastre tun quellen vþer wa la wa þat hit sculde iwurþen swa nu sæiden saxisce men in heore somrunen nime we six cnihtes wise men and wihte hæweres witere and senden we to hirede læten heom uorþ liþen an almesmonnes wisen and wunien an hirede mid heȝe þan kinge and æuerælche dæie þurhgon al þa duȝeþe and gan to þas kinges dale swulc heo weoren vnhale and imong þan wracchen harcnien ȝeorne ȝif mon mihte mid crafte a dæi oþer a nihte inne winchæstres tun cumen to vþer and mid morþspelle þene king aquellen þenne weoren heore iwil allunge iwurden þenne weoren heo carelæse of cunne nu wenden forþ þa cnihtes al bi dæies lihten on ælmesmonnes claþes cnihtes forcuþest to þas kinges hirede þer heo hærm wrohten heo eoden to þære dale swulc heo weoren unhale and hærcneden ȝeornen of þas kinges hærme hu me þæne king mihte to dæþe idihte þa imetten heo enne cniht from þan kinge he com riht he wes vþeres mæi and monnen him leofuest þas swiken þer heo sæten onlongen þere streten cleopeden to þan cnihte mid cuþliche worden lauerd we beoþ wracche men a þissere weorlderiche while we weoren on londe for gode men iholden a þat sæxisce men setten us adune and al biræiueden us and ure æhten binomen us nu we beden singeþ for vþer kinge ælche dæie on a mæl ure mete trukeþ ne cumeþ nauere inne ure disc neoþer flæs ma no fisc no nanes cunnes drænc buten water scenc buten water clæne for þi we beoþ þus læne þis iherde þe cniht aȝæn he eode forþriht and com to þan kinge þer he lai on bure and seide to þan kinge lauerd beo þu on sunde herute sitteþ six men iliche on heouwen alle heo beoþ iferen iscrudde mid heren while heo weoren a þissere worlderichen godfulle þeines mid goden afeolled nu habbeoþ sæxisce men isæt hom to grunden þat heo beoþ on weorlde for wracchen ihalden no raccheoþ heo to borde buten bræd ane no to heore drencches bute water scenches þus heo leodeþ heore lif inne þire leode and heore beoden biddeþ þat godd þe lete longe libben þa quaþ vþer þe king let heom cumen hider in ich heom wulle scruden and ich heom wulle ueden for mines drihtenes lufe þa wille þa ich liuie comen into bure beornes þa swikele þe king heom lette feden þæ king heom lette scruden and nihtes hom læiden ælc on his bedde and ælc on his halue heoȝede ȝeorne hu heo mihten þene king mid morþe aquellen ah ne mihten heo þurh naþing aquellen vþer þene king ne þurh nane crafte cumen to him ne mahten þa iwærd hit in ane time þe ræin him gon rine þa cleopede þer a læche þer he læi on bure to ane burcnihte and hahte hine forþrihtes irne to þere welle þe wes onvæst þere halle and setten þere ænne ohte swain to biwiten heo wiþ ræin for þe king ne mai on duȝeþe bruken nanes drenches buten cald welles stræm þat him is iqueme þat is to his ufele aþelest alre drencche þas speche uorþrihtes iherden þas six cnihtes to harme heo weoren wiþte and ut wenden bi nihte forþ to þere welle þer ho hærm wrohten vt heo droȝen sone amppullen scone ifulled mid attere weten alre bitterest six amppullen fulle heo ȝeoten i þan welle þa wes þa welle anan al mid attre bigon þa weoren ful bliþe þæ swiken on heore liue and forþ heo iwenden ne dursten heo þer bilæfen þa comen þer forþrihtes tweien burcnihtes heo beren on heore honde twæie bollen of golde heo comen to þare welle and heore bollen feolde aȝæin heo gunnen wende to vþer þan kinge forþ into þan bure þer he læi on bedde hail seo þu vþer nu we beoþ icumen her and we habbeoþ þe ibroht þat þu ær bedde cæld welle water bruc hit on wunne vp aras þe seocke king and sat on his bedde of þan watere he dronc and sone he gon sweten his heorte gon to wakien his neb bigon to blakien his wombe gon to swellen þe king gon to swelten næs þer nan oþer ræd þer wes vþer king dæd alle heo iwurþen dede þat drunken of þan watere þa þat hired isah þat sorhȝen of þan kinge and of þas kinges monnen þe mid attre weoren fordone þa wenden to þere welle cnihtes þe weoren snælle and þa welle forduden mid derfulle swincche mid eorþe and mid stanen stepne hul makeden þa nomen þa duȝeþe þene king dede vnimete uolc and forþ hine uereden stiþimodede men in to stanhengen and hine þer bureden bi leofen his broþer side bi side beiene heo þer liggeþ þa com hit al togadere þat hæhst wes on londe eorles and beornes and bocilarede men heo comen to lundene to muchelere hustinge nomen heom ro rade þeines riche þat heo wolden ouer sæ senden sonde into bruttainne after bezst alre ȝeoȝeþe þa a þissere weorldenriche a þan dæȝen weore ihaten bezst alre cnihten and suggen þat he cumen sone to his kinedome for dæd him wes vþer alswa wes ær and vþer nefde nenne oþerne sune þat mihte after his daȝen halden bruttes to laȝe mid wurþscipe halden and þisne kinedom walden for ȝæt weoren in þissen londe sæxes atstonden þe kene and moni þusend of his iueren þa ofte ure bruttes makeden hufele burstes bruttes ful sone þreo biscopes nomen and ridæres seouene ræiȝe on wisdome forþ heo gunnen buȝen into bruttaine and heo ful sone to comen hail seo þu aþelest cnihten vþer þe græten þa he sculde iwiten and bæd þat þu sculdest a brutten þe seoluen halden laȝen rihte and hælpen þine folke and witen þisne kinedom swa god king sculden don þine feond flæmen and driuen heom of londen and he bad þe to fultume þene milde godes sune þat þu mostes wel don and þat lond of godde afon for dæd is vþer and þu ært his sune and dæd is þe oþer his broþer þus heo gunnen tellen and sæt ful stille ænne stunde he wes blac and on heuwe swiþe wak ane while he wes reod and reousede on heorte þa hit alles up brac hit wes god þat he spac þus him sæide þerriht þe aþele cniht lauerd godes sune beon us nu a fultume þat ich mote on life goddes laȝen halden fiftene ȝere wes ald þa þis tiþende him wes itald and alle heo weoren wel bitoȝen for he wes swiþe iþoȝe forþrihtes cleopede his cnihtes and hæhte æuerælcne mon bonnien his weppnen and heore hors sadelie hiȝendliche swiþe for he wolde buȝe to þissere brutene to þere sæ wenden sele þeines at mihæles munte mid muchelere uerede þa sæ heo sætten a þat strond at suþhamtune heo comen alond forþ him gon ride þe riche riht to selechæstre þer him sel þuhte þer wes bruttene weored baldeliche isomned muchel wes þa blisse þa com to burhȝe þer wes bemene blæst and swiþe glade beornes þer heo houen to kinge þene ȝunge þa þe wes king hærne nu seollic þing he wes metecusti ælche quike monne cniht mid þan bezste wunder ane kene he wes þan ȝungen for fader þan alden for frouer and wiþ þan vnwise wunder ane sturnne woh him wes wunder laþ and þat rihte a leof ælc of his birlen and of his burþæinen and his bercnihtes gold beren an honden to ruggen and to bedde iscrud mid gode webbe nefde he neuere nænne coc þat he nes keppe swiþe god neuær nanes cnihtes swein þat he næs bald þein þe king heold al his hired mid hæȝere blise and mid swulche þinges he ouercom alle kinges mid ræhȝere strengþe and mid richedome swulche weoren his custes þat al uolc hit wuste nu wes god king his hired hine lufede æc hit wes cuþ wide of his kinedome þe king huld i lundene ane muchele hustinge þerto weoren ilaþede his leondcnihtes alle riche men and hæne to hæȝen þan king þa þe hit wes al icume uolc vnimete vp aræs aþelest kingen and lette bringen him biforen halidomes wel icoren þerto gon cneoli þe king sume þrie nuste noht his duȝeþe what he deme wolde heold up his riht hond ænne aþ he þer swor þat næuere bi his liue for nanes monnes lære ne sculden inne brutene sæxes wurþen bliþe londes beon wurþen no wurþscipe bruke ah he heom wolde flemen for heo weoren iuæid wiþ him sloȝen vþer þe wes sune swa heo duden þene oþer his broþer for þi heo weoren on londe laþest alre uolke forþrihtes nom his wise cnihtes weore heom lef weore heom laþ alle heo sworen þene aþ trouliche þat heo wolden mid halden and wreken þene king vþer þat sæxes aqualden her his writen sende wide ȝeond his londe after alle þan cnihten þe he biȝiten mihte þat heo ful sone to þan kinge comen and he heom wolde on londe leofliche athalden scipien heom mid londe mid seoluere and mid golde forþ þe king ferde mid vnimete uerde folc he ledde sællic and ferde riht to eouerwic þer he læi ane niht amærwe he ferde forþriht þer he wuste and his iueren mid him seoþþen wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen þe wes hengestes sune vt of sæxlonde icumen wes þe hæhst mon þat ut of saxlonde com after hengeste and horse his broþer and and and heore iuere ebissa heold a þan ilke dæȝen sæxes to laȝen ladde and radde mid ræȝere strengþe muchel wes þat moncun þat ferde mid iherde tidende of þan kinge þat he touward him com and wolde him vfel don hine biþohte whæt he don mahte and bonnede his uerde ȝeond al þan norþ ærde þer liþen tosomne alle scotleode peohtes and sæxes siȝen heom togæderes and moniennes cunnes men uuleden forþ he gon fusen mid vnimete verde toȝaines aþelest kingen he þohte to quellen þe king on his þeoden and his folc uallen uolden to grunden and setten al þis kinelond an his aȝere hond and fallen to þan grunde þene ȝunge forþ wende and his ferde mid him and wende mid his ferde þat he com to ane watere þat water is ihaten duglas duȝeþen hit aquelde þer com him aȝein ȝaru mid his fehte in ane brade forde þa ferden heom imetten fastliche onsloȝen snelle heore kempen feollen þa uæie uolden to grunde þer wes muchel blodgute balu þer wes riue brustlede scæftes beornes þer ueollen þat isæh on mode him wes unneþe hine biþohte whæt he don mahte and teh hine abacward in enne uald brade þa wenden his feond þat he flæn walde þa wes glad and al his ferde mid him heo wenden þat mid arhþe weore afallæd þere and tuȝen ouer þat water alse heo wode weoren þa þat isah þat him wes swa neh and heo weoren beien bihalues þan wateren þus seide aþelest kingen iseo ȝe mine bruttes here us bihalfues ure iuan uulle heom aualle þene stronge ut of sæxlonde his cun i þisse londe ure ælderne aqualden ah nu is þe dæi icumen þe drihten haueþ idemed þat he scal þat lif leosen and leosien his freonden oþer we sculle dæde beon ne muȝe we hine quic iseon scullen sæxisce men sorȝen ibiden and we wreken wurhliche ure winemaies vp bræid his sceld foren to his breosten and he gon to rusien swa þe runie wulf þenne he cumeþ of holte bihonged mid snawe and þencheþ to biten swulc deor swa him likeþ þa cleopede to leofe his cnihten forþ we biliue þeines ohte alle somed heom to alle we sculleþ wel don and heo uorþ hælden swa þe hæȝe wude þenne wind wode weieþ hine mid mæine fluȝen ouer þe woldes þritti þusend sceldes and smiten a cnihtes þat þa eorþe aȝæn quehte breken braden speren brustleden sceldes feollen sæxisce men folden to grunden þat isah þeruore wa wes him þe alre hendeste mon þe ut of sexlonde com gon to flænne feondliche swiþe and his hors hine bar mid hæhȝere strengþe ouer þat water deope and scelde hine wiþ dæþe saxes gunnen sinken sorȝe heom wes ȝiueþe wende his speres ord and forstod heom þene uord þer adruncke sexes fulle seoue þusend summe heo gunnen wondrien swa doþ þe wilde cron i þan moruenne þenne his floc is awemmed and him haldeþ after hauekes swifte hundes in þan reode mid reouþe hine imeteþ þenne nis him neouþer god no þat lond no þat flod hauekes hine smiteþ hundes hine biteþ þenne biþ þe kinewurþe foȝel fæie on his siþe ouer feldes flæh him biliues þat he com to eouerwic riden swiþe sellic he wenden into burȝe and faste heo biclusde hafuede he binnen ten þusend monnen burhmen mid þa beztse þe him bihalues weoren halde after mid þritti þusend cnihten and ferde riht to eouerwic mid folke swiþe sellic and bilæi þe weorrede aȝæin him seouen niht þer biuoren wes suþward ifaren þe hende broþer and lai bi þare sæbrimme and abad wes i þan daȝen cæiser of riche laȝen inne alemaine þat aþel wes his aȝene þa iherde þer he bi sæ lai þat hafde inne eouerwic biclused hæfde ibonned seouen þusend monnen baldere beornnen þe bi sæ leien heo nomen heom to ræden þat aȝæin heo wolden riden and bilæuen and faren into eouerwic and fehten wiþ and aquellen al his duȝeþe swor on his grome þat he wolde beon bone and bruken al þas riche mid his broþere nolde abide þan keisere ah þenne he ferde uorþ and droh him forþrihtes norþ from dæie to dæie mid baldre duȝeþe þat he com in ane wude in ane wilderne from ferde fulle seoue milen he hafde iþohte bi nihten mid seouen þusend cnihten to riden uppen ær þe king wore war and his folc afeollen and hine seolf aquelle ah al hit oþer iwarþ oþer he iwende for hafede on hirede ænne cniht bruttiscne he wes mæi ihaten bihalues to þan wude halde þurh wude and þurh feldes þat he com to teldes and þus seide sone to kinge hail seo þu kingene aþelest ich æm hidere icume ich æm of þine cunne her is icumen mid swiþe hærde hæregumen and þencheþ in þissere nihte to slæn þe and þine cnihtes to wracken his broþer þe swiþe is vnbalded ah godd him scal forwrænen þurh his muchele mihten and send nu uorþ þene eorl of cornwaile and mid him ohte cnihtes gode and wihte fulle seoue hundred selere þeines and ich heom wulle ræden and ich hom wulle leden hu heo muwen slæn alse enne wulf forþ ferde and alle þas cnihtes þat heo comen bihalues þer lai on comele heo him to helden on ælchere haluen heo sloȝen heo nomen al þat heo aneh comen þer weoren aqualde niȝen hundred alle italde wes bihalues igan him aburhȝen and þurh þa wilderne flæh feondliche swiþe and hafde his men leofe mid reouþe bilæfued and fleh him swa feor norþ þat he com swa uorþ þer lai in uolde mid richen his ferde al abuten eouerwic king swiþe seollic wes wiþinnen mid sæxisce monnen hine biþohte what he don mihte mid wulches cunnes ginne he mihte cumen binnen into þere burhȝe to his broþere þe wes him on liue leofest alre monne lette striken to þan bare lichen his bærd and his chinne and makede hine to crosse he lette sceren half his hæfd and nom him ane harpe an hond he cuþen harpien wel an his childhaden and mid his harpe he ferde to þas kinges hirede and gon þær to gleowien and muche gome to makien ofte me hine smæt mid smærte ȝerden ofte me hine culde swa me deþ crosce ælc mon þe hine imette mid bismare hine igratte swa nauere na mon nuste of custe buten hit weore crosse icumen to þan hirede swa he eode longe upward swa longe he eode adunward þæt heo weoren warre þe weoren þær wiþinnen þæt hit wes broþer heo wurpen ut enne rap and hine faste igrap and brudden up þat he binnen com mid swulches cunnes ginnes com wiþinnen þa wes bliþen and alle his cnihtes mid him and swiþe heo gunnen þrattien þene king bihalues wes and þis gomen isæh and wraþde hine sulfne wunderliche swiþe and hæhte anan wepnien al his wunliche uolc he þohte þe burhȝe mid strengþe to biwinnen alse wolde to þan walle ræse þa com þer riden þe ricche mon þat wes a scottisc þein scone an his londen and þus clupien agon to þan kinge anan hail seo þu aþelest brutten ich þe wulle tellen neouwe tidende of þan kæisere þan wode and þan richen þan strongen and þan balden he is inne scottlonde ihælde to are hafene and hames forberneþ and waldeþ al ure lond after his ahȝere hond he haueþ uerde wel idone al þa strengþe of rome he sæiþ mid his ȝelpe þenne me him win scenccheþ þat þu ne dærst in nare stude his ræsses abiden no on uelde no on wude no nauere nane stude and ȝif þu him abidest he þe wule binden quellen þine leoden and þi lond aȝen ofte wes wa nauere wurse þene þa and he droh hine abac bihalues þere burȝe clupede to ræde cnihtes to neode beornes and eorles and þa hali biscopes and bad þat heo him radden hu he mihte on richen mid his monweorede his monscipe halden and fehten wiþ þan stronge and þan richen þa hider wolde liþe to helpen þa andswarede bruttes þa þere weoren bihalues faren we riht to lundene and lete hine liþen after and ȝif he cumeþ riden sorȝe he scal ibiden he seolf and his ferde fæie scal iwurþen al bilufeden þat radden his leoden forþ he gon liþen þat he to lundene com wes in eouerwic and þær abad him gon wende ȝeon þan norþ ende and nom on honde muchæl dal of londe al scotþeode he ȝaf his ane þeine and al norþhumberlond he sette his broþer an hond galeweoie and orcaneie he ȝaf his ane eorle himseolf he nom from þat lond into lundene ne þohte he naueremare of habben are buten he wolden his mon bicume vþeres sune wes in lundene mid alle brutleoden he bed his ferde ȝeond alle þissen ærde þat æuerælc mon þe him god vþen ræþe and ful sone to lundene comen þa wes ænglene lond mid ærmþe offulled her wes wop and her wes rop and reouþen vniuoȝe muchel hunger and hæte at æuerælche monnes ȝete sende ouer sæ sele tweie cnihtes to hoele his mæie þe wes him leofest monnen þe ahte bruttaine cniht mid þan bezste and bad hine ful sone þat he hider come liþen to londe leoden to helpen for hafde an honde muchel of þissen londe and and him to iboȝen weoren and þohten þene king driuen ut of cuþþen binimen him his icunde and his kineriche þenne were his cun iscend mid scomeliche witen heore wurþscipe iloren a þissere worlderichen þenne weoren þan kingge betere þat he iboren neore þis iherde þa hahste of brutaine and he cleopien agon his sele cnihtes anan and bæd heom to horse hiȝenliche swiþe and faren into france to þan freo cnihten and seide heom þat heo comen raþe and ful sone to mihæles munte mid muchere strenþe alle þa þe wolden of seoluere and of golde wurhscipe iwinne a þissere weorlderichen to peito he sende sele his þeines and summe touward flandres feondliche swiþe and to turuine tweie þer wenden and into gascuinne cnihtes æc gode and hahten heom mid maine touward mihhæles munte and ær heo eoden to ulode heo sculden habbeon ȝiuen gode þat heo mihte þa bliþere buȝen from heore ærde and mid þan hende cumen to þissen londe to helpen aþelest kingen þreottene dæies igon weoren seoþþen þa beoden commen þære þa halden heo to sæ swa hahȝel deh from wolcne twa hundred scipene þer weoren wel biwitene me feolden heom mid folke and heo forþ wenden wind stod and þat weder after heore wille and heo at hamtone halden to londe up leoppen of scipe wode scalkkes beren to londe halmes and burnen mid spæres and mid sceldes heo wriȝen al þa feldes þer wes moni bald þat beot wes aræred heo beoteden swiþe bi heore quiken liue þat heo wolden igræten þene richen þene balde kæisere mid muchele harme þere and ȝif he nolde awæi fleon and touward alemaine teon and he wolde on londe mid fehte atstonden mid balde his beornen beorkes abiden here beo sculde bilauen þat heom weore alre leofest hafden and heore honden and heore white halmes and swa heo scullen on londen losien heore freonden hælden into hælle hæþene hundes wes i lundene aþelest kingen and iherde suggen suþere spellen þat was icumen to londe þe stronge to hamtune forþrihtes mid þritti þusen cnihten and mid vnimete uolke þat wolleȝede þan kinge him toȝaines bah mid hæhȝere blisse mid muchelere monweorede toȝæines his mæie tosomne heo comen blisse wes on hirede custen and clupten and cuþliche speken and anan forþrihtes somneden heore cnihtes þa weoren þer tosomne sele twa ferden sculde dihten þritti þusend cnihten and hafde an londe feouwerti þusend an honde forþrihtes he wenden touward þan norþ ænde toward lincolne þe þe kaisere bilai ah he heo þa ȝæte nefde noht biwunnen for þer weoren wiþinnen seoue þusen monnen ohte men and wihte dæies and nihtes mid his ferde fusde touward burȝe and forbæd his cnihtes dæies and nihtes þat heo liþen stille swulc heo stelen wolden liþen ouer leoden and luden bilefden hornes and bemen alle weoren bilafde nom enne cniht þe wes oht mon and wiht and sende hine to lincolne to leuen his monnen and he heom to soþe sæide mid muþe þat cumen wolde aþelest kingen to þere middernihte and mid him moni god cniht and ȝe wiþinne þenne beoþ eou iwarre þat þenne ȝe ihereþ þene dune þat ȝe ȝæten untunen and fuseþ ut of burȝe and eoure feond felleþ and smiteþ a þan strongen and þan richen and we heom sculleþ tellen bruttisse spelles hit was to þere middelniht þe mone scæn suþriht mid his ferde fusde to burh þat folc wes swa stille swa heo stelen wolden forþ heo comen liþen þat heo iseiȝen lincolne þus him cleopien agon þe kene mon whar beo ȝe mine cnihtes mine hærekemppen iseo ȝe þa teldes þer liþ i ueldes and mid baldere strengþe þat alemainisce uolc þat us hæfeþ ihærmed and þat sæxisce uolc þat sorȝen us bihateþ þat alle habbeoþ aqualde þa hæhste of mine cunne and and vþer þe wes fader min and mines fader broþer and moni þusend monnen of aþele mine cunne uten we heom to liþe and to grunde leggen and wreken wruþliche ure cun and heore riche and alle somed forþriht nu ride æueralc god cniht gon to riden þa ferde gon gliden swulc al þa eorþe wolde forbærnen and smiten i þa ueldes imong teldes þæt wes þæ æreste mon þe þer cleopien agon þe heȝe gume þe wes vþeres sune kenliche and lude swa bicumeþ kinge nu fulste us goddes milde moder and ich ibidde hire sune þat he us beon a fultume æfne þan wordes turnden heo heore ordes stikeden and sloȝen al þat heo neh comen and cnihtes ut of burhȝe buȝen heom toȝæines ȝif heo fluȝen to burȝen þer heo forwurden ȝif heo floȝen to þa wude þer hi heom forduden comen þer heo comen æuere heo heom sloȝen nis hit a nare boc idiht þat æuere weore æi fiht inne þissere bruttene þat balu weore swa riue for volken him wes ærmest þat æuere com to ærde þer wes muchel blodgute balu wes on folke dæþ þer wes rife þe eorþe þer dunede þe kæisere hæfede ænne castel here a lincolnes felde þer he læi wiþinnen þe wes neouwen iworht and swiþe wel biwust and þere weoren mid him and and iseȝen þat heore uolc fæiesih worhten and heo forþriht anon on mid heore burnen and fluȝen ut of castle kenscipe bidaled and fluȝen forþriht anan to þe wude of calidon heo hafden to iferen seouen þusend rideren and ho bilafden ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen feowerti þusunde ifeolled to þan grunde alemainisce men mid ærmþe fordemed and þa sexisce men ibroht to þan grunden þa isæh aþelest kingen þat wes ifloȝen into calidonie itoȝen and and mid him iboȝen weoren into þan haȝe wude into þan hæȝe holme and bæh after mid sixti þusend cnihten bruttene leoden þene wude al bileien and an are halfe hine feolden fulle seoue milen treo uppen oþer treoliche faste an oþer halue he hine bilai mid his leodferde þreo daȝes and þreo niht þat wes heom muchel pliht þa isæh alse he læi þerin þat þer wes buten mete scarp hunger and hete ne heom no heore horsen hælp nefde nenne and þus cleopede to þan kaisere sæie me lauerd soþere worden for whulches cunnes þinge ligge we þus here whi nulle we ut faren and bonnien ure ferden and biginnen fehtes wiþ and wiþ his cnihtes for betere us is on londe mid monscipe to liggen þene we þus here for hungere towurþen iswencheþ us sære folke to scare oþer we sendeþ wiþ and wiþ and ȝeornen griþ and bidden þus his milce and ȝisles him bitechen and wurchen freondscipe wiþ þan freo kinge þis iherde þer he læi wiþinne dic and he andswarede wiþ ærmliche stefene ȝif hit wulle þe is þin aȝe broþer and ma of ure iferen þe mid us sunden here þat we bidden griþ and sahtnesse him wurchen wiþ after æuwer wille don ich hit wulle for is swiþe hæh mon ihalden on leoden leof alle his monnen and of kinewurþe cunne al of kingen icume he wes vþeres sune and oft hit ilimpeþ a ueole cunne þeoden þer gode cnihtes cumeþ to sturne fihte þat heo ærest biȝiteþ after heo hit leoseþ and al swa us toȝere is ilumpen here and æft us bet ilimppeþ ȝif we moten liuien sone forþrihtes andswareden þa cnihtes alle us biluuieþ þisne ræd for þu hafest wel isæid heo nomen twælf cnihtes and senden forþrihtes þer he wes on telde bi þas wudes ende þe an cleopeden anan mid quickere stefne lauerd þi griþ we wolden speken þe wiþ hider þe kaisere us sent ihaten and and beien tosomne nu and æueremare heo biddeþ þine ære þine men heo wulleþ bicumen and þine monscipe hæȝen and heo wulleþ ȝiuen þe ȝisles inowe and halden þe for lauerd swa þe beoþ alre leofest ȝif heo moten liþe heonene mid liue into heore leoden and laþspæl bringen for her we habbeoþ ifunden feole cunne sorȝen at lincolne bilæued leofe ure mæies sixti þusend monnen þa þer beoþ ofslæȝene and ȝif hit þe weore wille an heorte þat we mosten ouer sæ winden mid seile nulle we naueremare æft cumen here for her we habbeoþ forloren leoue ure mæies swa longe swa biþ æuere her ne cume we næuere þa loh ludere stefene iþonked wurþe drihtene þe alle domes waldeþ þat þe stronge is sad of mine londe mi lond he hafeþ todæled al his duȝeþe cnihtes me seoluen he þohte driuen ut of mire leoden halden me for hæne and habben mine riche and mi cun ai foruaren mi uolc al fordemed ah of him biþ iwurþen swa biþ of þan voxe þenne he biþ baldest ufenan þan walde and hafeþ his fulle ploȝe and fuȝeles inoȝe for wildscipe climbiþ and cluden isecheþ i þan wilderne holȝes him wurcheþ faren whaswa auere fare naueþ he næuere nænne kare he weneþ to beon of duȝeþe baldest alre deoren þenne siȝeþ him to segges vnder beorȝen mid hornen mid hunden mid haȝere stefenen hunten þar talieþ hundes þer galieþ þene vox driueþ ȝeond dales and ȝeond dunes he ulih to þan holme and his hol isecheþ i þan bidæled nes þer nan swa rehȝ mon þe him durste ræden þet him ofþuhte sære sone þerafter com of comela to þan kinge and he his mon þer bicom mid his cnihten alle feouwer and twenti ȝisles þer bitæhte londe iseon heo ne mahten þat water wes stille after heore iwille heo letten tosomne sæiles gliden bord wiþ borden beornes þer spileden sæiden þat heo wolden eft to þissen londe and wreken wurþliche heore winemæies and westen lond and leoden aquellen and castles biwinnen and wilgomen wurchen swa heo liþen after sæ efne al swa longe þat heo commen bitwiȝe ænglelonde and normandie heo wenden heore lofes and liþen toward londe þat heo comen ful iwis to dertemuþe at totteneis mid muchelere blisse heo buȝen to þan londe sone swa heo a lond comen þat folc heo asloȝen þa cheorles heo uloȝen þa tileden þa eorþen heo hengen þa cnihtes þa biwusten þa londes alle þa gode wiues heo stikeden mid cnifes alle þa maidene heo mid morþe aqualden and þaie ilærede men heo læiden on gleden alle þa heoredecnauen mid clibben heo aqualden heo velledden þa castles þat lond heo awæsten þa chirechen heo forbarnden baluw wes on folke þa sukende children heo adrenten inne wateren þat orf þat heo nomen al heo sloȝen to heore inne ladden and suden and bradden al heo hit nomen þat heo neh comen alle dæi heo sungen of þan kinge and sæiden þat heo haueden hames biwunnen þæ scolden heom ihalden in heore onwalden and þer heo wolden wunien wintres and sumeres and ȝif weoren swa kene þat he cumen wolde to fihten wiþ þan strongen and þan richen heo wolden of his rugge makien ane brugge and nimen þa ban sceome ah al hit iwraþ on oþer sone þerafter heore ȝelp and heore gome ilomp heomseoluen to scame and swa deþ wel iwære þe mon þe swa ibereþ þe kaisere biwon al þat he lokede on he nom sumersete and he nom dorsete and al deuenescire þat volc al forferde and he wiltunscire mid wiþere igrætte he nom alle þa londes into þære sæstronde þa æt þan laste þa lette heo blawen hornes and bemen and bonnien his ferden and forþ he wolde buȝen and baþen al biliggen and æc bristouwe abuten birouwen þis was heore ibeot ær heo to baþe comen to baþe com þe kæisere and bilæi þene castel þere and þa men wiþinnen ohtliche agunnen stepen uppen stanene wal wel iwepned oueral and wereden þa riche wiþ þan stronge þer lai þe kaisere and his iuere and his broþer and moni anoþer wes bi norþe and noht herof nuste ferde ȝeond al scotlond and sette hit an his aȝere hond orcaneie and galeweie man and murene and alle þa londes þe þerto læien hit wende to iwislichen þinge þat iliþen weore to his aȝene londe and þat he naueremære nolde cumen here þa comen þa tidende to kinge þat þa kæisere icumen wes to londen and i þan suþ ende sorȝen þer worhten þa seide aþelest kingen walawa walawa þat ich sparede mine iua þat ich nauede on holte mid hungere hine adrefed oþer mid sweorde al hine toswungen nu he me ȝilt mede for mire god dede ah swa me hælpen drihten þæ scop þæs dæies lihten þerfore he scal ibiden bitterest alre baluwen harde gomenes his bone ich wulle iwurþen and beiene ich wulle aquellen and al heore duȝeþe dæþ scal iþolien ȝif hit wule ivnnen waldende hæfnen ich wulle wurþliche wreken alle his wiþerdeden ȝif me mot ilasten þat lif a mire breosten and hit wulle me iunne þat iscop mone and sunne ne scal nauere æft me bicharren nu cleopede aþelest kingen whar beo ȝe mine cnihtes ohte men and wiþte to horse to horse haleþes gode and we sculleþ buȝen touward baþe swiþe leteþ up fusen heȝe forken and bringeþ her þa ȝæsles biforen ure cnihtes and heo scullen hongien on hæȝe treowen þer he lette fordon feouwer and twenti childerren alemainisce men of swiþe heȝe cunnen þa comen tidende to þan kinge þat seoc wes his mæi þerfore he wes sari i clud ligginde and þer he hine bilæfde hiȝenliche swiþe forþ he gon liþe þat he bihalues baþe beh to ane uelde þer he alihte and his cnihtes alle and on mid heore burnen beornes sturne and he a fif dæle dælde his ferde þa he hafde al iset and al hit isemed þa dude he on his burne ibroide of stele þe makede on aluisc smiþ mid aþelen his crafte he wes ihaten wygar þe witeȝe wurhte his sconken he helede mid hosen of stele his sweord he sweinde bi his side hit wes iworht in aualun mid wiȝelefulle craften halm he set on hafde hæh of stele þeron wes moni ȝimston al mid golde bigon he wes vþeres þas aþelen kinges he wes ihaten goswhit ælchen oþere vnilic he heng an his sweore ænne sceld deore his nome wes on bruttisc ihaten þer wes innen igrauen mid rede golde stauen an onlicnes deore of drihtenes moder his spere he nom an honde þa ron wes ihaten þa he hafden al his iweden þa leop he on his steden þa he mihte bihalden þa bihalues stoden þene uæireste cniht þe verde scolde leden ne isæh næuere na man selere cniht nenne þene him wes aþelest cunnes þa cleopede ludere stæfne lou war her biforen us heþene hundes þe sloȝen ure alderen mid luþere heore craften and heo us beoþ on londe læþest alre þinge nu fusen we hom to and stærcliche heom leggen on and wræken wunderliche ure cun and ure riche and wreken þene muchele scome þat heo us iscend habbeoþ þat heo ouer vþen comen to dertemuþen and alle heo beoþ forsworene and alre freomeste þat fiht ich wulle biginnen nu we scullen riden and ouer lond gliden and na man bi his liue lude ne wurchen ah faren fæstliche drihten us fulsten þa riden agon þe riche mon beh ouer wælde and baþe wolde isechen þa tidende com to þan strongen and þan richen þat mid ferde com al ȝaru to fihte and his ohte men leopen heom to horsen igripen heore wepnen heo wusten heom ifæied þis isæh aþelest kinge isæh he ænne hæþene eorl hælden him toȝeines mid seouen hundred cnihten al ȝærewe to fihten þe orl himseolf ferde biforen al his genge and himseolf arnde biuoren al his ferde þe ræie ron nom an honde he stræhte scaft stærcne stiþimoden king his hors he lette irnen þat þa eorþe dunede sceld he braid on breosten þe king wes abolȝen he smat þene eorl þurhut þa breosten þat þæ heorte tochan and þe king cleopede anan þe formeste is fæie nu fulsten us drihte and þa hefenliche quene þa drihten akende þa cleopede aþelest kinge nu heom to nu heom to þat formest is wel idon bruttes hom leiden on swa me scal a luþere don heo bittere swipen ȝefuen mid axes and mid sweordes þer feolle men fulle twa þusend swa neuere ne les næuere ænne of his þer weoren sæxisce men folken alre ærmest and þa alemainisce men ȝeomerest alre leoden mid his sweorde fæiescipe wurhte al þat he smat to hit wes sone fordon al wæs þe king abolȝen swa biþ þe wilde bar þenne he i þan mæste monie swin imeteþ þis isæh and gon him to charren and beh him ouer auene to burȝen himseoluen and him læc to swa hit a liun weoren and fusde heom to flode monie þer weoren fæie þer sunken to þan grunde fif and twenti hundred þa al wes auene stram mid stele ibrugged ouer þat water flæh mid fiftene hundred cnihten þohte forþ siþen and ouer sæ liþen isæh climben to munten buȝen to þan hulle þa ouer baþen stondeþ and beh him after mid seoue þusend cnihtes heo þohten i þan hulle hæhliche atstonden weorien heom mid wepnen and awæmmen þa isæh aþelest kingen whar atstod and æc stal wrohte þa clupede þe king kenliche lude balde mine þeines buhȝeþ to þan hulles for ȝerstendæi wes monnen alre kennest nu him is al swa þere gat þer he þene hul wat hæh uppen hulle fehteþ mid hornen þenne comeþ þe wlf wilde touward hire winden þeh þe wulf beon ane buten ælc imane and þer weoren in ane loken fif hundred gaten þe wulf heom to iwiteþ and alle heom abiteþ swa ich wulle nu todæi al fordemen ich am wulf and he is gat þe gume scal beon fæie þa ȝet cleopede aþelest kingen ȝurstendæi wes cnihten alre baldest nu he stant on hulle and auene bihaldeþ hu ligeþ i þan stræme stelene fisces mid sweorde bigeorede heore sund is awemmed heore scalen wleoteþ swulc goldfaȝe sceldes þer fleoteþ heore spiten swulc hit spæren weoren þis beoþ seolcuþe þing isiȝen to þissen londe swulche deor an hulle swulche fisces in wælle ȝurstendæi wes þe kaisere kennest alre kingen nu he is bicumen hunte and hornes him fulieþ flihþ ouer bradne wæld beorkeþ his hundes he hafeþ bihalues baþen his huntinge bilæfued freom his deore he flicþ we hit scullen fallen and his balde ibeot to nohte ibringen and swa we scullen bruken rihte biȝæten efne þan worde þa þe king seide he bræid hæȝe his sceld forn to his breosten he igrap his spere longe his hors he gon spurie neh al swa swiþe swa þe fuȝel fliȝeþ fuleden þan kinge fif and twenti þusend whitere monnen wode under wepnen hælden to hulle mid hæhȝere strengþe and uppen smiten mid swiþe smærte biten and heom þer hente and feolde þa bruttes to grunde i þan uormeste ræse fulle fif hundred þat isæh aþelest kingen and wraþ him iwræþþed wunder ane swiþe and þus cleopien agon þe hæhȝe man war beo ȝe bruttes balde mine beornes her stondeþ us biuoren vre ifan alle icoren gumen mine gode legge we heom to grunde igrap his sweord riht and he smat ænne sexise cniht cuþþen wit scullen ræchen nu wit scullen þis lond dalen swa þe biþ alre laþþest æfne þan worde þa þe king sæide his brode swærd he up ahof and hærdliche adun sloh and smat hælm þat he amidde toclæf and þere burne hod þat hit at þe breoste atstod and he sweinde touward mid his swiþren honde and swipte þat hæfued of forþ mid þan helme þa loh þe aþele king and þus ȝeddien agon mid gomenfulle worden lien nu þere þu were iclumben haȝe and þi broþer liþ bi þire side nu ich al þis kinelond sette an eower ahȝere hond dales and dunes and al mi drihtliche uolc þu clumbe a þissen hulle wunder ane hæȝe swulc þu woldest to hæuene nu þu scalt to hælle þer þu miht kenne muche of þine cunne and gret þu þer hengest þe cnihten wes faȝerest ebissa and and of þine cunne ma and bide heom þer wunie wintres and sumeres and we scullen on londe libben in blisse bidden for eower saulen þat sel ne wurþen heom nauære and scullen her æuwer ban biside baþe ligen þe king cleopede þene kene of cornwale he wes and bi nihte þat þu cumme to þare sæ biforen and al þat þu miht biwinnen bruc hit on wunnen and ȝif þu miht þene kaisere ufele aquellen þere ich þe ȝifue to mede al doresete al swa þe aþele king þas word hafede isæid sprong to horse swa spærc him doh of fure fulle seoue þusend fuleden þan eorle þe kene and muchel of his cunne wenden ouer woldes and ouer wildernes ouer dales and ouer dunes ouer deope wateres cuþe þene wæi þe toward his cunde læi an oueste he wende fuliwis riht toward toteneis dæies and nihtes he com þere forþrihtes swa neuere nuste of his cume nane custe com to cuþþe biuoren and lette him fusen biforen al þas londes folc cheorles ful ȝepe mid clubben swiþe græte mid spæren and mid græte waȝen to þan ane icoren and duden heom alle clane into þan scipen grunde and hæhte heom þere lutie wel þat of heom neore war and þenne his folc come and in wolden climben heore botten igripen and ohtliche on smiten mid heore waȝen and mid heore speren murþren heren al duden þa ældren and wule biȝiten ferde and æft cumen hidere and wule faren hider in and þencheþ awræken and his broþer þæ bi baþen resteþ ah no abide he næuere þære dæȝen ne scal he no ȝif we maȝen æfne þere spæche þa spac þe eorl riche and onuest he gon riden þe reh wes on moden halden ut of wudescaȝe scalkes swiþe kene and after þan strongen and þan richen cnihtes bisehȝen heom baften isehȝen ouer wolden winden heoremærken winnien ouer ueldes fif þusend sceldes þa iwærþ chærful an heorten and þas word sæide þe riche kaisere þis is þe king þe alle us wule aquellen fleo we nu biliue and into scipen fusen and liþen forþ mid watere ne recchen we nauere wudere þa þe kaisere þas word hæuede isæid þa gon he to fleonne feondliche swiþe and þe kene com him after sone and his cnihtes to scipe comen forþrihtes heo wenden þa scipen stronge to scuuen from þan londe þæ cheorles mid heore botten weoren þer wiþinnen þa botten heo up heouen and adunriht sloȝen þer wes sone islaȝen moni cniht mid swiþe mare hul þat water tiþ þerunder þat teine is ihaten þa hulle ihaten teinnewic þiderward flæh swa swiþe swa he mihte mid feouwer and twenti cnihten þa isæh hu hit þa uerde þer þat þe kaisere flæh ouercumen and ælc al þat lond inumen he sette grit swiþe god þat þerafter longe stod þeh ælc mon beere an honde behȝes of golde ne durste nauere gume nan oþerne ufele igreten wes forþ iwende into scotlonden for lai inne clud faste biclused hafden scottes hine bilæien mid luþere heore craften and ȝif neore þe raþer icumen þenne weoren houwel inumen and al his folc þer islaȝen and idon of lif daȝen ah com sone mid selere strengþe and scottes to fleonne feor of þan ærde into muræine mid mucle monweorede and com to scotlonde þer he ifunde and into clud ferden and funden þer mid hahȝere blisse an sel of his seocnesse isund wes iwurþen muchel wes þa blisse þæ þa wes in burȝe scottes weoren inne mureine and þer þeohten wunien and mid bolde heore worden heore beot makeden and sæiden þat heo wolden þa riche walden and þer abiden mid baldere strenþe for ne durste nauere for his life come þer þa iherde ærhþen bidæled whæt scottes hafden isæid mid heore huxworden þa sæide aþelest kingen whær ært þu hæhst of mine cunne and þe kene ut of cornwaile leteþ blæwen bemen and bonnien ure ferden and to þere midnihte we sculleþ faren forþriht toward mureine ure monscipe to bitellen ȝif hit wule drihte þe scop þæs daȝes lihten we heom sculle tellen sorhfulle spelles heore ȝælp fellen and heomseolue aquellen to þere midnihte aras forþriht hornes me gon blawen mid hahȝere stafnen cnihtes gunnen arisen and ræhȝe word speken mid muche monweorede into mureine forþ gunnen wræsten þreottene þusend a feormeste flocke feondliche kene men seoþþen com þe eorl of cornwæille mid seouentene þusen selere þeinen seoþþen com heowel mid his kemppen swiþe wel mid an and twenti þusen mid aþelere kempen seoþþen com aþelest kingen mid seouen and twenti þusend siȝen heom afterward sceldes þer cliseden lihten hit gon dæȝen þat word com to scotten þær þar heo wuneden hu þe king com touward heore londe feondliche swiþe mid vnimete folke þa weoren ærhest þat ær weoren baldest and gunnen to fleonnen feondliche swiþe into þan watere þer wunderes beoþ inoȝe þat is a seolcuþ mere iset a middelærde mid fenne and mid ræode mid watere swiþe bræde mid fiscen and mid feoȝelen mid uniuele þingen þat water is unimete brade nikeres þer baþieþ inne þer is æluene ploȝe in atteliche pole sixti æitlondes beoþ i þan watere longe in ælc of þan æitlonde is a clude hæh and strong þer næstieþ arnes and oþere græte uoȝeles þe ærnes habbeoþ ane laȝe bi æuerælches kinges dahȝen whænneswa æi ferde fundeþ to þan ærde þeonne fleoþ þa fuȝeles feor i þan lufte moni hundred þusen and muchel feoht makieþ þenne is þat folc buten wene þat reouþe heom is to cumene of summes cunnes leoden þe þat lond wulleþ isechen tweien dæȝes oþer þreo þus scal þis taken heo ær unkuþe men to þan londe liþen ȝet þer is sellic to suggen of þan watere þer walleþ of þan mæren a moniare siden of dalen and of dunen and of bæcchen deopen sixti wateres alle þer isomned swa neuere ut of þan mære na man no uindeþ þat þer ut wenden buten an an ænde an imetliche broc þe of þan mere ualleþ and swiþe isemeliche into sæ wendeþ þa scottes weoren todeled mid muclen vniselen ȝeond þa monie munten þa i þan watere weoren biseohte scipen and gon heom to wenden and sloh þer vniuoȝe moni and inoȝe and moni þusend þer wes dæd for heom trukede ælc bræd þe aþele was an æst side þe sele wes a suþ halue and þe kene bi norþen heom biwusten and his smale uolc he setten alle bi weste siden þa weoren scottes ihalden for sottes þer heo leien ȝeond þa cliues faste biclused þer weoren sixti þusend mid sorreȝe forfarene þa wes irlondes king icume into hafene twalf milen from þer he lai mid ferde scotten to hælpen to forfarene þis iherden aþelest kinge and nom his ane ferde and þiderward fusden and funde þene king þe icumen wes to londe þar him faht wiþ and nolde him ȝiuen na griþ and feolde irisce men feondliche to grunden and mid twalf scipen teh from þan londe and ferde to irlonde mid harme swiþe stronge and a þan londe sloh al þat he uunde and seoþþen he wende to þan mere þer he his mæi lette þene hende hahst of brutlonde wiþuten aþelest kingen uunde þer he wes bi hauene bi þan mere brade þer he abiden hafde þa fainede swiþe folc an hirede of cume and of aþele his dede þer wes forþriht twei dæies and twa niht scottes leie ȝeond clude moni þusend dede mid hungere foruarene folkene alre ærmest i þan þridde dæiȝe faire hit gon daȝiȝen þa tuȝen touward hirede alle þat weoren ihadded and þreo biscopes wise a boke wel ilæred preostes and muneckes vnimete monie canones þer comen monie and wel idone mid alle þan halidomen þa hahst an londe weoren and ȝeornden griþ and his aþmeden þider þa wifes comen þa i þan londen wuneden heo wæiden in hære ærmen heore children ærmen heo weopen on wunder ane swiþe and heore uæx fæire wælden to volde curuen heore lockes and þer niþer læiden to þas kinges foten biforen al his duȝeþen nailes to heore nebbe þat æfter hit bledde neh þan alle clæne nakede heo weoren sorhliche heo gunnen clupien to þan kinge and summe þus iseiden þer heo on siþ weoren king we beoþ on ærde ærmest alre uolke we ȝeorneþ þine milzce þurh þæne milde godd þu hauest a þisse londe ure leoden aslæȝen mid hungere and mid hete mid feole cunne hærmen mid wapnen mid wæteren mid feole wansiþen vre children imaked faderlese and frofre bidæled þu ært cristine mon and we alswa sunden sæxisce men beoþ hæþene hundes heo comen to þisse londe and þis folc here aqualden ȝif we heom hereden þat was for ure hermen for we nefden nænne mon þe us wiþ heom mihten griþien heo us duden swiþe wa and þu us dest al swa þa heþene us hatieþ and þe cristine us sari makieþ wær scullen we bicumen queþen þa wif to þan kinge aȝef us ȝet þa quicke men þa liggeþ ȝeond þas cluden and ȝif þu ȝiuest milze þisse moncunnen þi monscipe biþ þa mare nu and æueremære lauerd ure king leoþe vre benden þu hafust al þis lond inomen and al þis folc ouercumen we beoþ under uote a þe is al þa bote þis iherde aþelest kingen þesne wop and þesne rop and reouþen vniuoȝe þa toc he to ræde and reosede on heorte he uunde on his ræde to don þat heo hine beden he ȝæf heom lif he ȝef heom lumen and heore lond to halden he lette blæwen bemen and þa scottes bæcnien and heo ut of cluden to þan scipen comen an auerælchen siden siȝen touward londe heo weoren swiþe iharmede mid scærpen þan hungre aþes heo sworen swiken þat nalden and heo þa iȝefuen ȝisles þan kingen and alle ful sone þas kinges men bicomen and seoþþen heo gunnen fusen þat folc þer todelden ælc mon to þan ende þer he wes wuniende and þer griþ sette god mid þan bezste whær ært þu mi mæi monne me leofest isixst þu þisne muchelne mære þer scottes beoþ amærred isihst þu þas hæhȝe treon and sihst þu þas ærnes teon inne þisse uenne is fisc unimete isihst þu þas æitlondes þe ȝeond þas watere stondeþ seollic þuhte of swulchere isihþe and wonddrede wide bi þan watere flode and þus þer cleopede hæhes cunnes seoþþen ich wes mon iboren of mire moder bosme no isah ich a none londe þus seolcuþe þinges swa ich here biuoren me mid æȝenen bihælde wundreden bruttes wunder ane swiþe þa cleopede aþelest kingen min aȝe mæi monnen me leofest lust mire worden of mucle mære wunder þat ic þe wulle tellen of soþe mine spellen bi þisse mære enden þer þis water wendeþ is an lutel wiht mære monnen to wundre he is endlonge feouwer and sixti munden he is imeten a bræde fif and twenti foten fif foten he is deop alfene hine dulfen feowernoked he is and þerinne is feower kunnes fisc and ælc fisc an his ende þer he his cun findeþ ne mai þer nan to oþere buten al swa tacheþ his icunde nes næuer nan mon iboren ne of swa wise crafte icoren no libbe he swa longe þe maȝen hit vnderstonde what letteþ þene fisc to uleoten to þan oþere for nis þer noht bitwenen buten water clæne þa ȝet cleopede aþelest kingen i þissen londes ænde neh þere sæstronde is a mære swiþe muchel þat water is unfæle and whænne þa sæ vledeþ swulc heo wulle aweden and falleþ inne þene mære vnimete swiþe no biþ næuere þæ mere on watere þa mare ah þenne þa sæ falleþ in and scen warþ þa uolden and heo biþ al inne in alden hire denne þenne swelleþ þe mære and swærkeþ þa vþen vþen þer
