leppeoþ ut vnimete grete fleoþ ut a þat lond þat leoden agriseþ an hond ȝif þer cumeþ æi mon þat noht ne cunne þeron þat seollic to iseonne bi þere sæstronde ȝif he his neb wendeþ touwærd þan mære ne beo he noht swa loh iboren ful wel he beoþ iborȝen þat water him glit bisiden and þe mon þer wuneþ softe after his iwille he wuneþ þer uul stille þat no biþ he for þan watere naþþing idracched þa sæide hæh mon of brutten nu ic ihere tellen seolcuþe spellen and seollic is þe lauerd þat al hit isette þa cleopede aþelest kingen blaweþ mine hornes mid hæhȝere stæfne and suggeþ mine cnihtes þat ic fare forþrihte bemen þer blewen hornes þer stureden blisse wes an hirede mid bisie þan kinge for ælc wes ifreoured and ferde toward his ærd and þe king forbæd heom bi heore bare liuen þat na mon on worlde swa wod no iwurþe no swa ærwitte gume þat his griþ bræke and ȝif hit dude æi mon he sculden dom þolien æfne þan worde fusde þa uærde þer sungen beornes seolcuþe leoþes of þan kinge and of his hereþringen and sæiden on songe to þisse worlde longe neore neueremære swulc king ase þurh alle þing king no kæisere in næuere nare kuþþe forþ to eouuerwic mid folke swiþe seollic and wunede þer wiken sixe mid muchelere wunne þa burhwalles weoren tobroken and tofallen þat al forbarnden and þa hallen alle clæne þa cleopede þe king ænne preost mæren he wes swiþe wis mon and witful on bocken þu ært min aȝe preost þe æþ þe scal iwurþen þe king nom ane rode hali and swiþe gode and bitok an hond and þermid swiþe muchel lond and þene ærchebiscopes staf þer he aȝaf ær wes preost god nu he is ærchebiscop þa hæhte hine aþelest kingen þat he rærde churechen and þa songes rihten and goddes folc biwusten and fæire heom dihtten and he hæhte alle cnihtes demen rihte domes and þa eorþetilien teon to heore cræften and æuerælcne gume oþerne igræten and wulc mon swa wurs dude þene þe king hafde iboden he wolde hine ifusen to ane bare walme and ȝif hit weore læþ mon he sculde hongie for þon þa ȝet cleopede aþelest kingen hæhte þat alc mon þe his lond hafde forgan mid wulches cunnes wite swa he biwæiued weore þat he aȝain come ful raþe and ful sone þe riche and þe laȝe and hefde æft his aȝen bute he weore swa fule biwite þat he weore lauerdswike oþer touward his lauerd manswore þene þe king demde forlore þer come þreo ibroþeren þe weore kiniborne lot and angel and vrien welle hwulche þreo men þeos hereþringes þreo comen to þan kinge and setten an heore cneowen biforen þan kæisere hal seo þu aþelest kingen and þi duȝeþe mid þe a mote heo wel beo we sundeþ þreo broþeren iboren of kingen is al ure icunde lond igan ut of ure hond for habbeoþ hæþene men us hene imakede and iwæst us al leonæis scotlond and muræf and we biddeþ þe for godes luue þat þu us beo fultume and for þire mucle wurþscipe þat þu us wurþe milde aȝif us ure icunde lond and we þe sculleþ luuien hælden þe for lauerd an ælche leodwisen þis iherde aþelest king hu þeos þreo cnihtes fæire hine bisohten reousede on heorte and he reordien gan and þas word sæide selest alre kinge vrien bicum mi mon þu scalt to muræiue aȝæn þerof þu scalt beon icleoped king of þan londe and hæh an mine hirede mid þine monweorede and angele ich sette an hond al togadere scotlond habbe hit an honde and beon king of þan londe from þan fader to þan sune þerof þu scalt mi mon bicumen and þu lot mi leofe freond godd þe wurþe liþe þu hauest mine suster to wiue þæ bet þe scal iwurþe ich þe ȝifue þat is a lond faier and ich wulle leggen þerto londes swiþe gode biside þere wurþ an hundred punden for mi fader vþer þe while þe he wes king here lufede wel his dohter þe wes his bæd iþohte and heo is mi suster and haueþ sunen tweien þeo me beoþ on londe children alre leofest þus spæc þe king þa wes wolwain lute child swa ves þe oþer modræd his broþer wale þat wes ibore muchel hærm com þerfore for to lundene and mid him his leoden he heold inne londe ane muchele hustinge and sette alle þa laȝen þat stoden bi his ælderne daȝen alle þa laȝen gode þe her ær stoden he sette griþ he sette friþ and alle freodomes þenene he for to cornwale to riche he funde þer a mæide vnimete fæier wes þas mæidenes moder of romanisce mannen maȝe and þat maide him bitahte and he heo fæire afeng and softe heo fedde heo wes of heȝe cunne of romanisce monnen næs in nane londe maide nan swa hende of specche and of dede and of tuhtle swiþe gode heo wes ihaten wifmonne hendest heo nom to wife and luuede heo wunder swiþe þis maiden he gon wedde and nom heo to his bedde wes i cornwale al þene winter þere and al for lufe wimmonne him leofuest þa þe winter wes agan and sumer com þer anan hine biþohte whæt he don mahte þat his folc gode aswunden ne læie þere he ferde to to þan midfesten and heold þer his hustinge of hehȝen his folke and seide þat he wolde into irlonde wenden al þat kinelond to his æhȝere hond buten þe king to him raþer come ær and mid listen him speken wiþ and ȝirnde griþ he wolde westen his lond and luþere him gon an hond mid fure mid stele streit gomen wurchen and þat londfolc aslæn þe wolde stonden him aȝein æfne þan worde þa þe king sæide þa andswarede þat folc fæire þan kinge lauuerd king hald þi word we beoþ alle ȝarewe to ganne and to ride oueral to þire neode þer wes moni bald þe hafde beres leches heouen up heore bruwen iburst an heore þonke wenden touwarde innen cnihtes mid heore monnen heo ruokeden burnen bonneden helmes heo wipeden hors leoue mid linnene claþe heo sceren heo scoiden scalkes balde weoren sum scæft horn sum scaft ban sum ȝarked stelene flan sum makde þwonges gode and swiþe strong summe beoveden speren and beonneden sceldes letten beoden ȝeond al his kineþeoden þat æuerælc god cniht to him come forþriht and euerælc oht mon comen forþriht anan and waswa bilæfden his leomen he sculde leosen and whaswa come gladliche he sculden wurþe riche seouen niht uppen æstre þa men hafden iuast þa comen alle þa cnihtes to scipen forþrihtes wind heom stod an honde þe scaf heom to irlonde a þet lond ferde and þa leoden amerden muchel uolc he asloȝ orf he nom vniuoh and æuere he hæhte ælcne mon chirechegriþ halden þet tidinde com to þan kinge þe lauerd wes of þan londe þat þer wes icumen and ærmþen iwrohte þer he sumnede al his leoden ȝeond his kinelonde and his irisce uolc fusden to fehte toȝæines þan aþele kinge and his cnihtes heom wepnede forþrihtes and foren heom toȝeines folc vnimete men weoren mid wepnen al biþehte þa irisce men weoren nakede neh þan mid speren and mid axen and mid swiþe scærpe sæxen men letten fleon vnimete flan and merden irisc folc and hit swiþe ualden ne mæhten heo iþolien þurh nanes cunnes þingen ah fluȝen awai on siþe swiþe uæle þusend and þe king flah and awæwardes teh and him after and þene king ikahte he nom bi þan honde þene king of þan londe þe hæȝe herbeorwe isohte an his mode him wes þa æþe þat him wes swa neh nu dude aþelest kingen swiþe muche freondscipe atforen al his folke he lette þene king scrude mid ælchere prude and æc bi sat and æc mid himseolue æt mid he win dronc þat him wes mucheles unþonc naþeles þa he isah þat wes swiþe glad þa cleopede an his horte him wes sær lauerd þi griþ ȝef me leomen and ȝif me lif ich wulle þi mon bicumen and biteche þe mine þreo sunen mine sunen deore to don al þine iwille and ȝet ich wulle mare ȝif þu me wult ȝefen ære ich wulle þe bitache ȝisles swiþe rich children sume sixti hæȝe and swiþe mæhti ȝet ich wulle mære ȝif þu me ȝifuest ære ælche ȝere of mine londe seouen þusend punde and senden heom to þine londe and sixti mark of golde and ȝet ich wulle mare ȝif þu wult me ȝifuen are alle þa steden mid alle heore iweden þa hæuekes and þa hundes and hehȝe mine mahmes ich bitache þe to honde of al mine londe and þenne þu hauest þis idon ich wulle nimen halidom of seint þe dude godes iwille and seint brændenes hæfed þe godd seolf haleȝede and seinte bride riht fot þe hali is and swiþe god and halidomes inoȝe þe comen ut of rome and swerien þe to soþe swiken þe þat ich nulle ah ich þe wulle luuien and halden þe for lauerd halden þe for hahne king and miseolf beon þin vnderling þis iherde aþelest king and he gan lihȝen luddere steftne and he gon andswerie mid ædmode worden beo nu glad ne beo þin heorte noht sær for þv ært a wis mon þa bet þe scal iwurþen for æuere me æhte wisne mon wurþliche igreten for þine wisdome no scal þe noht þa wurse muchel þu me beodest þe scal beon þa betere her forþrihtes biforen al mine cnihtes forȝiuen þe amare al þæ haluendæle of golde and of gærsume ah þu scalt mi mon bicumen and half þat gauel sende ælche ȝere to mine londe halfe þa steden and halfe þa iweden halue þa hauekes and halue þa hundes þæ þu me beodest ich wulle þe bilefen ah ich wulle habben þire hæhre monne children þeo heom beoþ alre leofuest ich heom mai þe bet ileouen and swa þu scalt wunien in wurþscipe þire a þine kinedome i þine rihte icunden and ic þe wulle ȝeuen to þat ne scal þe king woh don buten he hit abugge mid his bare rugge þeo hit sæide aþelest kingen þa hafden he an hond al tosomne irlond and þe king his mon bicumen and bitæht him his þreo seonen þa spæc to sele his cnihten faren to hislond and nimen we hit to ure honde ferde þer fusde and com to islonde ælcus þe king wes ihaten hæh mon of þan ærd he iherde þa tidende of þan kinge he dude al so wis mon and wende toȝeines him anan anan forþrihtes mid sixtene cnihtes he bar on his honde ænne mucle ȝeord of golde sone swa he isæh swa he on his cneowen bæh and þas word him iquaþ þe king wes afæred wulcume sire wilcume lauerd her ich biteche þe an hond al togadere islond þu scal beon min hæhȝe king and ich wul beon þin underling ich þe wullen heren swa mon scal don his hærren and ich wulle þi mon bicumen and bitæche þe minne leofue sune is ihaten and þu hine scalt iæþelien to cnihte hine dubben alse þin aȝene mon his moder ich habbe to wife þas kinges dohter of rusie and æc ælche ȝere ȝiuen þe wulle æhte seoue þusend punde of seoluere and of golde and to æuerælche ræde beon ȝæru to þire neode þis ich wullen þe swerien uppen mine sweorden þe halidom is a þere hilte þe hexste of þisse londe likien swa ne liken nulle ich þe nauere swiken þis iherde aþlest kingen wes wunsum þer he hafde his iwillen and he wes wod sturne wiþ his wiþeriwinnen þa liþe word iherde of þan leodkinge al þat he ȝirnde al he him ȝette ȝisles and aþes and alle his ibodes þa iherde suggen soþere worden þe king of orcaneie vnimete kene gonwais wes ihate haeþene kempe þat king wolde cume to his londe mid muchele scipferde fusen to leoden gonwais him uerde toȝæines mid wisen his þeines and sette an hond al orcaneies lond and twa and þritti æitlond þe þider in liggeþ and his monradene mid muchelere mensce and he him hafde a uoreward biforen al his duȝeþe ælche ȝere to iwiten fulle sixti scipen mid his aȝere costninge bringen heom to londenne ifulled to iwisse mid gode sæfisce þis forward he iuaste and ȝisles he funde and aþes he swor gode swiken þat he nolde and seoþþen he lefe nom and forþ he gon liþen lauerd haue wel godne dæi ich wulle cumen wenne ich mai for nu þu art mi lauerd leouest alre kingen þa hafde þis idon þa ȝet he wolde mare afon he nom his writen gode and senden to gutlonde and grætte þe king and hehte hine sone comen to him and himseolf his mon bicume and bringen him his tweien sunen and ȝif þu þat nulle do þat þu wulle ich þe wulle sende sixtene þusend heȝe herekempen to mucle þine harmen scullen þi lond wasten and þiire leoden aslan and þat lond setten swa heom bezst þincheþ and þe seoluen binden and to me bringen þis iherde þe king þræt þas kaiseres and he on uaste iueng fæiere his iweden hundes and hafekes and his gode horsses muchel seoluer muchel gold his tweien sunen an his hond and forþ he gon wenden to þan kingen and þas word sæide þe sele hail seo þu aþelest kingen her ich bringe tweiene mine sunen beiene heore moder is kinges istreon quene heo is min aȝene ich tache þe mine leofen sunen miseolf ich wulle þi mon bicumen ich heo biȝat mid ræflac ut of rusie and ic wulle sende gauel of mine londe æuerælche ȝere to ȝiueles þingen ich wulle senden þe into lundene seouen þusend punden þat ic wulle swerien þat nulle ich næuere swiken ah here ich wulle þi mon bicomen þi monscipe is þa mare swiken nulle ich nauere swa longe swa beoþ auere nom his sonde and sende to winentlonde to þan kinge and hehte him cuþen an hiȝinge þat he hæfde in his hond brutlond and scotlond gutlond and irlond orcaneie and islond he hæhte cumen and bringen him his ældeste sune and ȝif he þat nolde he wolde hine driuen of londe and ȝif he mihte afon he wolde hine slæn oþer anhon and his lond al fordon his leoden fordemen þis iherde þe riche king of winete swiþe he wes afered al swa þa oþere weoren arer laþe him weoren þa tidende from þan kinge noþeles þe king hercnede rædes he nom his ældeste sune and sele twælf eorles and ferde to þan kinge aþele and set æt his foten and feire hine gon greten hail seo þu aþelest brutten ich hatten þe king of winetlonde inoh ich habbe iherd kenne of kenscipe þine þat þu ært widen icuþ kingen alre kennest þu hauest moni kinelond biȝiten al to þire hond nis na king an londe þe þe maȝen stonde king ne na kaisere in nauere nane compe of al þat þu biȝinnest þu dest þine iwille her ich æm to þe icume and broht þe mine aldeste sune her ich sette þe an hond me seoluen and mi kinelond and minne sune leofe and mine leoden alle wif and mine weden and alle mine wunnen wiþ þat þu me griþie wiþ þine grim ræsen and beo þu min hæhȝe king and ich wulle beon þin underling and senden þe to honde fif hundred pund of golde þas ȝeuen ich finde þe wulle æueralche ȝere al him ȝette þat þe king ȝirde and seoþþen he heolde runen wiþ sele his þeinen and seide þat he wolde aȝæin to þisse londe and iseon þe wuneliche quene bemen he lette blawen and bonnien his ferden and to scipen wenden wunder bliþe þeines wind heom stod on willen weder alse heo wolden bliþe heo weoren alle for þi up heo comen at grimesbi þat iherden sone þa hæhste of þissen londe and to þære quene com tidende of þan kinge þat he wes isund icumen and his folc on selen þa weoren inne bruttene blissen inoȝe her wes fiþelinge and song her wes harpinge imong pipen and bemen murie þer sungen scopes þer sungen of þan kingen and of þan muchele wurþscipe þe he iwunnen hafeden folc com to hirede of feole cunne þeode widen and siden folc wes on selen al þat isæh al hit him to bæh riche men and pouere swa þe haȝel ualleþ nes þer nan swa wræcche þat he nes awælȝed her mon mai arede of þan king hu he twelf ȝere seoþen wuneden here inne griþe and inne friþe in alle uæȝernesse na man him ne faht wiþ no he ne makede nan unfriþ ne mihte nauere nan man biþenchen of blissen þat weoren in æi þeode mare þan i þisse ne mihte nauere moncunne nan swa muchel wunne swa wes mid and mid his folke here ich mai sugge hu hit iwarþ wunder þæh hit þunche hit wes in ane ȝeoldæie þat in lundene lai þa weoren him to icumen of alle his kinerichen of brutlonde of scotlonde of irlonde of islonde and of al þan londe þe hæfede an honde alle þa hæxte þeines mid horsen and mid sweines þer weoren seouen kingene sunes mid seouen hundred cnihten icumen wiþuten þan hired þe herede ælc hafede an heorte leches heȝe and lette þat he weore betere þan his iuere þat folc wes of feole londe þer wes muchel onde for þe an hine talde hæh þe oþer muche herre þa bleou mon þa bemen and þa bordes bradden water me brohte an uloren mid guldene læflen seoþþen claþes soften al of white seolke þa sat adun and bi him þa quene seoþþen sete þa eorles and þerafter þa beornes seoþþen þa cnihtes al swa mon heom dihte þa heȝe iborne þene mete beoren æfne forþrihten þa to þan cnihten þa touward þan þæinen þa touward þan sweinen þa touward þan bermonnen forþ at þan borden þa duȝeþe wærþ iwraþþed duntes þer weoren riue ærest þa laues heo weorpen þa while þa heo ilæsten and þa bollen seoluerne mid wine iuulled and seoþþen þa uustes uusden to sweoren þa leop þer forþ a ȝung mon þe ut of winetlonde com he wes iȝefen to halden to ȝisle he wes sune þas kinges of winette þus seide þe cniht þere to kinge lauerd buh raþe into þine bure and þi quene mid þe and þine mæies cuþe and we þis comp scullen todelen wiþ þas uncuþe kempen æfne þan worde he leop to þan borde þer leien þa cniues biforen þan leodkinge þreo cnifes he igrap and mid þan anæ he smat i þere swere þe cniht þe ærest bigon þat ilke fiht þat his hefued i þene flor hælde to grunde sone he sloh ænne oþer þes ilke þeines broþer ær þa sweordes comen seouene he afelde þer wes fæht swiþe græt ælc mon oþer smat þer wes muchel blodgute balu wes an hirede þa com þe king buȝen ut of his buren mid him an hundred beornen mid helmen and mid burnen ælc bar an his riht hond whit stelene brond þa cleopede aþelest kingen sitteþ sitteþ swiþe elc mon bi his liue and waswa þat nulle don he scal fordemed beon nimeþ me þene ilke mon þa þis feht ærst bigon and doþ wiþþe an his sweore and draȝeþ hine to ane more and doþ hine in an ley uen þer he scal liggen and nimeþ al his nexte cun þa ȝe maȝen iuinden and swengeþ of þa hafden mid breoden eouwer sweorden þa wifmen þa ȝe maȝen ifinden of his nexten cunden kerueþ of hire neose and heore wlite ga to lose and swa ich wulle al fordon þat cun þat he of com and ȝif ich aueremare seoþþen ihere þat æi of mine hirede of heȝe na of loȝe of þissen ilke slehte æft sake arere ne sculde him neoþer gon fore gold ne na gærsume hæh hors no hære scrud þat he ne sculde beon ded oþer mid horsen todraȝen þat is elches swiken laȝen bringeþ þene halidom and ich wulle swerien þeron swa ȝe scullen cnihtes þe weoren at þissen fihte eorles and beornes þat ȝe hit breken nulleþ ærst sweor aþelest kingen seoþþen sworen eorles seoþþen sweoren beornes seoþþen sweoren þeines seoþþen sweoren sweines þat heo naueremare þe sake nulde arere me nom alle þa dede and to leirstowe heom ladden seoþþen me bleou bemen mid swiþe murie dremen weoren him leof weoren him læþ elc þer feng water and clæþ and seoþþen adun seten sæhte to borden al for æiȝe aþelest kingen birles þer þurngen gleomen þer sungen harpen gunnen dremen duȝeþe wes on selen þus fulle seoueniht wes þan hirede idiht seoþþen hit seiþ in þere tale þe king ferde to cornwale þer him com to anan þat wæs a crafti weorcmon and þene king imette and feiere hine grætte hail seo þu aþelest kinge ich æm þin aȝe mon moni lond ich habbe þurhgan ich con of treowrekes wunder feole craftes ich iherde suggen biȝeonde sæ neowe tidende þat þine cnihtes at þine borde gunnen fihte a midewinteres dæi moni þer feollen for heore mucchele mode morþgomen wrohten and for heore hehȝe cunne ælc wolde beon wiþinne ah ich þe wulle wurche a bord swiþe hende þat þer maȝen sitten to sixtene hundred and ma al turn abuten þat nan ne beon wiþuten wiþuten and wiþinne mon toȝæines monne whenne þu wult riden wiþ þe þu miht hit leden and setten hit whar þu wulle after þine iwille and ne dert þu nauere adrede to þere worlde longen þat æuere ænie modi cniht at þine borde makie fiht for þer scal þe hehȝe beon æfne þan loȝe timber me lete biwinnen and þat beord biginnen to feouwer wikene uirste þat wrec wes iuorþed to ane heȝe dæie þat hired wes isomned and himseolf beh sone to þan borde and hehte alle his cnihtes to þan borde forþrihtes þo alle weoren iseten cnihtes to heore mete þa spæc ælc wiþ oþer alse hit weore his broþer alle heo seten abuten nes þer nan wiþuten æuere ælches cunnes cniht þere wes swiþe wel idiht alle heo weoren bi ane þa hehȝe and þa laȝe ne mihten þer nan ȝelpen for oþere kunnes scenchen oþer his iueren þe at þan beorde weoren þis wes þat ilke bord þat bruttes of ȝelpeþ and sugeþ feole cunne lesinge bi þan kinge swa deþ aueralc mon þe oþer luuien con ȝif he is him to leof þenne wule he liȝen and suggen on him wurþscipe mare þenne he beon wurþe ne beo he no swa luþer mon þat his freond him wel ne on æft ȝif on uolke feondscipe arereþ an æueræi time bitweone twon monnen me con bi þan læþe lasinge suggen þeh he weore þe bezste mon þe æuere æt at borde þe mon þe him weore laþ him cuþe last finden ne al soh ne al les þat leodscopes singeþ ah þis is þat soþþe bi þan kinge nes næuer ar swulc king swa duhti þurh alle þing for þat soþe stod a þan writen hu hit is iwurþen ord from þan ænden of þan kinge no mare no lasse buten alse his laȝen weoren ah bruttes hine luueden swiþe and ofte him on liȝeþ and suggeþ feole þinges bi þan kinge þat næuere nes iwurþen a þissere weorlderichen inoh he mai suggen þe soþ wule uremmen seolcuþe þinges bi kinge þa wes swiþe heh his hired swiþe hende þat nas na cniht wel itald no of his tuhlen swiþe bald inne wales no in ænglelond inne scotlond no in irlond in normandie no inne france inne flandres no inne denemarc no in nauere none londe þe a þeos halfe mungiu stondeþ þet weoren ihalde god cniht no his deden itald oht bute he cuþe of and of aþelen his hirede his wepnen and his weden and his horsleden suggen and singen of þan ginge and of his hiredcnihten and of heȝe heore mihten and of heore richedome and hu wel hit heom bicomen þenne weore he wilcume a þissere weorlderichen come þer he come and þeh he weore i rome al þat iherde of telle heom þuhte muchel seollic of selen þan kinge and swa hit wes iuuren iboded ær he iboren weoren swa him sæide þe witeȝe wes mære þat a king sculde cume of vþere þat gleomen sculden wurchen burd of þas kinges breosten and þerto sitten scopes swiþe sele and eten heore wullen ær heo þenne fusden and winscenches ut teon of þeos kinges tungen and drinken and dreomen daies and nihtes þis gomen heom sculde ilasten to þere weorlde longe and ȝet him seide mare þat wes to comene þat al þat he lokede on to foten him sculde buȝen þa ȝet him sæide a sellic þe wes mare þat sculde beon unimete care of þas kinges forþfare and of þas kinges ende nulle hit na ileue buten hit beon þe leste dæþ at þan muchele dome þenne ure drihte demeþ alle uolke ælles ne cunne we demen of deþen for he seolf sæide to sele his brutten suþ inne cornwale þer walwain wes forfaren and himseolf wes forwunded wunder ane swiþe þat he uaren wolde into aualune into þan æitlonde to þere hende for heo sculde mid haleweie helen his wunden and þenne he weore al hal he wolde sone come heom þis ilefde bruttes þet he wule cumen þus and lokieþ a whenne he cume to his londe swa he heom bihahte ar he heonne wende wes an weorlde wis king and riche god mon and griþful his gumen hine luueden cnihtes he hafede prute and græte on heore mode and speken to þan kinge of seollichen þinge and þus þat hired cleopede to heȝe þan kinge lauerd faren we to francene riche and iwinnen al þat lond to þire aȝere hond flemen alle þa freinscen heore king feollen alle þa castles bonien and setten heom to mid brutten and rixlien a þere riche mid rehȝere strengþe þa andswarede aþelest kingen eouwer wille ich wulle don ah ær ich wulle to norweien and ich wulle mid me leden lot minne oþem he is fader þa ich wel luuie for beoþ icumen of norweiȝe niwe tidende þat king þer is ded his duȝeþen bileued and hæ hafeþ al his kineriche biqueþe her loþþe for þe king is al bidæled sune and eke dohteren and lot is his suster sune þe bet him scal iwurþe for ich hine wulle in norwæȝe neowe king makien and hine wæl lere to witeȝen wel þa leoden and þenne ich þus habbe idon ich wullen seoþþen cumen ham and ȝarkien mine ferde and faren into france and ȝif þe king me stont wiþ and nulle ȝeornen mi griþ ich hine wulle mid fehte fallen to þan grunde lette blawen hornes and bemen and lette beoden to sæ bruttes swiþe balde scipen he hæfde gode bi þere sæflode fiftene hundred fusden from londe and fluȝen after þere sæ swulc heo fluht hafden and buhȝen into norwæȝen mid baldere strengþen sone swa heo comen hafne heo nomen mid muchelere strengþe stepen a þa riche senden his sonde wide ȝeond þan londe and hæhte heom cumen sone and lot habben to kinge and ȝif heo þat nolden alle heom he wolde aslan þa nomen heore sonden eorles norenissce and senden to þan kingen and hahten hine aȝain wenden and ȝif þu nult aȝæin faren sorhȝen þu scalt habben and kare for longe biþ auere þat ne iwurþ næuere þat we uncuþne mon to kinge scullen hæbben for ȝif is forþfaren her beoþ oþere icoren þe we maȝen bi vre iwille hæbben to kinge and þis is þat soþe nis þer nan oþer oþer far þe awæiward and wend þe riht hamward oþer todæi a seoueniht þu scalt habben græt fiht þa eorles norenissce nomen heom to ræde þat king heo wolden habben of seoluen heore cunden for al quiden sotscipe heo heolden and swa longe swa beoþ æuere ne scal hit stonde næuere ah we scullen nimen þe is swiþe riche eorl and hebben hine to kinge þis is us iqueme and sumnen ure ferde ȝeond al þissen ærde and faren to and flemmen hine mid fehte and lot we scullen fusen and flemen of londen oþer we mid fehten sculleþ hine fallen heo nome þene eorl of norene and hefuen hine to kinge þeh hit neore him noht icunde and sumneden uerde ȝeond nornisce ærde and an his ende ȝuond þat lond gon wende þat londe he þurharnde burhȝes he uorbarnde æhte he nom inoh muche moncun he þer ofsloh and him gon riden toȝæines anan togædere heo fusden and veht heo bigunnen bruttes buȝen heom to balu þer wes riue luken vt of scaþe sweordes longe hefden fluȝen a þene uelde faluwede nebbes beorn aȝein beorne scaft sette an breoste burnen þer breken bruttes bisie weoren brustleden sceldes scalkes ueolen and swa al þene dæiliht ilaste þis muchele fiht ferden heo æst ferden heo west þer noreine wes þa wurse ferden heo suþ ferden heo norþ þe norrene þer feollen bruttes weoren balde þa noreine heo aqualden noreinisce men þer feollen fif and twenti þusend and king þer wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen lutel þer eode to læue of þan leodfolke wulcswa hafuede þat wracche lif ȝirde griþ bisæh a lot þe leof him wes swiþe and þus him cleopien agon þe riche mon lot wend hider to me þu art mi wine deore her ich þe biteche al þas kineriche of me þu scalt halden and habben me to munde þa wes walwain þider icumen lottes ældeste sune of rome from þan pape þe supplice wes ihate þa longe him wes dihte and makede hine to cnihte wælle wel wes hit bitoȝen þat walwain wes to monne iboren for walwæin wes ful aþelmod an ælche þeouwe he wes god he wes metecusti and cniht mid þan bezste al hired wes swiþe ifurþed for þan kene þe icumen wes to hirede and for his fader lote þe iloten wes to kinge þa spac him wiþ and hehte hine halden god griþ and hehte hine luuien his griþfulle leoden and þa griþ nolden halden fallen heom to grunde þa ȝet cleopede aþelest kingen whær beo ȝe mine bruttes fareþ nu forþrihtes ȝarkieþ bi þan flode mine scipen gode al duden þa cnihtes swa heom hæhte þa þa scipen weoren ȝaru gon to sæ faren mid him he nom his cnihtes his norenissce þeines and balden his bruttes and bah forþ mid vþes and þe duhtie king com to denemarke he lette slæn teldes wide ȝeond þa feldes bemen he lette blawen and his cume bodien þa wes inne denemarke a king of mucle mæhte wes ihate hext ouer denene he isah þat biwon al þat him wes on willen king hine biþohte whæt he don mahte laþ him wes to leosen leouen his leoden he isah þat mid strengþe stonden he ne mahte aȝain mid nauere nane compe he sende gretinge to kinge hundes and hauekes and swiþe gode horsses seoluer and ræd gold mid ræhfulle worden and ȝet dude mare þe mære he sende to þan hæxten of hireden and bad heom arndien him to hæhȝen þan kingen þat he moste his mon bicumen and to ȝisle bitæchen his sune and ælche ȝere him senden gauel of his londe ænne bæt mid isunde from breorde to grunde of golde and of gærsume and of godliche pallen and seoþþen he wolde swerien swiken þat he nalden þis iherden aþelest kingen þat denene king wolde beon his vnderling buten ælche fihte he and alle his cnihtes þa iwraþ iaþeled þe riche and þus andswærede mid aþmode worden wel wurþe þan monne þe mid wisdome biwineþ him griþ and friþ and freondscipe to halden þenne he isiht þet he biþ mid strengþe ibunden iȝarked al to leosen leofue his richen mid liste he mot leoþien luþe his bendes hehte þene king cume and bringen his aldeste sune and he swa dude sone þe king of denemarke iwille sone he gon fulle tosomne heo comen and sæhten iwurþen þa ȝet cleopede aþelest kingen faren ich wulle to france mid muchele mire ferde ich wulle habben of noreweie niȝe þusend cnihtes and of denemarke ich wulle leden niȝe þusend of þan leoden and of orkaneie enleuen hundred and of mureinen þreo þuseond monnen and of galeweien fif þusend of þan leoden and of irlonde elleuen þusend and of brutaine mine cnihtes balde scullen þræsten biforen me þritti þusunde and of gutlonde ich wulle leden ten þuseond of þan leoden and of frislonde fif þusend monnen and of brutaine þene balde and mid swulche uolke france ich wulle isechen and swa ich ibiden godes ære ȝet ich wulle haten mare þat of alle þan londen þat stondeþ a mire honden ich haten ælcne ohtne mon þe his wepnen beren con alse he wule liuen and his lumen habben þat he faren wiþ me to fehten wiþ frolle þat is francene king fæie he scal iwurþe he wes iboren i rome of romanisce cunne forþ ferde þat he com to flandres þat lond he gon biwinnen and sette hit mid his monnen and seoþþe he beh þanene into buluine and al buluines lond nom hit to his aȝere hond and seoþþen he nom þene wæi þe in touward france læi þa bed he his bod allen his beornen for þær heo uoren þat na wiht heo ne nomen buten he mid rihte hit biȝiten mihte mid rihte chepinge i þas kinges hirede þat iherde frolle þer he wes inne france of ispede and of alle his deden and hu al biwonne þat he lokede on and al hit him to beh þat he mid eȝene isah þa wes þe king frolle laþliche offered a þere ilke worlde þa þis wes iwurþen wes francene lond gualle ihaten and frolle wes from rome ifaren into france and ælche ȝere sende gauel of þan londe ten hundred punde of seoluer and of golde nu iherde frolle þe ældere wes of france of þere londsorȝe þe dude an londe sonde he sende sone an uest touward rome and hehte romanisce folc reden heom bitweonen hu feole þusend cnihten heo þider wolden senden þat he þa æþ mihte wiþ uihte and ulemen of londe þene stronge cnihtes gunnen riden vt of romleoden fif and twenti þusend ferden touward france þis iherde frolle mid muchele his ferde þat þe romanisce uolc riden touward londe frolle and his ferde heom toȝeines ferde þa heo comen tosomne kene men and wihte of alle þan ærde vnimete uerde þæt iherde aþelest kingen and sumnede his ferde and heom toȝaines wende ah næs næuere king nan þa quic wes an eorþen þa eouere ær an uolde swulc folc awalde for of alle þan kinelonde þe hafuede an honde forþ he ladde mid him alle þa kenneste men þat nuste he neuere on weorlde hu feole þusend þer weoren sone swa heo comen tosomne and frolle harliche heo igrætten al þat heo imette cnihtes swiþe stronge igripen speren longe and ræsden heom togædere mid ræhȝere strengþe alle dæi þer weore duntes swiþe riue folc feol to uolden and fæiesiþ worhten græmende segges grasbæd isohten gullen þa helmes ȝeoumereden eorles sceldes þær scenden scalkes gunnen reosen þa cleopede aþelest kingen whar beo ȝe mine bruttes balde mine þaines þe dæi him forþ ȝeongeþ þis folc us aȝein stondeþ lette we heom to gliden scærpe gares inoȝe and techen heom to riden þene wæi touward romen æfne þan worde þe iseide he sprong forþ an stede swa sparc deþ of fure him weore fuliende fifti þusende hærde herekempen hælden to fihte smiten uppen frolle þær he wes on ulocke and brohten hine of fleme mid muclen his folke þer ofsloh muchel uolc and vniuoh þa fleh into parise frolle þe riche and þa ȝeten tunden mid teonen inoȝe and þa word seide sorhful an heorte leouere me weore þat ich iboren neore þa weoren inne paris plihtliche spelles ful iwis sorhfulle iberen burhmen gunnen beouien walles heo gunnen rihten þa ȝæten heo gunnen dihten mete heo nomen al þat heo neh comen an ælchere halue heo heolden to burȝe heo uerden þider alle þe heolden mid frolle þat iherde aþelest kingen þat inne paris wunede frolle mid unimete uerde and seiden þat he wolde wiþ stonden to paris ferde ærhþe bideled and bilæi þa walles and arerde his teldes a feower halue he heo bilai fouwer wiken and enne dæi auared weoren þa leden þa þere weoren wiþinnen þa burh wes wiþinnen afulled mid monnen and æten sone þene mete þe þer wes isomned þa feouwer wiken weoren aȝonged þa wes þær atstonden þæ wes inne burȝe vnimete sorȝe mid wræcche þan falke þe leie þer an hungre þer wes wop þer wes rop and reouþen vniuohȝe heo cleopeden to frolle and beden hine friþ wurchen mon bicumen and his monscipe bruken and þene kinedom halden of þan kenen and no lete noht þat wræcche uolk uorfaren al mid hungre þa andswarede frolle freo he wes an heorte nai swa me helpe god þæ alle domes awalt ne scal ich nauere his mon bicume no he mi kinelauerd miseolf ich wulle fihte a gode is al þat rihte þa ȝet cleopede frolle freo mon an heorte næi swa me helpe drihten þe scop þas dæies lihten nulle ic naueremare ȝirnen ære ah fehten ich wulle buten ælche cnihte licame wiþ licame biforen mine leoden hond aȝain honde wiþ kinge whaþer unkere swa beoþ þere wakere sone he biþ þe laþere wahþer vnkere swa þer ma luuien his freonden he biþ þe leouere and whaþer unkere þe mæi of oþere þat betere biwinne habben al þis oþeres lond and sette hit an his aȝere hond þis ic wulle ȝirne ȝif hit wule ȝetten and þis ich wulle swerien uppen mine sweorden and ȝisles ich wulle finden þreo kingene sunen þat ich þis forward wulle fastliche halden þat nulle ich hit liȝen bi mine quike liuen for leouere me is to liggen bifore mine leoden þan ich iseo an uolde forfaren heom mid hungre for we habbeoþ mid fehte ure cnihtes uorfarene scalkes auælled fifti þusende and moni ænne gode wifmon iwhorht to bleþere widewe moni child faderlæs and frouere bidaled and nu þis folc mid hungre wunderliche ihærmede forþi hit is betere bitwixen unke seoluen todælen and todihten þis kinelond mid fihte and habbe hit þa betere and bruken hit on wunne frolle nom twalf cnihtes mid þissen worden forþrihtes and sende heom an sonde to kinge and iwuste ȝif he wolde þis forewarde halde and mid his aȝere hond bitelen þat kinelond oþer uoreliggen his leoden to harmen and ȝif he hit bitalden hafde hit on an onwalde þat iherde aþelest kingen næs he neuere swa bliþe ær an his liue for him likede tidende from frolle þan kinge and þas word seide þe sele wel saiþ frolle þe king is of france betere is þat wit tweie bitelen þas riche þene þer beon ofslaȝene ure þeines snelle þis foreward ich biluuie bifore mine leoden to ane isette dæie to don þat he beodeþ þat scal beon tomarȝen biforen unker monnen þat fehten wit scullen unc seoluen and falle þe forcuþere and whaþer unker þe geþ abake and þis feoht wulle forsake beon he in ælche londe iqueþe for ane sconde þenne mæie me singe of ane swulche kinge þe his beot haueþ imaked and his cnihtscipe forsaken þæt iherde frolle þe king wes of france þat fehten wolden himseolf buten cnihte strong mon wes frolle and sterc mon on mode and his beot imaked hafde biforen al his duȝeþe and he ne mihte for scome muchelen scenden hine seoluen bilæuen his balde ibeot þat he i burh hafde iseid sæide þat he sæide to soþe he hit wende þat hit wolde forsaken and nawiht to þan fehte taken for ȝif hit wuste frolle þe king wes ane france þat him ȝetten wolde þat he iȝirnd hafde don he hit nolde for a scip ful of golde neoþeles wes frolle to fihte swiþe kene muche cniht and strong mon and modi on heorten and sæide þat he wolde þene dæi halde in þan æitlonde þe mid watere is biȝeonge þat æitlond stondeþ ful iwis inne þere burh of paris þer ich wulle mid fehte bitele mine irihte mid scelden and mid cnihtes iwede nu tomarȝen biþ þe dæi habben þe hit biȝiten mæi comen þa tiþende to þan kinge þat frolle wolde mid fæhte france bitellen næs he næuere swa bliþe ær an his liue and he lehȝen agon ludere stæfnenen and þas word seide þe kene nu ich wat þat frolle wiþ me wulle fihte tomarȝe in þan dæie alse he seolf demde i þan aitlonde þat mid watere is bistonde for hit bicumeþ kinge þat his word stonde leteþ blawen bemen and bodien mine monnen þat æuerælc god mon toniht wakien for þon and bidden ure drihten þe alle domes awalt þat he me iscilde wiþ frolle þene wilde and mid his riht honde witeȝe me wiþ sconde and ȝif ich mæi þis kinelond biȝiten to mire aȝere hond auereælche ærmen mon þe æþ scal iwurþen and wurchen ic wulle muchel godes wille nu me uulsten þerto þe alle þing mai wel idon þe heȝe heueneliche king stonde me an helping for ich hine luuien wulle þa while þe ich liuie þer wes al longe niht songes and candelliht hæhliche sungen clarckes hali godes salmes þa hit dæi wes amarȝen duȝeþe gunne sturien his wæpnen he nom an honden þe stronge warp he an his rugge a ræf swiþe deore ænne scurte and ænne pallene curtel ænne burne swiþe deore ibroiden of stele sette he an hefde ænne helm godne to his side he swende his sweorde his sconken he helede mid hosen of stele and duden on his uoten spuren swiþe gode þe king mid his weden leop on his stede me him to rehte anne scelde gode he wes al clane of olifantes bane me salde him an honde enne scaft stronge þer wes a þan ænde a spære swiþe hende hit wes imaked i kairmeþin bi a smiþ þe hehte griffin hit ahte vþer þe wes ær king her þa þe iwepned wes þe rahȝe þa gon he to uarene he mihte þa bihalde þe þer bihalfues weore þene king richne rehliche riden seoþþen þis weorlde wes astald nes hit nowhar itald þat æuere ai mon swa hende wunden uppen horse swa him wes sune vþeres riden after þan kinge balde hereþringes a þen feoremeste flocke feouwerti hundred heȝe herekempen bihonged mid stelen baldere brutten bisie mid wepnen after þan fusden fifti hundred þeo ladde þe wæs a wælkempe seoþþen þer gunnen ut siȝen sixti þusende bruttes swiþe balde þat wes þa bacwarde þer wes þe king angel þer wes lot and þer wes vrienes sune ihaten þer wes kæi and beduer and biwusten þa uerde þer þer wes þe king hah mon of brutlond þer wes æc þe kene wes on flocke þer wes of irlonde þe strong þer wes gonwais þe king orkaneies deorling þer wes þe kene ut of gutlonde þer wes þe king denemarkes deorling folc þer wes afoten swa feole þusend monnen þat nas nauere na swa witful mon a þissere weorlderichen a nauere nane spelle þat mihte þa þusend telle bute he hauede mid rihte wisdom of drihtene oþer he hafde mid him þat him hafde forþ gon liþe mid vnimete folke þat he com fuliwis into þere burh of paris a west halue þan watere mid mucle his genge an æst hælf wes frolle mid mucchelere ferde ȝaru to þan fehte biforen his cnihtes alle nom ænne bat godne and bæh þer an inne mid scelde mid stede and mid alle his iwede and he þat scip stronge scaf from þan londe and stop uppen þat æitlond and ladde his stede an his hond his men þe hine þer brohte alse þe king hehte leten þene bat buȝen forþ mid þan vþen frolle into scipe ferde þe king wes unuele þat he auere þohte wiþ to fehte ferde to þan æite mid aþele his wepnen uppen þan æit he stop and his stede him after droh þeo men þe hine þer brohten alse þe king hehte lette þene bat fusen forþ mid þan vþen and þa kinges tweien ane þer wuneden þa me mihte bihalden þe þer bihalues weoren folc a þan uolde feondliche adredde heo clumben uppen hallen heo clumben uppen wallen heo clumben uppen bures heo clumben uppe tures þat comp to bihalden of þan tweom kingen men beden mid muchele æþmoden godd þene gode and þa hali his moder þat heore lauerd þere siȝe moste habben and þa oþere eke bede for heore kinge stop a stel boȝe and leop an his blancke and frolle mid his iwede leop on his steden þe an an his ænde a þan æitlonde and þæ oþer an his ænde i þan æitlonde heo quehten heore scaftes kinewurþe cnihtes heo græneden heore steden gode cnihtes heo weoren næs he næuere ifunde a næuere nane londe nan swa wihtful mon þat hit wuste ær þan whæþer of þan kingen ouercumen sculde liggen for beien heo weoren cnihtes kene ohte men and wihte muchele men on mihte and a maine swiþe stronge heo muneȝeden heore steden and tosomne gunnen riden fusden feondliche þat fur him sprong after smat frolle mid feondstronge maine uppen þene sceld hehȝe and þe stede þe wes god leop ut i þe ulod ut mid his sweorde balu wes a þan orde and puinden uppen frolle þer he wes an ulode ær heore comp weore icumen to þan ænde ah frolle mid honde igræp his spere longe and kept anan alse he aneoust com and þene stede balde smat i þere breoste þat þat spere þurh raf and adun draf þa aras þe mondrem þat þe uolde dunede aȝen aqueþen þa weolcne for reme of þan uolke þær bruttes wolden ouer water buȝen ȝif up ne sturte stercliche sone and igræp his sceld godne ileired mid golde and toȝaines frolle mid feondliche lechen breid biforen breosten godne sceld brade and frolle him to fusden mid his feondræse and his sweord up ahof and adunriht sloh and smat an sceld þat he wond a þene feld þe helm an his hæuede and his hereburne gon to falsie foren an his hafde and he wunde afeng feouwer unchene long heo ne þuhte him noht sær for heo næs na mare þat blod orn adun ouer al his breoste wes abolȝe swiþe an his heorte and his sweord swipte mid maine and smat frolle uppen þæne hælm þat he atwa helden þurhut þere burne hod þat hit at his breoste atstod þa feol frolle folde to grunde uppen þan grasbedde his gost he bilæfde þa bruttes lohȝen ludere stefuene and leoden to fleonen feondliche swiþe þe riche wende to londe and þus cleopien agon aþelest kingen whær ært þu walwain monne me leofest heot þas romwæren alle mid griþen liþen heonne ælc mon bruke his ham swulc godd hit him on hat ælcne mon halde griþ uppen leome and uppen lif and ich hit wulle dihten todæi a seouennihte hat þis folc þenne liþen al tosomne and cumen to me seoluen þæ bet heom scal iwurþen heo scullen me monradene mid monscipe fremmen and ich heom wulle holden a mine onwolden and setten i leode laȝen swiþe gode for nu scullen romanisce laȝen to þan grunde reosen þa iuurn here stoden mid frolle þe liþ on æite ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen herafter ful sone scal his cun of rome heren tidinge of þan kinge for ich heom wulle wiþ speken and rome walles tobreken and munegie heom hu king bruttes ladde þider in and iwon him þa londes alle þat stondeþ into rome beh to þan ȝæte forn at þere burȝe comen witfulle men þe þa burh biwusten and letten binnen mid alle his monnen bitahten him halles bitahten him castles bitahten him ful iwis al þa burh of paris þer wes muchel blissce mid brutisce uolke þe dæi sæh to burhȝe þe iset hafde com al þa monweorede and his men bicomen nom his duȝeþe and atwa heom todalde and þa haluendæle bitætte and hehte hine uaren sone mid muchele þere uerde mid brutisce monnen londes iwinnen dude al swa alse hine hehte he biwon barri and alle þa londes þerbi angou and turuine aluerne and gascunne and þa hafuenes alle þe herden to þan londes þe duc hæhte þe peytouwe ahte he nolde buȝen ah heold toȝæines him æuere nolde he ȝirnen na griþ ah him faht wiþ ofte he uolc ualde and ofte he ulem makede al þat lond weste and ofsloh þa leode þa isæh þe i peitou wes lauerd þat alle his leoden him to lose eoden wiþ he griþ makede mid al his monweorede and bicom mon þas aþele kingen him warþ liþe and luuede hine swiþe and hehte hine his lond bruken for he him bæh to foten þa hafde hæhliche agunnen hafde france and freoliche heo sette he nom þa his ferde and wende ȝeond þan ærde to burguine he wende and sette hit an his honde and seoþþen he gon liþen into loherne and alle þa londes sette himseolue an honde al þat isæh al hit him to bæh and seoþþen he wende ful iwis aȝain ham to paris þa hafde france mid gode griþe astalde iset and isemed þat sel was an þeoden þa hehte he þa cnihtes alden þa he hafde ȝare athalden þat heo to þan kinge comen and heore læn afængen for heo feole ȝeren hafden ibon his iueren summen he ȝæf lond summen seoluer and gold summen he ȝæf castles summen he ȝaf claþes hehte heom uaren an wunne and beten heore sunnen forbed heom to berne wapnen for ælde heom eode ouenan and hehte heom luuien swiþe godd in þissen liue þat he an ende ful iwis ȝefen heom his paradis þæt heo mosten bruken blisse mid ænglen alle þa cnihtes alde foren to heore londe and þa ȝunge bilæfden mid leouen heore kingen alle þa niȝen ȝere wuneden þere niȝen ȝere he heold france freoliche on honde and seoþþen na lengere þat lond he ne walde ah þa while þe þat kinelond stod an hond þinges seolcuþe siȝen to þere þeode monienne modfulne mon makede milde and monienne hehne mon he helde to his foten hit wes an ane æsttere þat men hafden iuaste þat an æstere dæi hafde his aþele men atsomne al þat hæhste moncun þat herden into francen and of alle þan londen þe þider in læien þer he ȝette his cnihten alle heore irihten elc ane he ȝef æhte alse he iærned hafde þus him iquaþ aþelest kingen kæi bisih þe hiderward þu ært min haxte stiward her ich angou ȝiue þe for þire weldede and alle þa irihte þe þider in beoþ idihte cneole me to beduer þu art min hexte birle her þa while þa ich beo an liue luuien ich þe wulle her ich ȝiue þe neustrie aneuste mire riche þa hehte neustrie þat nu hatte normandie þe ilke tweien eorles weoren deore men at rede and at rune an æuerælche tune þa ȝet him seide aþelest kingen wend þe hider þu ært mi mon and mi cun haue þu bulune and bruc his on wunne cumme ner þu art cniht wis and war her ich þene mans þe mid monscipe bitæche and bruc þu his on wunne for þire weldede þus þe king delde his drihtliche londes after heore iwurhte for he heom þuhte wurþe þa weoren bliþe spelles in hallen þer wes harepinge and song þer weoren blissen imong þa æstre wes aȝonge and aueril eode of tune and þat gras was riue and þat water wes liþe and men gunnen spilien þat wes mæi at tune nom his folc feire and to þere sæ uerde and lette bonien his scipen wel mid þan bezsten and ferde to þissen londe and up com at londen up he com at lundene leoden to blissen al hit wes bliþe þat hine isæh mid eȝen sone heo gunnen singe of þan kinge and of þere wurþscipe muchele þe he iwunne hafde þer custe uader þene sune and seide to him welcume dohter þa moder broþer þene oþer suster custe suster þa softere heom wes an heorten a monie hundred studen stoden bi þan weie folc fraininge of feole cunne þingen and cnihtes heom talden of heore onwalden and heore ȝeolp makeden of muchele biȝeten ne mihte na mon suggen nære he na swa hende mon of halue þan blissen þa weoren mid þan brutten ælc ferde an his neode ȝeond þas kineþeode from burhȝe to burhȝe mid blissen uniuoȝe and þus hit ane stunde stod a þan ilke blisse wes on brutene mid balde þan kinge þa æstre wes aȝeonge and sumer com to londe þa nom his red wiþ riche his monnen þat he wolde inne karliun bere his crune him on and a whitesunedæi his folc þer isomnie a þen ilke daȝen men gunnen demen þat nes i nane londe burh nan swa hende na swa wide cuþ swa karliun bi uske buten hit weoren þa burh riche þe rome is ihaten þa ȝet wes mid þan kinge moni mon an londe þat quidde þa burh of karlion ricchere þene rome and þat uske weore selest alre wateren medewes þer weoren brade bihalues þere burhȝe þer wes fisc þer wes fuȝel and fæiernesse inoȝe þer wes wude and wilde deor wunder ane monie þer wes al þa murhþe þe æi mon mihte of þenche ah nauer seoþþen þider bæh þa burh seoþþe no iþæh no nauere ne mæi bitwene þis and domesdæi summe bokes suggeþ to iwisse þat þa burh wes biwucched and þæt is wel isene soþ þat hit sunde i þære burh weoren twa munstres swiþe mære þat an munstre wes of seint þerinne wes muchel halidom þat oþer of þan martir seint þe heh is mid drihten þer weoren nunnen wel idon moni heh iboren wifmon þe biscopstole wes at seint per wes moni sel mon canunes þer weoren þe cuþ weoren widen þer wes moni god clarc þe wel cuþe a leore muchel heo ferden mid þan crafte to lokien in þan leofte to lokien i þan steorren nehȝe and feorren þe craft is ihate astronomie wel ofte heo þan kinge seide of feole þinge heo cudden him on leoden what him sculde ilimpen swulc wes þe burh of karliun þer wes muchel ricchedom þer wes muchel blisse mid bisie þan kinge þe king nom his sonde and sende ȝeond his londe hæhte cumen eorles hehte cumen beornes hehte cumen kinges and æc hereþringes hehte cumen biscoppes hehte cumen cnihtes hahte alle þa freomen þa euere weoren an londe bi heore life hehte heom beon a whitesunedæi at kærleon cnihtes gunnen riden vnimete whiden riden touward kairliun of feole cunne londen to þan whitesunedæie þer com þe king angel king of scotlonde mid sceone his folke moni wes þe faire mon þe folȝede þan kingen of mureiue king vrien and his fæire sune stater king of suþ wales and king of norþ wales eorl of cornwale þa þe king luuede moruiþ of glouchæstre of winchastre eorl of herford and beof eorl of oxeuord gursal þe balde from baþe þer com ride vrgent of chastre of dorchestre ærnald of salesburi and kinmarc of cantuareburi balien of silechæstre wigein of leirchæstre eorl of warwic mid folk swiþe sellic dunwale apries sune and kegein elauþes sune þer wes coittes sune and cradoc sune ædlein sune grimarc kinmarkes sune run and netan clofard and aikan kerin neton and traher and þis weoren aþele eorles and þa haxte þeines ohte of alle þissere þeode wiþuten þan beornen of borden þa na man ne mihte ikennen ne al þat folc inemnen þa weoren ærchebiscopes þreo inne þissere þeode inne lunden and in eouuerwic and inne karliun seint he wes swiþe hali mon þurh alle þinge wel idon to lundene læi þe ærchebiscopstol þe to cantwareburi wes seoþþe idon seoþþe engliscemen þis lond heom iwunnen to tellen þat folc of kairliun ne mihte hit na mon idon þer wes þe king irisce monnen deorling king of islonde king of gutlonde king kailin of frislonde king of denelonde þer wes loþ þe kene þe king wes bi norþe and gonwæis orcaneie king utlaȝen deorling þider com þe wilde þe eorl of builuine læȝer wes ihaten and his leoden mid him of flandres þe eorl of chærtres þe eorl cherin þeos ferede mid him al þat frensce moncun twalf eorles swiþe ræihe þe rixleden ouer france eorl of peiters kæi þe eorl of angers eorl of normandie þat lond hehte þa neustrie of þe mans com þe eorl of brutaine þe eorl eorl wes freo mon and faire weoren his iwede and al þat folc frensce bihongen weoren feire iwepned wel alle and hors ho hafden uatte þer weoren bisides fiftene biscopes nes na cniht ne na swein ne oht mon þat weore þein from þa porz of spaine to þan tune of alemaine þat þider icomen nere ȝif he iboden weore al for æie aþeles cunnes þa al þis hired wes icumen ælc king mid his folke þer me mihte bihalde þe þer bihalues weore moni seolcuþne mon þe isiȝen wes to burhȝen and feole cunne tiþende mid þan kinge þer wes moni sellic claþ þer wes moni cniht wraþ þer weoren herberȝe hæhliche awurþe þer þa innes weoren mid strengþe biwunnen þer weoren on uelden moni þusend telden þer com spic and water and aten vnimete ne mai hit na mon suggen on his tale of þan win and of þan ale þer com hey þer com gras þer com al þat god was þa al þis folc isomned was at sele þan kingge þa com þe whitesunedæi alse drihten hine sende þa comen þa biscopes alle biuoren heore kinge and þa ærchebiscopes þreo biuoren and þene kinehelm nome þa him wes icunde and setten uppen his hafde mid heȝere blisse swa heo hine gunnen lede al mid godes rede seint eoden biuoren he wes icoren þe ærchebiscop of lundene eode an his riht honden and bi his luft side þe ilke of eouerwike fiftene biscopes biuoren of feole londen icoren heo weoren bihangen alle mid palle swiþe balde þe weoren alle ibrusted mid barninge golde þer feouwer kinges eoden biuoren þan kaiseren heo weȝeden on heore honde feouwer sweord of golde þus hehte þa an þe wes a swiþe duhti mon þat wes þe king deorling þe oþer of scotlonde sweord he weide an honde and þe king of norþ walles and þe king of suþ wales and þus heo gunnen leden þe king to chirechen þeo biscopes gunnen singe biuoren þan leodkinge bemen þer bleowen bellen þer ringeden cnihtes gunnen riden wifmen forþ gliden to iwissen hit is isaid and soþ hit is ifunden þat no isah no mon nauer ær mid eorþliche monne her half swa hahne ricchedom a nauer nane hepen swa mid was aþeles cunnes into chirchen bicom þe riche mon þe archebiscop drihten him wes ful god of rome he wes legat and of þan hirede prelat he song þa hali masse biuoren þan leodkinge comen mid þere quene wifmen wel idone þere richchere monne wif alle þe wunede on londe and þere hehere monnen dohtere þa quene hafden isohte al swa þa quene hafde ihate bi hire fulle wite i þere chireche i þere suþ halue sat þe king himseolf bi pere norþ side þa quene þer comen hire biforen feouwer quenen icoren ælc bar on luft honde enne beh of rede gold and þreo snauwhite culueren setten an heore sculderen þæt weoren þa feouwer quenen þere cnihte wifen þa beren an heore heonden þe feouwer sweordes of golde biuoren aþelest kingen moni mæide child wes þere mid mære þere quene þær wes moni pal hende on faire þan uolke of monies cunnes londe þer wes muchel onde for ælc wende to beon betere þene oþer feole cnihtes anan comen to þere chirechen summe for guþinge summe for þan kinge summe to bihalden þa wifmen þat weoren balde songes þer weoren murie þa ilaste swiþe longe ich weone ȝif hit weore ilast seoue ȝere þa ȝet heo weolden mare þe þerat weoren þa þe masse wes isungen of chircchen heo þrunge þe king mid his folke to his mete uerde mid mucle his duȝeþe drem wes on hirede þa quene an oþer halue hire hereberwe isohte heo hafde of wifmonne wunder ane monien þa þe king wes isete mid his monnen to his mete to þan kinge com þæ biscop seind þe wes swa god and nom of his hafde his kinehælm hæhne for þan mucle golde þe king hine beren nalde and dude enne lasse crune on þas kinges hafde and seoþþen he gon do a þere quene al swo inne troie þis wes laȝe bi heore ælderne daȝe þa bruttes of come þe weoren wel idone alle þa wepmen at heore mete seten sundi bi heomseoluen þat heom þuhte wel idon and al swa þa wifmen heore iwune hafden þa þe king wes isete mid alle his duȝeþe to his mete eorles and beornes at borde þas kinges þe stiward com steppen pe kæy wes ihaten hæxt cniht on londe vnder þan kinge of alle þan hæpe of hirede hehte him biuoren moni hæh mon icoren þer weoren a þusend cnihtes bald wunder wel italde þat þeineden þan kingen and his hereþringen ælc cniht hafde pal on and mid golde bigon and alle heore uingeres iriuen mid gold ringes þas beorn þa sunde from kuchene to þan kinge an oþer half wes beduer þas kinges hæȝe birle mid him weoren eorlene sunen of aþele cunne iboren and þere hehȝe cnihtene sunen þa þider weoren icumen seouen kingene sunen þat mid him quehten auormest eode mid guldene bolle after him a þusend þrasten to hirede mid alle þas cunnes drenche þe me cuþe on biþenche and þa quene an hire ende wifmen swiþe hende a þusend hire eode biuoren riche men and wel icoren to þæinen þere quene and þai þat mid hire weoren nes he næuere iboren of nane cnihte icoren ilæred no læwed a nauere nare leode þe cuþe him itelle an æies cunnes spelle of halue þan richedome þe wes inne kairliune of seoluere and of golde and gode iweden of hehȝe iborene monnen þa inne hirede wuneden of horsen and of hafueken of hunden to deoren and of riche iweden þa a þan hirede weoren and of alle þan folke þe wuneden þer on folde wes þisses londes folk leodene hendest itald and al swa þa wimmen wunliche on heowen and hahlukest iscrudde and alre bezst itoȝene for heo hafden on iqueþen alle bi heore quike liue þat heo wolden of ane heowen heore claþes habben sum hafde whit sum hafden ræd sum hafde god grene æc and alches cunnes fah claþ heom wes wunder ane laþ and elche untuhtle heo talden vnwurþe þa hafde ænglene ard þat alre bezste hereword and þis leodisce uolc æc leofuest þan kinge þa wifmen hehȝe iborene þa wuneden a þissen londe hafden iqueþen alle on heore quides soþe þat nan lauerd taken nolde inne þissere leode næuer nænne cniht neore he noht swa wel idiht bute he icostned weoren þrie inne compe and his ohtscipen icudde and ifonded hine seolue baldeliche he mitte þenne ȝirnen him brude for þere ilke tuhtle cnihtes weoren ohte þa wifmen wel idone and þa betere biwitene þa weoren i brutene blissen inoȝe þa þe king iȝeten hafde and al his monweorede þa buȝen of burhȝe þeines swiþe balde alle þa kinges and heore hereþringes alle þa biscopes and alle þa clærckes alle þa eorles and alle þa beornes alle þa þeines alle þa sweines feire iscrudde helde ȝeond felde summe heo gunnen ærnen summe heo gunnen urnen summe heo gunnen lepen summe heo gunnen sceoten summe heo wræstleden and wiþergome makeden summe heo on uelde pleouweden vnder scelde summe heo driuen balles wide ȝeond þa feldes monianes kunnes gomen þer heo gunnen driuen and whaswa mihte iwinne wurþsciþe of his gomene hine me ladde mid songe atforen þan leodkinge and þe king for his gomene ȝæf him ȝeuen gode alle þa quene þe icumen weoren þere and alle þa lafdies leoneden ȝeond walles to bihalden þa duȝeþen and þat folc plæie þis ilæste þreo dæȝes swulc gomes and swulc plæȝes þa a þan ueorþe dæie þe king gon to spekene and aȝæf his gode cnihten al heore rihten he ȝef seoluer he ȝæf gold he ȝef hors he ȝef lond castles and claþes eke his monnen he iquemde þer wes moni bald biuoren nu comen to þan kinge neouwe tidinde þe balde king sat at ane borde biuoren him seten kinges and feole hereþringes biscopes and clærekes and swiþe ohte cnihtes þer comen into halle spelles seolcuþe þer comen twalf þeines ohte mid palle biþehte hæȝe herekempen hehȝe men on wepne ælc hafde on heonde grætne ring of golde and mid æne bende of golde ælc hafde his hæfd biuonge æuer tweie and tweie tuhte tosomne ælc mid his honde heold his iuere and gliden ouer ulore biuoren swa longe þat heo comen biuoren þan leodkinge heo grætten anan mid aþelen heore worden hal seo þu king bruttene deorling and hal seo þi duȝeþe and al þi drihtliche uolc we sunden twælf cnihtes icumen her forþrihtes riche and wel idone we sundeþ of rome hider we sunden icumene from ure kaisere is ihaten þe waldoþ romeleoden he hahte us hider wende to þan kinge and þe hat græten mid his grim worden and sæiþ þat he awundred is wunder ane swiþe whar þu þat mod nime a þisse middenerde þat þu derst of rome wiþsuggen æi dome oþer hebben up þin eȝen aȝein ure ældren and wha hit þe durre ræden þat þu swa reh ært iwurþen þat þu þrattien darst domes walden þene kaisere hexst of quicke monnen þu haldest al þi kinelond a þire aȝere hond and nult noht þene kaisere of londe ihere of þan ilke londe þe hafde an honde þa inne iuurn daȝæn biwon hit mid fehten and þu hit hauest atholde a þire anwolde mid balden þine cnihten binimest us ure irihten ah sæi us sone and word send to rome we sculleþ bere þin ærde to ure kaisere ȝif þu wult icnawen þat he is king ouer þe and þu his mon bicumen wulle and hine for lauerd icnawen and don riht þan kaisere of frolle þan kinge þat þu mid woȝe at paris asloȝe and nu haldest al his lond mid unrihte a þire hond ȝif þu i þissen twælf wiken temest to þan rihten and þu wult of rome þolien æi dome þenne miht þu libben imong þine leoden and ȝif þu swa nult don þu scalt wursen vnderfon þe kaisere wule her cumen swa king scal to his aȝen king swiþe kene and nimen þe mid strengþe ibunden þe lede biuoren romleoden þenne most þu þolien þat þu ærst forhoȝedest æfne þisse worden bruttes buȝen from borden þer wes hird hehliche awraþþed and muchene aþ sworen uppen mære ure drihten þat alle heo dede weoren þa þeos arunde beden mid horsen al todraȝene dæþ heo sculden þolie þer heo buȝen to bruttes swiþe wraþe luken heom bi uaxe and laiden heom to grunde þer weoren men romanisce reouliche atoȝene ȝif ne leope to swulc hit a liun weore and þas word seide wisest alre brutten bilæueþ bilaueþ swiþe þas cnihtes on liue ne sceollen heo on mine hirede nenne harm þolien heo beoþ hider iriden ut of romleoden swa heore lauerd heom hehte is ihaten ælc mon mot liþen þer his lauerd hine hateþ gan nah na man demen erendesmon to dæþen bute he weoren swa ufele biwiten þet he weore lauerdswike ah sitteþ adun stille cnihtes inne halle and ich me biræde wulle of swulchere neode wulc word heo scullen aȝen beren to þan kaiseren þa seten adun alle þa duȝeþe on heore benche and þa luding alæid biuoren þan leodkinge þa stod him up aþelest kingen and he cleopede him to seouen sune kinges eorles and beornes and þa þe weoren baldest and alle þa wiseste men þa wuneden a þen folke wenden into ane huse þe wes biclused faste an ald stanene weorc stiþe men hit wurhten þer men gunnen rune his redȝeuen wise wulc andswere he ȝiuen wolde þan kaisere þa iboȝen weoren alle beornes to benche þa wes hit al stille þat wuneden inne halle þer wes vnimete æie mid mære þan kinge ne durste þer na man speken leste þe king hit wolde awreken þa stod þer up þe eorl swiþe riche ær and þas word sæide bifore þan riche kinge ich þonkie mine drihte þat scop þes dæies lihte þisses dæies ibiden þa to hirede is iboȝen and þissere tidinge þe icumen is to ure kinge þat we ne þuruen na mare aswunden liggen here for idelnesse is luþer on ælchere þeode for idelnesse makeþ mon his monscipe leose ydelnesse makeþ cnihte forleosen his irihte idelnesse græiþeþ feole uuele craften idelnesse makeþ leosen feole þusend monnen þurh eþeliche dede lute men wel spedeþ for ȝare we habbeoþ stille ileien ure wurþscipe is þa lasse ah nu ic þonkie drihtne þæ scop þas daȝes lihte þat romanisce leoden sunden swa ræie and heore beot makieþ to cumen ure burhȝes ure king binden and to rome hine bringen ah ȝif hit is soþ þat men saiþ alse segges hit telleþ þat romanisce leoden sunden swa ræȝe and sunden swa balde and swa balufulle þat heo wulleþ nu liþen into ure londen we heom scullen ȝarekien ȝeomere spelles heore ræhscipe scal heomseoluen to reouþe iwurþen for nauere ne lufede ich longe griþ inne mine londe for þurh griþe we beoþ ibunden and wel neh al aswunden þat iherde walwain þe wes mæi and wraþþede hine wiþ swiþe þa þas word kende and þus andswærede walwain þe sele þu ært a riche mon þine ræddes ne beoþ noht idon for god is griþ and god is friþ þe freoliche þer haldeþ wiþ and godd sulf hit makede þurh his goddcunde for griþ makeþ godne mon gode workes wurchen for alle monnen biþ þa bet þat lond biþ þa murgre þa iherde þat flit of þissen eorlen and þus spac þe riche wiþ raȝen his folke sitte adun swiþe mine cnihte alle and ælc bi his lifen luste mine worden al hit wes stille þat wunede inne halle þa spak þe king balde to riche his folke mine eorles mine beornes balde mine þeines mine duhti men mine freond deoren þurh eou ich habbe biwunnen vnder þere sunnen þat ich æm swiþe riche mon reh wiþ mine feonden gold ich habbe and gærsume gumenen ich æm ælder no biwan ich hit noht ane ah dude we alle clæne to moni feohte ich habbe eou ilad and æuere ȝet weoren wel irad swa þat feole kinelondes stondeþ a mine honde ȝe beoþ gode cnihtes ohte men and wihte þat ich habbe iuonded i wel feole londen þa ȝet him spac aþelest kingen nu ȝe habbeoþ iherd hæȝe mine þeines what romanisce men redeþ heom bitwenen and wulc word heo sendeþ us here into ure londe mid write and mid worde wiþ grætere wræþþe nu we mote biþenchen hu we ure þeoden and ure muchele wurþscipe mid rihte maȝen biwiteȝen wiþ þis riche moncun wiþ þas romeleoden and andsware heom senden mid aþelen ure worden mid mucle wisdome vre writ senden to rome and iwiten at þan kæisere for whan he us ofcunnen for whan he us mid þrætte and mid hokere igræteþ swiþe sære me gromeþ and vnimete me scomeþ þat he atwit us ure luren þat we ifeorn habbeoþ forloren heo suggeþ þat cesar hit biwon mid compe i fehten mid strengþe and mid fehte me deþ feole vnrihte for cesar isohte bruttene mid baldere strengþe no mihte bruttes wiþ him heore lond werien ah mid strenþe heo eoden an hond and bitahten him al heore lond and þerafter sone alle his men bicome sum ure cun heo hadden islaȝen and sum mid horsen todraȝen summe heo ladde ibunden ut of þissen londen and þis lond biwunne mid unrihte and mid sunnen and nu axeþ mid icunde gauel of þissen londe al swa we maȝen don ȝef we hit don wulleþ þurh rihte icunde of kinge and of brennen his broþer þan duc of burgunne þeos weoren ure ældre þa we beoþ of icumene þeos bilæie rome and þa riche al biwunnen and biuoren rome þere stronge heore ȝisles anhenge and seoþþen heo nomen al þat lond and setten hit an heore aȝere hond and þus we mid rihte ahten rome us biriden nu ich wulle leten and brenne bilæuen and speken of þan kaisere þan stronge he wes helene sune al of brutten icume he biwon rome and þa riche awelde lete we nu of þe rome iwon al to him and speken of þat was a swiþe strong mon he wes king of brutene he biwon france þe stronge rome he nom an honde and alemaine he biwon eke mid wunder muchele strengþe and al from romayne into normandie and þeos weoren mine ælderen mine aþþele uoregenglen and ahten alle þa leoden þa into rome leien and þurh swuche dome ich ahte to biȝeten rome heo ȝirneþ me an honde gauel of mine londe al swa ic wille of rome ȝif ich ræd habbe ich wilnie a mine þonke to walden al rome and he wilneþ me in brutene to binde swiþe uaste and slæn mine bruttes mid his balureses ah ȝif hit on mi drihten þe scop dæiȝes and nihtten he scal his balde ibeot sære abuggen and his romleoden þerfore scullen reosen and ic wulle ræh beon þer he nu rixleþ on wunieþ nu stille alle ic wulle suggen mine iwille ne scal hit na man oþer idon ah hit scal stonden þeron he wilneþ al and ich wilni al þæt wit beiene aȝæþ habben hit nu and aȝe þe hit æþ mæȝen iwinne for nu we scullen cunne wham hit godd unne þus spac þe balde þe brutene hafde an onwalde þat wes þe king bruttene deorling setten his kempen and his quides lusten summe heo sæten stille mucle ane stunde summe heo muche runen ræhten heom bitweonen summe hit þuhte heom god summe hit mengden heore mod þa heo hafden longe ilustned þan kinge þa spac þe hende hah mon of brutene and his quides ræhte biuoren raien þan kinge lauerd king hercne me alse ich ær dude þe þu hafest isæid word soþe selehþe þe beoþ ȝifþe hit wes ȝare iqueþen þat we nu sculleþ cuþen i þan iuurn ȝere þat nu is ifunden here sibeli hit sæide hire quides weoren soþe and sette hit on bocke uolke to bisne þat þreo kinges sculden buȝen ut of brutlonde þa biwinnen sculden rome and al þa riche and alle þa londes þe þerto liggeþ þe uorme wes þat wes a brittisc king þe oþer wes þe king wes on brutene þu scalt beon þe þridde þe rome scal habben and ȝif þu wult biginnen þu hit scalt biwinnen and ich wulle þerto helpe mid haȝere strenþe ich wulle ouer sæ sende to selen mine þeinen to balden mine brutten þa bet we scullen fusen ich wulle haten alle þa aþele of bruttainne bi leomen and bi heore liue ȝeond alle mine londe þat heo beon ȝarewe sone mid þe uaren to rome mi lond ich wulle sette to wedde for seoluere and alle þe æhten of mine londe for seoluere and for golde and swa we scullen uaren to rome and slan þene kaisere and bitellen þine irihten i þe lede ten þusend cnihtes þus spilede hext of brutaine þa þe iseid hafde þat him sel þuhte þa spæc angel þe king scotlondes deorling and stod uppen ane boncke and beien his broþeren þat was lot and vrien tweie swiþe aþele men þus angel þe king seide to þan kene læuerd ich sugge þe þurh soþe quides mine þat ilke þat hafeþ ispeken ne scal hit na man awreken ah we hit scullen ilæsten bi ure quicke liuen and lauerd þe hæhȝe lust me ane stunde cleope þe to ræde þine eorles riche and alle þa hæxte þa beoþ in þine hirede and bide heom þe suggen mid soþen heore worden whæt heo þe wulleþ fulste þine iuan to fordonne ich þe leden wulle cnihtes of mire leode þreo þusend kempen ohte alle icorene ten þusend men auote to uehte swiþe gode and fare we to rome and iwinnen þa riche ful swiþe us mæi scomien and ful swiþe us mai gromien þat heo sculle senden sonden after gauele to ure londe ah swa us helpe drihte þæ scop þas daȝes lihte heo hit scullen abugge mid heore bare liue for þenne we habbeoþ rome and alle þa riche we scullen nimen þa londes þa þerto liggeþ peoile and alemaine lumbardie and brutaine france and normandie þa hit hæhte neustrie and swa we sculleþ meþegie heore mod vnimete þa þe king isaid hafde þa andswarede alle iniþered wurþe þe ilke mon þe þerto nule helpen mid ahten and mid wepnen and mid alle his imihten þa wes hired sturneliche awraþþed cnihtes anburste weoren þat alle heo gunnen biuien þa iherd hafde his hired iberen þa cleopien agon þe king wes abolȝen sitteþ adun stille cnihtes inne halle and ich eou wulle telle what ich don wulle mine writen ich wulle maken þa wel beon idihte and sende þan kæisere modes sorȝe and muchel kare and ich wulle ful sone faren into rome nulle ich þider na gauel bringe ah þane kaiser ich wulle binden and seoþþen ich wullen hine anhon and al þat lond ich wulle uordon and foruaren þa cnihtes alle þe aȝein me stondeþ i fehte his writ nom an honden mid wiþerfulle worden and þan beornen hit bitahte þæ þa ærnde hafde ibrohte and seoþþe he lette heom scruden mid ælchere pruden mid þan hæxte scrude þa he hafde on bure and hehte heom faren sone to of rome and he cumen after wolde swa raþe swa he mihte þas twælfe heore wai ferden touward heore londen mid seolure and mid golde cnihtes swa iscrudde no þurh al swa wel idihte þus heom dihte al for heore worde þas twalf cnihtes foren þat heo to rome comen heo gretten heore kaisere heore kinelauerd hail seo þu þu art hæxt ouer us we woren at þan raȝe at þan kinge we habbeoþ writen ibroht þe word swiþe grate is þe kenneste mon þat we æuere lokeden on and he is wunder riche and his þeines beoþ balde þer is æuerælc swein swulc he cniht weore þer is æuerælc swein swulc he weore riche þein þer beoþ þa cnihtes swulc hit weoren kinges mete þer is vnimete and men swiþe balde and þa ueieȝereste wifmen þa wunieþ on liuen and himseolf þe balde uæiȝerest ouer alle bi us he sende word þe þat he wule to þisse londe na gauel he nule bringen ah þe seoluen he wule binden and seoþþ he wule þe anhon and þis lond al fordon and alemaine lunbardie burguine france and normandie frolle he sloh is iua swa he wulle us alle do and ahnien him ane þa we aȝen alle clane herto he wule leden kinges eorles and hereþringes and her we habbeoþ an honden writen þat he sende þe þe quiddieþ what he wule don þenne he cumeþ hider on þa þæ ærnde wes iseid þæ kaisere wes ful særi mon and astured weoren romweren alle mid sterclichere wræþþe ofte heo eoden to ræde ofte heo heolden rune ær heom mihte iwurþen waht heo don wolde noþeles a þan ende enne ræd heo ifunden þat was þurh þa senaturs þa þet sinaþ heolden þan kaisere heo radden þat he write runen and sende his sonde ȝeond feole kinelonde and hehte heom cume sone alle to rome of euerælche londe þe heom oht lufeden and alle þa wulleþ mid fehte biȝiten lond oþer ahte folc þer com sone to þere burh of rome swa muchel swa þer neuere ærer na mon no isumnede heo seiden þat heo wolden ouer munt giu iwenden and wiþ fehten wharswa heo hine ifunden and slæn oþer anhon and his hired al fordon and ahnien þan kaisere riche þe æreste king þe þer com he wes swiþe kene mon king of grece ethion duc of boece per com mid mucle wiȝe irtac king of turckie king of egipte of crete þe king ipolitte of syrie þe king of frigie þe duc teucer of babilone of spaine þe kaisere meodras of medie þe king boccus of libie þe king of bittunie pollidices of iturie þe king sexes ofustesar king of aufrike nes þer na king his ilike mid him com moni aufrican of ethiope he brohte þa bleomen þa seolue romleoden liþen heom tosomne þat weoren at nexte of rome þa hexte marces lucas and catel gaius and metel þis weoren þa sixe þe þat senaht al biwusten þa þis folc isomned wes of feole cunne londes þa sette þe kaisere arimen al þæne here þa weoren þer riht italde to fihte swiþe balde feouwer hundred þusende cnihtes a þan hæpe mid wepnen and mid horsen swa bihoueþ to cnihten nes he neuere iboren i nauere nane burȝe þat mihte þat folc tellen þat þer eoden auoten auormest heruestes dæie uorþ heo gunnen sturien auer riht þene wæi þet touward munt giu lai lete we nu ane while þeos ferde bilæue and speke we of aþelest kinge þa þe he bisoht hafde his þeines sele and ælc wes ham iuare þer he lond hafde and raþe aȝæin comen cnihtes to hireden mid wepnen wel idihten þurh allen heore mihte of scotlond of irlond of gutlond of islond of noreine of denene of orcaneie of maneie of þan ilke londen beoþ an hundred þusende iwepnede þeines ohte on heore londes wise neoren hit noht cnihtes no þes wæies idihte ah hit weoren men þa kenlukeste þa æi mon ikende mid mucle wiaxen mid longe saxen of normandie of angou of brutaine of peitou of flandres of bulunne of loherne of luueine comen an hundred þusende to þas kinges hirede cnihtes mid þan bezsten þurhcostned mid wepnen þer comen þa twalf iueren þa france sculden heren twelf þusend cnihtes heo brohten forþrihtes and of þissen londe nom an honde fifti þusend cnihtes kene and ohte men to fihte of brutaine cnihtes mid þan bezste ten þusend ladde of his leodfolke of ganninde monnen þa heo forþ wenden þurh nane cunnes spelle ne cuþe heom na mon telle þa hehte aþelest kinge to ane isette time þat folc isomnien bi heore bare lifen at barbefleote and þer he wolde gædere sele his þede þis lond he bitahte ane selcuþe cnihte he wes broþer næs þer nan oþer wes ihaten forcuþest monnen treouþe nefde he nane to nauer nane monne he wes mæi of aþelen his cunne ah cniht he wes wunder god and he hafde swiþe muchel mod suster sune to þere quene wes his iwune þat wæs ufele idon his æme he dude swikedom ah al hit wes stille in hirede and in halle for na man hit ne wende þat hit sculde iwurþe ah men to soþe iwenden for walwain wes his broþer þe alre treoweste gume þe tuhte to þan hirede þurh walwain wes modræd monnen þa leouere and þe kene ful wel him iquemde he nom al his kinelond and sette hit an hond and his quene wurþlukest wiuen þa þe in þissere leode wunede an londe bitahte al þat he ahte and þere quene þat heom was iqueme þat was ufele idon þat heo iboren weoren þis lond heo forradden mid ræuþen uniuoȝen and a þan ænden heomseoluen þe wurse gon iscenden þat heo þer forleoseden lif and heore saulen and æuer seoþþe laþen in auerælche londe þat nauer na man nalde sel bede beoden for heore saule for þan swikedome þat he dude his æme al þat ahte he bitahte lond and his leoden and leofen his quene and seþþen he nom his ferde of folken swiþe hende and ferde ful sone touward suþhamtune þer comen seilien sone ȝeond þa sæ wide scipes uniuoȝe to þas kinges folke þe king þat folc beide ȝeond þa scipen longe bi þusend and bi þusend to þan scipen þrasten þe uader weop a þene sune suster a þene broþer moder a þa dohter þa þa duȝeþe sturede weder stod on wille wind wex an honde ankeres heo up droȝen drem wes on uolken wunden into widen sæ þeines wunder bliþe scipen þer forþ þrungen gleomen þer sungen seiles þer tuhten rapes þer rehtten wederen alre selest and þa sæ sweuede for þere softnesse gon to slæpen alse þe king slepte a sweuen him imette feorlic wes þat sweouen þene king hit auerde þa þe king him awoc swiþe he wes idræcched and granen agon ludere stefenen næs þer nan swa þriste cniht under þat durste þene king fræine of his farecoste ær þe king himseolf speke and spilede wiþ his beornen þere and þus him seide þa he awoc of slæpe lauerd drihten domes waldende midelarde mund monnen froure þurh þine aþmode wil walden ænglen let þu mi sweuen to selþen iturnen þa spac angel þe king scottene deorling lauerd sæi us þi sweuen seleȝehþe us beo ȝeueþe bluþeliche quaþ þe king to blisse hit iwurþe þer ich lai a sweuete agan ich forto slepe me þuhte þat in þere weolcne com an wunderlic deor æst in þan leofte ladlic an sehte wiþ leite mid storme sturnliche wende nis in nare leode nan swa ladlic beore þa com þer westene winden mid þan weolcnen a berninge drake burhȝes he suelde mid his feure he lihte al þis londriche me þuhte a mire sihȝeþe þat þa sæ gon to berne of leite and of fure þa þe drake ferede þes drake and beore beien tosomne radliche sone togadere heo come heo smiten heom togaderen mid feondliche ræsen floȝen of heore hæȝene swulc furburondes ofte wes þe drake buuen and eft seoþþen bineoþen neoþeles a þan ænde heȝen he gon wende and he flah dunrihte mid feondliche ræsen and þene beore he ismat þat he to þere eorþe iwhat and he þer þene beore ofsloh and hine limmele todroh þa þat feht wes ido þe drake aȝen wende þis sweuen me imette þer ich lai and slapte biscopes þis iherden and bocilærede men þis iheorden eorles þis iherden beornes ælc bi his witte wisdom sæiden þis sweuen aræhten ne durste þer na cniht to ufele ræcchen na wiht leoste he sculden leosen his leomen þat weoren him deore forþ heo gunnen liþen an eouste bilife wind heom stod on wille selest alre wedere heo hæfden al þat heom wes neod to londen heo comen at barbefleot to barbefleot at þer com muchel moncun in of alle þan londe þa hafde an honde swa sone swa heo mihten ut of scipe heom rehten þe king his folc hehte herberwe isechen an badien þe king wolde þat his folc come nes he þere buten ane niht þa com him to an hende cniht he talde tidinge þan kinge he seide þat þer wes icumen a scaþe liþe of westward spaine wel dreori feond and inne brutaine bisi wes to harme bi þere sæside þet lond he weste wide nu hit hatte munt seint michel þat lond ewelde iwidel lauerd king queþ þe cniht to soþe ich þe cuþe herriht he hafueþ inome þine maȝe mid hahliche strenþe heȝe wimmon iboren dohter icoren wes ihaten aþelest maidenen to þan munte he heo uerede aþelest maidene nu fulle feowertene niht þe feond heo hafueþ ihalden þerriht nute we on liue þeh he heo nabbe to wife alle he makeþ him to mete þa men þa he igripeþ ruþeren hors and þa scep gæt and þa swin eke al þis lond he wule forfare buten þu afeollen ure kare lond and þas leode a þe is ure neode ȝet þe cniht seide to þan uolckinge isihst þu lauerd þe munt and þene wude muchele þer wuneþ þe scaþe inne þa scendeþ þas leode we habbeþ wiþ him iuohten wel feole siþen bi sæ and bi londe þes leoden he amærde ure scipen he aseingde þat folc he al adrente þeo þat feuhten a þan londe þeo he adun leide we habbeoþ idriuen þat swa longe þat we hine læteþ ane faren heu swa he wule after iwille him þis londcnihtes ne durren wiþ him mare na fehten þis iherde aþelest alre kinge he cleopede him to þene eorl kæi þe wes his stiward and his mæi beduer eke to him he cleopede he wes þes kinges birle he hæhte heom forþriht beon al war to midderniht mid alle heore wepne to wenden wiþ þan kinge þat na mon under of heore uare nuste buten þe king and þa tweien cnihtes mid him and heore sweines sixe ohte men and wihte and þe cniht þe radde hit þan king heom ladde to þere midnihte þa men weoren aslepe forþ him wende aþelest alre kinge biforen rad heore londcniht þat hit was dæiliht heo lihten of heore steden and rihten heore iweden þa iseȝen heo nawiht feorren a muchel fur smokien uppen ane hulle mid sæulode biuallen and anoþer hul þer wes swiþe heh þæ sæ hine bifledde ful neh þeruuenon heo iseȝen a fur þat wes muchel and swiþe stor þæ cnihtes þa tweoneden to whaþere heo faren mihten þet þe eotend war neore of þeos kinges fore þa nom him to rede þe ræȝe þat heo sculden somed faren aneosten þan ane furen and ȝif hine þer funden aquellen hine to deþen forþ þe king wende þat he com aneuste noht he þer ne funde bute a muchel fur þer berninde eode abute and his cnihtes bi his siden na whit heo ne funden quikes uppen wolden buten þat fur muchele and ban vnimete bi atlinge heom þuhte þritti uoþere þa nuste nenne red godne and bigon him to spekene to beduer his eorle beduer far biliue adun of þissen hulle and wend þe ouer þat water deope mid allen þine iwede and mid wisdome wend to þan fure and bihalues þe iga and bihald ȝeorne ȝif þu miht afinden oht of þan feonden and ȝif þu hine miht ofȝiten on aiȝes cunnes wisen wend adun stille þat cume to þan watere and seien me þer sone what þu iseȝen habbe and ȝif hit ilimpeþ swa þat þu liþen to þan fure and þe feond þe ofȝite and þu to fuse hafe mine godne horn þe al mid golde is ibon and blawe hine mid maine swa mon scal for neode and fus þe to þan feonde and bigin to fihten and we þe scullen fusen to
