swa we hit swiþest maȝen don and ȝif þu hine ifindest aneouste þan fure and þu al unaȝeten aȝein miht iwende þenne forbeode ich þe bi þine bare life þat þu nauere wiþ þene scucke feht no biginne beduer iherde what his lauerd him seide his wepnen he on him dude and forþ him iwende and up astæh þene munt þe is unimete he bar an his honde ænne gære swiþe stronge ænne sceld an his rugge irust al mid golde hælm an his hafde hehne of stele his bodi wes bifeong mid fæire are burne he hafde bi his side enne brond al of stele and forþ he gon steppen stiþ imainede eorl þat he com fusen an neouste þan furen and he under ane treo gon him atstonden þa iherde he wepen wunder ane swiþen wepen and weinen and wanliche iberen þa þe cniht wende þat hit þe eotend weoren and he anbursten agon swulc weore a wilde bar and forȝæt sone þat his lauerd him sæide his sceld he bræid on breoste his spere he igrap faste and an neoste gon fuse touward þan fure he wende to finden þene feond sturne þat he fehten mihte and fondien hine seolue þa fond he þer ane quene quecchen mid hafde heorlockede wif weop for hire weisiþ wanede hire siþes þat heo wæs on liues þat set bi þan fure mid reolichen ibere and sæt and biheold æuere ænne burinæsse and hire ȝeddes sæide ȝeomere stefne wale wale deore maide wale þat ich þe uedde þat ich þe uostredde wale þat þæ waldscaþe here þe haueþ þus foruare wale þat ich wes iboren mine leomen he haueþ tobroken þa bisæh þat wif abuten whar þe eotend come buȝen biseh a þene eorl beduer þa icumen wes þer þa sæide þat wif here þer heo sæt bi fure whæt ært þu fære whit eært þu angel eært cniht beoþ þine feþerheomen ihaneked mid golden ȝif þu ært of heuene þu miht isund faren heonene and ȝif þu ært eorþlic cniht ærm þu iwurþest forþriht for nu anan cumeþ þe scaþe þe alle þine leomen wule todraȝen þeh þu weore stel al he þe awalt iwildel he uerde to brutaine to aþelest alre bolde to castle hæh mon inne brutene þa ȝaten alle he tobrac and binnen he gon wende he nom þare halle wah and helden hine to grunde þæs bures dure he warp adun þat heo tobarst a uiuen he funde i þan buren fæirest alre bruden wes ihaten aþelest kunnen dohter hæh mon of brutene maȝe of swiþe heȝe cunne ich wes hire uostermoder and feire heo uostredde þer þe eotend unc ifeng forþ mid himseoluen fiftene mile into þisse wilde wude hider to þissen ilke stude þus he us diste todæi a seouen nihte sone swa he hider com swa he þat maide inom he wolde monradene habben wiþ þan maidene ælde næfde heo na mare buten fihtene ȝere ne mihte þat maiden his mone iþolien anan swa he lai hire mide hire lif heo losede sone and her he heo biburede burden alre hendest min aȝen uoster dohter þa he hafde þis idon swa me seoluen inom a uolden he me laiden and lai mid me seoluen nu hafeþ he mine ban alle ladliche abrokene mine leomen al toleþed mi lif me is alaþed nu ich habbe þe itald hu we beoþ her ihæd flih nu swiþe lest he þe ifinde for ȝif he cumeþ abolȝen mid his baluræsen nes he neuere iboren þe maȝen stonden þe biuoren efne þissen worden þa þat wif seide beduer heo gon hirten mid hendeliche worden leofe moder ich æm mon and cniht æm wel idon and ich þe wule suggen þurh soþe mine worden næs nan kempen iboren of nauer nare burden þat mon ne mæi mid strenþe stupen hine to grunde and hire þe ane alde wifmon swiþe lutle beoþ þine mæhten ah hafuen nu swiþe godne dæi and ich wulle faren minne wæi adun him ferde beduer to his duȝeþekinge and talde him hu he hafde kare and hu he hafde al ifare and what þat wif alde of þan maidene him talde and hu þe eotend ælche dæi bi þan alde wiue lai þer heo heom bitwenen heolden heore runen hu heo mihten taken on þat þe scucke weore fordon þeo while com þe eotende faren and fusden to his fure he bar uppen his rugge burþene grete þat weore twælf swine iteied tosomne mid wiþen swiþe grete ywriþen al togadere adun he warp þa dede swin and himseolf sæt þerbi his fur he beten agon and muchele treowen læiden on þa six swin he todroh and euere he to þan wiue loh and sone umbe while he lai bi þan wife ah he nuste noht þan tidende þat comen to his wifeþinge he droh ut his gleden his flæsce he gon breden and þa six swin he gon æten alle ær he arise of selde al biwaled on axen wanliche weoren þa sonden and seoþþen he gon ræmien and raxlede swiþe and adun lai bi þan fure and his leomen strahte lete we nu þene eotend bilafuen and atlien to þan kinge at þan watere his wapnen nom an honde and þe eorl beduer god cniht wis and war and þe þridde wes kæi þes kinges stiward and his mæi ouer þan watere heo comen iwepned mid þan bezsten and stiȝen up þan hulle mid allen heore maine þat heo comen fusen aneuste þan furen þer þe eotende lai and slæp and þa quene sæt and weop hine teh bisiden his iferen forbad heom bi heore leomen and bi heore bare liuen þat nan neoren swa kene þat heom neh comen buten he iseȝen þat hit ned weoren beduer atstod him þere and kæi his iuere gon stepe vorþ stiþimoded kempe þat he com to þan ulette þer þe feond lai and slæpte æuere wes ærhþe bideled þet wes sutel þeron sellic þah hit þunche for mihte þere þene eotende al tohæuwe slan þene scucke þer he lai and slapte þa nolde on slepen na wiht hine areppen leste he an uferre daȝe upbræid iherde þa cleopede anan aþelest kingen aris aris feondscaþe to þine fæiesiþe nu wit scullen delen þene dæd of mire maȝen ær þe king hæfde þæs ful isæide þe eotend up asturte and igrap his mucle clubbe and wende mid þan dunten al todriuen ah bræid heȝe his sceld buuen his hælme and þe eotend smat þeranouenan þat al he gon toscenen and him swende to an hiȝende mid his sweorde and þen chin him ofswipte mid alle þan cheuele and sturte him biaften ane treo þe þer stod aneouste and þe eotend smat after biliue and noht hine ne hutte ah he þat treo smat þat al his clubbe todraf and aneouste þat treo bieorn abute and swa and þe scucke biurnen hit þreie abuten þa wes þe eotend heui swiþe and wes swiftre and oftoc þene eotend and up ahof his gode brond and þat þih him ofsmat and eotend adun wæt and atstod and biheold þa gon to spekene þe ueond lauerd lauerd ȝef me griþ wha is þat me fihteþ wiþ ne wende ich þat na man a þissere weorlderichen me mihte þus lehtliche aleggen mid fehte bute hit weore aþelest alre brutte and neoþeles næs ich nauere of afæred sære þa him sæide aþelest kingen ich æm þe king bruttene deorling tel me of þine cunne and whar beo heore beonste and wha þe weore on uolde fader oþer moder ihalde and of wulche londe þu art iliþen hidere and whi þu mine maȝe aualled hafuest mid morþe þa andswarede þe feond þer he læi and biheold al þis ich wulle don and þine treoþe underfon wiþ þat þu me lete liuien and mine leomen hælen hine iwræþþede wunder ane swiþe and he beduer cleopede balde his kempe ga aneouste beduer and hefd him binim her and fere hit forþ mid þe adun of þisse munte beduer aneouste com and his hæfued him binom and swa heo þeonene ferden adun to heore iferen þa sat þe king adun and hine gon to resten and þas word seide þe sele no uæht ich nauere ueht non uppen þissere uolden buten þa ich sloh þene king riun uppen þan munte of rauinite seoþþen heo uorþ wenden and to þere uerde comen þa þe þat hafd iseȝe sellic heom þuhte whar weore under heuene swulc hafed ikenned of brutaine beh to þan kinge and þe king him seide al of þan maidene þa wes sari and sorhful an heorte forþi and nom al his feren and ferde to þan munte þer þat brutisce maide bibured læi on eorþe he lette þer areren sone ane chireche swiþe faire a seinte nomen drihtenes moder and seoþþen he ȝæf nome þan hulle ær he þonne wende and hehte hine æleine tunbel nu hit hæhte munt seint myhhel þa wes hired sellich isomned of irlonde and of scotlonde þider weoren iscriþene þa lette þe king blauwen bemen an hireden and wenden of brutaine bisie men and kene þurhut normandie þæ hehte þa neustrie heo uerden þurhut france and folc heom after ferde heo buȝen ut of france into burguine his hauwæres þer comen and heolden his iferen and cudde þan kinge þer i þare cuþþe þat þe kaisere and al his romanisce here þiderward heo comen fromward heore þeoden and swa heo wolden fusen in touwward france and al þat biwinnen and seoþþen wenden hidere and bruttes alle aquellen quicke þer heo heom funde and þene kene ibunde lede to rome þa wes abolȝen baldest alre kingen and hehte a þan feldes slen alle his teldes and þer he wikien wolde þat he þat soþe wuste whær he minte þene kæisere iwisliche kepen þat water hehte albe þer lai þe king balde an wis cniht þer com ride to þas kinges uerde þe wes al forwunded and his folc afelled swiþe hafden romanisce men al his lond biræiued him he talde þan kinge neouwe tiþende whar lai þe kaisere and al his romanisce here and whær he hine mihte iwinde ȝif he hine wolde wiþ him fihten oþer griþ makien wiþ romanisce monnen ah lauerd quaþ þe cniht ich þe wulle cuþen herriht þat betere þe is freondscipe to habben þene for to fihten for aȝan þine tweie heo habbeoþ twælue swa feole kinges swa feole heredringes nis he in nare kuþþe þe hit þe maȝe icuþþe for alle þan uolke þe uulieþ þan kinge wiþuten þan romleoden of his aȝere þeoden and wiþute þan uolke þe ȝirneþ þas kinges are þa þe talen weoren alle italde and heo hafden understonde þa cleopede þe king forþrihtes his deoreste cnihtes and radden heom bitwenen enne castel to areren onuast þan wateren þe albe wes ihaten on ane swiþe feiere stude itimbred he wes ful sone þer feng moni hond to an hiȝende he wes ido for ȝif misferde þenne he come to fihte oþer his uolc ueolle oþer setten to fleonne þenne þohte he to atstonden at þan castle stronge þa cleopede he eorles tweie aþele men and wise heȝe men icunned þan kinge swiþe deore þæ an wes of chartres and hehte gerin muchel wisdom wunede mid him þe oþer hehte beof of oxeneuord welle wide sprong þas eorles word þe ȝet þe king cleopede walwæin þe wes his deoreste mæi for walwain cuþe romanisc walwain cuþe bruttisc he wes iued inne rome wel feole wintre þe king nom þas þreo cnihtes hende and to þan kaisere heom sende and hehte hine mid his ferde faren aȝæin to rome and þat he næuere into france his ferde no ladde and ȝif þu þider wendest and þine ferde ledest þu scalt beon underuonge to þine uæiesiþe for france is min aȝen and ich heo mid fehte biwon and ȝif þu nult bilauen þat þider nult liþen fare wit to uihte and falle þe uorcuþere and lete we þat folc wræcche wunien an ære while romleoden iwunnen þa þeoden and seoþþen heo þa þeoden mid fehte forloseden and ich heo mid feohte biwon and mid fehte wule halden forþ þa cnihtes wenden godliche kempen þat weoren gerin and beof þe hende and walwain þe balde iburned and ihelmed an hæȝen heore steden and ælc weiede an sculdre sceld swiþe godne heo beren on heore honde gares swiþe stronge forþ heo gunnen ride riche men from hirede muchel of þere duȝeþe þe mid wunede mid eoden and æþmodliche hine beden þat he wiþ romleode summe sake arerde þat we maȝen mid fehte fondien us seolue for hit is feole ȝere þat heore þrættes comen here and heore beot makieþ þat heo us wulle bihafdi nu is hit muchel leodscome ȝif hit scal þus aligge bute þer sum sake beo ær we iwurþe sæhte scaftes tobrokene brunies totorne sceldes toscened scalkes toheouwen sweordes ibaþede i blode þan rede forþ þa eorles wenden þurh æne wude muchelen and mærcoden enne wæi þe ouer anne munte læi þat heo bicomen sone to þan uolke of rome wurþliche iwepned wunden an horsen þer me mihte bihalden þe mon þe bihalues weore moni þusenden þrasten ut of telden al to bihalden þeos þreo cnihtes balde and biheolden heore steden and biheolden heore iweden and hercnede tidende from þan kinge and aneouste forþrihtes fræinede þa cnihtes and ȝif þe king heom isend hæfde to þan kaisere to speken þan kæisere wiþ and to ȝirnen his griþ ah for nauer nare speche þas þreo eorles riche nolden abiden ær heo comen riden forn to þas teldes deoren þerinne wes þe kaisere adun heo gunnen lihten and bitahten hore steden and swa heo iwepned mid alle wenden into telde forn to þan kaisere þe wes ihate þer he sæt an his bedde heore ærnde heo him cudde ælc his saȝe sæide swa him sel þuhte and hehten hine wenden aȝæin to his londen þat he nauere mid unfriþe france no isohte þa while þa þeos eorles þreo seiden heore erende aset þe kaisere swulc he akimed weore and andsware nauer nan no aȝæf þissen eorlen ah he lustnede ȝeorne luþer on his þohte þa anbælh walwain swulc an iburst þein and þas word sæide walwain þe kene þe riche þu ært kæisere of rome we beoþ men aþelest brutten he sent þe his sonde wiþuten gretinge he hat þe faren to rome þa riche is þin aȝen let hine halden france þe he biwon mid fehte and hald þu richen and þine romleoden while þine aldren france ieoden mid fehte heo þer biwunnen unimete wunnen swa ane while heo þer liueden and seoþen heo hit leoseden mid fehte hit biwon and he hit wule walden he is ure lauerd we beoþ his leodkempen he us hæhte suggen soþ to þe seoluen ȝif þu nult aȝen buȝen þi bone he wule iwurþen and ȝif þu nult aȝen wenden ah iwurþien þin iwillen and þu wult þat kinelond bitellen to þire hond nu tomorȝen is þe dæi haue ȝif þu biȝete mæi þæ andswarede þe kaisere mid grættere wræþþe nulle ich noht aȝæin faren ah france ich wulle bitellen mine ældren hit heolden and ich hit wulle habben ah ȝif he wolde bicumen mi mon and for lauerd me icnawen and treouliche me heren and me for hærre halden griþien ich him wulle and his gumen alle and lete halde brutlond þæ hafde in his hond and oþere londes monie þe hafde an honde þat he naueþ nane rihte to þæ riche þæh he walde þa he scal alle leose buten he leoþ makie þa andswarede walwain þæ wes mæi and brenne beiȝene þa ibroþere brutlond heo ahten and france heo biwunnen and seoþþen heo uerden sone and biȝeten rome and þer heo wuneden seoþþe wel feole ȝere þa þis wes al iuare þa wes kæisere and walde romleoden and alle þa þeoden and rome is ure icunde þa þu haldest an honde and ȝif we mote libben we hit wulleþ habben beute ȝif þu wulle icnawen beo þat is king ouer þe and ælche ȝere him senden gæuel of þine londen and ȝif gæst him a leoþ þu miht libben þa eþ þa sæt bi þan kaisere a cniht of his cunne quencelin ihaten hæh mon inne rome þes cniht andswarede biuoren þan kaisere and þus him seide þe cniht was unisele cnihtes fareþ eou aȝæin and cuþeþ eower kinge bruttes beoþ bolde ac heo beoþ unwræste italde for æuere heo ȝelp makieþ heore monscipe is luttel mare he þohte to suggen þa walwain bræid to sweorden and smat hine ufenen þat hafde þat he atweo hælde and he hiȝenliche anan heolde to his horsen and heo up leopen mid grimliche lechen and þas word seide walwain þe sele swa me helpe þe ilke lauerd þe scop þes daȝes lihte ȝif æueræie is swa kene of eouwer moncunne þat us after kenne ich hine wulle aquelle he scal beo toswungen mid brade mine sweorden efne þare ilke tale þa cleopede þe kaisere haldeþ heom haldeþ alle heo sculleþ heongien heȝe uppen treouwe oþer mid horsen beon todraȝene efne þissere sæȝe þa þe kaisere seide þe eorles gunnen riden and spureden heore steden heo scæken on heore honden speren swiþe stronge beren biforen breosten brade heore sceldes aneouste gunnen ride eorles ræȝe and æuere þæ kaisere lude gon cleopie nimeþ heom slæh heom iscend heo us habbeoþ þer me mihte ihere þe þer bihalues weore clupien þusende of þan þeodfolke hider hider wepnen wende we heom æfter hider ure sceldes þe scalkes atwendeþ sone heom after wenden iwepnede kempen þer sixe þer seouene þer æhte þer niȝene and æuere þa eorles arnde biliues and æuere umbe stunde biseȝen heom bihinde and euere þa cnihtes of rome after biliue come and þer com aneouste alre swiþest ærne and euere cleopede kenlich swiþe wendeþ aȝæin cnihtes and werieþ eo mid fihtes hit is eo muchel scome þat ȝe wulleþ atsceken walwain icneo þene reme of þan romanisce men he wende his stede and to him gon ride and smat hine þurh mid þan spere swa he ispited weore and bræid to him þat spere þe gume iwat sone and þæs word kende walwain þe kene cniht þu ride to swiþe betere þe weore at rome hehte þe cniht heȝere monnen þa walwain isæh þat he to grunde bæh sone his sweord he ut abræid smat of þat hefd and þas word sæide walwain þe sele far to helle and tel heom þer spelles and wune þer toȝere mid quencelien þin ifere and haldeþ þer unker rune betere inc weoren inne rome for þus we eou scullen techen ure bruttisce speche gerin isæh hu hit ferde hu þe romanisce lai þer dune and his hors muneȝede and ænne oþerne imette and smat hine þurhut mid his spere and þas word spilede rid nu swa romain and reos þe to hellen and þus we scullen grundien ȝif godd us wule fulsten nis noht wurþ þratte buten þer beo dede æc bos isæh þe ohte mon hu his iueren hafden idon and his hors wende wunder ane swiþe and mid alle his mitte teh to ane cnihte and smat hine buuen þan scelde þat tobarst his gode burne and þurhut þene sweore þe swælt ful sone and þus þe eorl cleopien agon kenliche on his feren bruttes us wulleþ scenden ȝif we heonne wendeþ bute we bet aginnen ær we heonene iwenden efne þere speche þe þe eorl kende heo biwenden heom sone wunder ane swiþe and ælc his sweord swiþe adroh and ælc his rumain ofsloh and seoþþen heore hors wenden and heore wæi heolden and þæ romanisce men riden eouere after heom ofte heo heom on smiten ofte heo heom atwiten ofte heo sæiden heom to abuggen ȝe scullen þa dede ah ne mihten heo þurh nane þinge heore nenne adun bringe no nenne hærm þer don heom i þan wiþerhappen ah æuere umbe whilen þe eorles aȝain wenden and ær heo totwemden þe wurse wes romleoden þus heo iuerden fiftene milen þat heo comen to ane stude vnder ane ueire wude onuast þan castle þer lei uaste þreo milen þerfrom to þan wuden þrungen niȝe þusende þe þider senden baldere brutten þe bezst þat lond cneowen heo wolden wite þat soþe of walwain þan kene and of his iueren hu heo iuaren weoren whaþer heo liue weoren þa heo bi wæie læien þæs cnihtes siȝen þurh þene wude wunder ane softe uppen ane hullen and ȝeorne biheolden heo letten alle þa horsmen i þan wude alihten and rihten heore iwepnen and alle heore iweden buten an hundred monnen þe þer sculden bihalden ȝif heo onȝiten mihten þurh æies cunnes þingen þa iseȝen heo feorren in ane uelde muchelen þreo cnihtes ærnen mid allen heore mainen after þan þreom cnihten þritti þer comen after þan þrittie heo iseȝen þreo þusende þerafter comen þrasten þritti þusen anan romanisce leoden mid ræue bihonged and þa eorles biuoren heom aneuste atarnden euere þene rihte wæi þe touward þan wude lai þer heore iueren wel ihudde weoren þa eorles ærden to þan wuden þa romanisce after riden þa bruttes toræsden on heore iræste steden and smiten to auorenon and feollen an hundred anan þa wenden romleoden þat come riden and weoren afered feondliche swiþe and bruttes after heom and sloȝen of þan folke fiften hundred þa com heom to fulste of heore aȝe uolke þa þider hafde isend sixtene þusund baldere brutten mid burnen bihonged þa com þer ride þat wes an eorl riche ihate heh of rome mid six þusend kempen þan romanisce to helpen and mid muchelere strengþe leopen to þan brutten and lut þerof nomen ah monie heo ofsloȝen bruttes to wude hælden þe oþere after wenden and þa bruttes auoten uaste aȝæin stoden and þa romanisce men fuhten ridende and bruttes heom to heolden and heore hors sloȝen and moni þer nomen and in þene wude droȝen þa iwarþ wraþ þat his wes þa wurse þer and he mid his uerde from þan wude wende and bruttes heom to buȝen and biæften heom sloȝen þa bruttes weoren ut of wude iȝein to þan felde þa atstoden romleoden mid ræȝe strenȝe þa bigon þat muchele fiht þer ueollen eorlles and moni god cniht þer ueollen a dæi fiften þusend aþelere monnen ær hit weore æfen þer he finden mihte þe his main wolde fondien hond aȝan honde strongne aȝein stronge sceld aȝein scelde scalkes þer ueollen vrnen þa streten mid blodestræmen leien ȝeond þan ueldes goldfaȝe sceldes al þene dæi longe heo heolden þat feht stronge an his halue his folc heold tosomne þa iwræþ sone þat bruttes hafden þat wurse þat isæh þe eorl heȝe of oxeneuorde beof wæs ihæten hæh bruttisc mon þat a nare wisen ne mihte hit iwurþen þat bruttes ne mosten reosen buten heo ræd haueden þa eorl þa cleopede cnihtes aþele of þan alre bezsten of alle þan brutten and of þan kennesten þe þer quike weoren and tuhte hine ut a þan felde aneouste þere ferde and þus him iseide an heorte him wes unneþe cnihtes hercnieþ nu to me drihten us helpe we beoþ hidere icumen and þis feht habbeoþ undernumen buten rede þe is ure hexte ȝif us oht ilimpeþ we him þa bet likieþ and ȝif us ilimpeþ uuelen he us wule hatien ah ȝif ȝe wulleþ minne ræd þenne ride we al glad we beoþ þreo hundred cnihtes ihelmede þeines ohte men and kene aþele iborene cuþeþ eouwer cnihtscipe we beoþ of are cuþþe rideþ þenne ich ride and fulieþ mine rede alle haldeþ him to to þan cnihte þa ich do ne nime ȝe nenne stede no nanes cnihtes iwede ah æuerælc god cniht slæn æuere adunriht æfne þan worde þe þe cniht sæide of oxeneuorde to his iueren bisiden þe gon he to riden æfne al swa swiþe swa hund þene heort driueþ and his iueren after mid allen heore mahten þurhut þene muchele uehte al þa cnihtweorede fluen an heore steden uolc heo þere aqualden wo wæs heom iboren þa i þan weie heom weoren biuoren for alle heo hit totreden mid horsen and mid steden and swa aneouste heo iwenden and iuengen beof him biarnde and mid ærmen biclupte and bræid hine of his stede and to eorþe hine istræhte he wuste him bihalues balde his cnihte bruttes adun sloȝen heo droȝen and þa romleoden ræhliche fuhten and a þan laste ne mihte mon wite wha oþerne smite þer wes muchel blodgute balu wes on compe þa isæh walwain þer he wes bihaluen mid seouen hundred cnihten þider he gon hælden in his wæiȝe þat he funde al he hit aqualde and ridende igrap on richen his steden and ladde uorþ læþ þeh hit weore him þat heo to þan wude comen þer heo wel wusten sikerliche to halden þene riche mon of rome and æft ut a þene ueld wenden and bigonnen to fehten þer me iseon mihte sorȝen inoȝe sceldes scenen scalkes fallen halmes tohælden hæhȝe men toswelten blodie ueldes falewede nebbes bruttes heom toræsden þa fluȝen romleoden bruttes heom sloȝen and monie heo quic nomen and þe dæiende þæ wa wes romleoden þa þa bond men uaste kempen romanisce and lædden heom to þan wude biuoren heom biwakeden a þere nihte twenti hundred cnihten þa hit dai wes amarȝen duȝeþe gon sturie forþ heo gunnen liþe to heore kinelauerde and swulc lac him brohte þat leof him wes to habben þa spac him þus wulcume nu ic þe wulle teche bruttisce spæche þu ȝulpe biforen þan kaisere þat þu me woldest aquellen nimen mine castles alle and mine kineriche and muchel þe sæl iwurþen of þat þu wilnedest to habben ich wulle bitachen þe ful iwis minne castel inne paris and þer þu scalt wunien swa þe beoþ alre leoþest ne scalt þu nauere mare þi lif þenne lede þa cnihtes nom þe þer iuongen weoren þreo hundred rideres he nom eke anan þe alle weoren iueren cnihtes swiþe ohte and kene men to uihte and hæhte heom amorȝen monliche arisen binden romanisce men mid stronge raketehȝen and lede to þere borh of paris feouwer eorles he hæhte forþ heom ibringen beduer and richer he hehte heom beon iueren þat heo siker weoren and cumen aȝain sone to heore kinelauerde þis wes al þus ispeken ah hit wes sone underȝeten hæwæres foren ȝeond þas kinges ferden and iherden suggen soþere worden wuder wolde senden þæ cnihtes þe he hafde i benden and þa hauweres forþrihte wenden uorþ bi nihte þat heo comen sone to þan kaisere of rome and talden al heore tale hu þas feouwer eorles sculden uare and forþ lede to þære burh of paris and al heo talden þene wæi þe intowardes parise læi and whar me heom kepen mihte in ane slade deopen and biraiuien of heom þene riche mon and þa feouwer eorles ileggen and fasten heom binden þis iherden þe kaiser of rome and he leopt to wepne swulc hit a liun weore and ten þusend hehte kempen iþoȝene to horse and to wepnen aneouste foren wenden he cleopede of libie he wes king of turkie dux he sende after þe of babiloine wes icumen þer he cleopede to þan senaturs bal catel þeos weoren alle kineborne and þeos weoren alle icoren aneouste to riden and aredden anan swa hit was euen forþ heo iwenden heom ladden twelue of þan leodfolke þa swiþe warre weoren and þa weiȝes cuþen þa riden romleoden riseden burnen quahten on hafden helmes heȝen seldes on rugge ræȝe romleoden heo ferden alle nihte neodliche swiþe þet heo comen in þe wai þa into parise lei þa weoren heo biuoren and bruttes biaften ah wale þat hit nuste þe kene þat þa romleoden heom forriden hafueden heo comen in ænne wude on ænne swiþe faire stude in ane dale deope diȝelen bihælues sweoren heom bitwænen þat þer heo wolden kepen þer heo leien stille ane lutle stunde and hit agon daiȝen and deor gunnen waȝeȝen þa comen men quecchen after streten riht þene ilke wæi þer þe oþer uerde læi heo riden singinge segges weoren bliþe neoþeles wes þer swiþe wis and swiþe war he and þe eorl riche buȝen heom togæderes and nomen heom bitweonen fif hundred cnihtes and biuoren wenden iwepnede kempen richer and beduer wenden heom bafte þer and þa cnihtes fereden þa heo iuongen hafden and his iueren þa iwunne weoren þa heo comen riden uppen romleoden and romleoden ræsden to mid ræȝere strengþen and smiten a þan brutten mid swiþe bitere duntes breken bruttene trume balu wes on folke þe wude brastlien gon beornes þer feollen bruttes heom wiþstoden and stærcliche heom weoreden þat iherde richer and þe eorl beduer hu heore iueren heom biuoren fuhten heo nomen and heore inume allen and mid þreo hundred sweinen into wude senden and heomseolue fusden toward heore ifæren and smiten a romleoden mid raȝere strengþen þer wes moni dunt iȝeuen and moni mon þer wes islaȝen þa underȝæt þe heþene king wes swiþe war þat heore uolc gon waxen and bruttes gunnen wonien and buȝen heom tosomne his cnihtes seleste and uuenon þan brutten swulc heo heom wolden abiten bruttes wokeden þa and heore wes þat wurse heo sloȝen heo nomen al þat heo neh comen wa wes brutten þere buten heore helþ wes to lutel þere at heȝere neode þer wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen king hine aqualde mid luþere his crafte and þreo bruttes eke heȝe men iborene þer islaȝen weoren þreo hundred of heore iueren and monie quike nomen and narwe heom ibunden þa nusten heo godne ræd nanne for alle heo wenden beon dede neoþeles heo fuhten swa ohtliche swa heo mahte þa wes ut ifaren from ferden þæ king of peytouwe har mon iblowen he hehte gascunne he ahte he hæfde to iueren fif hundred rideren þreo hundred scuhten kene men to uehten and seouen hundred auoten þa fuse weoren to harmen heo weoren ifaren into þan londe fodder to biwinnen æiþer uodder and mete to læden to heore ferde þa luden heo iherden of þan romleoden heore deden heo bilafden and þiderward gunnen liþen stiþimodede men and swifte slauþe bidæled þat heo comen sone anneouste þan fehte and his cnihtes þerriht forþrihtes igrippen heore sceldes swiþe balde cnihtes and alle þa scutten scuuen heom bisides and þa men auoten to gunnen fusen and alle somed smiten on mid smarten heore dunten at þan uorme smællen romaniscen veollen fiftene hundred folden to grunden þer wes islæȝen þe king wes ful sturne ær of rome forȝæt his domes þære þæ astalden þer flem þat ær staþel heolden þa rugges towenden and fluȝen romleoden bruttes heom after buȝen and mid baluwe heom igrætten and swa monie heo þer nomen and swa monie heo þer sloȝen þat no mihte bruttene uerde biueolen namare and þa romanisce men þe þer atfaren mihten atarnede ful sone to þan kaisere and talden him tidende of þan kinge for heo wenden to soþe þat þider comen þer wes auared swiþe þe kaisere and his ferde þe bruttes islaȝen hafden þat heom sel þuhten aȝeinward heo buȝen þa mid baldere biȝete and to þan stude wenden aȝæin þer þat feht hafde ibeon and bureden þa deden and þa quike gunnen forþ leden and senden after þæ heo ær nomen and after his iueren þæ ær inumen weoren and senden heom alle fuliwis into þære burȝe of paris and þreo castles fulden and faste heom biclusden after heste aþelest kingen alle brutleoden luueden alle heom stod him æie to þat wuneden a þan ærde swa dude þan kaisere of he hafde muchele kare and alle romleoden of weoren afærde þa wæs mid soþe ifunde þat sæide whilen þat sculden for rome ifullen afure and þa wal of stanen quakien and fallen þas ilke tacninge sculde beon of þan kæiseren and of þan senature þa mid him come of rome and of þan seoluen wisen þæ þer gunnen resen þat i furndaȝen seide al heo hit funden þere swa heo duden ære and seoþþen wel iwhare ær iboren weore al hit bodede þe kaisere iherde suggen soþere worden hu his men weoren inumen and hu his folc æc ofslaȝen þa weoren inne his ferde feolevalde sorȝe summe mænden heore freond summe þrætteden heore ueond summe bonneden wepnen balu heom wes ȝeueþe þa iseh þat luþere him ilimped wæs for ælche dæi he losede of his leodfolke ah he herm iuredde his heȝe men he losede he iwærþ afered þa wunder ane swiþe and nom him to ræde and to somrune þat he wolde to æust mid alle his iuerde forþ bi lengres he wolde uare of he hafde muchele kare hafde his hauwares an hirede þas kaiseres and sone duden him to witen whuder he wolde wenden lette sone somnien his ferde stilleliche bi nihte his cnihtes seleste and forþ þe king wende mid sele his folke an his riht honde he lette lengres stonde and i þæne wæi biforen ferde þe faren wolde þa he com in ane dale vnder ane dune þer he gon atstonden kennest alre kingen þat dale is mid soþe sosie ihaten þer adun lihte and hæhte al his duȝeþe græþien heom to fihte swa scolden cnihtes ohte þat whenne romleoden þer comen riden þat heo uengen heom on swa ohte cnihtes sculden don alle þa sweines and þa unwræste þeines and of þan smale uolke feole þusunde þe king heom sette in ane hulle mid feole heremarken þat he dude for ȝepscipe þerof he ȝelpen þohte al swa hit iwarþ seoþþe þerafter ful sone ten þusend nom of aþelen his cnihten sende a riht honde mid raue bihonge he lette oþere ten þusende an his lift honde ten þusend biuoren ten þusend biæften mid heomseoluen heo heolden sixtene þusund bihalues he sende into ane wude hende seouentene þusend selere cnihten wel iwepnede men þene wude to biwitteȝen þat heo mihte þider uare ȝif him neod weore þa wes inne gloucestre an eorl mid þan bezste moruiþ wes ihate mon swiþe kene him he bitahte þene wude and þa ferde and ȝif hit ilimpeþ swa wule þe liuiende godd þat heo ouercumen beon and biginnen to fleon setteþ heom after mid allen æouwer mahten and al þat ȝe oftake maȝen doh hit of lifdaȝen þa uatte and þa lene þa riche and þa hene for no beo in nauer nare leode no in none leode cnihtes al swa sele swa beoþ mid me seolue cnihtes al swa ræȝe cnihtes al swa riche cnihtes al swa stronge in nauer ane londe ȝe beoþ under cnihten alre kennest and ich æm rihchest alre kinge vnder gode seolue do we wel þas dede godd us wel spede cnihtes þa andswarede stilleliche under lufte alle we scullen wel don and alle we scullen touon niþing wurþe þe cniht þe ne cuþe his mahten herriht þa sænde heo a ba siden al þa men auoten þa lette he sette up þene drake heremærken unimake bitæhte hine ane kinge þe wel hine cuþe halde angel kinge of scotlonde þa uormeste uerde heold an honde þe eorl of cornwaille þa uerde heold baften bof hafde ane þe eorl of oxenuorde þe eorl of chæstre gerin þa ueorþe uerde heold mid him þa uerden uppen þere dune heold king þe denisce lot heold þa ane þe leof was þan kinge of brutaine heold ane oþere walwain þe kene wes bi þan kinge kai wuste ane stiward wæs þas kinges beduer ane oþer þe wes þes kinges birle þe eorl of flandres ane uerde hefde mid him ane muchele uerde hefde þe king of gascunnes ærd wigein eorl of leicestre and eorl of dorchestre heo wusten þa twa uerden þe þer weoren auoten þe eorl of chastre curselein and eorl of baþe þe hehte ho biwusten ba þa uerden þa weoren þær auoten þeos sculden a twa haluen halden to þan uehte to þissen twam eorlen þa ohte cnihtes weoren hafden treouþe þe eorles weoren treowe þa weoren alle þa uerden isette alse sel þuhte þa cleopede him to þe king of brutaine his redȝiuen alle þa ræiȝest weoren to dome and þus seide anan to aþelen his monnen hercneþ nu touwardes me mine wines deore iræsed ȝe habbeoþ tweien to romanis monnen and twien heo beoþ ouercumen and islaȝen and inumen for heo al mid wronge wilneden of ure londe and min heorte seiþ me þurh ure drihten hehne þat ȝet heo scullen beon ouercumen baþe islæȝen and inumen ȝe habbeoþ ouercumen noreine ȝe habbeoþ ouercume denene scotlond and irlond al iwunen to eouwer heond normandie and france biwunnen mid fehte þreo and þritti kinelond ich halde a mire aȝere hond þæ ȝe hit under sunnen habbeoþ me biwunnen and þis beoþ þa forcuþeste men of alle quike monnen hæþene leode godd heo seondeþ laþe ure drihten heo bilæueþ and to heo tuhteþ and þe kæisere of godd seolf naueþ nane care þat hafueþ to iueren haþene hundes goddes wiþeriwinnen we heom scullen awelden leggen heom to grunde and us seoluen beon isunde mid drihtenes willen þe waldeþ alle deden þa andswarede eorles þare alle we beoþ ȝarewe to libben and to liggen mid leouen vre kingen þa þas ferde wes al idiht þa wes hit dailiht at lengeres boȝede and al his romleode he hehte his men blawen his guldene bemen bonnien his ferden forþ he wolde riden from lengres to auste swa læi his weie rihte forþ gunnen riden romanisce leoden þat heo ane mile comen neh þa iherde romleoden ræȝe tiþenden iseȝen alle þa dales alle þa dunes alle þa hulles mid helmes biþahte heȝe haremarken hæleþes heom heolden sixti þusende þrauwen mid winde sceldes blikien burnen scinen palles goldfaȝe gumen swiþe sturne steden lepen sturede þa eorþe þe keiser isah þæne king fare þer he was bi wudescaȝe he þa sæide þæ lauerd of rome and spac wiþ his monnen ludere stefnen what beoþ þeos utlaȝen þa þisne wei us habbeoþ foruaren nime we ure wepnen and heom to wenden heo sculleþ beon islaȝene and summe quic iulaȝene alle heo sculle beon dede mid wite fordemde efne þan worden heo iuengen heore wepnen þa heo igæred weoren mid gode heore wepnen þa spac sone þæ lauerd of rome biliue we heom to alle we scullen wel do þer weoren icumen mid him fif and twenti kingen heþene uolc alle þa heolden of rome eorles and dukes eke of æstene weorlde lauerdinges quæd þa eou beo liþe ȝe beoþ kinges riche and hereþ into rome rome is mi rihte rihcchest alre burȝe and ich ah hæxst to beon of alle quike monnen ȝe iseoþ her on uolden þa ure ifan sunden heo þencheþ to rixlien heȝe ouer ure riche halden us for hænen heomseoluen riche iwurþen ah we heom scullen forbeoden mid baldere strengþen for ure cun hæxst was of alle quike monnen and alle þa lond biwinnen þa heo on lokeden and into brutlonde ferde þe stronge and biwon him to hondes feole kinelondes nu wolden ure underlingges beon ouer us kingges ah heo hit scullen abuggen mid heore bare ruggen no scullen heo nauere liþen aȝæin to brutaine æfne þan worde þa sturede þa uerde bi þusend and bi þusende heo þrunggen tosomne ælc king of his folke ȝarkede ferde þa hit al was iset and ferden isemed þa weoren þarriht italde fulle fiftene ferden twein kinges þere æuere weoren ifere feouwer eorles and a duc dihten heom togadere and þe kæisere himseolf mid ten þusend kempen þa gon þat folc sturien þa eorþen gon to dunien bemen þer bleowen bonneden ferden hornes þer aqueþen mid hæhȝere stefnen sixti þusende bleowen tosomne ma þer aqueþen of iueren þene sixti þusende segges mid horne þa wolcne gon to dunien þa eorþe gon to biuien tosomne heo heolden swulc heouene wolde uallen ærst heo lette fleon to feondliche swiþe flan al swa þicke swa þe snau adun ualleþ stanes heo letten seoþþen sturnliche winden seoþþen speren chrakeden sceldes brastleden helmes tohelden heȝe men uellen burnen tobreken blod ut ȝeoten ueldes falewe wurþen feollen heremærken wondrede ȝeond þat wald iwundede cnihtes oueral sixti hundred þar weoren totredene mid horsen beornes þer swelten blodes aturnen stræhten after stretes blodie stremes balu wes on uolke þe burst wes vnimete swa al swa suggeþ writen þæ witeȝen idihten þat wes þat þridde mæste uiht þe auere wes here idiht þeo at þan laste nuste nan kempe whæm he sculde slæn on and wham he sculde sparien for no icneou na man oþer þere for vnimete blode þa hæf þat fiht of þan studen þer heo ær fuhten and bigunnen arumþe ræsen tosomne and neouwe ueht bigunnen narewe iþrungen þer weoren romleoden reouliche iladde þa comen þer kinges þreo of hæþene londe of ethiope wes þe an þe oþer wes an aufrican þe þridde wes of libie of hæþene leode heo comen to þere uerde a þere æst ænde and þene sceldtrume breken þe bruttes þer heolden and anan fælden fiftene hundred baldere þeinen of þeoden þa wenden bruttes sone to þa rugges þa comen þer riden tweien eorles kene þat was beduer and kæi birle and his mæi heore bruttes heo isehȝen mid bronden tohawen þer iwurþen tobursten eorles swiþe balden mid ten þusend cnihten hælden to þan uihten amidden þan þrunge þer heo þihkest weoren and sloȝen romleoden reouliche swiþen and ȝeond þan uehte wenden after heore iwillen þa weoren heo to þriste and to ufele heom biwusten wala wa wala wa þat heo neoren war þa þat heo ne cuþen biwiten heom wiþ heore wiþeriwinnen for heo weoren to kene and to ærwene and to swiþe fuhten and to ueor wenden and spradden to wide ȝeond þat feht brade þa com þe king of mede þe muchele and þe brade heþene hereþrihng þer he hærm wrohte he ladde to iueren twenti þusend rideren he heold on his honde ænne gare swiþe stronge þene gare he uorþ strahte mid strongen his maine and smat þene eorl beduer forn a þan breoste þat þa burne tobarst sone biuoren and bihinde anopened wes his breoste þa blod com forþ luke þer feol beduer anan ded uppen uolden þer wes sarinesse sorreȝen inoȝe þer kai funde beduer ded liggen him þer and kai þat lich wolde leden mid himseolue mid twenti hundred cnihten he hælde þer abuten and feondliche feuhten and falden romleoden and of medie þer sloȝen moni hundred monnen þat ueht wes strong swiþe and heo weoren þer to longe þa com þer liþen a swiþe ladlic king an mid sixti þusend monnen sele of his londen setor þe kene þe com him from libie þer þe king stronge wiþ kæi him gon fehte and forwundede kai swiþe inne strongen þan fehte to þan bare deþe reoulich wes þa dede his cnihtes þerrihte hine ladden of þan uihte mid muchelere strengþe þurh þat feht stræhten wa wes kinge for þa tidinge þæt iseh þe riche þein wes ihaten suster sune of heȝe bruttes he wes icume þat boccus mid his spere stronge bedver hafde istunge wa wæs him on liue þa his æm wes an deþe for he of alle monnen mæst hine lufede he cleopede of his cunne cnihtes swiþe gode and of þan alre leofeste þe he on liue wuste fif hundred bi tale fusden tosomne þa sæide riche mon of bruttene cnihtes ȝe beoþ of mine cunne cumeþ hidere to me and wreke we beduer min æm þa bezst wes of ure cunne þa buccus hafd ofstungen mid his spere strongen fuse we alle tosomne and ure ifan feollen æfne þan worde forþ he iwende and alle mid him anan aþele his iueren and buccus þene king icneowen þer he was i compen mid his spere and mid his scelde monine king he aqualde braid ut his sweord sone and him to sweinde and smat þane king a þene helm þat he a twa toueol and æc þere burne hod þat hit at þe toþen atstod and þe heþene king hælde to grunde and his fule saule sæh into helle þa seide ræh he was on mode boccus nu þu hafst aboht beduer þu sloȝe and þi saule scal toȝere beon þas wurse iuere æfne þan worde swulc hit þe wind weore he þraste to þan fihte swa þode doþ on felde þenne he þat dust heȝe aȝiueþ from þere eorþe al swa ræsde to his feonden al heo hit sloȝen þat heo aneh comen þe while þe heo mihte walden heoren kinewurþe wepnen neouren in al þan fihte cnihtes nane betere þe while þat heom ilaste þat lif on heore breoste boccus þene king heo ofsloȝen and a þusend of his cnihten þa wes beduer awræken wel mid þan bezsten þer wes an oht eorl aþeles cunnes wes ihaten lauerd of buluine he isæh i þan fihte enne ueond fusen þat on admirail of babiloine he wes ældere muchel uolc he aualde uolde to grunde and þe eorl þat bihædde an heorte him was unneþe he bræid an his breoste ænne sceld bradne and he igrap an his hond a sper þat wes swiþe strong and his hors muneȝeden mid alle his imaine and þene admiral hitte mid smærten ane dunte vnder þere breoste þat þa burne gon to berste þat him þer bæfte þat sper þurhræhte fulle ane ueþme þe ueond feol to grunde þat isah sone þeos admirale sone gecron is ihate and his spere grap anan and smat þene eorl sære a þa lift side þurhut þa heorte þe eorl adun halde walwain þat bihedde þer he wes on uehte and he hine iwraþede wunder ane swiþe þat isæh hæh mon of brutten and he þider halde mid fiftene hundred monnen herde herekempen mid fusden and walwain heom uuenon swiþe stiþimoded mon he hefde to iferen fif and twenti hundred baldere brutten þa bigunnen heo to fehten þer weoren romleoden reouliche iledde heom kepte walwain heom imette þer wes wunderlic grure þa welcnen aqueþen þa eorþe gunnen to buuien stanes þer bursten urnen stremes of blode of ærmen þan folke þat wel wes unimete þa weoren bruttes werie þe eorle of strugul bilefde þene king and inom mid him rimarc and boclouius þis weoren þa keneste men þat æi king ahte þeos weoren on moncunne eorles main stronge heo nalden for heore mucle mode fulien þan gode ah bi heomseoluen heo sloȝen alle þe heo neh come þat isæh a riche mon of þan romleoden hu þe kene heore uolc þer aqualde and þe cniht gon him alihten of leofuen his steden and nom him on his honde a spere imaked of stele and biwalede hine a blode and bihalues him eode þat he com a þan ende þer fæht þe stronge burne he up ahof and he þene eorl þer ofsloh þa ȝeiden lude alle romleode and buȝen to þan brutten and heore trume breken and feollen heremarken uolc adun helden sceldes þer scenden scalkes þer feollen þer ueollen to grunde fiftene þusende baldere brutten balu þer wes riue swa ilaste longe þat uiht swiþe stronge walwain gon ȝeonge ȝeond þat wæl muchele and somnede his cnihtes alle þer he heom funde i fihte aneouste þer com ride þe riche heo somneden heore beire uolc anon and forþ heo gunnen fusen and riden to romleoden mid raȝere wraþþen and fastliche heom to buȝen and breken þere freinsce trumen and walwain forþrihte þer he ifunde þene kaiser leouien under scelde and walwain him to sweinde mid þe stelene sweorde and þe kaisere hine þat gome wes swiþe sturne sceld aȝein scelden sciuren þer wunden sweord aȝein sweorde sweinde wel ilome fur fleh of þe stelen þa ueond weoren abolȝen þer wes viht swiþe strong stureden al þa ferden þe kaisere wende walwain to scende þat he miht an uuere daȝe ȝelpen uor þere deden ah bruttes him þrungen to þræfliche swiþe and þa romanisce men arudden heore kæiseren and heo tosomne heolde swulc heouene wolde ualle alle þene dailiht heo heolden seoþþen þat fiht ane lutle stunde ær þe sunne eode to grunde þa cleopede aþelest alre kinge nu we heom to alle mine cnihtes ohte and godd seolf us fulste ure feond to afallene æfne þan worden þa bleou men þa bemen fiftene þusend anan þraste to blauwen hornes and bemen þa eorþe gon beouien for þan vnimete blase for þan mucle ibeote romleoden wenden rug to þan feohten feollen heremarken heȝe men swulten fluȝen þa þe mihten þa ueie þær feollen muchel monslæht wes þere ne mihte hit na man tellen hu feole hundred monnen toheouwen þer weoren i þan mucle þrunge i þan monslæhte wes þe kaisere ofslæȝen a seolcuþe wisen þat nuste hit nauer seoþen na mon to sugen of nauer nare cuþþe wha þene kaisere qualde bute þa þet feht was al idon and þat folc wes al iblissed þa funde men þene kaisere ofstungen mid ane spere word com to þer he wes on telde þat þe kaisere wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen lette slæn an teld amidden ænne bradne ueld and þider iberen lette þene kaisere and lette hine bitillen mid goldfaȝe pallen and biwiten hine þer lette þreo daȝes fulle þe while he wurchen lette an werc swiþeriche ane cheste longe and wreon heo al mid golde and lette leggen þerinne of rome þat wes a swiþe duhti mon þa while his daȝes ilasten þa ȝet dude mære aþelest alre brutte asechen lette alle þa riche kinges and eorles and þa riccheste beornes þa i þan fehte weoren islaȝen and idon of lifdæȝen he lette heom burien mid baldere pruten buten þreo kinges he beren lette þan kaisere and lette makien beren riche and swiþe maren and lette heom sone senden to rome and grette romweren alle mid græten ane huxe and seide þat he heom sende þat gauel of his londe and efte wold heom alswa senden heom gretinge ma ȝif heo ȝirnen wolden of golden and þerafter wulle sone riden into rome and tellen heom tiþinge of brutlondes kinge and rome walles rihten þe ȝare weoren tofallen and swa ich wulle awelden þe wode romleoden al þis ȝelp wes idel ido for eoþer weis hit eode al oþer hit itidde þe leoden he bilæfden al þurh modred is mæin forcuþest alle monnen a þan muchele fihte of his cnihtes losede fif and twenti þusend a uolden tohavwen of brutten swiþe balde biræued at liue kæi wes forwunded seore wunder a swiþe to kinun he wes ilad and sone þerafter he wes ded bibured he wes þere bihalue þan castle imong heremiten þat wæs þe riche mon kæi hehte þe eorl kinun þe castel ȝæf him þene tun and he þerto tumde and sette þer þene nome after himseoluen for keises dæþe kain he hit hehte nu and auere mare swa hit hehte þere seoþþen beþuer wes islæȝen and idon of lifdahȝen hine beren lette to bæios his castle and biburied he wes þere inne þere burȝe wiþuten þan suþ ȝæte in eorþe me hine sette iulut wes forþ into flandres and alle his bezste cnihtes þer flutten uorþrihtes into þan eorldomen þenne heo þer comen and alle þa dede in eorþe me heom leide inne teruane heo liggeoþ alle clane þene eorl me ladde into buluine and þeræfter seoþþe wunede in ane londe inne burguine þer him bezst þuhte þat lond he al biwuste and alle þe castles sette and seide þat he wolde himseolue þat lond holde and seoþþen he his beot makede a sumere þat he wolde faren into rome and ahnien al þa riche and beon himseolf kaisere þe wuneden ære and monie of romleoden wolden þat hit swa eoden for heo weoren adradde to heore bare deþe þat monie þer awæi fluȝen and heore castles bibuȝen and monie sende sonde to þan stronge and monie him speken wiþ and ȝirnden griþ and summe heo wolde aȝein halden and halden wiþ him rome and weren þa leode and neoþeles heo auered weoren for heore uæiesiþen þat nusten heo under nenne ræd godne þa wes hit itimed þere þat saide while þat romwalles sculden aȝein touallen þat was agan þære bi þan kaisere þa ueol þerinne fehte mid fifti þusund monne ruren þer to grunde riche romleoden þa wende to soþe to aȝen al rome and wunede inne burguine richest alre king þa com þer in are tiden an oht mon riden and brohte tidinge þan kinge from his suster sune he wes wilcume for he wende þat he brohte boden swiþe gode lai alle longe niht and spac wiþ þene ȝeonge cniht swa nauer nulde he him sugge soþ hu hit ferde þa hit wes dæi a marȝen and duȝeþe gon sturien þa up aras and strehte his ærmes he aras up and adun sat swulc he weore swiþe seoc þa axede hine an uæir cniht lauerd hu hauest þu iuaren toniht þa andswarede a mode him wes uneþe toniht a mine slepe þer ich læi on bure me imætte a sweuen þeruore ich ful sari æm me imette þat mon me hof uppen are halle þa halle ich gon bistriden swulc ich wolde riden alle þa lond þa ich ah alle ich þer ouer sah and walwain sat biuoren me mi sweord he bar an honde þa com faren þere mid unimete uolke he bar an his honde ane wiax stronge he bigon to hewene hardliche swiþe and þa postes forheou alle þa heolden up þa halle þer ich iseh eke wimmonnen leofuest me al þere muche halle rof mid hire honden heo todroh þa halle gon to hælden and ich hæld to grunden þat mi riht ærm tobrac þa seide modred haue þat adun ueol þa halle and walwain gon to ualle and feol a þere eorþe his ærmes brekeen beine and ich igrap mi sweord leofe mid mire leoft honde and smæt of modred is hafd þat hit wond a þene ueld and þa quene ich al tosnaþde mid deore mine sweorede and seoþþen ich heo adun sette in ane swarte putte and al mi uolc riche sette to fleme þat nuste ich under whar heo bicumen weoren buten miseolf ich gon atstonden uppen ane wolden and ich þer wondrien agon wide ȝeond þan moren þer ich isah gripes and grisliche fuȝeles þa com an guldene leo liþen ouer dune deoren swiþe hende þa ure drihten makede þa leo me orn foren to and iueng me bi þan midle and forþ hire gun ȝeongen and to þere sæ wende and ich isæh þæ vþen i þere sæ driuen and þe leo i þan ulode iwende wiþ me seolue þa wit i sæ comen þa vþen me hire binomen com þer an fisc liþe and fereden me to londe þa wes ich al wet and weri of sorȝen and seoc þa gon ich iwakien swiþe ich gon to quakien þa gon ich to biuien swulc ich al fur burne and swa ich habbe al niht of mine sweuene swiþe iþoht for ich what to iwisse agan is al mi blisse for a to mine liue sorȝen ich mot driȝe wale þat ich nabbe here mine quene þa andswarede þe cniht lauerd þu hauest unriht ne sculde me nauere sweuen mid sorȝen arecchen þu ært þe riccheste mon þa rixleoþ on londen and þe alre wiseste þe wuneþ under weolcne ȝif hit weore ilumpe swa nulle hit ure drihte þat modred þire suster sune hafde þine quene inume and al þi kineliche lond isæt an his aȝere hond þe þu him bitahtest þa þu to rome þohtest and he hafde al þus ido mid his swikedome þe ȝet þu mihtest þe awreken wurþliche mid wepnen and æft þi lond halden and walden þine leoden and þine feond fallen þe þe ufel unnen and slæn heom alle clane þet þer no bilauen nane þa andswarede aþelest alre kinge longe biþ æuere þat no wene ich nauere þat æuere mi mæi wolde me biswiken for alle mine richen no mi quene wakien on þonke nulleþ hit biginne for nane weorldmonne æfne þan worde forþriht þa andswarede þe cniht ich sugge þe soþ leofe king for ich æm þin vnderling þus hafeþ modred idon þine quene he hafeþ ifon and þi wunliche lond isæt an his aȝere hond he is king and heo is quene of þine kume nis na wene for no weneþ heo nauere to soþe þat þu cumen aȝain from rome ich æm þin aȝen mon and iseh þisne swikedom and ich æm icumen to þe seoluen soþ þe to suggen min hafued beo to wedde þat isæid ich þe habbe soþ buten lese of leofen þire quene and of þire suster sune hu he hafueþ brutlond þe binume þa sæt hit al stille in halle þa wes þer særinæsse mid sele þan kinge þa weoren bruttisce men swiþe vnbalde uor þæn þa umbe stunde stefne þer sturede wide me mihte iheren brutten iberen and gunne to tellen a feole cunne spellen hu heo wolden fordeme modred and þa quene and al þat moncun fordon þe mid modred heolden þa cleopede hendest alre brutte sitteþ adun stille cnihtes inne halle and ich eou telle wulle spelles vncuþe nu tomærȝe þenne hit dæi biþ and drihten hine sende forþ ich wulle buȝe in toward bruttaine and ich wulle slan and þa quen forberne and alle ich wulle fordon þa biluueden þen swikedom and her ich bileofuen wulle me leofuest monne minne leofue mæi hexst of mine cunne and half mine uerde ich bilæfuen a þissen ærde to halden al þis kinelond þa ich habbe a mire hond and þenne þas þing beoþ alle idone aȝan ich wulle to rome and mi wunliche lond bitæche mine mæie and iuorþe mi beot seoþþe bi mine bare life scullen alle mine feond wæisiþ makeȝe þa stod him up walwain þat wes mæi and þas word saide þe eorl wes abolȝe ældrihten godd domes waldend al middelærdes mund whi is hit iwurþen þat mi broþer modred þis morþ hafueþ itimbred ah todæi ich atsake hine here biuoren þissere duȝeþe and ich hine fordemen wulle mid drihtenes wille miseolf ich wulle hine anhon haxst alre warien þa quene ich wulle mid goddes laȝe al mid horsen todraȝe for ne beo ich nauere bliþe þa wile a beoþ aliue and þat ich habbe minne æm awræke mid þan bezste bruttes þa andswarede mid baldere stefne al ure wepnen sunden ȝarewe nu tomarȝen we scullen uaren a marȝen þat hit dæi wes and drihten hine senden uorþ him wende mid aþelen his folke half he hit bilæfde and half hit forþ ladde forþ he wende þurh þat lond þat he com to whitsond scipen he hæfde sone monie and wel idone ah feowertene niht fulle þere læi þa uerde þeos wederes abiden windes bidelde nu was sum forcuþ kempe in ferde anæn swa he demen iherde of deþe he nom his swein aneouste and sende to þissen londe and sende word heou hit was iwurþen and hu wes on uore mid muclere ferde and hu he wolde taken on and al hu he wolde don þa quene com to modred þat wæs hire leofuest monnes and talde him tidende of þan kinge hu he wolde taken an and al hu he wolde don modræd nom his sonde and sende to sexlond after þe king wes swiþe riche and bæd hine cume to brutaine þerof he bruke sculde modræd bad þene stronge and þene riche wide senden sonde a feouwer half sexlonde and beoden þa cnihtes alle þat heo biȝeten mihte þat heo comen sone to þissen kinedome and he wolde ȝeouen of his riche al biȝeonde þere for he him scolde helpe to fihten wiþ his æme kinge beh sone into brutlonde þa modred hafde his ferde isomned of monnen þa weoren þere italde sixti þusende herekempen harde of heþene uolke þa heo weoren icumen hidere for hærme modred to helpen forcuþest monnen þa þe uerde wes isome of ælche moncunne þa heo weoren þer on hepe an hunddred þusende heþene and cristene mid kinge lai at whitsond feouwertene niht him þuhte to long and al modred wuste wat þær wolde ælche dai him comen sonde from þas kinges hirede þa ilomp hit an one time muchel rein him gon rine and þæ wind him gon wende and stod of þan æst ende and to scipe fusde mid alle his uerde and hehte þat his scipmen brohten hine to romerel þer he þohte up wende into þissen londe þæ he to þere hauene com him wes auornon ase þe dæi gon lihte heo bigunnen to fihten alle þene longe dæi moni mon þer ded læi summe hi fuhten a londe summe bi þan stronde summe heo letten ut of scipen scerpe garen scriþen walwain biforen wende and þene wæi rumde and sloh þer aneuste þeines elleouene he sloh sune þe was þer mid his fader icume to reste eode þa sunne wæ wes þa monnen þer wes walwain aslæȝe and idon of lifdaȝe þurh an eorl sexisne særi wurþe his saule þa wes særi and sorhful an heorte forþi and þas word bodede ricchest alre brutte nu ich ileosed habbe mine sweines leofe ich wuste bi mine sweuene whæt sorȝen me weoren ȝeueþe islaȝen is angel þe king þe wes min aȝen deorling and mi suster sune wa is me þat ich was mon iboren up nu of scipen biliue mine beornes ohte æfne þan worde wenden to fihte sixti þusend anon selere kempen and breken trume and wel neh himseolue wes inome modred bigon to fleon and his folc after teon fluȝen ueondliche feldes beoueden eke ȝurren þa stanes mid þan blodstremes þer weore al þat fiht idon ah þat niht to raþe com ȝif þa niht neore islaȝen hi weoren alle þe niht heom todelde ȝeond slades and ȝeon dunen and modred swa vorþ com þat he wes at lundene iherden þa burhweren hu hit was il ifaren and warnden him inȝeong and alle his folke modred þeone wende toward winchastre and heo hine underuengen mid alle his monnen and after wende mid alle his mahte þat he com to winchestre mid muchelere uerde and þa burh al biræd and modred þerinne abeod þa modred isæh þat him wes swa neh ofte he hine biþohte wæt he don mahte þa a þere ilke niht he hehte his cnihtes alle mid alle heore iwepnen ut of burhȝe wenden and sæide þat he weolde mid fihte þer atstonden he bihehte þere burȝewere auermare freo laȝe wiþ þan þa heo him heolpen at heȝere neoden þa hit wes dæiliht ȝaru þa wes heore fiht þat bihedde þe king wes abolȝe he lette bemen blawen and beonnen men to fihten he hehte alle his þeines and aþele his cnihte fon somed to fihten and his ueond auallen and þe burh alle fordon and þat burhfolc ahon heo togadere stopen and sturnliche fuhten modred þa þohte what he don mihte and he dude þere alse he dude elleswhare swikedom mid þan mæste for auere he dude unwraste he biswac his iueren biuoren winchestren and lette him to cleopien his leofeste cnihtes anan and his leoueste freond alle of allen his folke and bistal from þan fihte þe feond hine aȝe and þat folc gode lette al þer forwurþe fuhten alle dæi wenden þat heore lauerd þer læi and weore heom aneouste at muchelere neode þa heold he þene wai þat touward hamtone lai and heolde touward hauene forcuþest hæleþe and nom alle þa scipen þa þer oht weore and þa steormen alle to þan scipen neodde and ferden into cornwalen forcuþest kingen a þan daȝen and winchestre þa burh bilai wel faste and al þat moncun ofsloh þer wes sorȝen inoh þa ȝeonge and þa alde alle he aqualde þa þat folc wes al ded þa burh al forswelde þa lette he mid alle tobreken þa walles alle þa wes hit itimed þere þat seide while ærm wurþest þu winchæstre þæ eorþe þe scal forswalȝe swa sæide þe witeȝe wes mære þa quene læi inne eouwerwic næs heo næuere swa sarlic þat wes þa quene særȝest wimmonne heo iherde suggen soþþere worden hu ofte modred flah and hu hine bibah wa wes hire þere while þat heo wes on life ut of eouerwike bi nihte heo iwende and touward karliun tuhte swa swiþe swa heo mahte þider heo brohten bi nihte of hire cnihten tweiȝe and me hire hafd biwefde mid ane hali rifte and heo wes þer munechene karefullest wife þa nusten men of þere quene war heo bicumen weore no feole ȝere seoþþe nuste hit mon to soþe whaþer heo weore on deþe þa heo hireseolf weore isunken in þe watere modred wes i cornwale and somnede cnihtes feole to irlonde he sende aneoste his sonde to sexlonde he sende aneouste his sonde to scotlonde he sende aneouste his sonde he hehten heom to cume alle anan þat wolde lond habben oþer seoluer oþer gold oþer ahte oþer lond on ælchere wisen he warnede hine seoluen swa deþ ælc witer mon þa neode cumeþ uuenan þat iherde wraþest kinge þat modred wæs i cornwale mid muchele monweorede and þer wolde abiden þat come riden sende sonde ȝeond al his kinelonde and to cumen alle hehte þat quic wes on londe þa to uihte oht weoren wepnen to beren and whaswa hit forsete þat þe king hete þe king hine wolde a folden quic al forbernen hit læc toward hirede folc vnimete ridinde and ganninde swa þe rim falleþ adune for to cornwale mid unimete ferde modred þat iherde and him toȝeines heolde mid vnimete folke þer weore monie uæie uppen þere tambre heo tuhten togadere þe stude hatte camelford euermare ilast þat ilke weorde and at camelforde wes isomned sixti þusend and ma þusend þerto modred wes heore ælder þa þiderward gon ride þe riche mid unimete folke uæie þah hit weore uppe þere tambre heo tuhte tosomne heuen heremarken halden togadere luken sweord longe leiden o þe helmen fur ut sprengen speren brastlien sceldes gonnen scanen scaftes tobreken þer faht al tosomne folc vnimete tambre wes on flode mid vnimete blode mon i þan fihte non þer ne mihte ikenne nenne kempe no wha dude wurse no wha bet swa þat wiþe wes imenged for ælc sloh adunriht weore he swein weore he cniht þer wes modred ofslaȝe and idon of lifdaȝe in þan fihte þer weoren ofslaȝe alle þa snelle heredmen heȝe and lowe and þa bruttes alle of borde and alle his fosterlinges of feole kineriches and forwunded mid walspere brade fiftene he hafde feondliche wunden mon mihte i þare laste twa glouen iþraste þa nas þer namare i þan fehte to laue of twa hundred þusend monnen þa þer leien tohauwen buten þe king ane and of his cnihtes tweien wes forwunded wunder ane swiþe þer to him com a cnaue þe wes of his cunne he wes sune þe eorles of corwaile hehte þe cnaue he wes þan kinge deore him lokede on þer he lai on folden and þas word seide mid sorhfulle heorte þu art wilcume þu weore sone ich þe bitache here mine kineriche and wite mine bruttes a to þines lifes and hald heom alle þa laȝen þa habbeoþ istonden a mine daȝen and alle þa laȝen gode þa bi vþeres daȝen stode and ich wulle uaren to aualun to uairest alre maidene to þere quene aluen swiþe sceone and heo scal mine wunden makien alle isunde al hal me makien mid haleweiȝe drenchen and seoþe ich cumen wulle to mine kineriche and wunien mid brutten mid muchelere wunne æfne þan worden þer com of se wenden þat wes an sceort bat liþen sceouen mid vþen and twa wimmen þerinne wunderliche idihte and heo nomen anan and aneouste hine uereden and softe hine adun leiden and forþ gunnen liþen þa wes hit iwurþen þat seide whilen þat weore unimete care of forþfare bruttes ileueþ ȝete þat he bon on liue and wunnien in aualun mid fairest alre aluen and lokieþ euere bruttes ȝete whan cumen liþe nis nauer þe mon iboren of nauer nane burde icoren þe cunne of þan soþe of sugen mare bute while wes an witeȝe ihate he bodede mid worde his quiþes weoren soþe þat an sculde ȝete cum anglen to fulste þus leouede on londe and bruttes hine lufede and swiþe deore heom he wes and wrþeliche heo hine heolden nu hæfuede modred sunen tweie an maine swiþe stronge hei iseȝen hu hit ferde here of þan kaisere and hu heore fader wes ofslaȝe and idon of lifdaȝen and hu bruttes todreued weoren mid feole cunne bursten þa ilke tweie broþeren speken heom bitweohnen and somneden þa cnihtes alle selest þa heom þuhte þa weoren wide tofloȝen ut of þan wiþeruehte and somneden uerde wide ȝeond þan arde and þuhten to slan and al his lond binimen him þat iherde sugge þe king wes abolȝen and sende his sonde wide ȝeond his londe and hirede hehte cume þan kingge to helpe siȝen toward hirede ȝeonglinges snelle þritti þusend anan somned comen þrasten and þe king forþrihtes makeden hom cnihtes þa oþere cnihtes þer comen þa at þan fehte ar weoren þa hafde he tosomne sixti þusende þat iherde bodien beien sunen and nomen heom to rade and to somrune þat þe an liþen wolde into lundene and þe oþer liþen wolde into winchastre and þer heo wolden abiden þat þe king comen riden and wolden wiþ him fehten mid allen heore mehten ah þæ hit com to neode oþer weis hit eode gon liþe touward lundenne þat iherden bodien þeo þa burh biwusten hælden tosomne to heore hustinge heo nomen heom to rade and to somrune þat heo wolden halden alle mid þan kinge and forsaken sune þæ þat morþ wrohte sune flah and into ane munestere teh and him after wende and þer hine icæhte þe king mid his sweorde þat hefd him ofswipte and þus þe king wordede wræþ on his þonke liȝe þer þu laþe mon leof þu beo þan sucke slæþ heom aneouste al þat ȝe findeþ þere mine wiþeriwinnen weorpeþ heom to grunden þis slaht wes sone idon for moni mon þer wenden to seoþen lette þe king wes on londe blawen his bemen and bonnien his ferden and wende riht þene wai þe touward winchæstre lai and forþ ladde mid him þa bruttes of lundene and to winchæstre comen and aneouste binnen wenden þat isæh meleou þe wes sone and from his iueren cherde and fleh to are chirche and forþriht anan wende forn to ane wefde braid ut his sweorde and þat hafde him ofswipte þat seint anfibales weofd iwraþ þerof a blode and seoþen he lette slen alle melaeoues men þeo wes king here of þessere kineriche þa bigunnen blissen in brutene to wunien her wæs griþ her wes friþ and freoȝ laȝen mid folke and ful wel heolden þa ilke laȝen þat stoden on daȝen ah þat ilke ilaste to lutele while for no ilast he buten feouwer ȝer his feond hine aqualde and his folc hine uerede into stanhenge and þer hine leide bi leofen his aldren seoþþen wes ihouen her to kinge þat wes þe forcuþeste mon þet sunne here scean on suster sune his æm he biswac to deþe for he hefde rihte to þissere kineriche mid attere his æmes sune aqualde he bigon unfriþ is men him fuhten wiþ and he gon sechien to his twam susteren alc burh i þan londe ferde al to sconde astured wes al þas þeode strongliche swiþe six ȝere ilaste þas særinesse on londe þa veol þe king of horse and fæisiþ makede wel wes al þis folke for his fæiesiþe þa þis wes al ido þus þa iwarþ king þeo comen sexisce men seilen to londe and muchelne harm wrohten biȝeonde þere sloȝen and nomen al þat heo neh comen and þe hende sende after genge and ferede heom ouenon and feolde sexisce men and monie þusend sente to þare segrunde and þus he heom aferde and flemde of londe þat næuer seoþþen bi his daȝen ne lusten heom hider uaren his daȝes ilaste seuen ȝere and seoþþen he deiȝede and seoþþen nom þas riche þe reȝe þat was þe faireste mon wiþuten adam and swa alse þe boc us suggeþ þa æuere iboren weore þes lette his hired dihte al wiþ ohte cnihten þuhten alle þes sweines swulche heo weoren þeines haueden alle his hiredcnafe ælches godes sweines laȝe ne durste nauere nan vnhende mon þas kinges hus isechen he biwun þa londes alle þa stoden him an honde þa wes al þas bruttene afeolled mid blisse þa bleden uorþ comen ȝeond al þis kinedomen þe king ne rohte of æhte ah al he hit ȝaf his cnihten no mihte no mon sugge of wundere namare þene wes mid þan kinge buten of ane þinge he luuede þane sunne þe laþ is ure drihtene þa wifmen heo forsoken to mare sunne heo token wapmon luuede wapmon wifmen heom laþe weoren swa þat monie þusende wenden of þissen lond wifmen swiþe feire ferden to oþere þeoden for mucchel scome heom þuhte þat wepmen heom ne rohte þurhut alle cunnes þinge þis ilke wes a god kinge buten of þere sunne þat ich iseid habbe þa com an of his cunne wes ihaten and nom þisne kinedom and mid seorȝen wunede þeron snel cniht wes ah he nes noht iseli þat wes for unleoden spilden al his þeoden þeos king wes aþel bruttisc mon hux and hoker me warp him on he forlætte and hine cleopede and ȝet on feole bocken his nome me swa writeþ folc hine gunnen hænen folc hine gunne hatien and hoker loþ sungen bi laþen þan kingen þa bigon weorre ouer al þissen arde and sexisce men sone seileden to londe and herberȝe token aneouweste biȝeonde þere and þe king wæilien agon wide ȝeon þas þeoden læþ he wes al folke þa him on lokede þa wes in aufrike a king swiþe riche he wes an aufrican anster ihaten he hafde sonen tweien snelle cnihtes beien hehte þe eldere and gerion hehte þe ȝeongere þe alde king deȝede his daȝes weoren aȝeongen he bitahte his sune selen his riche ah hit forhoȝede and habbe he heo nolde and þohte al oþer and ȝef heo his broþer and seiden þat he nolde aȝen nane riche bute he heo biwunne mid wepnen and mid monnen ah mid compe he wolde aȝen kineriche oþer nauermare nolde he habbe nane was kempe icostned on mæine and he wes þe strongeste mon þæ æi mon lokede on he bigon to sende ȝeond al þan londe into babilonie into macedonie in turkie into persie into nubie into arrabie and bad alle þe ȝeonglinges ȝeond þa hæþene londes þat heo heom biȝeten wurþliche wepnen and he heom forþrihtes wolden makien cnihtes and seoþþen mid heom wenden and fonden whar he mihten mid strongen kempen biwinnen kineriche hit halde touward aufrike of feole kuneriche monies riches monnes sune monie haþene gume comen to þan hæþene þringe þa þis ferde wes isomned and his folc arimed þa weoren þer italde cnihtes swiþe balde an hundred and sixti þusend freoliche iwapned wiþuten heore scutten þa biuoren scolden scuuen wiþuten þan craftmonnen þe comen to forþ heo iuusden vnimete uerden to þare se wenden þa heo wind hafden into scipe halden haþene kempen seouentene þer foren þat kinges sunen weoren þer weoren twenti and æhten of eorlene streone suipten from londe seouen hundred scipene a formeste flocke wiþuten þa feoliende forþ flet mid vþe folc vnimete þa æitlondes allen þa heo biforen funden alle heo eoden an honde þan kinge moniane kinge he faht wiþ and alle heo ȝirnden his griþ and alle þe londes he biwon þat he lokede on and þa a þan ende he com to irlonde and þat lond he al biwon and aqualden þa leoden and wes icleoped king þere of þan kinelonde and seoþþen he gon wende into þissen londe seil heo droȝen to hune and comen to suþhamtune þa wunede biȝeonde þere of hengestes cunne in þan norþ ende drenches sume sixe heo iherden tiþinde of þan kinge ofte heo heom biþohte what heo don mihten hu heo mihten biswiken of his richen and bruttes alle aquellen mid luþeren heore craften sexisce men senden sonde to þan king and seiden þat heo wolden wiþ hine griþ iwurchen leofere heom weore to here þene þan vncuþe kinge ȝef he heom wolde griþien þat heo mosten liuien and aȝeuen heom þat lond þat while þe king hengeste bitahte þa he nom his dohter leoue and heo him wolden senden gauel of þan londe halden hine for hehne king heore deorling and þis heo him toȝeornden mid ȝislen to isoþien and heom ilefde al heore leosinge and þis griþ ȝette and dai heom sette þa wes biswiken al mid heore craften auer seoþen kineric he hehten al mid hokerworden þe king heo forhusten ileouede to soþe sexisce monne lare vnder þan worden heo letten writ makien and senden heore sonden to þen kinge and þus þa word seiden þa a þan writ stoden hail seo þu hal seo þu heþene king heil seo þi duȝeþe hail þine drihtliche men we sunden men sexisce selest of þan kunne þa hengest of sexlonde hider mid him brohte wunieþ inne brutaine bi norþe þere þu art heþene king we heþene kempen is cristine mon he is us laþ forþan and ȝif þu wult al þis lond nimen to þire aȝere hond we wulleþ mid þe uehten mid fullere strenþen and ofslæn and alle his cnihtes flan and setten al þis kinelond a þire aȝere hond ȝif þu hit wult us aȝiuen we þe wulleþ ȝelden sixti hundred punden to alches ȝeres firsten and we wulleþ þine men bicumen to ȝislen sullen þe ure sunen and ȝif hit þi wille weore þat þu hider woldest wende þas forwarde makien and þas spechen uæstnien we wulleþ oueral atlien to þe seluen a watere and a londe halden þe uor kinge þa bigon to spekene þe kene ȝarkieþ mine scipen biliue forþ ic wulle liþe seiles heo up droȝen forþ heo gunnen siȝen luken rapes longe liþen forþ mid uþen and swa heo gunnen wenden to norþhumbrelonde and speken wiþ sexisce men and sæhte iwurþen and sworen þat heo wolden heore forward halden þa weoren heo al an and sexesce men þa somneden heo uerde vnimete an ærde and ferde touward þan kinge of þissere riche and æuere heo sungen mid hokere of þan kinge his bruttes gaderede and beide heom tosomne and him to wende al þat was on londe for rihtere neode nusten heo red betere muchel folc hafde and ferde vnimete and ofte he com to compe to kinge and ofte he him faht wiþ and neuere no ȝirde his griþ and for heo hokerede him on he iwarþ swiþe kene mon and ȝif he hafde genge efne wiþ weore sone islaȝen his folc idon of lifdaȝen ah æuere a þan ende wæx genge and æuere a þan ende feol genge draf wide ȝeond þas riche and at cherinchestre biclusde hine ful faste and moni dæi þer biuoren he lette þider fusen al þat he hafde ihalden þat corn of þissen londe and þa walles fastnede wunder ane stronge þet iherde and þider he gon ride and bilæi chirenchestre wiþutene swiþe faste and al þis kinelond walde to his aȝere hond burȝes he forbarnde tunes he forswelde bruttes he aqualde balu wes on londe munekes he forpinede on mani are wise þa riche wif he lette his hiredmen makien to horen preostes he alle ofslæh alle þa chirchen he todroh clærkes he aqualde alle þa he funde eche child he lette seoþe alle þa cnihtes he lette hon forþrihtes al þis lond forferde a ueole cunne wise wulc wræcche folc swa mihte fleh ut of þeode sum to wales wende sum to cornwale sum into neustrie þe hatte nu normandie sum fleh biȝeonden sæ into bruttaine and gunnen wunien seoþþe æn þet lond heht armoriche and summe heo fluȝen to irlonde for þan æie of and þer wuneden þeouwe inne þraldome heo and al heore cun and her ne come nauere aȝen and þus losede bruttes al þas kinelondes and bilæi chirenchestre abuten swiþe uaste and wes wiþinnen and moni of his monnen wa wæs þan leoden þe þa weoren on liuen hit was in ane dæie þat mid his duȝeþe dringes heþene riden a slatinge þa com þer an gume riden to kingen he wes ihaten inne france wes his ærd he wes louweises sune þas kinges of þere þeode his fader hine hafuede ut idriuen of al his kinerichen þat no moste he neouwar wunie on al his onwalde and he fleh to þissen londe to kinge he hafde to iueren twa þusend rideren and mon he bicom ne mihte he na wurse don for seolue he forsoc and to þan wursen he tohc and þer forlete he cristindom and heþescipe nom him on and swa heo uoren beien mid mucle heore uerde and bileien chirenchestre an elche halue wel faste wel ofte men comen ut of burhȝen and ræsden an mid ræȝere strenþe and sloȝen of his folke feole þusende and senden heom to helle heþene hundes alle wes swiþe goud cniht and swiþe wel he heold his fiht and faste he heold chirchestre mid strengþe þan mæste þat ne mihte næuere mæren his ferde ar he lette heom mid ginnen biswiken wiþinnen castles makede abuten chirenchestre þreo he bitahte þreom heþene cnihte himseoluen he heold þat ane þat oþer makede ænne tur þerinne he bulde ænne bur þerinne he pleoȝede his plaȝen þa me luuede a þeon daȝen þerinne he hafde his þa he heold for his god hit ilomp on ane dæiȝe þat mid his duȝeþe weoren swiþe bliþe and druncken of wine þa com þer an heþene mon awaried wurþen he forþan and askede tidende þe kinge seie me lauerd þu art swiþe riche king heou longe wult þu beoȝie abuten þissere burȝe what wult þu ȝiuen me ȝif ich þe burh ȝiuen þe and al þat is wiþinne to don þine iwille þat noht no biþ to leue al þu hit slat aȝe þa andswarede þe riche heþene king ich ȝiue þe ane eorldom auere to aȝe wiþ þat þu aneoste þe burh me bitache þis forward wes imaked anan lut men hit wuste þa þes heþene cniht up aras forþrit and nettes bisohte ibroiden swiþe narewe and þa tolen þerto and cuht heom swiþe narewe þer biforen he gon ȝeoten draf and chaf and aten þus he hit gon dihten and sparewen þerto liht and he a þan uorme drahte swiþe monie he ilahte and he from þan grunde nom heom mid isunde þat alle heore whingen noht awemmed neoren þa bisohte he nutescalen and lette þe curneles ut draȝen and tinder nom and lette i þan scalen don and foren to þære nihte fur þeron brohte and to þan sparewen uoten uaste heom icnutten þeos he lette forþ wenden swiþe ueole sparewen þa sparwen heore flut nomen and fluȝen to heore innen ȝeond þare burȝen þær heo ar wuneȝende weoren i þan eouesen he grupen swa heo duden in þen muȝen anan swa þet fur wes hat swa þe sparewe innere crap þe wind com mid þere nihte and þat fur awehte and þa burh a feole studen gon hure to bernen an æst halue an west halue wa wes brutten þere þenne heo wenden beon sikere and fluȝen in ane ende þenne aras þat fur anan biuoren and bihinden lette blawen hornes and bemen fiften þusende þarsten to blase bruttes forburnen bruttes gunnen irnen heo leopen ut of walle and me heom sloh alle nes hit nohwhar iseid no a bocken irad þat æi folc swa feire swa forfare weore swa wes and his genge þe king wes of bruttene þa burh born alle niht þe brune wes vnimete þat feht wes sone idon þat fur heom eoden ouenon and king him isah þat he ouercume wæs þe king him gon crepen an heonden and a futen swulc he mid unsunde al uorwunded weore and swa he swiþe stille bistal from his duȝeþe and west him gon wenden into þe walsce londen and þas waiȝes he wende ut of þisse londe and nuste nauere na man whar him bicom buten ænes an ane tide an cniht þer com ride and seide of tidende þat he in irlonde somnede genge and wolde mid fehte æft faren hidere ah nuste nauere na man to whan þe þret him bicom and þus wes chirenchestre and his londes aweste and ihouen to kinge of al þisse kinelonde for þenne þe burh wes biwunnen mid swulcches cunnes ginnen mid sparewen þat beren þat fur and sparewen heo forbarnden and feole wintere seoþþen þat folc þa þer wunede cleopeden heo sparewenchestre in heore leodspellen and ȝet hit dude summe men to imuȝen þe alde deden and þus wes þa riche burh mid reouþen fordemed and wes on londe iheouen her to kinge and wes an heþene mon and fordude þane cristindom þa þis wes al þus ifare þæ wes her sorȝe and muchel care falde þa munstres and anheng alle þa munkes of cnihten he carf þe lippes of madenen þa tittes preostes he blende al þis folc he scende ælcne bilefued mon he lette bilimien and þus he gon to taken on and fordude al þisne cristindom and seoþþen he uor to lundene to ane muchele hustinge þider gunnen siȝe alle sexleode þa wuneden i þissen londe mid kinge and his men bicome monie and vniuoȝe heom heold forward and aȝef heom sone al þis ærd of him to heoldenne and habben hine for kinge and þe king hehte al þat hine lufede þat wharswa heo mihten finde bruttes i þissen londe þat hine anan sloȝen oþer mid horsen todroȝen buten he libben wolden his lif in þraldome and forsaken godes mæsse and luuien hæþenesse þenne moste he libben þeou a þisse londe bisiden allemaine is a lond angles ihaten þer weoren iborne þa ilke þe weorn icorne þa an hond bitahte al þis kinelond alse he heom a forward hædde ȝif he hit biwunne al his biheste he heom bilaste of englen heo comen and þerof heo nomen nomen and letten heom cleopien ful iwis þat folc þat wes ænglis and þis lond heo cleopeden ænglelond for hit wes al on heore honde seoþþe ærest bruttes bæhȝen to þissen londe brutaine hit wes ihaten of brutten nom taken a þat þis folc com þa þisne nome him binom and moniee of þan burȝen and monie of þan tunen and monie of þan londen and of þan hamen heo binomen heore namen al for bruttene sceome and nomen al þis lond and setten hit al an heore hond for hit heom al ȝette and himseolf aȝein wende þa comen heo to lundene to þan muchele hustinge and wolden ane king makien to þissere kineriche þa ne mihtte heom iwurþe wha þis lond scolde aȝen and towende mid alle a muchelere wraþþe and fif kinges aneouste heo makeden in þisse londe and ælc nom of oþere al þat heo mihten ane while unsome and an oþere while isahte and þus heo wuneden here an hundred and fif ȝere þat neuere com here cristindom icud i þissen londe no belle irungen no masse isunge na chirche þer nes ihaleȝed no child þer nes ifuleȝed þa wes inne rome a pape of godes dome wes ihate godd seolf hine lufede þa wes hit in ane stunden þat þe pape wolde wenden þat he wolde speden an ane of his neoden þa com he in are strete þat strahte to rome þa isah he leden of englisce leoden þreo swiþe fæire men faste ibunden heo scolden beon iseolde and þa paneȝes weoren italde þa fræinede þa pape anan of feiȝere þan monnen whonnene heo weoren and hu heo þare comen and of wulche stronde heo istroned weoren þæ andswarede þe an þat wes a swiþe fair mon we beoþ heþene men and hider beoþ iladde and we weoren ut isalde of anglene londe and fulluht we to þe ȝeorneþ ȝef þu us wult ifreoiȝen þat seiden men anglisce aþele iborene þa reousede godd hine luuede and þas andsware saide þe pape wes isele iwis ȝe beoþ ænglisce englen ilicchest of alle þan folke þa wunieþ uppen uolde eouwer cun is feȝerest of alle quike monnen þe pape heom freinede of feole tidinde of laȝen and of londen and of þissere leodene kinge and heo him al seiden soþ þat heo wusten and he heom ureoiȝen lette and fulluht on sette and charde aȝein sone eft into rome anne cardinal cleopede icoren of his uolke wes ihotæn aþelest clærken þe pape him seide in his somrune þu scalt wende mid soþfæste þonke into englelonde to kinge and beode þer godes goddspel þe scal spede ful wel and ich þe feouwerti bitæche wel gode clærkes nu tomarȝen biþ þe dæi þa þu scalt do þe i þene wæi forþ ferde and his clærkes mid him þat him wes ful iwil at tanette he com hider in and swa he up is iwend þat he com into kent swa he uorþ to cantuareburi þer him þuhte swiþe muri þer he funde þat king wes a þan ærd he talde tidende of þan heoueneliche kinge he seide him þat goddspel and þe king him luste swiþe wel wel he þat larspel undernom aneouste he ȝirnde cristindom iuulȝed iwarþ king and al his duȝeþe mid him and anan he gon to wurche ane swiþe feire chirche a seinte trinetþes nome wel wes þan kinge þeruore þa iwende seint vorþ æst and west and suþ and norþ and seoþþe þurhut englelond and turnde hit to godes hond clærkes he lerde chirreches he arerde seoke men he helde þur halindes mihte and swa he droh suþward þat he com to dorchestre þer he funde þa wurste men þa on londe wuneden he talde heom godes leore and duden him to scare he tahten heom cristindom and heo grenneden him hon þer stod seint and his clærkes mid him and speken of godes sune al swa wes ær heore iwune þer heo iwurþen to to wraþere hele and nomen tailes of rehȝen and hangede on his cape an elchere halue and bihalues urnen and wurpen hine mid banen and seoþþe ȝeiden him on mid ȝeomerliche
