stanen and swa heo hine gunnen sende an driuen hine ut of þan ende seint heo weoren laþ and he iwraþ swiþe wraþ and he fif milen iwende from dorchestre and com to ane munte þe muchel wes and hende þer he lai on cneowe ibede and cleopede auere touward gode þat he hine awreke a þan awarriede uolke þa hine isend hafden mid heore scaþe deden vre drihte hine iherde into þere heouene and his wreche sende an wræstliche þan folke þa þe rihȝen tailes hangede a þan clarkes þa tailes heom comen on þeruoren heo maȝen iteled beon iscend wes þat moncun muggles heo hafden and inne hirede ælches men cleopeþ heom muglinges and euerelc freo mon ful telleþ heom on and englisce freomen in uncuþe londen for þan ilke dede heo habbeoþ neb rede and monies godes monnes sune in vncuþe londe þe nauere ne com þer neh is icleoped cued him wunede vnder ane munede and his clarkes mid him eke þeo comen of rome cleopede to drihtene þe scop daȝes lihte særimod and sorhfulle heom sceomeden wel sære þat þat vniwraste moncun heom iscend hafden þa wolde he þerafter sone wenden to rome and menen to þan holi appostolie hu dorchestreseten hine gunnen greten al swa he wes al ȝareou and wolde his wei uaren a þere ilke nihte þa ateoden him ure drihte and nemnede him his rihte nome welle uain wes he þeruore whæt þenchest þu what þenchest þu leof min woldest þu þus sone faren aȝein to rome no scalt þu noht ȝete fusen of londe þu ært swiþe leof me and ich wulle wunien mid þe and þu scalt irædliche into hefneriche heofne is þe al ȝaru þider scal þi saulen uaren þus spac ure drihten wiþ his cnihten þa þe underȝæt whæt ure drihten hæden isæid and he isah ure drihte þe þus him bihehte and ure drihten waht to heofene and a cneowe heolde adun to þere uolde þer he iseh ure drihten stonde weopende he cleopede to heuenliche kinge ȝeorne he bad are to þan almihtie gode ær he mid alle ueolle adun to þere uolde a þan ilke stude þer stod ure drihten þer he pihte his stæf himseolf he cneoulede þer neh and his iueren he seide larspel and hit likede him ful wel þa he isaid hauede þa sæȝen of ure drihten his staf he nom an honde and wolde to his inne ȝeonge up he læc þene staf þat water þerafter leop þe ueȝereste welles stræm þe irneþ on uolden ær nes þer na tun no wunende na man sone uolc gaderede to þan gode and al bi his læuen þider gunnen liþen and bigunnen þer to bulden bi þan watere þa was hende moni mon þer uætte hele þene stude he cleopede cernele cerno cernis þat is latin ful iwis cerno an englisc leoden ich iseo swa hit is iqueþen el is ebreowisc þat is godd ful iwis þene tun he cleopede cernel ich iseo drihten iwildel to þissere weorlde longe þe nome þer scal stonde alse hit is iqueþen after godes leoden þene stude to iwurþien þer stod ure drihten and his engles mid him þa he spac wiþ wende wide ȝeond englene londe he fullehtede kingge and heore heredringes he fullehtede eorles he fullehtede beornes he fullehtede englisce men he fullehtede sexisce men and sette an godes honde al þat was on londe þa wes he ful bliþemod þat folc he hafde iblissed norþ in englelonde bruttes hæfden an honde muchel del of londe and castles swiþe stronge þa bruttes nalden þan enlisce buȝen imong heom munekes weoren muchelere weorede seint funde inne þisse londe seouen biscopes to iwisse singende masse and enne ærchebiscop þe at karliun atstod and at bangor wes a munecclif mid muneken uniuoȝe hæhte heore abbeod he wes of heȝe monnen he hæfden on seuen hepen sixtene hundred muneken and ȝet ma þerto munekes swiþe balde and of bruttisce streonen stiþe imodede men writen sende to þan seouen biscopen and hehte heom comen sone and speken wiþ himseolue and don him hersumnesse and þurh him singen masse for he hauede an honde þa hehnesse of þissen londe he was icleopped legat of þissen londe he wæs primat and þas þinges weoren idone þurh þene pape of rome þas biscopes reiȝe weoren and andswere aȝeuen ne beo we nawit under him þe is ihaten ah we beo on londe heȝe men and stronge and habbeoþ ure irihte of ure archebiscpe þe wuneþ inne karliun godd clarc and wel idon þa haueþ his cantelcape on of þan pape and mid wurþscipe mucle haldeþ his wike for no scal hit nauere iwurþen a þissere worlderichen þat we auere buȝen þan uncuþen for he is ure fulle ifa and his iferen alswa for is iboȝen hidere into þissen londe and haueþ ifulleȝed þene king cantuaren aþeling ihaten heh inne anglene and he hafueþ ifunden here hundes heþene þa comen of sexlonde mid þan kinge þeo he alle fullehteþ and to gode fuseoþ þeo haldeoþ ure kinelond mid unrihte on heore hond cristine we beoþ alle and of cristine cunne and ure elderne swa weoren agan is þreo hundred ȝeren and heo beoþ neowene icumen and cristindom habbeoþ undernumen and heom fullehteþ and to gode fuseoþ for þan we hine hatiȝen uulleþ and heren hine nulleþ nauere to ure liue no scullen we him wurþen liþe þæs tiþende come to sone hu þe biscopes hine scenden and wulc andsweore him senden and hu bruttisce clerekes him seiden hokeres þa wes he sarimod and sorhful an heorten and fuse him gon sone and ferde to þan kinge and mænde to þan kinge of æstangle hu bruttisce biscopes hine grætte mid huxes and hu heo uorhoȝeden to halden hine for herre þe king hine iwraþede wunder ane sweþe and saide þat he wolde aquellen heom a londe and swe he dude seoþþe þerafter ful sone wes inne kintte king of þan londe þa hafde he enne mæi wes ihaten inne norþhumberlonde furcuþest alre kinge he radde al þa redes þat dede weoren þa biscopes þat heo weoren alle ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen nu nuste noht bruttes þere þat balu heom wes ȝiueþe sende sonde wide ȝeond his londe sende sonde ȝeond norhhumberlonde heo somneden uerde mucle on arde and wolden þa bruttes al fordon þa clærkes fordemen heo uoren to leirchæstre and þa burh bileien uaste heo wusten þerinne þat wæs a bruttisc eorl cniht mid þan bezsten wunede inne leirchastre ut wende and ȝarewede his ferde and wende him ut to uihtes wiþ cnihtes and sone wes him ouercumen and alle his bruttes weoren inumen and swa heo gunnen þrasten into leirchæstren sloȝen and nomen al þat heo neh comen and seiden þat heo wolden into wales wenden and slæn al þa bruttes þa þer weoren bihalues luuede murie inne leirchastre vnder þan ilke þinge comen to þan kinge munekes and eremite and canunes white biscopes and clærckes and preostes mid godes mærkes and feolen to his foten and his griþ ȝeornden and beden hine for godes leoue leten heom beon on londe and ho him wolden foren bidden to þan heȝen kingen þa andswarede forcuþest kinge lusteþ nuþe alle whæt ich sugge wulle wendeþ ut a þan felde mid eower monwerede and ich eou wulle word senden hu hit scal iwurþen and mine rædȝiuen reden me wulleþ vt wenden munekes and þa massepreostes vt wenden clærkes vt wenden canones alle ut wenden þa þer icumen weoren þes kinges griþ to wilnien for lufe of godd seolfne wiþuten þere burȝe an ane uelde brade wes isomned þat folc sone sorȝe heom wes ȝefþe nom to rede þeh na man hine ne bede þat he al þas wolde feollen to þan grunde he sende forþrihtes fif hundred cnihtes and niȝen hundred mid heom balde men afoten mid mucle wiaxen a þene ueld wenden and mid unrihtes sloȝen al þat heo neh comen heo ualden to grunde fiftene hundred and fife and sixti anan selere monnen bocilerede men balu wes on uolken þis sone wes itald wide and side þa weoren on londe þreo heȝe men italde and al þa bruttes anan halden to þan ilken þe kene eorl of cornwale swa hehte þe an heh mon on londen he heold deuenescire al an his honde alse þet water desse wendeþ into þere sæ bruttes þat lond heolden wel swiþe longe a þat þe stronge þe king of þissen londe heom binom þas londes alle and drof heom ouer tambre þat nauere heo þas kineþeode seoþþen no walde inne norþ wales wes a king þe kene of suþ wales monnen alre uæȝerest al þat lond sele into sæuerne from þan ufere ende þat wendeþ into þare sæi inne maluerne aneouste seuarne king wunede mid swiþe mucle uolke and him laþ to þe king of þissere leode and heom heold swa harde and mid hærme heom igrette and dreof heom mid his wepnen ut ouer weȝen and þat lond binom heom þat liþ þer bitwixen seuerne and weȝe no walden heo hit seoþþen and and þe balde somneden ferde of folke unimete and foren uppen þan kinge of norþhumbre and hardliche wiþ him fuhten and his ferde felden þer iwarþ sone forwunded ful sære þe king of norþhumbre þat comp wes vnimete þer wes eorl anan mid bronden toheouwen i þan compe þer ueollen ten þusend cnihten þurh steles biten baldere brutten anglisce and sexisce seouentene þusend mid machen weoren toheowen þa hep wes þa lassen him uorþ heolde into norþhumbre forwunded swiþe sare sorhful wes his duȝeþe comen i þissen londe to ane hustinge and and heore monweorede buȝen uorh mid heom al brutleoden to leirchestre foren and þa burh nomen þa hehten heo an hiȝinge cumen to hustinge al þat wolde libben inne þissere leoden þer comen ænglisce þer comen sexise þer heo makeden to kinge þene kene al hit him aloþede þat he on lokede þa weoren wunden inne norhhumbre alle iheled ah þe helþe was neoþered for lurre of his monnen and for his leoden uallen iherde from þes kinges hirede feole tidende of kinge þrattes unimete of alre laþest monne sende sonde into scotlonde and into norþ londe þer he cnihtes mihte uinden and after al þan uolke þe þer cumen mihte and bad heom heore helpes to heȝere neodes gaderede uerde ȝeond alle þissen ærde and al of wælisce londe comen to his honden and heolde hine forþ seoþþen toward norþhumbren þis iherden and him toȝæines wenden þat nas heom bitweounen buten bare twa milen fusden þa uerden swulc heo wolden uehten þa isæȝen eorles þa iseȝen beornes biscopes þa iseȝen and bocilarede men ȝif heo togadere comen and mid wepnen onsloȝen þat þær sculde ualle moni beorn fæie ofte heo biþohten what heo don mahten heo setten griþ heo sette friþ to anes dæiȝes firste heo speken heom tosomne and spileden bitweonen þat heo wolden alle þa kinges sehtnie þer iwurþen sahte þa kinges beie tweien sæhte and some heo custen wel ilome þas kinges wel ilomen mid luue heom icusten eorl custe oþer swulc hit weore his broþer sweines þer ploȝeden blisse wes mid þeinen wes king on londe bi norþen þere and wes king sele a suþ half þere blisse wes on hireden mid balden þat kingen næs hit isæid næuere an sæȝe no on leoþe þat mare luue weore ifunden bitweone twei kingen for þat þe an hafden þat heo hafden beien þe an heold þene oþer deorluker þene broþer beien heo wifes nomen ofte heo togadere comen þa þe wifes iwedded weoren on ane time to bedde heo eoden æiþer mid his lufe wende toward heore wife he streoneden tweien sunen beien an ane timen beien an ane dæie heo weoren afte iborne togadere heo weoren ibredde togadere heo weoren iuedde þa children wuxen and wel iþoȝen wel wes heore aldren for to uæstnen þa luuen of leofuen heore uæderen tosomne me heom tahte tosomne me heom tuhte beien heo wereden anes kunnes iweden al swa duden þa children swa ær duden þa aldren swa mouchel luue heolden þat sellic þuhte monnen and þus heo wuneden here wel feole ȝere þat þæ children weoren muchele iwaxen riden uppen steden and luueden cnihtes iweden heore maines heo uondeden wel ueole siþen heore armes weore stronge heo breken scaftes longe mid longe sweorden heo smitten þa ȝifen smærte biten heore uaderes þa comen mid mucle faȝernessen inne bruttaine mid muclere blisse þa ȝet þat londriche hehte armoriche þa ȝunge men me dubbede beiȝene to cnihte wiþ an luttel ȝeren þa uaderes dede weoren and þa twa children weoren ihouen to kingen æiþer heold his icunden swa duden ær heore ældren þæ wes inne cantwareburi þa burh wes þa swiþe muri an ærchebiscop þe wes mon swiþe god he forbad þan kingen kinehelm to nimene a þat hinseolf comen and setten hine an heore hafden þat bod wes ihalden a þas ærchebiscopes onwalden and his lond haueden a þis hælue þere and edwine al biȝeonde touward þan norþ ende kinges heo weoren ihouene and kinges isworene ah forbode wes þa crune an ure drihtenes nome þohte þe wes sune ofte he hine biþohte what he don mahte seoþþen heore faderes beiene forþ weoren ifarene næfde þa sehtnesse ilast buten seouen ȝere urist hefde castles swiþe monieȝe and þe richedom stod mære on hond gon liþe into londene he sende men gode after þan erchebiscope and hehte ful sone þat he to lundene come þa he to lundene com iqueme hit wes þan kingen þe king auoten eode toȝeines þan erchebiscope wiþuten his halle dure and sæide þu art wilcume and leofliche hine bihedde and lauerd hine cleopede he aȝaf ure drihten ælchere irihten he spac of feire lære and al of godes are his spechen weoren gode wiþ þan ærchebiscope þe king hine biþohte feire and swiþe ofte þat he on his icunde king hine makede to ane isette dæiȝe þat folc þær isomnede þer mæ sone makede to kinge muchel wes þa blisse þat wæs in þære burȝe of þisse uarecoste naþing nuste ah sone swa he hit wiste wraþ he wes an heorte and seide auere wiþ and wiþ ich wulle makien unfriþ and al ic wulle aquellen þat ich quike uinde of uolke ualsest alre monne uerde he gon gaderen of feole þusend monnen he hehde ituht to herie a þas half þære eoden heom to ræde cnihtes swiþe gode alle þa wiseste men þa weore inne londe heo lerden edwine king þe wes heore lauerd þat he sende his sonde to kinge and bisohte hine uæire alse his leofe broþer and for þere muchele luue þa heolde heore aldren þat hine letten king beon and his kinehalm avon and he wolde aȝein wenden heom to his folke ouer þere and griþ þær halden and ner æft aȝen teon wiþ þan he moste king beon ihouen and ihalden þurh þene heȝe godd and he wolden bi his liuen luuien and beon ȝaru to his neode an ælchere þeode þis iherde þe king wes bi suþþen and he andswerede mid aþelere speche nu ich iherd habbe wordes wise of edwine his bisocne þe is mi broþer deore ich me biræde wulle of swulchere neode and after ane lutel daȝen him andsware ȝeuen whaþer he hit wolde iunne oþer him forbeode hu swa his riche men ræden him wolden þe dæi wes isæt ah lutel mon wes þe bet þa þis al wes iwurþen þa comen heo to ane uorde duglas þa water wes ihaten þer heo touwenden þer wes þa motinge bituxe þan twam kinge ædwine bisohte mid alle þat he mahte þat him þolede kinehelm to beberene and he hine wolde luuien a to his liuen riche men eoden to ræde of swulchere neode summe hit gonnen ræden summe to forbeoden summe þer heolden wel to summe nolden hit no þa while þa cnihtes wise þa spechen sculden rihte þe king in are medewe alihte of his stede þan kinge luste slepe þa riche weoren at rede com þer a burcniht he wes þes kinges suster sune brien hehte his nome he nom his lauerdes hefd þe leof him wes on uolke in his bærm he hit læide and his lockes he toscædde þe king him gon to slæpen and brien gon to wepen urnen þa teres uppen þes kinges leores and þe king awoc of slepen wete weoren his wongen he grapede an his nebbe he wende þat hit bledde and bisæh uppen brien mid braden his lechen þa isah he of brien his teres ut luken sære gon þe kempe wepen ouer kinge þa axede þe king anan ihaten whæt is þe leofe mæi þat þu swa wepest todæi þu ært ihalden kene gume hauest þu nu quene þeouwes inume sæiȝe me biliue hu þe beon on siþe brien þa andswerede cniht mid þan bezste nu we maȝen wepen mid wanliche iberen halden us for hæne þer we weoren heȝe nu þu wult underuon þat nauer ær nes idon tweien kinges halden kinehelmes on londen nuþe we scullen wepen þæ ær richen weoren for wurþscipe ualleþ adune þer wes ær wunne þis iherde þe king wes on londe and iwærþ him abolȝe bitter ane swiþe and aneouste sende sonde to edwine kinge and hehte hine hihȝenliche uaren of his riche for ne scal he nauere bi mine quiken liuen kinehelm broken and ȝif he hit wul auon ich hit wulle wernen and ic hine biræuien wulle at his baren liue and nimen al norþhumberlond to mire aȝære hond and walden al his riche and he scal wurþen hene þas tidende me brohten to kinge and he iwræþ abolȝen wunder ane swiþe swa biþ a bar wilde þenne he biþ in holte bistonden mid hunden and þas andsware kende wraþest alre kingen swa me helpen drihten þa scop þas dæiȝes lihten and þa halidomes alle þa wunieþ inne rome kinehelm ich wulle bruke and he hit scal abugge and þeruore ibiden bitterest alre balewen he scal habben paþes weste and wildernesse inoȝe and moni modsorhȝe his monscipe scal ualle al swa hit ilomp suþþe þæræfter ful sone æiþer þratte oþer swiþe and þruste mid worde and swa heo todelden dæd heo bihehten ædwine wes kempe his men weoren kene wes cniht god and he hafde muchel mod edwine wende ouer and to lundene þas kinges weoren wraþe þa aræs þa weore heo riden and heo arnden heo herȝede and heo barnde heo sloȝen and heo nomen al þat heo neh comen wa wes þan beondes þa on londe wuneden wes inne lundene and somnede his leoden wide he sende sonde ȝeond feole kinelonde he hafde on his ferde fifti þusende herekempen heȝe to hermen swiþe kene bi norþe his writen nom aneouste and sende in to denene to galwaþe and to scotlond þat stod on edwines hond he somnede uerde ȝeond alle his ærde þat he isomned hafde sixti þusende cnihtes swiþe kene wode to uihte gon liþe ut of lundenne touward norþhumbre hærmes he wrohte he for ouer hiȝenliche swiþe and bigon to westen þat lond þat stod on edwines hond þa wes edwine king ærhþen bideled and he forþrihtes spac wiþ his cnihtes wurþe for niþing þe mon þe nule hine sturien habben bares heorte and remes brede cuþen þan kinge þat we quiken sunde he lette blawen bemen and bonnien his uerden forþ he gon wende þat he com to þan ende þer þe king wunede on cumelan togadere gunnen resen þeines riche breken speren longe sceldes brastleden an honde heouwen heȝe helmes scænden þa brunies feollen ærm kempes æmteden sadeles drem wes on uolcke þa eorþe gon to dunien urnen þa brockes of reden blodes feollen þa folckes falewede nebbes bruttes gunnen breoþen balu wes on uolken þus heo gunnen delen þene dæi longe riht to þan euening þa fleh þe king and edwine him after gende mid allen his imihten alle niht flah mid his cnihten nefden he of his ferde buten fif hundred cnihten heo fluȝen to scotlonde sorhen heom com on honde and edwine after annon mid fiftene þusend monnen baldere þeines heore beot wes iuorþed fulede þere uerde folc unimete from dæiȝe to daȝe þene king heo gunnen driuen soþ is on þan spellen heo þohten hine aquellen flæh to þere sæ scipen he þer funde þa scipen heo gunnen hure mid ahten swiþe deore into irlonde þa scipen gunnen wende hauene heo þer nomen isund þa scipen comen þa ahte irlond a king þat wes swiþe strong he hehte gille god king i þan rich he underfeng faire nid his cossen and ȝaf him wickinge ȝeond irlonde lette we nu beon and ga we to edwine aȝan edwine in þissen londe amarden þas leoden burȝes he barnde castles he ualde his here wrohte on londe harmes vniuoȝe al lond he walde to his aȝere hond þa comen hauweres to hirede þas kinges and seiden tidende edwine kinge wa wrþe heom for þon þat heo iboren weore saȝen heo him sæiden of ane mæidenne þat wes briennes suster hende ueirest wifmonne heo wunede i winchæstre inne þan castle and edwine mid his ferde þiderward wende sone swa he þider com mid strenþe he heo nom ladden heo to eouuerwic anan cnihtes swiþe wel idon to bure me ladde to þas kinges bedde þe king dude vnwisdom þat he þat ilke maide nom for þe wifmon a wes þes ilke kinges iua þa wunede i þan hirede an clarc þe com from spaine wes ihaten of heȝere laren feole craftes he cuþe þa he isah in þan lufte on sterren and on sunne and on þare sæ brade insiht he cuþe a winde and a mone of þan uisce þer he wlæt and of wurmen þer heo crepe in irlonde gaderede genge and to scipe flutte mid muchelre uerde swiþe ueorre isah on þan sterre þat ferde cumen wolde uppen ædwine kinge and hine lerde hu he þas leoden mihtte alre bezst biwiten ba bi londen and bi scipen and his men ofte gunnen fusen to cumen to þissen londen biuoren wes æuere edwine and þa hafne heom forwarnde þurh lare ne mihten heo cumen here wa wes þat he wes on liuen for he bigon þene swikedom uppen his sweordbroþeren and þeruore himself hafde hærm þene meste him to cleopede his bezste cnihtes alle and seide þat he wolde wende to brutaine and þene king iseon þe wes ihaten an heorte him weore þe selere for heo weoren isibbe heo weoren of ane cunne þa kinges beiȝe tweien bruttes heo weoren beine ah swiþe heo weoren unbalde to scipen com and seh forþ mid uþen and seilede after vþe unsel him wes on mode to ane æitlonde heo bicomen þat stondeþ bi gernemuþe likede swa heom likede þer heo gunnen wikie þer heo abiden wederes for þe wind heom stod toȝæines þa iwarþ þe king þere isæcled ful swiþe and hafde þat uuel hate binumen him wes þa hele þa niȝen dæȝes weoren aȝeong þe king wes swiþe unstrong þa wes he wræccheliche oflust after deores flæsce brien his mæi he cleopede and sone hit him cudde þat buten he hafde deores flasc anan dæd he moste þolien ofte wes briene wa and neouuere wurse þene þa hundes nom brien and hiredmen wel idon ȝeond wudes and ȝeond feldes heo uerden bilifes þurh nanes cunnes ginne no mihten heo deor iwinne nouþer heort no hinde no mihte heo nauere ifinde þe king sende his sonde after brien þa wes to longe leof was þe king briene wa wes him on liue ofte he hine biþohte what he don mahte and biþohten him enne ræd seoþþen he þohten him swiþe god he igrap a nailsax selliche kene and wel iwhæt and feng himseolue swa neh þat he nom his aȝe þeh for unimete neode þerof he makede brede he bredde heo an hiȝinge and brohte heo þan kinge hail seo þu þu ært mi kinelauerd ich habbe þe here ibroht breden alre deorest þat ich auere an æi borde beren biuoren kinge held me to and æt herof sone þin hele heo scal iwurþen þe king sæt on his bedde his beornes hine biheolde of þere brede he æt sone þerafter him wes þæ bet þe king him gon to sweten þat ufel hine gon forleten wiþinnen þan fif niht þe king iwræþ fere forþriht swa næuer þe king nuste whæt he inoted hafde þe king iwræþ al uere his folc iwarþ bliþe wind heom com on wille heo wunden up seiles to coppe scipen gunnen liþen leodscopes sungen ba weoren sehte sæ and þa sunne wind and þa wide se ba eke isome flod ferede þa scipen scopes þer sungen at ridelæt he com alond þer wes blisse and muche song bitwixe dinan and þere sæ ȝet hit is isene sone swa he þer com feire he wes underuon þa kinges weoren bliþe beiene togaderes þer wunede þe king al þene winter a skenting þerafter com leinten and dæȝes gunnen longen þer heo gunnen somnien scipen uniuoȝen folc unimete grunden an uolde þus dude and peluz hit wuste anan þurh his dweomercræften þe wunede in þan lufte and al þat he auunde in þan lufte and bi þan grunde þurh ælches cunnes þing he warnede æuere ædwine king and dude him al to witen of þare uerde and of þan scipen wes in brutaine mid þan kinge þe wes his moddrie sune and muchel hine lufede and þat iherde suggen wel feole siþen þat þe hende þe com ut of spaine warnede edwine þene king æuer þurh alle þing of feole cunne þinge þat him weoren to cumene þan gode wa wes on mode and ofte spæc wiþ brien þe wes his deoreste mon and nomen heom to rede and to somrune þat alle þa while þe weore alife no mihte comen to þissen londe mid nauer nare lisse þat edwine hit nuste brien bonnede his fare brien hafde mucle care nom him an honde of seoluer and o golde maþmes unimete moniare cunne nom he tunnen gode and þa æhte dude þerinne to þære sæ he wende and seilede mid vþe he hafde on his uore wintunnen inoȝe on sæ and on londe his win he lette fonden and on alle wissen he toc him on swulc he weore a chepmon in he wende at barbefleot and at suþhamtune up aleop þer he ut draȝen lette win of his tunne and hendeliche hit delde alle þare duȝeþe þa him abuten weore riche and henen and alle luuede þene chapmon þa him lokede on vmbe seouennihten he spac wiþ his cnihten alle weoren his iueren swulc heo chapmen weoren and eorþhus heo hureden stiþ biwaled on eorþen heo cluseden þer wiþinnen alle heore wintunnen heo scupten heore lauerde ænne nome neowe heo hahten hine kinebord ut of spainisce ard he saiden þat he wenden wolde wide ȝeond þissen londe and fondien wher he mihte his win sullen on wille forþ he wende bi nihte mid one of his cnihte forþ he gon liþe into lundene and aneouste gunnen wende onfast westmustre and fraineden tiþinde of edwine kinge sone men him talde soþ þat heo funde þat þe king in eouerwic wnede mid allen his folke mid muchere blisse men he hafde inoȝe brien gon to farene uorþ mid ane iuere ut of lundene derneliche he liþede þene wæi touward eouuerwike wraþ on his mode þa he iuaren hafde fulle seouen nihte þa imette he enne pilegrim pic bar an honde hiȝendliche þe com from þas kingges hirede brien hine gon fræine of his farecoste þe pillegrim him talde al þat he wolde wiþ him warfte brien al his iweden and æiþer gon liþe þider him to luste brien enne smiþ funde þe wel cuþe smiþie and saide þat he wes pelegrim ah pic nefden he nan mid him þene þridde dæi þer bifore at his inne he wes forlore his foreward he makede þe smiþ gon to smiþeȝe ane pic swiþe long swiþe muchel an swiþe strong swiþe scarp wes þe pic þe staf wes swiþe sellic þene staf he nom an honde and ferde ouer þan londe þat he com sone liþe to þas kinges hirede brien eode upward brian eode dunward ne mihte he iheren word of his suster nan no he uraini ne durste for þes kinges folke þa hit wes dai amarȝe þat drihten hine sende þe king lette feden alle þa neode hafden alle þe blæþe þe wuneden on þe burȝe me heom hehtte onneouste cume to þan castele bi þusend and bi þusunde þræsten gunnen binward brien wenden binne mid oþer wrecche monnen his lætes weoren alle swulc he lome weore alle his hateren weoren totoren nas he noht to þan iboren þe an hine putte hiderward and þe oþer hine putte ȝeondward uncuþ him wes swiþe swulc craft on folcke his pic he heold bisiden and sat imong þan oþeren þe king him gon to þeinen mid alle his herecnihten þæ quene bar to drinken and alle hire burlutlen þa ilomp hit seoþþe þerafter ful sone þat galarne þat maiden com hire ȝeongen bolle heo hafde an honden þermide heo bar to dringen þa isæh heo brien þer deore hire broþer on wræcches monnes liche þeh he weoren riche anan swa þat maiden hine isæh sone heo him to bæh and droh of hire uingre an of hire ringe and salde him an honde ænne ring of rede golde and þus sæide galerne þat godfulle maide haue þis gold wræcche godd þe wurþe milde and buȝe þe þermide hateren þat wiþ chele þe maȝen werien þa wuste he to soþe þat his suster icneou hine and þas word seide brien þe sele forȝelde hit þe drihten þe sop þas daȝes lihten þat þu þissen lome monne ȝiue of þine golde ymong þan wrecche uolke þat maiden heo hudde bitwxen twam windewen þat maiden iwarþ an selden and spæc wiþ hire broþren þa bet hire wes on heorten and talden him tiþende al of þas kinges hirede and heo him tahte þene clarc þe com from spæine and he lokien agon in læþest alre monne þa heo togadere hafden ispeken sone heo gunen todelen for nauer neoþer nalde for his æfne wiht of golde þat þe king hit wusten þat heo togaderen weoren for sone heo weoren fordon ba oþer ofslaȝen oþer anhon þat folc hafden alle iȝeten and arisen from heore seten dremeden drunkene men dune wes on folke wes aneoste and ȝemde þene nap brien him atlede to for he hafde him ful wa ido his pic he nom an honden and helede hine under capen swa longe he gon atlen þat he com him baften and imong al þan þrunge þærsten him i þan ruge þat he brac ut biforen under his breosten and forþ he biwafde þene pic he bilæfde and forþ imong þan uolke þa wes he al fere and wende him aneoste of þas kinges hirede æuere forþ þene wæi suþriht alse he læi þa he þus hafde idon to axcetre he bicom þer he funde forþrihtes monie of his cnihtes and freineden ȝeorne of his leodkinge and brien heom gon tellen þat wilspelles weoren and seiden þat cumen wolde anan mid swa muchele uerde of feole cunne ærde þat ne durste edwine king cumen toȝæines him naþing no in nauer nare burȝe ne durste he him ibide þat iherde deuene and þa men of deorchestre and þan cornwælscen wel heom wes on liuen brien sende his sonde ouer sæ to brutlonde and dude þan kinge to witen aiþer bi worden and bi writen of alle his deden and þat wes on deþen and bad hine an hihȝende comen to þissen londe and þe king duden swa swa swiþe swa he mæhte and brien sende sonde into suþhamtune and longien him to lette his maþmes leoue and alle þa beornes anan þe buȝen him to wolden comen aneouste into exchæstre and stiþimodede men þa burh gunnen walden þat iherde þe king wes ful bliþe and inne brutaine bonnede ferde þat he þreo hundred hauede hæȝere scipene and al he hafden þerto þat heom bihouede and þe king wide gon sende and forþ he gon liþen mid his brutleoden þat is to iwitene mid twa hundred scipene to helpen his cunne kinge weder stod an wille wind mid þan bezste heo rihten heore loues and up droȝen seiles liþen ouer sæstræm swa sel þuhte heom þa comen he to tottenes beien þa kinges selemon þe sele and þæ kene þat londfolc wes bliþe for heore leodkinge þa wes in æstlonde a king þe hehte he biwuste a þan daȝen þat folc of merchene laȝen and he lufde edwine edwine lufde hine and euere he wolde reden edwine to his neoden and iherde suggen soþere worden þat brien heold exchestre biclused wiþinnen faste and þe king wide gon sende þa and sumede uerde and forþ him fusen and wenden to exchastre mid vnimete genge and bilæi uul faste þa burh of exchestre brien þe wihte mid twa hundred cnihte wes þer wiþinnen and þa burh wereden sone þa tidende icumen wes to þære hauene of totenes to kinge hu brien wes biþrungen he lette blawen bemen and bonnien his ferden and ferde æuere þene wæi þæ touward exchestre lai and delde a þreo ulockes his duhtie cnihtes and þus cleopien agon þe king wes abolȝen æuerælc god cniht faren heom to forþriht for we beoþ cnihtes gode mid wepnen wel idihte arude we brien þe is min ibore mon for ȝif heo nimeþ brien heo hine wulleþ aquelen and seoþþen heo wulleþ hine ahon and alle his iferen fordon and us þerafter sone mid alle heore imæhte to heo gunnen riden gæres heo letten gliden breken bræde weiȝes brustleden scaftes golduaȝe sceldes scanden bilifes feollen þa cnihtes faleweden nebbes ȝeond þan feldes wide swulten men uæiȝe blod orn in þe weiȝe strames swiþe brade þer neoren eorles no wurþer þene cheorles þer weoren þa ofslæȝene seouen þusend fulle marcchisce monnen þa þer icumen weoren þa falden heo adune heremarken uaȝe heo wurpen sceldes sone dunede þa eorþe þa sette to fleme alre ȝeomerest folke and after heom mid allen his imahten and mid his aȝene honden nom þene king he wes mærwales fader mildburȝe aldeuader heo nomen and duden hine i benden wiþinnen excestre and biwusten hine wel faste swa sellic hit ferde in alle þan uahte þat nas þe king amarred nanes kunnes þing and hine biwuste wel þurh alle custe and fæire heo hine uedde and faire he eode to bedde þa weoren agan seouen niht þa nom enne cniht þe wes swiþe wis mon and wel cuþe speken and cleopede hine to rade and seide him of his neode and ȝeorne hine bisohte for lufe of ure drihte þat he speke wiþ þe wes his kinelauerd þat he hine griþede þurh þene godd heȝe and he wolde bicumen his mon his monscipe hæhȝen dæiȝes and nihtes he and al his cnihtes þe cniht him forþ wende to kinge þer he hine imette and fæire hine igrette and dude alse god mon sel him wurþe for þan for a is treowe monnen treouþe ihalden hal seo þu þu art mi kinelauerd þe ibundene king hider me gon sende and ȝerneþ þine ære nu and aueremære and he wulle þi mon bicume and to ȝisle seollen þe his sune and of þe his kinelond halden and for lauerd þe ikenne and on ælchere þeode beon ȝaru to þine neode he wule beon þi mon icoren aȝein ælcne mon iboren þa andswærien agon mid aþelen his worden þe kene þe king of suþlonde ȝif wolde halde þat he me bihateþ to don and bitechen me his sune his gold and his gærsume and treouwe mon auere beon and neouwar min herm iseon and likede swa him likede næuere me biswike ich me biræden wolde of swulchere neode þer anan forþriht andswarede þe gode cniht la swa ic auere mote iþeon ich wulle his an barh beon and habbeon to iueren an hondret rideren uppen alle ure londe uppen seoluer and uppen golde and swa ich bide are ȝet he wulle mare ane suster he haueþ hende in þan æst ende nis nan feirure wifmon þa whit sunne scineþ on þe king of france ȝirneþ hire ful iwis and he wulle hire to morȝeue þene mans bitæchen and habben heo to quene þat mæiden helene and ich suggen þe to soþe þæh ich þi broþer weore æuere þe is selere þisulf þat þu heo habbe þurh hire þu miht biwinnen lufe of hire cunnen and iwinnen al þi kinelond to þire aȝere hond and wunien on londe and walde þine riche þa andswarede þe king wes on londen hit is on mine rede to don þat þu bede ȝif þu miht under þis forward me ileste ich þe ȝeuen to hure al deuenescire al for heleine lufe hiȝendliche let heo cume þe cniht him gon wende mid muchelere genge to þan castle of deoure on þere sæ oure he nom þer helene wunderliche and fæire and forþ he heo ladde into winchæstre þer wes muchel blisse burhmen weoren bliþe þer þe king com him toȝeines heom he weddede þat mæiden and nom heo to his bedden þer wes wifþing riche and vnimete blisse þa hit wes dæi amarȝen and duȝeþe gunnen sturien and þe king iuæstned hafde alle his forwarde þa nom he muchele genge and after sende þer he wes ful faste in þan castle of and mid muche lufe hine hehte cumen to lundenne to lundene com he wes ahtliche underuon and þe kene mid lufe hine custe and bicom his mon þer his monscipe wes þe mare þa weoren lundenisce men bliþest arle leoden þa wes hit seoþþe þerafter noht longe gan liþe wide ȝeond þis londe alle þa hine lufeden he heom gon griþien alle þa him heolden wiþ he binom heore lif and heore leoden and al þat heo leof hafden and hiȝendliche gon wende touward þere and gon þat lond westen mid hærmen þan mæsten þat iherde edwine and alle þat luueden hine swiþe heo gunnen dreden of deden edwine nom his sonde and senden to sexlonde he sende into denene he sende into noreine into wellisce londe into scotlonde into orcaneiȝe into galwaiȝe into islonde into frislonde into gutlonde þer gumen weoren kene he bed heom cumen sone mid wepnen wel idone to driuen ut þa bruttes þe bisie weoren to harmes and þenne he bruttes hæfden mid bronden tohæuwen he wolde al þis kinelond setten an heore hond bute þat he icleoped weore king of þan londe he wolde þere duȝeþen þis lond al todalen ah he ful lutel wuste what ilomp seoþþe comen touward londe touward edwine kinge bi sæ and bi londe feole cunne leoden þer comen seouen kinges and six sunen kinges seouentene eorles and sixti þusend beornnes næs he boren nauere in nauer nare burhȝe þe mihte in æi spelle þat oþer uolc telle nas hit nauere isæid no on bocken irad þat æuer ær weore æi swa muchel ferde æuere in ængelonde þurh ænie king togadere edwine gon to uarene mid mucle his ferde and after wende mid unimete folke þe stude hehte hædfeld þer heo atstoden under scelde twelf milen is þe wald þe is ihaten heþfeld edwine an his ende his teldes alle sette his marken and his mare and eke his monweorede and þe kene him com toȝaines sone þer fusden tosomne uerden unimete heo fuhten feondliche feollen þa uaiȝe brokes þer urnen mid unimete stremen of bloden þan ræde þe balu wes unimete helmes þer gullen beornes þer ueollen sceldes gunnen scenen scalkes gunnen swelten at þan forme rese fifti þusende baldere beornen heore beot wes þæ lasse þer wes edwines ferde ȝeoumerest alre uolke and edwine himseolf anan ærmest alre kingen þer wes edwine ofslaȝen and his sunen tweien þer feollen seouen kinges and six sunen kinges his eorles his beornes his cnihtes his cheorles þer wes þe swein and þe cnaue beinen of are laȝe nefden heo nane are of þan lasse no of þan mare ah al þa ferde wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen of þan fehte fleh a gume edwines ȝungeste sune wellen henden wes þe mon ihaten nefde he to iueren buten an hundred rideren þeos to wuden wenden and þer gunnen wunien and barnden lond and eoden him luþere an hond and his folc sloȝen a feole cunnes wissen þat iherde þe king wes on londen hu edwines sune dude utlaȝen wune muchel uolc nom and lette heom to wuden gan and heo funden and wiþ him fehten þer heo sloȝen and alle his iueren nu wes þe king bliþest alre kempen nu wes icleoped king ouer anglen wes king under him and ma þa iqueme weoren him aquald hefde of edwines cunne al þat þer wes hende wiþuten ane monne he wes ihaten under drihtene bald he wes of edwines cunne and him leofuest monne and he wes hex monnen of edwines cunnen nom on his hond al togadere edwines lond eorles and kempen his men al bicomen me heold hine king hæhne biȝeonde þere þat iherde and þus quaþ to his eorlen somnie we nu ferde ȝeond alle mine ærde nu ich mi lond habben bitald nu hauiþ hit ah þeruore him scal ileoten bitterest alre baluwen for þan kinelond ich hine aqualle wulle and al his ferde fallen to grunde and al þat he of com ich hit wulle fordon and swa me scal him tache to walden kineriche aleggen ich wulle his muchele mod monnen he is me laþest somnede uerde mucle in þissen ærde and ferde touward þere ȝaru al to fehte þis iherde þas heȝes godes icorne and nom him al his ferde þa hafde in his ærde and forsoc þat feht sone forsaken him weoren laþe and ferde æuere forþward and him after wende ah oftaken he hine ne mahte þa wes adred for wiþ scotten he wes iuæid for he þat norþerne uolc hæuede ineouþered ful swiþe and nom him to rede of swulchere neode þat he aȝain wolde for þer he kare hafde and biteche þe wes his underkinge folc and his ferde to flemen of arde edwines mæi and driuen hine of londe and al spede swa he ispeken hafde aȝæn he gon wende into þisse londe and in þan norþ ende sette þene king to fleomen ut of þissen londe þat iherde þat chærde and þer wunede to driuen hine of londe þa was þæ king an his þonke swiþe bald and aȝæin him gon wende muchele his ferde toȝeines þan kinge to fleomen hine þenne hine biþohte swiken hu he mahte he sende to þen norþerne kinge and seide þat he wolde sahtnesse wurche and timliche him speken wiþ and makeȝen sehtnesse and griþ and beon saht and some swulc heo weoren broþeren and faren of þan ende to kinge and leten þene king habben his riche and his lond þene dæi and þe stude heo setten sæhnesse to makien and þerafter ful sone heo cumen tosomne com muchel biforen he wes to godes hond icoren þe studen hehte houenfeld þer sette his teld he lette sone arere a muchel cros and mare and hehten al his ferde fallen on heore cneowen and bidden þane almihti godd þurh his milde mihti mod þat he heom ȝiue mildze of heore misdede and ȝif þat griþ breke þat ure drihten hit awreke þa weren iended þas beden þa com him riden and word seide swikelest alre kinge þu art wilcume wunne þe is ȝeueþe hafue þu al þi kinelond ah nim þi seoluer and þi gold nim an hundred hunden nim an hundred haueken nim an hundred steden nim goldfah iwede and send þas gretinge to kinge and þus þu maht him wiþ makien þe sahtnesse and griþ and ich wulle a þine stude beon þat þa lufe scal wel iþeon and ȝet ich þe suggen wulle ane sunder rune hu þu mihte fon on þat hit ne buþ nauere undon and cleope mid þe tweien þat þine treowe men beon beien and ich wulle tweien to me þa wel scullen reden þa rad forþ a þan felde falsest alre kinge and rad a þene feld næfde he sper ne nænne sceld his sweord ut adroh and he ofsloh þis wes seint þe amurþered wes aquald and gon to fleonne mid alle his ferde þat isehȝen forþrihtes cnihtes and after heom setten mid allen heore mihten mucchel del heo sloȝen of þan monweorede and þe king uneþe gon awende and neoþeles he atræd þe seint biswac com to þissen londe to kinge and talde al þan kinge hu he iuaren hafden hit likede wel þan kinge buten for ane þinge hit ofþuhte him ful sone for þan swikedome nu hafde þe a morþe wes aquald ænne ælpine broþer nes þer nan oþer he wes icleoped þe wes a swiþe duhti mon þa þringes norþerne makeden hine to kinge for wa wes heom on life for heore lauerdes deþe nom to his hond al his broþer kinelond hafde emes sunen þe weoren swiþe prute gumen and ma of his cunne þa weoren modfulle heo hafden muchele onde to þan kinelonde and makeden mucchel unfriþ and ofte fuhten him wiþ and þohten hine aquellen for his kinelonden ah wes cniht sturne þat he þer cudde alle þa him beren onde he draf of þan londe hiȝendliche he heom quehte ouer þere þat nes þer nan to laue of þan þe him weoren laþe and heo gunnen wenden to þan kinge and menden heom to of þan kinge þat he heom idriuen ut hafde of al heore icunde and heo bisohten þene king of æstlonde þat heom fulste to foruarne and heo wolden bicumen his men and his monscipe heȝen ȝif he wolde fordon oþer slæn oþer ahon þa andswerede þe king of æstlonde at me nabbe ȝe nenne ræde for ich æm wiþ iuæid for ich aqualde wihteste alre kinge and his broþer is oht cniht and arþ heorte nawiht ȝif he me mihte cacchen he me wolde quellen ah fareþ to þe king is on londe and ȝif he me wulle sende þat folc of his londe vt of corwale cnihtes icudde and of walisce londe mid seolure and mid golde þenne wlle ich anan mid ærmþen igreten driuen hine of londe leoden to sconde oþer slan hine mid egge laþest alle ginge þas cnihtes gunnen wende to kinge to heo come mid falsæn dome þan kingen heo tolden al þat heo wolden hit ilomp an ane time to þan whitesunetide þat þe king hehte of londen comen al to lunden alle þe wolden his griþ and wiþ þan kinge habben friþ þider comen kinges and æc hereþringes þider comen eorles þider comen beornes biscpes þider comen and bocilerede men riche and hene þider heo comen alle alches cunnes leoden þa þene king lufeden and þe king a þan daiȝe his crune bar an hæfde þer wes muchel blisse mid balde þan kinge for þe king wes swiþe treowe mon his treouþe wel he iheold þa þas leoden alle iliþen weoren tosomne þa stod him up biuore kinge and þus he gon tellen on false his spellen lauerd we beoþ icumen alse þu hafdest iqueþen alle þine men iborne englisce and bruttisce eorles and beornes cnihtes and clærckes and we þine kinges þa beoþ þine underlinges ah seide æuere þat nulle he come nauere no þine heste iuorþen ah bihateþ hærm to don nert þu noht swa modi swa him is he forhoȝeþ ful iwis to isechen þine hiredes ah ȝif þu wult me lenen and þine læue iunnen and þu me wulle fulsten and ferde bitæchen and swa muchel of þine garsume god swa þe þunche ich wulle uorþ aneouste and faren ouer and þer makien ærmest alre kingen no scal he mid strenþe þene stude uinde þat ich hine nulle þe an hond sulle oþer quic oþer ded þat me þuncheþ god ræd and ȝif þu þis nult don þu scalt wurse underfon for is a swulc mon þine scome he wulle don þa andswarede þe kene ich hit þe sugge oueral haueþ forwal oþer he liþ ibedde ibunden mid ufele oþer uncuþe leoden icumen beoþ to his þeoden for nulle he nauere icnawen þat he nolde him to cumen þa ich hehte alle cumen mid griþe mid friþe and mid lufe ah ga þider ut anan ich wulle wiþ mine eorlen mine rune halden and minne red finden wheþer ich þe ȝetten wullen þa þing þe þu bede and ich wulle after senden aþele mine sonde and haten hine hiȝindliche cumen to mine riche þider ut eode an eorl wes his iuere and wes þerinne mid swiþe feole monne þus him spac þe king wes of englen ȝe beoþ mine men alle þa beoþ a þisse mote and ȝe habbeoþ alle iherd whæt king hafueþ iseid and hu he wulle taken on and king al fordon ȝif ic him lenen wulle mine leoden to vulste and ic wulle þat ȝe me reden of wlchere deden þa ich lete fordo þa ich lete hine cumen me to and ȝif he for mire sonde forsakeþ hider to cumene mine here ich lete seoþþen hine hene makien þa iwærþ abolȝen a welisc king in þe hepen he wes ihaten monnen wurþe him ȝeomerist for æuere he ænglisce men bihehte hærm þene meste þus seide of suþ wales he wes duc her nu me whæt ich þe wulle cuþe þu hauest þine willen iseid ah þis nis noht god red hit is swiþe ȝare þat bruttes comen here and mid him ure ældre þe bruttes weoren aþele and þis lond ieoden bruttisce leoden and longe hit walden after heore willen þa while þa hit wes on heore hond hit wes ihaten brutlond nu nabbe we of þan londe buten þene west ende þa bruttes hafden iwuned here wel feole wintre þa comen englisce men mid heore ufele craften heo weore wiȝelfulle and þis lond al biwunne and biswiken heore lauerd sonen and alle his leoden and ȝiuenen heore kinge ane heþene quene þa comen of sexlonde þa leoden us beoþ laþe þurh þere quene ure cun aqualden here and swa habbeoþ englisce men ure icunden atheolden þet we nauere seoþþen bisechen hit no mihten king is englisc and alswa ful iwis let þu þa hundes hannen togaderes eiþer freten oþer swa hund deþ his broþer and leten heore whelpes whæruen heom bisides elc oþer quelle þat þer nan quic no leue and ȝif cumeþ bufen and þat feht maȝen ouercumen we him sculleþ to luken and neouþer hine aleggen lond and his leoden and his laȝen uallen and ȝif biþ buuen and þat comp maȝen ouercumen þin aȝe mon is mid alle his kinelonda þenne hauest þu englisc lond to þire aȝere hond and alle þine wurþscipe þus þu miht biwinnen and libben a þin lif swa þe arle leofest biþ no findest þu nauermare mon þa þe durre haten on þa andswarede a mon þe bald wes on hireden lust nu me lust me ane stunden nis þar nan betere red þene haueþ ised and ȝif þat nult don þu scalt wurse afon and alle þine leoden þa later þu hafuest to neoden efne þissere saȝe þa þe sæide þa wes icleoped and com into hirede and him ȝette al þat he wolde þa wes bliþe and igladed swiþe and his cnihtes to horsen forþrihtes and aneousten gunnen wenden toward norhhumberlonden and iherden suggen þat hine sohte and ȝarecode his ferden and fusde toȝæines faht heo bigunnen ræȝe heo weoren beien feondliche heo fuhten uæiden heo weoren vnimete feollen fæie men on folden þa hit wes uppen non þa sunne gon to nipen þer wes ofslaȝen and idon of lifdaȝen and his sune and his æm and eorles sume uiuen þer weoren niȝe þusunde þringes norþerne islaȝen i þan dæiȝe þa duȝeþe wes þa lasse and þe king sære wes iwunded þa and þonene gon wende æst to his londe hæfden ænne sune wes his nome he wes ane stunde mid kinge in his hirede iued and deorliche ifostred bisohte swa mon scal his lauerde don þat he moste beon his mon and his fader lond habbeon him ȝet al þat he ȝirde he bitahte him an hond al his fader kinelond hehte hine hit habben and halde mid wunne god king wes swa him wes icunden he wes king hire seouen and feouwerti ȝere þa uerde he to lunden to gladien þa leoden and heold ane metsunge mid þan uolke of lundene he æt of ane uisce uretliche swiþe ær þe uisc ieten weore iuueled was þe king seouen niht and enne dæi þe king a þan ufele læi nes þer nan oþer red seoþþen wes þe king ded heo bureden hine in lunden særi weoren þa leoden enne sune hafde ihaten he wes suster sune al of kingen icume þeos feng to his riche after his fader daiȝe swiþe leoflic wes þe mon his leoden hine luueden he wes swiþe god cniht and swiþe sturne inne fiht æh an his daȝen ilompen reoþen on leoden ærst aswond þat corn here ȝeond al þas kineriche þerafter hit wes swa deore and al folc gon to deȝen swa þat þu mihtes fare fulle seouen nihte þat no mihtest þu þurh nene chep finde neouwer na bred an burȝe and on londe leoden weoren ȝeoumere no nan uolc on londe þat offingred nes sære þa þat wes idriuuen longe ȝeond þas leoden þa com þer anoþer sorȝe þerafter ful sone þat quale com on orue vnimete swiþe þer cheorl draf his sulȝe ioxned swiþe fæire oþer while he brohte ham halue his oxen oþer brohte enne þe oþer no brohte nenne and swa hit on leode ilaste wel longe þerafter sone sorȝen vnimete comen to folke ȝeond al þas kineþeode uppen þan monen morþ wes iwurþen quelen þa eorles quelen þa beornes quelen þa þeines quelen þa sweines quelen þa lareden quelen þa leouweden quelan þa ældren quelen þa ȝeongeren quelæn þa wifmen quelen þa wanclen þat no mihte on þan ende þat folc on þan londe burien þa dede swiþe heo gunnen deȝe þat ofte in þan putte þer me þene dede isette þer deiȝede þe quike uppen þen dede and swa hit ilomp wide ȝeond ænglene þeode þat folc ut of londe flah on ælche ænde monie hundred tunen bilæued weoren of monnen þat lut me uinde mihte men uaren ȝeond londe wa wæs þe king wes on londe for scome he ne mihte fleon no for hærme her beon neoþeles he hine biþohte hu he faren mahte he nom his maþmes alle and his men deore and bah suþ ouer sæ into brutaine and nom þer wickinge mid alaine þan kinge þe wæs sune þas sele kinges þe swiþe lufede þe while his daiȝes ilaste þær alæin þe king underueng and funde him in þan londe al þat he wolde þurh elleouen ȝere þe king wunede þere and elleouen ȝere þe sorhȝe wunede here þat wes hunger and hette nefede þat folc nenne mete and þe qualm muchele þe wes on moncunne þat folc flah into wuden and wuneden in þe cluden leien in þa stangraffen and liueden bi deoren heo liueden bi wuden heo lifeden bi wurten bi moren and bi rote nas þer nan oþer boten þa elleue ȝer weoren on fast aȝeongen þa sunne gon to scine þe rein bigon to rine þe qualm gon to stunte men gunnen to sturien ut of wude heo droȝen and wuneden in tunen heo speken tosomne and spileden bitweonen and nomen heore sonde and sende into sexlonde and cudden heore cunne of heore qualesiþe and hu heo ifaren hafden elleue ȝeren and hu þat ufel wes atstunt and hu þa tunes ibuld and hu þer wes fæiȝer lond inoh seoluer and gold and beden heom cumen swiþe hider to heore icunde for þa bruttes þa ær weoren here æuere heo weren fleme no durste heo næuere mængen imong englisce monnen no nawhit heo nusten of heore uarecosten þat weoren heore sonden isend to sexlonden þa heȝe sexisce men iherden þas sonden þa fusden touward sæ fifti þusende baldere beornen mid scelden and mid burnen mid wifen and mid children to þissen londe wenden mid þan formeste swipen her comen þreo hundred scipen siȝen after seoþþe sixti tosomne bi sixe bi seouene bi tene bi eolleue bi twelue bi twenti bi þritti bi feowerti mid heom com þe æþele ut of sexen inne lundene hine cruneden and houen hine to kingen edward þe king þesne biȝat on are chiuese þis wes þe formeste englisce mon þe al ænglelond biwon he wes icruned and ieled þis lond wes al his aȝen and seoþþen he wuneden here sixtene ȝere hit ilomp inne frimdæȝen feor her biæften þat her wes an heh mon inne wes ihaten þe king wende to rome to þan heȝe dome and he weofed þere wunliche isohte brohte þer to lake his maþmes leofe þa ȝet he dude mare to are of æuerelche huse þat husbonde wunede and his biweddede wif weore on þere ilke wike þe king enne peni ȝette to huse inne wes þe uormeste mon þe peni bigon þa inne king wes him ded and his laȝen weoren aleid þa afeol þat feoh here fif and sixti ȝere a þet com liþen into þissen londen and hafden iwuned here fulle fiftene ȝere þe king his fet custe and faire hine igrette and eft þat ilke feoh ȝete þat inne king dude ære and swa hit hafeþ ist onde æuer seoþþe a þisse londe drihten wat hu longe þeo laȝen scullen ilæste þa tiden comen sone to kinge into brutaine þer þar he wunede mid alaine kinge þe wes of his cunne me dude him to understonde of al þisse londe hu her com liþen ut of sexlonden and hu he al anglelond sette on his aȝere hond and hu he sette moting and hu he sette husting and hu he sette sciren and makede friþ of deoren and hu he sette halimot and hu he sette hundred and þa nomen of þan tunen on sexisce runen and ȝilden he gon rere mucle and swiþe mære and þa chirchen he gon dihten after sexisce irihten and sexis he gan kennen þa nomen of þan monnen and al me him talde þe tiden of þisse londe wa wes þat he wes on liue leofere him weore on deþe þeone quic on life særi wes his heorte and sorhful wes his duȝeþe wiþ his freond he spac ofte hu he faren mihte and iwinnen his rihte and wulchere wise he mihte wiþ fihte and iwinnen his cunde æft to his honde þa and his cnihtes eke heolde mid unrihte sume him radde to uehten summe wriþ to wurchen þat he mosten of halden his lond and beon his mon vnder þissen uarecoste he sumnede ferde of alle þane monne þat he biȝeten mihte and somnede alle þa scipen þa bi þare sæ fluten and þohte mid strengþe steppen to londe þa þe ȝaru wes þa uerde and þas scipen ibone com þe wind suþerne þa sæt an heore wille þa sæide þe king nu to scipe an hiȝing and þe king into chirche gon wenden godes werk to worchen and masse þer iherden of mære ane preoste þe king læi on cneouwen and cleopede to and bed ure drihten þe walt alle deden þat he from himselue taken him sende ȝif hit weore iqueme þan heouenliche deme wheþer he scolde liþen þe he scolde bilauen þe while þe he spac touward goden þa gon he to slepen þa gon he to slumme selehþe him wes ȝiueþe of seoluen ure drihten þe scop þis dæȝes lihte þenne þe king imætte a cneouwen he slepte þat him com biforen gon a wunder ane fair mon and þas word kende to bruttene kinge awake þe haueþ deore and ȝarke þine uore and far swiþe to rome þu uindest ænne pape preost mid þan bezste he þe scal scriuen of þine weorldlifen þat hine sunen alle scullen þe from falle and þu scalt wurþe clene al þurh godes dome of alle þine misdede þurh mihte of ure drihte and seoþþen þu scalt iwiten and faren to heofnerichen for no most þu naueremære ænglelond aȝe ah alemainisce men ænglen scullen aȝen and næuermære bruttisce men bruken hit ne moten ær cume þe time þe iqueþen wes while þat þe witeȝe bodede mid worde þenne sculle bruttes sone buȝen to rome and draȝen ut þine banes alle of þene marmestane and mid blissen heom uerien uorþ mid heomseoluen in seoluere and in golde into brutlonde þenne sculle bruttes anan balde iwurþen al þat heo biginneþ to done iwurþeþ after heore wille þenne scullen i bruttene blissen wurþen riue wastmes and wederes sele after heore iwille þa awoc wunder him þuhte strongliche he wes auæred ladliche offurhte to wulche þinge hit iteon wolde þat him wes itacned þere ofte he lette runen ofte he lette ræde and seowede hit þan kinge þe wunede in þan londe þe inemned wes alain nexte mæi þe king sende his sonde ȝeond al his londe and lette beoden alle þa bocares wise and talden heom þa tacninge of kinge þær heo gunnen ræde þer heo gunnen rune and radden him to taken on al swa godd him hafde itakned to don þer he bilafde his scipen and his leode his wæi and his iwille he cleopede heom to stille and iuore beiȝen heo weoren him deore wes his stepsune and his suster sune beien heo weoren him leofe beine heo weoren him deore heo weoren cnihtes beien and swiþe wel idihte þus spac þe king wes of bruttene and beiene ȝet senden of mine leode hercnieþ mine lare no scal hit eou reouwe nauere of heouene me beoþ icume hiȝe godes tacne þat ich scal faren to rome to þan pape wel idone þe pape hatte sergius he weteþ hus me and mine wiue he scal bletseiȝen and scriue and þer we scullen ure daȝes ba driuen to þan ende longe biþ auer no iseo ȝe me æft næuere ah here ich bitache inc walisc lond þat ȝet stond a mire hond and nimeþ þas muchele uerde and fareþ to þan londe and haldeþ hit on wunne þa wile ȝe maȝen hit werie and ich inc halsi beien þurh þan heouen kinge þat unker æiþer oþer luuie swa his broþer and habbeoþ þat lond auermære tou æure liues ende and brukeþ hit on wunne and eouwer bernen alle hit wes itacned me alse ȝe scullen nu iseo for þe wise hit seide mid worde al of mine forþfare and of mire unimete care and sibillie þa wise a bocken hit isette þat ich scal iuullen mines drihtes wille alc faren nu his wæi and habbeoþ alle godne dæi fusde þat he com to rome þer he sergius funde þene iselie pape he scraf þe king wes of bruttenne ne wunede þe king þer bute uifte half ȝere þa com him ufel on swa godd hit wolde habben idon elleoue daȝes biforen maiȝe he ferde of þisse liue and his saule sende to þan heouenlicche kinge his ban beoþ iloken faste i guldene cheste and þer heo scullen wunie þat þa daȝes beon icumene þa ine iuurn daȝen vastnede mid worden ga we nu to aȝan and to iuore his weddebroþere heo somneden ferde wide ȝeond þan ærde forþ heo gunnen fusen mid fif hundred scipenen nes hit nawit longe þat heo ne comen to walisce londe al þas bruttes weoren todriuen ȝeond cludes and ȝeond cliuenen ȝeond chirchen and ȝeond muneccliuen ȝeond wudes and ȝeond liþen sone me heom saiden þat isiȝen weoren to londe mid iuore and ten siþen fifti scipen bradefulle of brutten swiþe balde þæs bruttes on ælc ende foren to walisce londe and heore laȝen leofeden and heore leodene þæuwen and ȝet wunieþ þære swa heo doþ aueremære and ænglisce kinges walden þas londes and bruttes hit loseden þis lond and þas leoden þat næuere seoþþen mære kinges neoren here þa ȝet ne com þæs ilke dæi beo heonneuorþ alse hit mæi iwurþe þet iwurþe iwurþe godes wille
